atha śrīśivamahāpurāṇaṃ vidyeśvarasaṃhitā prārabhyate ।। śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ ।। śrīgurubhyo namaḥ ।। śrisarasvatyai namaḥ ।।
atha śivapuraṇe prathamā vidyeśvarasaṃhitāprārabhyate ।। ādyantamaṃgalamajātasamānabhāvamāryaṃ tamīśamajarāmaramātmadevam ।।pañcānanaṃ prabalapañcavinodaśīlaṃ saṃbhāvaye manasiśaṃkaramambikeśam ।। chapter vyāsa uvāca dharmakṣetre mahākṣetre gaṃgākālindisaṃgame ।।prayāge parame puṇye brahmalokasya vartmani ।।munayaḥ śaṃsitātmanassatyavrataparāyaṇāḥ ।।mahaujaso mahābhāgā mahāsatraṃ vitenire ।।tatra satraṃ samākarṇya vyāsaśiṣyo mahāmuniḥ ।।ājagāma munīndraṣṭuṃ sūtaḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ ।।taṃ dṛṣṭvā sūtamāyāṃtaṃ harṣitā munayastadā ।।cetasā suprasannena pūjāṃ cakruryathāvidhi ।।tato vinayasaṃyuktā procuḥ sāṃjalayaścate ।।suprasannā mahātmānaḥ stutiṃ kṛtvāyathāvidhi ।।romaharṣaṇa sarvajña bhavān vai bhāgyagauravāt ।।purāṇavidyāmakhilāṃ vyāsātpratyarthamīyivān ।।tasmādāścaryabhūtānāṃ kathānāṃ tvaṃ hi bhājanam ।।ratnānāmurusārāṇāṃ ratnākara ivārṇavaḥ ।।yacca bhūtaṃ ca bhavyaṃ ca yaccānyadvastu vartate ।।na tvayā aviditaṃ kiṃcittriṣu lokeṣu vidyate ।।tvaṃ maddiṣṭavaśādasya darśanārthamihāgataḥ ।।kurvankimapi naḥ śreyo na vṛthā gaṃtumarhasi ।।tattvaṃ śrutaṃ sma naḥ sarvaṃ pūrvameva śubhāśubham ।।na tṛptimadhigacchāmaḥ śravaṇecchā muhurmuhuḥ paradravyābhilāṣiṇaḥ ।।parastrīsaktamanasaḥ parahiṃsāparāyaṇāḥ ।।dehātmadṛṣṭayā mūḍhā nāstikāḥ paśubuddhayaḥ ।।mātṛpitṛkṛtadveṣāḥ strīdevāḥ kāmakiṃkarāḥ ।।viprā lobhagrahagrastā vedavikrayajīvinaḥ krūrasvabhāvā malināśayāḥ ।।kṣatriyāśca tathā sarve svadharmatyāgaśīlinaḥ ।।asatsaṃgāḥ pāparatā vyabhicāraparāyaṇāḥ ।।aśūrā araṇaprītāḥ palāyanaparāyaṇāḥ ।।kucauravṛttayaḥ śūdrāḥ kāmakiṃkaracetasaḥ ।।śastrāstravidyayā hīnā dhenuviprāvanojjhitāḥ ।।śaraṇyāvanahīnāśca kāminyūtimṛgāssadā ।।prajāpālanasaddharmavihīnā bhogatatparāḥ ।।prajāsaṃhārakā duṣṭā jīvahiṃsākarā mudā ।।vaiśyāḥ saṃskārahīnāste acyutamāyataśramaṃ pranaṣṭaharṣaṃ tu nanarta harṣāt ।।uvāca cainaṃ paramārthamacyutaṃ ṣaṃḍhāttavādaḥ sa vidhistato acyutam ।।staṃbhāgrametatsamudīkṣitaṃ hare tatraiva sākṣī nanu ketakaṃ tvidam ।।tato avadattatra hi ketakaṃ mṛṣā tatheti taddhātṛvacastadaṃtike ।।hariśca tatsatyamitīva ciṃtayaṃścakāra tasmai vidhaye namaḥ svayam ।।ṣoḍaśairupacāraiśca pūjayāmāsa taṃ vidhim ।।vidhiṃ prahartuṃ śaṭhamagniliṃgataḥ sa īśvarastatra babhūva sākṛtiḥ ।।samutthitaḥ svāmi vilokanātpunaḥ prakaṃpapāṇiḥ parigṛhya tatpadam ।।ādyaṃtahīnavapuṣi tvayi mohabuddhyā bhūyādvimarśa iha nāvati kāmanotthaḥ ।।sa tvaṃ prasīda karuṇākara kaśmalaṃ nau mṛṣṭaṃ kṣamasva vihitaṃ bhavataiva kelyā ।।īśvara uvāca vatsaprasanno asmi hare yatastvamīśatvamicchannapi satyavākyam ।।brūyāstataste bhavitā janeṣu sāmyaṃ mayā satkṛtirapyalapthāḥ ।।itaḥ paraṃ te pṛthagātmanaśca kṣetrapratiṣṭhotsavapūjanaṃ ca ।।iti devaḥ purā prītaḥ satyena haraye param ।।dadau svasāmyamatyarthaṃ devasaṃghe ca paśyati ।। chapter nandikeśvara uvāca sasarjātha mahādevaḥ puruṣaṃ kaṃcidadbhutam ।।bhairavākhyaṃ bhruvormadhyādbrahmadarpajighāṃsayā ।।sa vai tadā tatra patiṃ praṇamya śivamaṃgaṇe ।।kiṃ kāryaṃ karavāṇyatra śīghramājñāpaya prabho ।।vatsayo ayaṃ vidhiḥ sākṣājjagatāmādyadaivatam ।।nūnamarcaya khaḍgaṃ svaṃ tigmena javasā param ।।sa vai gṛhītvaikakareṇa keśaṃ tatpañcamaṃ dṛptamasatyabhāṣaṇam ।।chittvā śirāṃsyasya nihaṃtumudyataḥ prakaṃpayankhaḍgamatisphuṭaṃ karaiḥ ।।pitā tavotsṛṣṭavibhūṣaṇāṃbarasraguttarīyāmalakeśasaṃhatiḥ ।।pravātaraṃbheva lateva caṃcalaḥ papāta vai bhairavapādapaṃkaje ।।tāvadvidhiṃ tāta didṛkṣuracyutaḥ kṛpālurasmatpatipādapallavam ।।niṣicya bāṣpairavadatkṛtāṃjaliryathā śiśuḥ svaṃ pitaraṃ kalākṣaram ।।acyuta uvāca tvayā prayatnena purā hi dattaṃ yadasya pañcānanamīśacihnam ।।tasmātkṣamasvādyamanugrahārhaṃ kuru prasādaṃ vidhaye hyamuṣmai ।।ityarthito acyuteneśastuṣṭaḥ suragaṇāṃgaṇe ।।nivartayāmāsa tadā bhairavaṃ brahmadaṃḍataḥ ।।athāha devaḥ kitavaṃ vidhiṃ vigatakaṃdharam ।।brahmaṃstvamarhaṇākāṃkṣī śaṭhamīśatvamāsthitaḥ ।।nātaste satkṛtirloke bhūyātsthānotsavādikam ।।brahmovaca svāminprasīdādya mahāvibhūte manye varaṃ varada me śirasaḥ pramokṣam ।।namastubhyaṃ bhagavate baṃdhave viśvayonaye ।।sahiṣṇave sarvadoṣāṇāṃ śaṃbhave śailadhanvane ।।īśvara uvāca arājabhayametadvai jagatsarvaṃ na śiṣyati ।।tatastvaṃ jahi daṃḍārhaṃ vaha lokadhuraṃ śiśo ।।varaṃ dadāmi te tatra gṛhāṇa durlabhaṃ param ।।vaitānikeṣu gṛhyeṣu yajñe ca bhavān guruḥ ।।niṣphalastvadṛte yajñaḥ sāṃgaśca sahadakṣiṇaḥ ।।athāha devaḥ kitavaṃ ketakaṃ kūṭasākṣiṇam ।।re re ketaka duṣṭastvaṃ śaṭha dūramito vraja ।।mamāpi prema te puṣpe mā bhūtpūjāsvitaḥ param ।।ityukte tatra devena ketakaṃ devajātayaḥ ।।sarvāni vārayāmāsustatpārśvādanyatastadā ।।ketaka uvāca namaste nātha me janmaniṣphalaṃ bhavadājñayā ।।saphalaṃ kriyatāṃ tāta kṣamyatāṃ mama kilbiṣam ।।jñānājñānakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ nāśayatyeva te smṛtiḥ ।।tādṛśe tvayi dṛṣṭe me mithyādoṣaḥ kuto bhavet ।।tathā stutastu bhagavānketakena sabhātale ।।na me tvaddhāraṇaṃ yogyaṃ satyavāgahamīśvaraḥ ।।madīyāstvāṃ dhariṣyaṃi janma te saphalaṃ tataḥ ।।tvaṃ vai vitānavyājena mamopari bhaviṣyasi ।।ityanugṛhya bhagavānketakaṃ vidhimādhavau ।।virarāja sabhāmadhye sarvadevairabhiṣṭutaḥ ।। chapter nandikeśvara uvāca tatrāṃtare tau ca nāthaṃ praṇamya vidhimādhavau ।।baddhāṃjalipuṭau tūṣṇīṃ tasthaturdakṣavāmagau ।।tatra saṃsthāpya tau devaṃ sakuṭuṃbaṃ varāsane ।।pūjayāmāsatuḥ pūjyaṃ puṇyaiḥ puruṣavastubhiḥ ।।pauruṣaṃ prākṛtaṃ vastujñeyaṃ dīrghālpakālikam ।।hāranūpurakeyūrakirīṭamaṇikuṃḍalaiḥ ।।yajñasūtrottarīyasrakkṣaumamālyāṃgulīyakaiḥ ।।puṣpatāṃbūlakarpūracaṃdanāgurulepanaiḥ ।।dhūpadīpasitacchatravyajanadhvajacāmaraiḥ ।।anyairdivyopahāraiśca vāṅmanotītavaibhavaiḥ ।।patiyogyaiḥ mahānāsīttatra tadvastu gṛhṇatām ।।tatraiva brahmaviṣṇubhyāṃ cārcitaḥ śaṃkaraḥ purā ।।prasannaḥ prāha tau namrau sasmitaṃ bhaktivardhanaḥ ।।īśvara uvāca tuṣṭo ahamadya vāṃ vatsau pūjayā asminmahādine ।।dinametattataḥ puṇyaṃ bhaviṣyati mahattaram ।।śivarātririti khyātā tithireṣā mama priyā ।।etatkāle tu yaḥ kuryātpūjāṃ malliṃgaberayoḥ ।।kuryāttu jagataḥ kṛtyaṃ sthitisargādikaṃ pumān ।।śivarātrāvahorātraṃ nirāhāro jiteṃdriyaḥ ।।arcayedvā yathānyāyaṃ yathābalamavaṃcakaḥ ।।yatphalaṃ mama pūjāyāṃ varṣamekaṃ niraṃtaram ।।tatphalaṃ labhate sadyaḥ śivarātrau madarcanāt ।।nānyasya kasyacittasmādanyaḥ sarvopyanīśvaraḥ ।।purastātstaṃbharūpeṇa paścādrūpeṇa cārbhakau ।।brahmatvaṃ niṣkalaṃ proktamīśatvaṃ sakalaṃ tathā ।।dvayaṃ mamaiva saṃsiddhaṃ na madanyasya kasyacit ।।tasmādīśatvamanyeṣāṃ yuvayorapi na kvacit ।।tadajñānena vāṃ vṛttamīśamānaṃ mahādbhutam ।।tannirākartumatraivamutthito ahaṃ raṇakṣitau ।।tyajataṃ mānamātmīyaṃ mayīśe kurutaṃ matim ।।matprasādena ।।anugrahādyaṃ sargāṃgaṃ jagatkṛtyaṃ ca paṃkajam ।।īśatvādeva me nityaṃ na madanyasya kasyacit ।।ādau brahmattvabuddhyarthaṃ niṣkalaṃ liṃgamutthitam ।।tasmādajñātamīśatvaṃ vyaktaṃ dyotayituṃ hi vām ।।sakalohamato jātaḥ sākṣādīśastu tatkṣaṇāt ।।sakalatvamato jñeyamīśatvaṃ mayi satvaram ।।yadidaṃ niṣkalaṃ staṃbhaṃ mama brahmatvabodhakam ।।liṃgalakṣaṇayuktatvānmama liṃgaṃ bhavedidam ।।tadidaṃ saberamapi sarvataḥ ।। chapter brahmaviṣṇū ūcatuḥ sargādipañcakṛtyasya lakṣaṇaṃ brūhi nau prabho ।।śiva uvāca matkṛtyabodhanaṃ guhyaṃ kṛpayā prabravīmi vām ।।sṛṣṭiḥ sthitiśca saṃhārastirobhāvo ।।sṛṣṭirbhūmau sthitistoye saṃhāraḥ pāvake tathā ।।tirobhāvo anile tadvadanugraha ihāmbare ।।sṛjyate dharayā sarvamadbhiḥ sarvaṃ pravardhate ।।ardyate tejasā sarvaṃ vāyunā cāpanīyate ।।vyomnānugṛhyate sarvaṃ jñeyamevaṃ hi sūribhiḥ ।।pañcakṛtyamidaṃ boḍhuṃ mamāsti mukhapañcakam ।।caturdikṣu caturvaktraṃ tanmadhye pañcamaṃ mukham ।।yuvābhyāṃ tapasā labdhametatkṛtyadvayaṃ sutau ।।sṛṣṭisthityabhīdhaṃ bhāgyaṃ mattaḥ prītādatipriyam ।।tathā rudramaheśābhyāmanyatkṛtyadvayaṃ param ।।anugrahākhyaṃ kenāpi labdhuṃ naiva hi śakyate ।।tatsarvaṃ paurvikaṃ karma yuvābhyāṃ kālavismṛtam ।।na tadrudra maheśābhyāṃ vismṛtaṃ karma tādṛśam ।।rūpe veśe ca kṛtye ca vāhane cāsane tathā ।।āyudhādau ca matsāmyamasmābhistatkṛte kṛtam ।।maddhyānavirahādvatsau mauḍhyaṃ vāmevamāgatam ।।majjñāne sati naivaṃ syānmānaṃ rūpe maheśavat ।।tasmānmajjñānasiddhyarthaṃ maṃtramoṃkāranāmakam ।।itaḥ paraṃ prajapataṃ māmakaṃ mānabhaṃjanam ।।upādiśaṃ nijaṃ maṃtramoṃkāramurumaṃgalam ।।oṃkāro manmukhājjajñe prathamaṃ matprabodhakaḥ ।।vācako ayamahaṃ vācyo maṃtro ayaṃ hi madātmakaḥ ।।tadanusmaraṇaṃ nityaṃ mamānusmaraṇaṃ bhavet ।।akārauttarātpūrvamukāraḥ paścimānanāt ।।makāro dakṣiṇamukhādbiṃduḥ prāṅmukhatastathā ।।nādo madhyamukhādevaṃ pañcadhā asau vijṛṃbhitaḥ ।।ekībhūtaḥ punastadvadomityekākṣaro bhavet ।।nāmarūpātmakaṃ sarvaṃ vedabhūtakuladvayam ।।vyāptametena maṃtreṇa śivaśaktyośca bodhakaḥ ।।asmātpañcākṣaraṃ jajñe bodhakaṃ sakalasyatat ।।ākārādikrameṇaiva nakārādiyathākramam ।।asmātpañcākṣarājjātā mātṛkāḥ pañcabhedataḥ ।।tasmācchiraścaturvaktrāttripādgāya trireva hi ।।vedaḥ sarvastato jajñe tato vai maṃtrakoṭayaḥ ।।tattanmaṃtreṇa tatsiddhiḥ sarvasiddhirito bhavet ।।anena maṃtrakaṃdena bhogo mokṣaśca siddhyati ।।sakalā maṃtrarājānaḥ sākṣādbhogapradāḥ śubhāḥ ।।naṃdikeśvara uvāca punastayostatra tiraḥ paṭaṃ guruḥ prakalpya maṃtraṃ ca samādiśatparam ।।nidhāya tacchīrṣṇi karāṃbujaṃ śanairudaṅmukhaṃ saṃsthitayoḥ sahāṃbikaḥ ।।triruccāryāgrahīnmaṃtraṃ yaṃtrataṃtroktipūrvakam ।।śiṣyau ca tau dakṣiṇāyāmātmānaṃ ca samarpayat ।।prabaddhahastau kila tau tadaṃtike tameva devaṃ jagaturjagadgurum ।।brahmācyutāvūcatuḥ namo niṣkalarūpāya namo niṣkalatejase ।।namaḥ sakalanāthāya ।।sakalākalarūpāya śaṃbhave gurave namaḥ ।।iti stutvā guruṃ padyairbrahmā viṣṇuś ca nematuḥ ।।īśvara uvāca vatsakau sarvatattvaṃ ca kathitaṃ darśitaṃ ca vām ।।japataṃ praṇavaṃ maṃtraṃ devīdiṣṭaṃ madātmakam ।।jñānaṃ ca susthiraṃ bhāgyaṃ sarvaṃ bhavati śāśvatam ।।ārdrāyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ tajjāpyaṃ tvakṣayaṃ bhavet ।।sūryagatyā mahārdrāyāmekaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet ।।mṛgaśīrṣāṃtimo bhāgaḥ punarvasvādimastathā ।।ārdrāsamaḥ sadā jñeyaḥ pūjāhomāditarpaṇe ।।darśanaṃ tu prabhāte ca prātaḥsaṃgavakālayoḥ ।।caturdaśī tathā grāhyā niśīthavyāpinī bhavet ।।pradoṣavyāpinī caiva parayuktā praśasyate ।।liṃgaṃ beraṃ ca metulyaṃ yajatāṃ liṃgamuttamam ।।tasmālliṃgaṃ paraṃ pūjyaṃ berādapi mumukṣubhiḥ ।।liṃgamoṃkāramaṃtreṇa beraṃ pañcākṣareṇa tu ।।svayameva hi dravyaiḥ pratiṣṭhāpyaṃ parairapi ।।pūjayedupacāraiśca matpadaṃ sulabhaṃ bhavet ।।iti śāsya tathā śiṣyau tatraivāṃ atarhitaḥ śivaḥ ।।
chapter ṛṣaya ūcuḥ kathaṃ liṃgaṃ pratiṣṭhāpyaṃ kathaṃ vātasya lakṣaṇam ।।kathaṃ vā tatsamabhyarcyaṃ deśe kāle ca kena hi ।।sūta uvāca yuṣmadarthaṃ pravakṣyāmi buddhyatāmavadhānataḥ ।।anukūle śubhe kāle puṇye tīrthe taṭe tathā ।।yatheṣṭaṃ liṃgamāropyaṃ yatra syānnityamarcanam ।।pārthivena tathāpyenaṃ taijasena yathāruci ।।kalpalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ liṃgaṃ pūjāphalaṃ labhet ।।sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ sadyaḥ pūjāphalapradam ।।care viśiṣyate sūkṣmaṃ sthāvare sthūlameva hi ।।salakṣaṇaṃ sapīṭhaṃ ca sthāpayecchivanirmitam ।।maṃḍalaṃ caturasraṃ vā trikoṇamathavā tathā ।।khaṭvāṃgavanmadhyasūkṣmaṃ liṃgapīṭhaṃ mahāphalaṃ ।।prathamaṃ mṛcchilādibhyo ligaṃ lohādibhiḥ kṛtam ।।yena liṃgaṃ tena pīṭhaṃ sthāvare hi viśiṣyate ।।liṃgaṃ pīṭhaṃ care tvekaṃ liṃgaṃ bāṇakṛtaṃ vinā ।।liṃgapramāṇaṃ kartḥṇāṃ dvādaśāṃgulamuttamam ।।nyūnaṃ cetphalamalpaṃ syādadhikaṃ naiva dūṣyate ।।karturekāṃgulanyūnaṃ carepi ca tathaiva hi ।।ādau vimānaṃ śilpena kāryaṃ devagaṇairyutam ।।tatra garbhagṛhe ramye dṛḍhe darpaṇasaṃnibho bhūṣite ।।navaratnaiśca digdvāre ca pradhānakaiḥ ।।nīlaṃ raktaṃ ca vai dūryaṃ śyāmaṃ mārakataṃ tathā ।।muktāpravālagomedavajrāṇi navaratnakam ।।madhye liṃgaṃ mahaddravyaṃ nikṣipetsahavaidike ।।saṃpūjya liṃgaṃ sadyādyaiḥ pañcasthāne yathākramam ।।agnau ca hutvā bahudhā haviṣāsa kalaṃ ca mām ।।abhyarcya gurumācāryamarthaiḥ kāmaiśca bāṃdhavam ।।dadyādaiśvaryamarthibhyo jaḍamapyajaḍaṃ tathā ।।sthāvaraṃ jaṃgamaṃ jīvaṃ sarvaṃ saṃtoṣya yatnataḥ ।।suvarṇapūrite śvabhre navaratnaiśca pūrite ।।sadyādi brahma coccārya dhyātvā devaṃ paraṃ śubham ।।udīrya ca mahāmaṃtramoṃkāraṃ nādaghoṣitam ।।liṃgaṃ tatra pratiṣṭhāpya ligaṃ pīṭhena yojayet ।।liṃgaṃ sapīṭhaṃ nikṣipya nityalepena baṃdhayet ।।evaṃ beraṃ ca saṃsthāpyaṃ tatraiva paramaṃ śubham ।।pañcākṣareṇa beraṃ tu utsavārthaṃ vahistathā ।।beraṃ gurubhyo gṛhṇīyātsādhubhiḥ pūjitaṃ tu vā ।।evaṃ liṃge ca bere ca pūjā śivapadapradā ।।punaśca dvividhaṃ proktaṃ sthāvaraṃ jaṃgamaṃ tathā ।।sthāvaraṃ liṃgamityāhustarugulmādikaṃ tathā ।।jaṃgamaṃ liṃgamityāhuḥ kṛmikīṭādikaṃ tathā ।।sthāvarasya ca śuśrūṣā jaṃgamasya ca tarpaṇam ।।tattatsukhānurāgeṇa śivapūjāṃ vidurbudhāḥ ।।pīṭhamaṃbāmayaṃ sarvaṃ śivaliṃgaṃ ca cinmayam ।।yathā devīmumāmaṃke dhṛtvā tiṣṭhati śaṃkaraḥ ।।tathā liṃgamidaṃ pīṭhaṃ dhṛtvā tiṣṭhati saṃtatam ।।evaṃ sthāpya mahāliṃgaṃ pūjayedupacārakaiḥ ।।nityapūjā yathā śaktidhvajādikaraṇaṃ tathā ।।iti saṃsthāpayelliṃgaṃ sākṣācchivapadapradam ।।athavā caraliṃgaṃ tu ṣoḍaśairupacārakaiḥ ।।pūjayecca yathānyāyaṃ kramācchivapadapradam ।।āvāhanaṃ cāsanaṃ ca arghyaṃ pādyaṃ tathaiva ca ।।tadaṃgācamanaṃ caiva snānamabhyaṃgapūrvakam ।।vastraṃ gaṃdhaṃ tathā puṣpaṃ dhūpaṃ dīpaṃ nivedanam ।।nīrājanaṃ ca tāṃbūlaṃ namaskāro visarjanam ।।athavā arghyādikaṃ kṛtvā naivedyāṃ taṃ yathāvidhi ।।athābhiṣekaṃ naivedyaṃ namaskāraṃ ca tarpaṇam ।।yathāśakti sadākuryātkramācchivapadapradam ।।athavā mānuṣe liṃgepyārṣe daive svayaṃbhuvi ।।sthāpite apūrvake liṃge sopacāraṃ yathā tathā ।।pūjopakaraṇe datte yatkiṃcitphalamaśnute ।।pradakṣiṇānamaskāraiḥ kramācchivapadapradam ।।liṃgaṃ darśanamātraṃ vā niyamena śivapradam ।।mṛtpiṣṭagośakṛtpuṣpaiḥ karavīreṇa vā phalaiḥ ।।guḍena navanītena bhasmanānnairyathāruci ।।liṃgaṃ yatnena kṛtvāṃte yajettadanusārataḥ ।।aṃguṣṭhādāvapi tathā pūjāmicchaṃti kecana ।।liṃgakarmaṇi sarvatra niṣedhosti na karhicit ।।sarvatra phaladātā hi prayāsānuguṇaṃ śivaḥ ।।athavā liṃgadānaṃ vā liṃgamaulyamathāpi vā ।।śraddhayā śivabhaktāya dattaṃ śivapadapradam ।।athavā praṇavaṃ nityaṃ japeddaśasahasrakam ।।saṃdhyayośca sahasraṃ vā jñeyaṃ śivapadapradam ।।japakāle makārāṃtaṃ manaḥśuddhikaraṃ bhajet ।।samādhau mānasaṃ proktamupāṃśu sārvakālikam ।।samānapraṇavaṃ cemaṃ biṃdunādayutaṃ viduḥ ।।atha pañcākṣaraṃ nityaṃ japedayutamādarāt ।।saṃdhyayośca sahasraṃ vā jñeyaṃ śivapadapradam ।।praṇavenādisaṃyuktaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ viśiṣyate ।।dīkṣāyuktaṃ gurorgrāhyaṃ maṃtraṃ hyatha phalāptaye ।।kuṃbhasnānaṃ maṃtradīkṣāṃ mātṛkānyāsameva ca ।।brāhmaṇaḥ satyapūtātmā gururjñānī viśiṣyate ।।dvijānāṃ ca namaḥpūrvamanyeṣāṃ ca namontakam ।।strīṇāṃ ca kvacidicchaṃti namo taṃ ca yathāvidhi ।।viprastrīṇāṃ namaḥ pūrvamidamicchaṃti kecana ।।pañcakoṭijapaṃ kṛtvā sadā śivasamo bhavet ।।ekadvitricatuḥkoṭyābrahmādīnāṃ padaṃ vrajet ।।japedakṣaralakṣaṃvā akṣarāṇāṃ pṛthakpṛthak ।।athavākṣaralakṣaṃ vā jñeyaṃ śivapadapradam ।।sahasraṃ tu sahasrāṇāṃ sahasreṇa dinena hi ।।japenmaṃtrādiṣṭasiddhirnityaṃ brāhmaṇabhojanāt ।।aṣṭottarasahasraṃ vai gāyatrīṃ prātareva hi ।।brāhmaṇastu japennityaṃ kramācchivapadapradān ।।vedamaṃtrāṃstu sūktāni japenniyamamāsthitaḥ ।।ekaṃ daśārṇaṃ maṃtraṃ ca śatonaṃ ca tadūrdhvakam ।।ayutaṃ ca sahasraṃ ca śatamekaṃ vinā bhavet ।।vedapārāyaṇaṃ caiva jñeyaṃ śivapadapradam ।।anyānbahutarānmaṃtrāñjapedakṣaralakṣataḥ ।।ekākṣarāṃstathā maṃtrāñjapedakṣarakoṭitaḥ ।।tataḥ paraṃ japeccaiva sahasraṃ bhaktipūrvakam ।।evaṃ kuryādyathāśakti kramācchiva padaṃ labhet ।।nityaṃ rucikaraṃ tvekaṃ maṃtramāmaraṇāṃtikam ।।japetsahasramomiti sarvābhīṣṭaṃ śivājñayā ।।puṣpārāmādikaṃ vāpi tathā saṃmārjanādikam ।।śivāya śivakāryāthe kṛtvā śivapadaṃ labhet ।।śivakṣetre tathā vāsaṃ nityaṃ kuryācca bhaktitaḥ ।।jaḍānāmajaḍānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ bhuktimuktidam ।।tasmādvāsaṃ śivakṣetre kuryadāmaraṇaṃ budhaḥ ।।liṃgāddhastaśataṃ puṇyaṃ kṣetre mānuṣake viduḥ ।।sahasrāratnimātraṃ tu puṇyakṣetre tathārṣake ।।daivaliṃge tathā jñeyaṃ sahasrāratnimānataḥ ।।dhanuṣpramāṇasāhasraṃ puṇyaṃ kṣetre svayaṃ bhuvi ।।puṇyakṣetre sthitā vāpī kūpādyapuṣkarāṇi ca ।।śivagaṃgeti vijñeyaṃ śivasya vacanaṃ yathā ।।tatra snātvā tathā dattvā japitvā hi śivaṃ vrajet ।।śivakṣetraṃ samāśritya vasedāmaraṇaṃ tathā ।।dāhaṃ daśāhaṃ māsyaṃ vā sapiṃḍīkaraṇaṃ tu vā ।।ābdikaṃ vā śivakṣetre kṣetre piṃḍamathāpi vā ।।sarvapāpa vinirmuktaḥ sadyaḥ śivapadaṃ labhet ।।athavā saptarātraṃ vā vasedvā pañcarātrakam ।।trirātramekarātraṃ vā kramācchivapadaṃ labhet ।।svavarṇānuguṇaṃ loke svācārātprāpnute ।।prātarvidhikaraṃ jñeyaṃ madhyāhnaṃ kāmikaṃ tathā ।।sāyāhnaṃ śāṃtikaṃ jñeyaṃ rātrāvapi tathaiva hi ।।kālo niśītho vai proktomadhyayāmadvayaṃ niśi ।।śivapūjā viśeṣeṇa tatkāle abhīṣṭasiddhidā ।।evaṃ jñātvā naraḥ kurvanyathoktaphalabhāgbhavet ।।kalau yuge viśeṣeṇa phalasiddhistu karmaṇā ।।uktena kenacidvāpi adhikāravibhedataḥ ।।sadvṛttiḥ pāpabhīruścettatatphalamavāpnuyāt ।।ṛṣaya ūcuḥ atha kṣetrāṇi puṇyāni samāsātkathayasva naḥ ।।sarvāḥ striyaśca puruṣā yānyāśritya padaṃ labhet ।।sūta yogivaraśreṣṭha śivakṣetrāgamāṃstathā ।।sūta uvāca śṛṇuta śraddhayā sarvakṣetrāṇi ca tadāgamān ।। chapter sūta uvāca śṛṇudhvamṛṣayaḥ prājñāḥ śivakṣetraṃ vimuktidam ।।tadāgamāṃstato vakṣye lokarakṣārthameva hi ।।pañcāśatkoṭivistīrṇā saśailavanakānanā ।।śivājñayā hi pṛthivī lokaṃ dhṛtvā ca tiṣṭhati ।।tatra tatra chapter ṛṣaya ūcuḥ deśādīnkramaśo brūhi sūta sarvārthavittam ।।sūta uvāca śuddhaṃ gṛhaṃ samaphalaṃ devayajñādikarmasu ।।tato daśaguṇaṃ goṣṭhaṃ jalatīraṃ tato daśa ।।tato daśaguṇaṃ bilvatulasyaśvatthamūlakam ।।tato devālayaṃ vidyāttīrthatīraṃ tato daśa ।।tato daśaguṇaṃ nadyāstīrthanadyāstato daśa ।।saptagaṃgānadītīraṃ tasyā daśaguṇaṃ bhavet ।।gaṃgā godāvarī caiva kāverī tāmraparṇikā ।।siṃdhuśca sarayū revā saptagaṃgāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।tato abdhitīraṃ daśa ca parvatāgre tato daśa ।।sarvasmādadhikaṃ jñeyaṃ yatra vā rocate manaḥ ।।kṛte pūrṇaphalaṃ jñeyaṃ yajñadānādikaṃ tathā ।।tretāyuge tripādaṃ ca dvāpare ardhaṃ sadā smṛtam ।।kalau pādaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ tatpādonaṃ tatordhake ।।śuddhātmanaḥ śuddhadinaṃ puṇyaṃ samaphalaṃ viduḥ ।।tasmāddaśaguṇaṃ jñeyaṃ ravisaṃkramaṇe budhāḥ ।।viṣuve taddaśaguṇamayane taddaśa smṛtam ।।taddaśa mṛgasaṃkrāṃtau taccaṃdragrahaṇe daśa ।।tataśca sūryagrahaṇe pūrṇakālottame viduḥ ।।jagadrūpasya sūryasya viṣayogācca rogadam ।।atastadviṣaśāṃtyarthaṃ snānadānajapāṃ caret ।।viṣaśāṃtyarthakālatvātsa kālaḥ puṇyadaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।janmarkṣe ca vratāṃte ca sūryarāgopamaṃ viduḥ ।।mahatāṃ saṃgakālaśca koṭyarkagrahaṇaṃ viduḥ ।।taponiṣṭhā jñānaniṣṭhā yogino yatayastathā ।।pūjāyāḥ pātramete hi pāpasaṃkṣayakāraṇam ।।caturviṃśatilakṣaṃ vā gāyatryā japasaṃyutaḥ ।।brāhmaṇastu bhavetpātraṃ saṃpūrṇaphalabhogadam ।।patanāttrāyata iti pātraṃ śāstre prayujyate ।।dātuśca pātakāttrāṇātpātramityabhidhīyate ।।gāyakaṃ trāyate pātādgāyatrītyucyate hi sā ।।yathā arthahino loke asminparasyārthaṃ na yacchati ।।arthavāniha yo loke parasyārthaṃ prayacchati ।।svayaṃ śuddho hi pūtātmā narānsatrātumarhati ।।gāyatrījapaśuddho hi śuddhabrāhmaṇa ucyate ।।tasmāddāne jape home pūjāyāṃ sarvakarmaṇi ।।dānaṃ kartuṃ tathā trātuṃ pātraṃ tu brāhmaṇorhati ।।annasya kṣudhitaṃ pātraṃ nārīnaramayātmakam ।।brāhmaṇaṃ śreṣṭhamāhūya yatkāle susamāhitam ।।tadarthaṃ śabdamarthaṃ vā sadbodhakamabhīṣṭadam ।।icchāvataḥ pradānaṃ ca saṃpūrṇaphaladaṃ viduḥ ।।yatpraśnānaṃtaraṃ dattaṃ tadarthaphaladaṃ viduḥ ।।yatsevakāya dattaṃ syāttatpādaphaladaṃ viduḥ ।।jātimātrasya viprasya dīnavṛtterdvijarṣabhāḥ ।।dattamarthaṃ hi bhogāya bhūrlokedaśavārṣikam ।।vedayuktasya viprasya svarge hi daśavārṣikam ।।gāyatrījapayuktasya satye hi daśavārṣikam ।।viṣṇubhaktasya viprasya dattaṃ vaikuṃṭhadaṃ viduḥ ।।śivabhaktasya viprasya dattaṃ kailāsadaṃ viduḥ ।।tattallokopabhogārthaṃ sarveṣāṃ dānamiṣyate ।।daśāṃgamannaṃ viprasya bhānuvāre dadannaraḥ ।।parajanmani cārogyaṃ daśavarṣaṃ samaśnute ।।bahumānamathāhvānamabhyaṃgaṃ pādasevanam ।।vāso gaṃdhādyarcanaṃ ca ghṛtāpūparasottaram ।।ṣaḍrasaṃ vyaṃjanaṃ caiva tāṃbūlaṃ dakṣiṇottaram ।।namaścānugamaścaiva svannadānaṃ daśāṃgakam ।।daśāṃgamannaṃ viprebhyo daśabhyo vai dadannaraḥ ।।arkavāre tathā a arogyaṃ śatavarṣaṃ samaśnute ।।somavārādivāreṣu tattadvāraguṇaṃ phalam ।।annadānasya vijñeyaṃ bhūrloke parajanmani ।।saptasvapi ca vāreṣu daśabhyaśca daśāṃgakam ।।annaṃ dattvā śataṃ varṣamārogyādikamaśnute ।।evaṃ śatebhyo viprebhyo bhānuvāre dadannaraḥ ।।sahasravarṣamārogyaṃ śarvaloke samaśnute ।।sahasrebhyastathā dattvā ayutavarṣaṃ samaśnute ।।evaṃ somādivāreṣu vijñeyaṃ hi vipaścitā ।।bhānuvāre sahasrāṇāṃ gāyatrīpūtacetasām ।।annaṃ dattvā satyaloke hyārogyādi samaśnute ।।ayutānāṃ tathā dattvā viṣṇuloke samaśnute ।।annaṃ dattvā tu lakṣāṇāṃ rudraloke samaśnute ।।bālānāṃ brahmabuddhyā hi deyaṃ vidyārthibhirnaraiḥ ।।yūnāṃ ca viṣṇubuddhyā hi putrakāmārthibhirnaraiḥ ।।vṛddhānāṃ rudrabuddhyā hi deyaṃ jñānārthibhirnaraiḥ ।।bālastrībhāratībuddhyā buddhikāmairnarottamaiḥ ।।lakṣmībuddhyā yuvastrīṣu bhogakāmairnarottamaiḥ ।।vṛddhāsu pārvatībuddhyā deyamātmārthibhirjanaiḥ ।।śilavṛttyoñchavṛttyā ca gurudakṣiṇayārjitam ।।śuddhadravyamiti prāhustatpūrṇaphaladaṃ viduḥ ।।śuklapratigrahāddattaṃ madhyamaṃ dravyamucyate ।।kṛṣivāṇijyakopetamadhamaṃ dravyamucyate ।।kṣatriyāṇāṃ viśāṃ caiva śauryavāṇijyakārjitam ।।uttamaṃ dravyamityāhuḥ śūdrāṇāṃ bhṛtakārjitam ।।strīṇāṃ dharmārthināṃ dravyaṃ paitṛkaṃ bhartṛkaṃ tathā ।।gavādīnāṃ dvādaśīnāṃ caitrādiṣu yathākramam ।।saṃbhūya vā puṇyakāle dadyādiṣṭasamṛddhaye ।।gobhūtilahiraṇyājyavāsodhānyaguḍāni ca ।।raupyaṃ lavaṇakūṣmāṃḍe kanyādvādaśakaṃ tathā ।।godānāddattagavyena gomayenopakāriṇā ।।dhanadhānyādyāśritānāṃ duritānāṃ nivāraṇam ।।jalasnehādyāśritānāṃ duritānāṃ tu gojalaiḥ ।।kāyikāditrāṇāṃ tu kṣīradadhyājyakaistathā ।।tathā teṣāṃ ca puṣṭiśca vijñeyā hi vipaścitā ।।bhūdānaṃ tu pratiṣṭhārthamiha cā amutra ca dvijāḥ ।।tiladānaṃ balārthaṃ hi sadā mṛtyujayaṃ viduḥ ।।hiraṇyaṃ jāṭharāgnestu vṛddhidaṃ vīryadaṃ tathā ।।ājyaṃ puṣṭikaraṃ vidyādvastramāyuṣkaraṃ viduḥ ।।dhānyamannaṃ samṛddhyarthaṃ madhurāhāradaṃ guḍam ।।raupyaṃ retobhivṛddhyarthaṃ ṣaḍrasārthaṃ tu lāvaṇam ।।sarvaṃ sarvasamṛddhyarthaṃ kūṣmāṃḍaṃ puṣṭidaṃ viduḥ ।।prāptidaṃ sarvabhogānāmiha cā amutra ca dvijāḥ ।।yāvajjīvanamuktaṃ hi kanyādānaṃ tu bhogadam ।।panasāmrakapitthānāṃ vṛkṣāṇāṃ phalameva ca ।।kadalyādyauṣadhīnāṃ ca phalaṃ gulmodbhavaṃ tathā ।।māṣādīnāṃ ca mudgānāṃ phalaṃ śākādikaṃ tathā ।।marīcisarṣapādyānāṃ śākopakaraṇaṃ tathā ।।yadṛtau yatphalaṃ siddhaṃ taddeyaṃ hi vipaścitā ।।śrotrādīṃdriyatṛptiśca sadā deyā vipaścitā ।।śabdādidaśabhogārthaṃ digādīnāṃ ca tuṣṭidā ।।vedaśāstraṃ samādāya buddhvā gurumukhātsvayam ।।karmaṇāṃ phalamastīti buddhirāstikyamucyate ।।baṃdhurājabhayādbuddhiśraddhā sā ca kanīyasī ।।sarvābhāve daridrastu vācā vā karmaṇā yajet ।।vācikaṃ yajanaṃ vidyānmaṃtrastotrajapādikam ।।tīrthayātrāvratādyaṃ hi kāyikaṃ yajanaṃ viduḥ ।।yena kenāpyupāyena hyalpaṃ vā yadi vā bahu ।।devatārpaṇabuddhyā ca kṛtaṃ bhogāya kalpate ।।tapaścaryā ca dānaṃ ca kartavyamubhayaṃ sadā ।।pratiśrayaṃ pradātavyaṃ svavarṇaguṇaśobhitam ।।devānāṃ tṛptaye atyarthaṃ sarvabhogapradaṃ budhaiḥ ।।ihā amutrottamaṃ janmasadābhogaṃ labhedbudhaḥ ।।īśvarārpaṇabuddhyā hi kṛtvā mokṣaphalaṃ labhet ।। f। ya imaṃ paṭhate adhyāyaṃ yaḥ śṛṇoti sadā naraḥ ।।tasya vaidharmabuddhiśca jñānasiddhiḥ prajāyate ।। chapter ṛṣaya ūcuḥ pārthivapratimāpūjāvidhānaṃ brūhi sattama ।।yena pūjāvidhānena sarvābhiṣṭamavāpyate ।।sūta uvāca susādhupṛṣṭaṃ yuṣmābhiḥ sadā sarvārthadāyakam ।।sadyo duḥkhasya śamanaṃ śṛṇuta prabravīmi vaḥ ।।apamṛtyuharaṃ kālamṛtyoścāpi vināśanam ।।sadyaḥ kalatraputrādidhanadhānyapradaṃ dvijāḥ ।।annādibhojyaṃ vastrādisarvamutpadyate yataḥ ।।tato mṛdādipratimāpūjābhīṣṭapradā bhuvi ।।puruṣāṇāṃ ca nārīṇāmadhikārotra niścitam ।।nadyāṃ taḍāge kūpe vā jalāṃtarmṛdamāharet ।।saṃśodhya gaṃdhacūrṇena peṣayitvā sumaṃḍape ।।hastena pratimāṃ kuryātkṣīreṇa ca susaṃskṛtām ।।aṃgapratyaṃgakopetāmāyudhaiśca samanvitām ।।padmāsanasthitāṃ kṛtvā pūjayedādareṇa hi ।।vighneśādityaviṣṇūnāmaṃbāyāśca śivasya ca ।।śivasyaśivaliṃgaṃ ca sarvadā pūjayeddvija ।।ṣoḍaśairupacāraiśca kuryāttatphalasiddhaye ।।puṣpeṇa prokṣaṇaṃ kuryādabhiṣekaṃ samaṃtrakam ।।śālyannenaiva naivedyaṃ sarvaṃ kuḍavamānataḥ ।।gṛhe tu kuḍavaṃ jñeyaṃ mānuṣe prasthamiṣyate ।।daive prasthatrayaṃ yogyaṃ svayaṃbhoḥ prasthapañcakam ।।evaṃ pūrṇaphalaṃ vidyādadhikaṃ vai dvayaṃ trayam ।।sahasrapūjayā satyaṃ satyalokaṃ labheddvijaḥ ।।dvādaśāṃgulamāyāmaṃ dviguṇaṃ ca tato adhikam ।।pramāṇamaṃgulasyaikaṃ tadūrdhvaṃ pañcakatrayam ।।ayodārukṛtaṃ pātraṃ śivamityucyate budhaiḥ ।।tadaṣṭabhāgaḥ prasthaḥ syāttaccatuḥkuḍavaṃ matam ।।daśaprasthaṃ śataprasthaṃ sahasraprasthameva ca ।।jalatailādigaṃdhānāṃ yathāyogyaṃ ca mānataḥ ।।mānuṣārṣasvayaṃbhūnāṃ mahāpūjeti kathyate ।।abhiṣekādātmaśuddhirgaṃdhātpuṇyamavāpyate ।।āyustṛptiśca naivedyāddhūpādarthamavāpyate ।।dīpājjñānamavāpnoti tāṃbūlādbhogamāpnuyāt ।।tasmātsnānādikaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ prayatnena prasādhayet ।।namaskāro japaścaiva sarvābhīṣṭapradāvubhau ।।pūjānte ca sadākāryau bhogamokṣārthibhirnaraiḥ ।।saṃpūjya manasā pūrvaṃ kuryāttattatsadā naraḥ ।।devānāṃ pūjayā caiva tattallokamavāpnuyāt ।।tadavāṃtaraloke ca yatheṣṭaṃ bhogyamāpyate ।।tadviśeṣānpravakṣyāmi śṛṇuta śraddhayā dvijāḥ ।।vighneśapūjayā samyagbhūrloke abhīṣṭamāpnuyāt ।।śukravāre caturthyāṃ ca site śrāvaṇabhādrake ।।bhiṣagṛkṣe dhanurmāse vighneśaṃ vidhivadyajet ।।śataṃ pūjāsahasraṃ vā tatsaṃkhyākadinairvrajet ।।devāgniśraddhayā nityaṃ putradaṃ ceṣṭadaṃ nṛṇām ।।sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ tattadduritanāśanam ।।vārapūjāṃśivādīnāmātmaśuddhipradāṃ viduḥ ।।tīthinakṣatrayogānāmādhāraṃ sārvakāmikam ।।tathā bṛddhikṣayābhāvātpūrṇabrahmātmakaṃ viduḥ ।।udayādudayaṃ vāro brahmaprabhṛti karmaṇām ।।tithyādau devapūjā hi pūrṇabhogapradā nṛṇām ।।pūrvabhāgaḥ pitḥṇāṃ tu niśi yuktaḥ praśasyate ।।parabhāgastu devānāṃ divā yuktaḥ praśāsyate ।।udayavyāpinī grāhyā madhyāhne yadi sā tithiḥ ।।devakārye tathā grāhyāsthiti ṛkṣādikāḥ śubhāḥ ।।samyagvicārya vārādīnkuryātpūjājapādikam ।।pūjāryate hyaneneti vedeṣvarthasya yojanā ।।pūrṇabhogaphalasiddhiśca jāyate tena karmaṇā ।।manobhāvāṃstathā jñānamiṣṭabhogārthayojanāt ।।pūjāśabdartha evaṃ hi viśruto lokavedayoḥ ।।nityanaimittikaṃ kālātsadyaḥ kāmye svanuṣṭhite ।।nityaṃ māsaṃ ca pakṣaṃ ca varṣaṃ caiva ।।varṣabhogapradā jñeyā kṛtā vai siṃhabhādrake ।।śravaṇyādityavāre ca saptamyāṃ hastabhe dine ।।māghaśukle ca saptamyāmādityayajanaṃ caret ।।jyeṣṭhabhādrakasaumye ca dvādaśyāṃ śravarṇakṣake ।।dvādaśyāṃ viṣṇuyajanamiṣṭaṃsaṃpatkaraṃ viduḥ ।।śrāvaṇe viṣṇuyajanamiṣṭārogyapradaṃ bhavet ।।gavādīndvādaśānarthānsāṃgāndatvā tu yatphalam ।।tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti dvādaśyāṃ viṣṇutarpaṇāt ।।dvādaśyāṃ dvādaśānviprānviṣṇordvādaśanāmataḥ ।।ṣoḍaśairupacāraiśca yajettatprītimāpnuyāt ।।evaṃ ca sarvadevānāṃ tattaddvādaśanāmakaiḥ ।।dvādaśabrahmayajanaṃ tattatprītikaraṃ bhavet ।।karkaṭe somavāre ca ।।māghakṛṣṇacaturdaśyāṃ sarvābhīṣṭaphalapradā ।।āyuṣkarī mṛtyuharā sarvasiddhikarī nṛṇām ।।jyeṣṭhamāse mahārdrāyāṃ caturdaśīdinepi ca ।।mārgaśīrṣārdrakāyāṃ vā ṣoḍaśairupacārakaiḥ ।।tattanmūrtiśivaṃ pūjya tasya vai pādadarśanam ।।śivasya yajanaṃ jñeyaṃ bhogamokṣapradaṃ nṛṇām ।।vārādidevayajanaṃ kārtike hi viśiṣyate ।।kārtike māsi saṃprāpte sarvāndevānyajedbudhaḥ ।।dānena tapasā homairjapena niyamena ca ।।ṣoḍaśairupacāraiśca pratimā vipramaṃtrakaiḥ ।।brāhmaṇānāṃ bhojanena niṣkāmārtikaro bhavet ।।kārtike devayajanaṃ sarvabhogapradaṃ bhavet ।।vyādhīnāṃ haraṇaṃ caiva bhavedbhūtagrahakṣayaḥ ।।madhusvarṇājyadānena bhogavṛddhirbhavennṛṇām ।।kṛttikāśukravāreṣu gajakomeḍayājanāt ।।gaṃdhapuṣpānnadānena bhogyavṛddhirbhavennṛṇām ।।vaṃdhyā suputraṃ labhate svarṇaraupyādidānataḥ aṃ hrīnamaḥ aṃnamaḥ aṃklīṃnamaḥ aṃhrīṃnamaḥ aṃhrīṃnamaḥ aṃhrīṃ huṃ namaḥ aṃhuṃnamaḥ aṃhuṃnamaḥ aṃhrīṃhuṃnamaḥ aṃhrīṃnamaḥ namaḥ aṃhrīṃhuṃnamaḥ aṃkroṃ kṣauṃ rauṃ namaḥ aṃhrīṃnamaḥ aṃnama bhaktiśraddhāyutaścaiva sarvakāmārthasiddhaye ।।rudrākṣāndhārayenmaṃtrairdevanālasya varjitaḥ ।।vinā maṃtreṇa ho dhatte rudrākṣaṃ bhuvimānavaḥ ।।sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ yāvadindrāścaturdaśa ।।rudrākṣamālinaṃdṛṣṭvā bhūtapretapiśācakāḥ ।।ḍākinīśākinī caiva ye cānye drohakārakāḥ ।।kṛtrimaṃ caiva yatkiṃcidabhicārādikaṃcayāt ।।tatsarvaṃdūratoyātidṛṣṭvā śaṃkitavigraham ।।rudrākṣamālinaṃ dṛṣṭvā śivo viṣṇuḥ prasīdati ।।devīgaṇapatissūryaḥsurāścānyepipārvati ।।evaṃjñātvātumāhātmyaṃrudrākṣasyamaheśvari ।।samyagdhāryāssamaṃtrāścabhaktyādharmavivṛddhaye ।।ityuktaṃgirijāgrehiśivenaparamātmanā ।।bhasmarūdrākṣamāhātmyaṃ bhuktimuktiphalapradam ।।śivasyātipriyaujñeyau bhasmarudrākṣadhāriṇau ।।taddhāraṇaprabhāvaddhi bhuktirmuktirna saṃśayaḥ ।।bhasmarudrākṣadhārī yaḥ śivabhaktassa ucyate ।।pañcākṣarajapāsaktaḥ paripūrṇaścasanmukhe ।।vinābhasmatripuṃḍreṇavinārudrākṣamālayā ।।pūjitopimahādevonābhīṣṭaphaladāyakaḥ ।।tatsarvaṃ ca samākhyātaṃ yatpṛṣṭaṃhimunīśvara ।।bhasmarudrākṣamāhātmyaṃ sarvakāmasamṛddhidam ।।etadyaḥśṛṇuyānnityaṃmāhātmyaparamaṃśubham ।।rudrākṣabhasmanorbhaktyāsarvānkāmānavāpnuyāt ।।iha sarvasukhaṃ bhuktvā putrapautrādisaṃyutaḥ ।।labhetparatra sanmokṣaṃ śivasyātipriyo bhavet ।।vidyeśvarasaṃhiteyaṃ kathitā vo munīśvarāḥ ।।sarvasiddhipradā nityaṃmuktidā śivaśāsanāt ।। atha śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamī vāyavīyasaṃhitā prārabhyate ।। śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ ।। śrīgaurīśaṃkarābhyāṃ namaḥ ।।
atha saptamī vāyavīyasaṃhitā prārabhyate ।। chapter vyāsa uvāca namaśśivāya somāya sagaṇāya sasūnave ।।pradhānapuruṣeśāya sargasthityaṃtahetave ।।śaktirapratimā yasya hyaiśvaryaṃ cāpi sarvagam ।।vedāṃtasārasarvasvaṃ purāṇaṃ śrāvayāśu naḥ ।।evamabhyarthitassūto munibhirvedavādibhiḥ ।।ślakṣṇāṃ ca nyāyasaṃyuktāṃ pratyuvāca śubhāṃ giram ।। sūta uvāca pūjito anugṛhītaśca bhavadbhiriti coditaḥ ।।labdhavidyena vidhinā prajāsṛṣṭiṃ vitanvatā ।।prathamaṃ sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ purāṇaṃ brahmaṇā smṛtam ।।anaṃtaraṃ tu vaktrebhyo vedāstasya vinirgatāḥ ।।pravṛttissarvaśāstrāṇāṃ tanmukhādabhavattataḥ vyastāśca vedāśca dvāparedvāpare dvijāḥ ।।nirmitāni purāṇāni anyāni ca tataḥ param ।।sa punardvāpare cāsminkṛṣṇadvaipāyanākhyayā ।।araṇyāmiva havyāśī satyavatyāmajāyata ।।saṃkṣipya sa punarvedāṃścaturdhā kṛtavānmuniḥ ।।vyastavedatayā loke vedavyāsa iti śrutaḥ ।।purāṇānāñca saṃkṣiptaṃ caturlakṣapramāṇataḥ ।।adyāpi devaloke tacchatakoṭipravistaram ।।yo vidyāccaturo vedān sāṃgopaṇiṣadāndvijaḥ ।।na cetpurāṇaṃ saṃvidyānnaiva sa syādvicakṣaṇaḥ ।।itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ vedaṃ samupabṛṃhayet ।।bibhetyalpaśrutādvedo māmayaṃ pratariṣyati ।।sargaśca pratisargaśca vaṃśo manvaṃtarāṇi caturviṃśatsahasrakam ।।śaivantatra purāṇaṃ vai caturthaṃ saptasaṃhitam ।।vidyeśvarākhyā tatrādyā dvitīyā rudrasaṃhitā ।।tṛtīyā śatarudrākhyā koṭirudrā caturthikā ।।pañcamī kathitā comā ṣaṣṭhī vyomayugādhikam ।।dvisāhasraṃ ca dviśataṃ tathomaṃ bhūsahasrakam ।।catvāriṃśatsāṣṭaśataṃ kailāsaṃ bhūsahasrakam ।।catvāriṃśacca dviśataṃ vāyavīyamataḥ param ।।catussāhasrasaṃkhyākamevaṃ caivāśraddhadhānāya nāpurāṇavide tathā ।।parīkṣitāya śiṣyāya dhārmikāyānasūyave ।।pradeyaṃ śivabhaktāya śivadharmānusāriṇe ।।purāṇasaṃhitā yasya prasādānmayi vartate ।।namo bhagavate tasmai vyāsāyāmitatejase ।।
chapter sūta uvāca purā kālena mahatā kalpetīte punaḥpunaḥ ।।asminnupasthite kalpe pravṛtte sṛṣṭhikarmaṇi ।।pratiṣṭhitāyāṃ vārtāyāṃ prabuddhāsu prajāsu ca ।।munīnāṃ ṣaṭkulīyānāṃ bruvatāmitaretaram tataḥ paraṃ tu yannityaṃ jñānamānaṃdamavyayam ।।tanniṣṭhaistatparairbhaktairdṛśyaṃ tadvratamāśritaiḥ ।।bahunātra kimuktena guhyādguhyataraṃ param ।।śive bhaktirna sandehastayā yukto vimucyate punarāvartya mucyate ।।kaścidadhvagatastasmin sthitvāsthitvā vimucyate ।।tasmānnaikaprakāreṇa narāṇāṃ muktiriṣyate ।।jñānabhāvānurūpeṇa prasādenaiva nirvṛtiḥ ।।tasmādasya prasādārthaṃ vāṅmanodoṣavarjitāḥ ।।dhyāyaṃtaśśivamevaikaṃ sadāratanayāgnayaḥ ।।tanniṣṭhāstatparāssarve tadyuktāstadupāśrayāḥ ।।sarvakriyāḥ prakurvāṇāstameva manasāgatāḥ ।।dīrghasūtrasamārabdhaṃ divyavarṣasahasrakam ।।satrāṃte maṃtrayogena vāyustatra gamiṣyati ।।sa eva bhavataḥ śreyaḥ sopāyaṃ kathayiṣyati ।। tato vārāṇasī puṇyā purī paramaśobhanā ।।gaṃtavyā yatra viśveśo devyā saha pinākadhṛk ।।sadā viharati śrīmān bhaktānugrahakāraṇāt ।।tatrāścaryaṃ mahaddṛṣṭvā matsamīpaṃ gamiṣyatha ।।tato vaḥ kathayiṣyāmi mokṣopāya dvijottamāḥ ।।yenaikajanmanā muktiryuṣmatkaratale sthitā ।।anekajanmasaṃsārabaṃdhanirmokṣakāriṇī ।।etanmanomayaṃ cakraṃ mayā sṛṣṭaṃ visṛjyate ।।yatrāsya śīryate nemiḥ sa deśastapasaśśubhaḥ ।।ityuktvā sūryasaṃkāśaṃ cakraṃ dṛṣṭvā manomayam ।।praṇipatya mahādevaṃ visasarja pitāmahaḥ ।।te api hṛṣṭatarā viprāḥ praṇamya jagatāṃ prabhum ।।prayayustasya cakrasya yatra nemiraśīryata ।।cakraṃ tadapi saṃkṣiptaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ cāruśilātale ।।vimalasvādupānīye nijapāta vane kvacit ।।tadvanaṃ tena vikhyātaṃ naimiṣaṃ munipūjitam ।।anekayakṣagaṃdharvavidyādharasamākulam ।।aṣṭādaśa samudrasya dvīpānaśnanpurūravāḥ ।।vilāsavaśamurvaśyā yāto daivena coditaḥ ।।akrameṇa haranmohādyajñavāṭaṃ hiraṇmayam ।।munibhiryatra saṃkruddhaiḥ kuśavajrairnipātitaḥ ।।viśvaṃ sisṛkṣamāṇā vai yatra viśvasṛjaḥ purā ।।satramārebhire divyaṃ brahmajñā gārhapatyagāḥ ।।ṛṣibhiryatra vidvadbhiḥ śabdārthanyāyakovidaiḥ ।।śaktiprajñākriyāyogairvidhirāsīdanuṣṭhitaḥ ।।yatra vedavido nityaṃ vedavādabahiṣkṛtān ।।vādajalpabalairghnaṃti vacobhirativādinaḥ ।।sphaṭikamayamahībhṛtpādajābhyaśśilābhyaḥ prasaradamṛtakalpassvacchapānīyaramyam ।।atirasaphalavṛkṣaprāyamavyālasattvaṃ tapasa ucitamāsīnnaimiṣaṃ tanmunīnām ।। chapter sūta uvāca tasmindeśe mahābhāgā munayaśśaṃsitavratāḥ ।।arcayaṃto mahādevaṃ satramārebhire tadā ।।tacca satraṃ pravavṛte sarvāścaryaṃ maharṣiṇām ।।viśvaṃ sisṛkṣamāṇānāṃ purā viśvasṛjāmiva ।।atha kāle gate satre samāpte bhūridakṣiṇe ।।pitāmahaniyogena vāyustatrāgamatsvayam ।।śiṣyassvayaṃbhuvo devassarvapratyakṣadṛgvaśī ।।ājñāyāṃ maruto yasya saṃsthitāssaptasaptakāḥ ।। prerayañchaśvadaṃgāni prāṇādyābhiḥ svavṛttibhiḥ ।।sarvabhūtaśarīrāṇāṃ kurute yaśca dhāraṇam ।।aṇimādibhiraṣṭābhiraiśvaryaiśca samanvitaḥ ।।tiryakkālādibhirmedhyairbhuvanāni bibharti yaḥ ।।ākāśayonirdviguṇaḥ sparśaśabdasamanvayāt ।।tejasāṃ prakṛtiśceti yamāhustattvaciṃtakāḥ ।।tamāśramagataṃ dṛṣṭvā munayo dīrghasatriṇaḥ ।।pitāmahavacaḥ smṛtvā praharṣamatulaṃ yayuḥ ।।abhyutthāya tatassarve praṇamyāṃbarasaṃbhavam ।।cāmīkaramayaṃ tasmai viṣṭaraṃ samakalpayan ।।sopi tatra samāsīno munibhissamyagarcitaḥ ।।pratinaṃdya ca tān sarvān papraccha kuśalaṃ tataḥ ।।
vāyuruvāca atra vaḥ kuśalaṃ viprāḥ kaccidvṛtte mahākratau ।।kaccidyajñahano daityā na bādheransuradviṣaḥ ।।prāyaścittaṃ duriṣṭaṃ vā na kaccitsamajāyata ।।stotraśastragṛhairdevān pitḥn pitryaiśca karmabhiḥ ।।kaccidabhyarcya yuṣmābhirvidhirāsītsvanuṣṭhitaḥ ।।nivṛtte ca mahāsatre paścātkiṃ vaścikīrṣitam ।।ityuktā munayaḥ sarve vāyunā śivabhāvinā ।।prahṛṣṭamanasaḥ pūtāḥ pratyūcurvinayānvitāḥ ।।munaya ūcuḥ adya naḥ kuśalaṃ sarvamadya sādhu bhavettapaḥ ।।asmacchreyobhivṛddhyarthaṃ bhavānatrāgato yataḥ ।।śṛṇu cedaṃ purāvṛttaṃ tamasākrāṃtamānasaiḥ ।।upāsitaḥ purāsmābhirvijñānārthaṃ prajāpatiḥ ।।sopyasmānanugṛhyāha śaraṇyaśśaraṇāgatān ।।sarvasmādadhiko rudro viprāḥ paramakāraṇam ।।tamapratarkyaṃ yāthātmyaṃ bhaktimāneva paśyati ।।bhaktiścāsya prasādena prasādādeva nirvṛtiḥ ।।tasmādasya prasādārthaṃ naimiṣe satrayogataḥ ।।yajadhvaṃ dīrghasatreṇa rudraṃ paramakāraṇam ।।tatprasādena satrāṃte vāyustatrāgamiṣyati ।।tanmukhājjñānalābho vastatra śreyo bhaviṣyati ।।ityādiśya vayaṃ sarve preṣitā parameṣṭhinā ।।asmindeśe mahābhāga tavāgamanakāṃkṣiṇaḥ ।।dīrghasatraṃ samāsīnā divyavarṣasahasrakam ।।atastavāgamādanyatprārthyaṃ no nāsti kiṃcana ।।ityākarṇya purāvṛttamṛṣīṇāṃ dīrghasatriṇām ।।vāyuḥ prītamanā bhūtvā tatrāsīnmunisaṃvṛtaḥ ।।tatastairmunibhiḥ pṛṣṭasteṣāṃ bhāvavivṛddhaye ।।sargādi śārvamaiśvaryaṃ samāsāda vadadvibhuḥ ।। chapter sūta uvāca tatra pūrvaṃ mahābhāgā naimiṣāraṇyavāsinaḥ ।।praṇipatya yathānyāyaṃ papracchuḥ pavanaṃ prabhum ।।naimiṣīyā ūcuḥ bhavān kathamanuprāpto jñānamīśvaragocaram ।।kathaṃ ca śivabhāvaste brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।।vāyuruvāca ekonaviṃśatiḥ kalpo vijñeyaḥ śvetalohitaḥ ।।tasminkalpe caturvaktrassraṣṭukāmo atapattapaḥ ।।tapasā tena tīvreṇa tuṣṭastasya pitā svayam ।।divyaṃ kaumāramāsthāya rūpaṃ rūpavatāṃ varaḥ ।।śveto nāma munirbhūtvā divyāṃ vācamudīrayan ।।darśanaṃ pradadau tasmai devadevo maheśvaraḥ ।।taṃ dṛṣṭvā pitaraṃ brahmā brahmaṇo adhipatiṃ patim ।।praṇamya paramajñānaṃ gāyatryā saha labdhavān ।।tatassa labdhavijñāno viśvakarmā caturmukhaḥ ।।asṛjatsarvabhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca ।।yataśśrutvāmṛtaṃ labdhaṃ brahmaṇā parameśvarāt ।।tatastadvadanādeva mayā labdhaṃ tapobalāt ।।munaya ūcuḥ kiṃ tajjñānaṃ tvayā labdhaṃ tathyāttathyaṃtaraṃ śubham ।।yatra kṛtvā parāṃ niṣṭhāṃ puruṣassukhamṛcchati ।।vayuruvāca paśupāśapatijñānaṃ yallabdhaṃ tu mayā purā ।।tatra niṣṭhā parā kāryā puruṣeṇa sukhārthinā ।।ajñānaprabhavaṃ duḥkhaṃ jñānenaiva nivartate ।।jñānaṃ vastuparicchedo vastu ca dvividhaṃ smṛtam ।।ajaḍaṃ ca jaḍaṃ caiva niyaṃtṛ ca tayorapi ।।paśuḥ pāśaḥ patiśceti kathyate tattrayaṃ kramāt ।।akṣaraṃ ca kṣaraṃ caiva kṣarākṣaraparaṃ tathā ।।tadetattritayaṃ bhūmnā kathyate tattvavedibhiḥ ।।akṣaraṃ paśurityuktaḥ kṣaraṃ pāśa udāhṛtaḥ ।।kṣarākṣaraparaṃ yattatpatirityabhidhīyate ।।munaya ūcuḥ kiṃ tadakṣaramityuktaṃ kiṃ ca kṣaramudāhṛtam ।।tayośca paramaṃ kiṃ vā tadetad brūhi māruta ।।vāyuruvāca prakṛtiḥ kṣaramityuktaṃ puruṣo akṣara ucyate ।।tāvimau prerayatyanyassa parā parameśvaraḥ ।।munaya ūcuḥ kaiṣā prakṛtirityuktā ka eṣa puruṣo mataḥ ।।anayoḥ kena sambandhaḥ koyaṃ preraka īśvaraḥ ।।vāyuruvāca māyā prakṛtiruddiṣṭā puruṣo māyayā vṛtaḥ ।।saṃbandho mūlakarmabhyāṃ śivaḥ preraka īśvaraḥ ।।munaya ūcuḥ keyaṃ māyā samā khyātā kiṃrūpo māyayā vṛtaḥ ।।mūlaṃ kīdṛk kuto vāsya kiṃ śivatvaṃ kutaśśivaḥ ।।vāyuruvāca māyā māheśvarī śaktiścidrūpo māyayā vṛtaḥ ।। malaścicchādako naijo viśuddhiśśivatā svataḥ ।। munaya ūcuḥ āvṛṇoti kathaṃ māyā vyāpinaṃ kena hetunā ।।kimarthaṃ cāvṛtiḥ puṃsaḥ kena vā vinivartate ।।vāyuruvāca āvṛtirvyapino api syādvyāpi yasmātkalādyapi ।।hetuḥ karmaiva bhogārthaṃ nivarteta malakṣayāt ।।munaya ūcuḥ kalādi kathyate kiṃ tatkarma vā kimudāhṛtam ।।tatkimādi kimantaṃ vā kiṃ phalaṃ vā kimāśrayam ।।kasya bhogena kiṃ bhogyaṃ kiṃ vā tadbhogasādhanam ।।malakṣayasya ko hetuḥ kīdṛk kṣīṇamalaḥ pumān ।।vāyuruvāca kalā vidyā ca rāgaśca kālo niyatireva ca ।।kalādayassamākhyātā yo bhoktā puruṣo bhavet ।।puṇyapāpātmakaṃ karma sukhaduḥkhaphalaṃ tu yat ।।anādimalabhogāntamajñānātmasamāśrayam ।।bhogaḥ karmavināśāya bhogamavyaktamucyate ।।bāhyāṃtaḥkaraṇadvāraṃ śarīraṃ bhogasādhanam ।।bhāvātiśayalabdhena prasādena malakṣayaḥ ।।kṣīṇe cātmamale tasmin pumāñcchivasamo bhavet ।।munaya ūcuḥ kalādipañcatattvānāṃ kiṃ karma pṛthagucyate ।।bhokteti puruṣaśceti yenātmā vyapadiśyate ।।kimātmakaṃ tadavyaktaṃ kenākāreṇa bhujyate ।।kiṃ tasya śaraṇaṃ bhuktau śarīraṃ ca kimucyate ।।vāyuruvāca dikkriyāvyaṃjakā vidyā kālo rāgaḥ pravartakaḥ ।।kālo avacchedakastatra niyatistu niyāmikā ।।avyaktaṃ kāraṇaṃ yattattriguṇaṃ prabhavāpyayam ।।pradhānaṃ prakṛtiśceti yadāhustattvaciṃtakāḥ ।।kalātastadabhivyaktamanabhivyaktalakṣaṇam ।।sukhaduḥkhavimohātmā bhujyate guṇavāṃstridhā ।।sattvaṃ rajastama iti guṇāḥ prakṛtisaṃbhavāḥ ।।prakṛtau sūkṣmarūpeṇa tile tailamiva sthitāḥ ।।sukhaṃ ca sukhahetuśca samāsātsāttvikaṃ smṛtam ।।rājasaṃ tadviparyāsātstaṃbhamohau tu tāmasau ।।sāttvikyūrdhvagatiḥ proktā tāmasī syādadhogatiḥ ।।madhyamā tu gatiryā sā rājasī paripaṭhyate ।।tanmātrāpañcakaṃ caiva bhūtapañcakameva ca ।।jñāneṃdriyāṇi pañcaikyaṃ pañca karmendriyāṇi ca ।।pradhānabuddhyahaṃkāramanāṃsi ca catuṣṭayam ।।samāsādevamavyaktaṃ savikāramudāhṛtam yathā ghaṭādikaṃ kāryaṃ mṛdādernātibhidyate ।।śarīrādi tathā vyaktamavyaktānnātibhidyate ।।tasmādavyaktamevaikyakāraṇaṃ karaṇāni ca ।।śarīraṃ ca tadādhāraṃ tadbhogyaṃ cāpi netarat ।। munaya ūcuḥ buddhīndriyaśarīrebhyo vyatirekasya kasyacit ।।ātmaśabdābhidheyasya vastuto api kutaḥ sthitiḥ ।।vāyuruvāca buddhīndriyaśarīrebhyo vyatireko vibhordhruvam ।।astyeva kaścidātmeti hetustatra sudurgamaḥ ।।buddhīndriyaśarīrāṇāṃ nātmatā sadbhiriṣyate ।।smṛteraniyatajñānādayāvaddehavedanāt ।।ataḥ smartānubhūtānāmaśeṣajñeyagocaraḥ ।।antaryāmīti vedeṣu vedāṃteṣu ca gīyate ।।sarvaṃ tatra sa sarvatra vyāpya tiṣṭhati śāśvataḥ ।।tathāpi kvāpi kenāpi vyaktameṣa na dṛśyate ।।naivāyaṃ cakṣuṣā grāhyo nāparairindriyairapi ।।manasaiva pradīptena mahānātmāvasīyate ।।na ca strī na pumāneṣa naiva cāpi napuṃsakaḥ ।।naivordhvaṃ nāpi tiryak nādhastānna kutaścana ।।aśarīraṃ śarīreṣu caleṣu sthāṇumavyayam ।।sadā paśyati taṃ dhīro naraḥ pratyavamarśanāt ।।kimatra bahunoktena puruṣo dehataḥ pṛthak ।।apṛthagye tu paśyaṃti hyasamyakteṣu darśanam ।।yaccharīramidaṃ proktaṃ puruṣasya tataḥ param ।।aśuddhamavaśaṃ duḥkhamadhruvaṃ na ca vidyate ।।vipadāṃ vījabhūtena puruṣastena saṃyutaḥ ।।sukhī duḥkhī ca mūḍhaśca bhavati svena karmaṇā ।।adbhirāplavitaṃ kṣetraṃ janayatyaṃkuraṃ yathā ।।ājñānātplāvitaṃ karma dehaṃ janayate tathā ।।atyaṃtamasukhāvāsāssmṛtāścaikāṃtamṛtyavaḥ ।।anāgatā atītāśca tanavo asya sahasraśaḥ ।।āgatyāgatya śīrṇeṣu śarīreṣu śarīriṇaḥ ।।atyaṃtavasatiḥ kvāpi na kenāpi ca labhyate ।।chāditaśca viyuktaśca śarīraireṣu lakṣyate ।।caṃdrabiṃbavadākāśe taralairabhrasaṃcayaiḥ ।।anekadehabhedena bhinnā vṛttirihātmanaḥ ।।aṣṭāpadaparikṣepe hyakṣamudreva lakṣyate ।।naivāsya bhavitā kaścinnāsau bhavati kasyacit ।।pathi saṃgama evāyaṃ dāraiḥ putraiśca baṃdhubhiḥ ।।yathā kāṣṭhaṃ ca kāṣṭhaṃ ca sameyātāṃ mahodadhau ।।sametya ca vyapeyātāṃ tadvadbhūtasamāgamaḥ ।।sa paśyati śarīraṃ taccharīraṃ tanna paśyati ।।tau paśyati paraḥ kaścittāvubhau taṃ na paśyataḥ ।। brahmādyāḥ sthāvarāṃtaśca paśavaḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।।paśūnāmeva sarveṣāṃ proktametannidarśanam ।।sa eṣa badhyate pāśaiḥ sukhaduḥkhāśanaḥ paśuḥ ।।līlāsādhanabhūto ya īśvarasyeti sūrayaḥ ।।ajño jaṃturanīśo ayamātmanassukhaduḥkhayoḥ ।।īśvaraprerito gacchetsvargaṃ vā śvabhrameva vā ।। sūta uvāca ityākarṇyānilavaco munayaḥ prītamānasāḥ ।।procuḥ praṇamya taṃ vāyuṃ śaivāgamavicakṣaṇam ।।
chapter munaya ūcuḥ yo ayaṃ paśuriti prokto yaśca pāśa udāhṛtaḥ ।।abhyāṃ vilakṣaṇaḥ kaścitkoyamasti tayoḥ patiḥ ।।vāyuruvāca asti kaścidaparyaṃtaramaṇīyaguṇāśrayaḥ ।।patirviśvasya nirmātā paśupāśavimocanaḥ ।।abhāve tasya viśvasya sṛṣṭireṣā kathaṃ bhavet ।।acetanatvādajñānādanayoḥ paśupāśayoḥ ।।pradhānaparamāṇvādi yāvatkiṃcidacetanam ।।tatkartṛkaṃ svayaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ buddhimatkāraṇaṃ vinā ।।jagacca kartṛsāpekṣaṃ kāryaṃ sāvayavaṃ yataḥ ।।tasmātkāryasya kartṛtvaṃ patyurna paśupāśayoḥ ।।paśorapi ca kartṛtvaṃ patyuḥ preraṇapūrvakam ।।ayathākaraṇajñānamaṃdhasya gamanaṃ yathā ।।ātmānaṃ ca dadhni vā sarpirarpitam ।।yathāpaḥ srotasi vyāptā yathāraṇyāṃ hutāśanaḥ ।।evameva mahātmānamātmanyātmavilakṣaṇam ।।satyena tapasā caiva nityayukto anupaśyati ।।ya eko jālavānīśa īśānībhissvaśaktibhiḥ ।।sarvāṃllokānimān kṛtvā eka eva sa īśate ।।eka eva tadā rudro na dvitīyo asti kaścana ।।saṃsṛjya viśvabhuvanaṃ goptā te saṃcukoca yaḥ ।। viśvataścakṣurevāyamutāyaṃ viśvatomukhaḥ ।।tathaiva viśvatobāhuviśvataḥ pādasaṃyutaḥ ।।dyāvābhūmī ca janayan deva eko maheśvaraḥ ।।sa eva sarvadevānāṃ prabhavaścodbhavastathā ।।hiraṇyagarbhaṃ devānāṃ prathamaṃ janayedayam ।।viśvasmādadhiko rudro maharṣiriti hi śrutiḥ ।।vedāhametaṃ puruṣaṃ mahāṃtamamṛtaṃ dhruvam ।।ādityavarṇaṃ tamasaḥ parastātsaṃsthitaṃ prabhum ।।asmānnāsti paraṃ kiṃcidaparaṃ paramātmanaḥ ।।nāṇīyo asti na ca jyāyastena pūrṇamidaṃ jagat ।।sarvānanaśirogrīvaḥ sarvabhūtaguhāśayaḥ ।।sarvavyāpī ca bhagavāṃstasmātsarvagataśśivaḥ ।।sarvataḥ pāṇipādo ayaṃ sarvato akṣiśiromukhaḥ ।।sarvataḥ śrutimāṃlloke sarvamāvṛtya tiṣṭhati ।।sarvendriyaguṇābhāsassarvendriyavivarjitaḥ ।।sarvasya prabhurīśānaḥ sarvasya śaraṇaṃ suhṛt ।।acakṣurapi yaḥ paśyatyakarṇo api śṛṇoti yaḥ ।।sarvaṃ vetti na vettāsya tamāhuḥ puruṣaṃ param ।।aṇoraṇīyānmahato mahīyānayamavyayaḥ ।।guhāyāṃ nihitaścāpi jaṃtorasya maheśvaraḥ ।।tamakratuṃ kratuprāyaṃ mahimātiśayānvitam ।।dhātuḥ prasādādīśānaṃ vītaśokaḥ prapaśyati ।।vedāhamenamajaraṃ purāṇaṃ sarvagaṃ vibhum ।।nirodhaṃ janmano yasya vadaṃti brahmavādinaḥ ।।eko api trīnimāṃllokān bahudhā śaktiyogataḥ ।। vidadhāti vicetyaṃte viśvamādau maheśvaraḥ ।।viśvadhātrītyajākhyā ca śaivī citrā kṛtiḥ parā ।।tāmajāṃ lohitāṃ śuklāṃ kṛṣṇāmekāṃ tvajaḥ prajām ।।janitrīmanuśete anyojuṣamāṇassvarūpiṇīm ।।tāmevājāmajo anyastu bhaktabhogā jahāti ca ।।dvau suparṇau ca sayujau samānaṃ vṛkṣamāsthitau ।।eko atti pippalaṃ svādu paro anaśnan prapaśyati ।।vṛkṣesmin puruṣo magno guhyamānaśca śocati ।।juṣṭamanyaṃ yadā paśyedīśaṃ paramakāraṇam ।।tadāsya mahimānaṃ ca vītaśokassukhī bhavet ।।chaṃdāṃsi yajñāḥ ṛtavo yadbhūtaṃ bhavyameva ca ।।māyī viśvaṃ sṛjatyasminniviṣṭo māyayā paraḥ ।।māyāṃ tu prakṛtiṃ vidyānmāyinaṃ tu maheśvaram ।।tasyāstvavayavaireva vyāptaṃ sarvamidaṃ jagat ।।sūkṣmātisūkṣmamīśānaṃ kalalasyāpi madhyataḥ ।। sraṣṭāramapi viśvasya veṣṭitāraṃ ca tasya tu ।।śivameveśvaraṃ jñātvā śāṃtimatyaṃtamṛcchati ।।sa eva kālo goptā ca viśvasyādhipatiḥ prabhuḥ ।।taṃ viśvādhipatiṃ jñātvā mṛtyupāśātpramucyate ।।ghṛtātparaṃ maṃḍamiva sūkṣmaṃ jñātvā sthitaṃ prabhum ।।sarvabhūteṣu gūḍhaṃ ca sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।eṣa eva paro devo viśvakarmā maheśvaraḥ ।।hṛdaye saṃniviṣṭaṃ taṃ jñātvaivāmṛtamaśnute ।।yadā samastaṃ na divā na rātrirna sadapyasat ।।kevalaśśiva evaiko yataḥ prajñā purātanī ।।nainamūrdhvaṃ na tiryakca na madhyaṃ paryajigrahat ।।na tasya pratimā cāsti yasya nāma mahadyaśaḥ ।।ajātamimamevaike buddhā janmani bhīravaḥ ।।rudrasyāsya prapadyaṃte rakṣārthaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ sukham ।।dve akṣare brahmapare tvanaṃte samudāhṛte ।।vidyāvidye samākhyāte nihite yatra gūḍhavat ।।kṣaraṃ tvavidyā hyamṛtaṃ vidyeti parigīyate ।।te ubhe īśate yastu so anyaḥ khalu maheśvaraḥ ।।ekaikaṃ bahudhā jālaṃ vikurvannekavacca yaḥ ।।sarvādhipatyaṃ kurute sṛṣṭvā sarvān pratāpavān ।।diśa ūrdhvamadhastiryak bhāsayan bhrājate svayam ।।yo niḥsvabhāvādapyeko vareṇyastvadhitiṣṭhati ।।svabhāvavācakān sarvān vācyāṃśca pariṇāmayan ।।guṇāṃśca bhogyabhoktṛtve tadviśvamadhitiṣṭhati ।।te vai guhyopaṇiṣadi gūḍhaṃ brahma parātparam ।।brahmayoniṃ jagatpūrvaṃ vidurdevā maharṣayaḥ ।।bhāvagrāhyamanīhākhyaṃ bhāvābhāvakaraṃ śivam ।।kalāsargakaraṃ devaṃ ye viduste jahustanum ।।svabhāvameke manyaṃte kālameke vimohitāḥ ।।devasya mahimā hyeṣa yenedaṃ bhrāmyate jagat ।।yenedamāvṛtaṃ nityaṃ kālakālātmanā yataḥ ।।teneritamidaṃ karma bhūtaiḥ saha vivartate ।।tatkarma bhūyaśaḥ kṛtvā vinivṛtya ca bhūyaśaḥ ।।tattvasya saha tattvena yogaṃ cāpi sametya vai ।।aṣṭābhiśca tribhiścaivaṃ dvābhyāṃ caikena vā punaḥ ।।kālenātmaguṇaiścāpi kṛtsnameva jagat svayam ।।guṇairārabhya karmāṇi svabhāvādīni yojayet ।।teṣāmabhāve nāśaḥ syātkṛtasyāpi ca karmaṇaḥ ।।karmakṣaye punaścānyattato yāti sa tattvataḥ ।।sa evādissvayaṃ yoganimittaṃ bhoktṛbhogayoḥ ।।parastrikālādakalassa eva parameśvaraḥ ।।sarvavit triguṇādhīśo brahmasākṣātparātparaḥ ।।taṃ viśvarūpamabhavaṃ bhavamīḍyaṃ prajāpatim ।।
devadevaṃ jagatpūjyaṃ svacittasthamupāsmahe ।।kālādibhiḥ paro yasmātprapañcaḥ parivartate ।।dharmāvahaṃ pāpanudaṃ bhogeśaṃ viśvadhāma ca ।।tamīśvarāṇāṃ paramaṃ maheśvaraṃ taṃ devatānāṃ paramaṃ ca daivatam ।।patiṃ patīnāṃ paramaṃ parastādvidāma devaṃ bhuvaneśvareśvaram ।।na tasya vidyeta kāryaṃ kāraṇaṃ ca na vidyate ।।na tatsamo adhikaścāpi kvacijjagati dṛśyate ।।parāsya vividhā śaktiḥ śrutau svābhāvikī śrutā ।।jñānaṃ balaṃ kriyā caiva yābhyo viśvamidaṃ kṛtam ।।tasyāsti patiḥ kaścinnaiva liṃgaṃ na ceśitā ।।kāraṇaṃ kāraṇānāṃ ca sa teṣāmadhipādhipaḥ ।।na cāsya janitā kaścinna ca janma kutaścana ।।na janmahetavastadvanmalamāyādisaṃjñakāḥ ।।sa ekassarvabhūteṣu gūḍho vyāptaśca viśvataḥ ।।sarvabhūtāṃtarātmā ca dharmādhyakṣassa kathyate ।।sarvabhūtādhivāsaśca sākṣī cetā ca nirguṇaḥ ।।eko vaśī niṣkriyāṇāṃ bahūnāṃ vivaśātmanām ।।nityānāmapyasau nityaścetanānāṃ ca cetanaḥ ।।eko bahūnāṃ cākāmaḥ kāmānīśaḥ prayacchati ।।sāṃkhyayogādhigamyaṃ yatkāraṇaṃ jagatāṃ patim ।।jñātvā devaṃ paśuḥ pāśaissarvaireva vimucyate ।।viśvakṛdviśvavitsvātmayonijñaḥ kālakṛdguṇī ।।pradhānaḥ kṣetrajñapatirguṇeśaḥ pāśamocakaḥ ।।brahmāṇaṃ vidadhe pūrvaṃ vedāṃścopādiśatsvayam ।।yo devastamahaṃ buddhvā svātmabuddhiprasādataḥ ।।mumukṣurasmātsaṃsārātprapadye śaraṇaṃ śivam ।।niṣphalaṃ niṣkriyaṃ śāṃtaṃ niravadyaṃ niraṃjanam ।।amṛtasya paraṃ setuṃ dagdheṃdhanamivānilam ।।yadā carmavadākāśaṃ veṣṭayiṣyaṃti mānavāḥ ।।tadā śivamavijñāya duḥkhasyāṃto bhaviṣyati ।।tapaḥprabhāvāddevasya prasādācca maharṣayaḥ ।।atyāśramocitajñānaṃ pavitraṃ pāpanāśanam ।।vedāṃte paramaṃ guhyaṃ purākalpapracoditam ।।brahmaṇo vadanāllabdhaṃ mayedaṃ bhāgyagauravāt ।।nāpraśāṃtāya dātavyametajjñānamanuttamam ।।na putrāyāśuvṛttāya nāśiṣyāya ca sarvathā ।।yasya deve parābhaktiryathā deve tathā gurau ।।tasyaite kathitāhyarthāḥ prakāśaṃte mahātmanaḥ ।।ataśca saṃkṣepamidaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ śivaḥ parastātprakṛteśca puṃsaḥ ।।sa sargakāle ca karoti sarvaṃ saṃhārakāle punarādadāti ।। chapter munaya ūcuḥ kālādutpadyate sarvaṃ kāladeva vipadyate ।।na kālanirapekṣaṃ hi kvacitkiṃcana vidyate ।।yadāsyāṃtargataṃ viśvaṃ śaśvatsaṃsāramaṇḍalam ।।sargasaṃhṛtimudrābhyāṃ cakravatparivartate ।।brahmā hariśca rudraśca tathānye ca surāsurāḥ ।।yatkṛtāṃ niyatiṃ prāpya prabhavo nātivartitum ।।bhūtabhavyabhaviṣyādyairvibhajya jarayan prajāḥ ।।atiprabhuriti svairaṃ vartate atibhayaṃkaraḥ ।।ka eṣa bhagavān kālaḥ kasya vā vaśavartyayam ।।ka ।।niyogarūpamīśasya balaṃ viśvaniyāmakam ।।tasyāṃśāṃśamayī muktiḥ kālātmani mahātmani ।।tato niṣkramya saṃkrāṃtā visṛṣṭāgrerivāyasī ।।tasmātkālavaśe viśvaṃ na sa viśvavaśe sthitaḥ ।।śivasya tu vaśe kālo na kālasya vaśe śivaḥ ।।yato apratihataṃ śārvaṃ tejaḥ kāle pratiṣṭhitam ।।mahatī tena kālasya maryādā hi duratyayā ।।kālaṃ prajñāviśeṣeṇa ko ativartitumarhati ।।kālena tu kṛtaṃ karma na priyaiścaiva hyaciṃtitagamāgamaiḥ ।।saṃyojayati bhūtāni viyojayati ceśvaraḥ ।।yadaiva duḥkhitaḥ kaścittadaiva sukhitaḥ paraḥ ।।durvijñeyasvabhāvasya kālāsyāho vicitratā ।।yo yuvā sa bhavedvṛddho yo balīyānsa durbalaḥ ।।yaḥ śrīmānso api niḥśrīkaḥ kālaścitragatirdvijā ।।nābhijātyaṃ na vai śīlaṃ na balaṃ na ca naipuṇam ।।bhavetkāryāya paryāptaṃ kālaśca hyanirodhakaḥ ।।ye sanāthāśca dātāro gītavādyairupasthitāḥ ।।ye cānāthāḥ parānnādāḥ kālasteṣu samakriyaḥ ।।phalaṃtyakāle na rasāyanāni samyakprayuktānyapi cauṣadhāni ।।tānyeva kālena samāhṛtāni siddhiṃ prayāṃtyāśu sukhaṃ diśaṃti ।। nākālato ayaṃ mriyate jāyate vā nākālataḥ puṣṭimagryāmupaiti ।।nākālataḥ sukhitaṃ duḥkhitaṃ vā nākālikaṃ vastu samasti kiṃcit ।।kālena śītaḥ prativāti vātaḥkālena vṛṣṭirjaladānupaiti ।।kālena coṣmā praśamaṃ prayāti kālena sarvaṃ saphalatvameti ।।kālaśca sarvasya bhavasya hetuḥ kālena sasyāni bhavaṃti nityam ।।kālena sasyāni layaṃ prayāṃti kālena saṃjīvati jīvalokaḥ ।।itthaṃ kālātmanastattvaṃ yo vijānāti tattvataḥ ।।kālātmānamatikramya kālātītaṃ sa paśyati ।।na yasya kālo na ca baṃdhamuktī na yaḥ pumānna prakṛtirna viśvam ।।vicitrarūpāya śivāya tasmai namaḥparasmai parameśvarāya ।। chapter ṛṣaya ūcuḥ kena mānena kālesminnāyussaṃkhyā prakalpyate ।।saṃkhyārūpasya kālasya kaḥ punaḥ paramo avadhiḥ ।।vāyuruvāca āyuṣo atra nimeṣākhyamādyamānaṃ pracakṣate ।।saṃkhyārūpasya kālasya ।।kalpe caturdaśaikasminmanūnāṃ parivṛttayaḥ ।।etena kramayogena kalpamanvaṃtarāṇi ca ।।saprajāni vyatītāni śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।।ajñeyatvācca sarveṣāmasaṃkhyeyatayā punaḥ ।।śakyo naivānupūrvyādvai teṣāṃ vaktuṃ suvistaraḥ ।।kalpo nāma divā prokto brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।।kalpānāṃ vai sahasraṃ ca brāhmaṃ varṣamihocyate ।।varṣāṇāmaṣṭasāhasraṃ yacca tadbrahmaṇo yugam ।।savanaṃ yugasāhasraṃ sahitāni ca ।।abde pañca sahasrāṇi catvāriṃśadyutāni ca ।।catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi pañca lakṣāṇi cāyuṣi ।।brahmā viṣṇordine caiko viṣṇū rudradine tathā ।।īśvarasya dine rudrassadākhyasya tatheśvaraḥ ।।sākṣācchivasya tatsaṃkhyastathā so api sadāśivaḥ ।।catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi pañcalakṣāṇi cāyuṣi ।।tasminsākṣācchivenaiṣa kālātmā sampravartate ।।yattatsṛṣṭessamākhyātaṃ kālāntaramiha dvijāḥ ।।etatkālāntaraṃ jñeyamaharvai pārameśvaram ।।rātriśca tāvatī jñeyā parameśasya kṛtsnaśaḥ ।।ahastasya tu yā sṛṣṭī rātriśca pralayaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।aharna vidyate tasya na rātririti dhārayet ।।eṣopacāraḥ kriyate lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।।prajāḥ prajānāṃ patayo mūrtayaśca surāsurāḥ ।।indriyāṇīndriyārthāśca mahābhūtāni pañca ca ।।tanmātrāṇyatha bhūtādirbuddhiśca saha daivataḥ ।।ahastiṣṭhaṃti sarvāṇi chapter munaya ūcuḥ kathaṃ jagadidaṃ kṛtsnaṃ vidhāya ca nidhāya ca ।।ājñayā paramāṃ krīḍāṃ karoti parameśvaraḥ ।।kiṃ tatprathamasaṃbhūtaṃ kenedamakhilaṃ tatam ।।kenā vā punarevedaṃ grasyate pṛthukukṣiṇā ।।vāyuruvāca śaktiḥ prathamasambhūtā śāṃtyatītapadottarā ।।tato māyā tato avyaktaṃ śivācchaktimataḥ prabhoḥ ।। śāntyatītapadaṃ śaktestataḥ śāntipadakramāt ।।tato vidyāpadaṃ tasmātpratiṣṭhāpadasaṃbhavaḥ ।।nivṛttipadamutpannaṃ pratiṣṭhāpadataḥ kramāt ।।evamuktā samāsena sṛṣṭirīśvaracoditā ।।ānulomyāttathaiteṣāṃ pratilomyena saṃhṛtiḥ ।।asmātpañcapadoddiṣṭātparassraṣṭā samiṣyate ।।kalābhiḥ pañcabhirvyāptaṃ tasmādviśvamidaṃ jagat ।।avyaktaṃ kāraṇaṃ yattadātmanā samanuṣṭhitam ।।mahadādiviśeṣāṃtaṃ sṛjatītyapi saṃmatam ।।kiṃ tu tatrāpi kartṛtvaṃ nāvyaktasya na cātmanaḥ ।।acetanatvātprakṛterajñatvātpuruṣasya ca ।।pradhānaparamāṇvādi yāvatkiñcidacetanam ।।tatkartṛkaṃ svayaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ buddhimatkāraṇaṃ vinā ।।jagacca kartṛsāpekṣaṃ kāryaṃ sāvayavaṃ yataḥ ।।tasmācchaktassvatantro yaḥ sarvaśaktiśca sarvavit ।।anādinidhanaścāyaṃ mahadaiśvaryasaṃyutaḥ ।।sa eva jagataḥ kartā mahādevo maheśvarāḥ ।।pātā hartā ca sarvasya tataḥ pṛthagananvayaḥ ।।pariṇāmaḥ pradhānasya pravṛttiḥ puruṣasya ca ।।sarvaṃ satyavratasyaiva śāsanena pravartate ।।itīyaṃ śāśvatī niṣṭhā satāṃ manasi vartate ।।na cainaṃ pakṣamāśritya vartate svalpacetanaḥ ।।yāvadādisamāraṃbho yāvadyaḥ pralayo mahān ।।tāvadapyeti sakalaṃ brahmaṇaḥ śāradāṃ śatam ।।paramityāyuṣo nāma brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।।tatparākhyaṃ tadardhaṃ ca parārdhamabhidhīyate ।।parārdhadvayakālāṃte pralaye samupasthite ।।avyaktamātmanaḥ kāryamādāyātmani tiṣṭhati ।।ātmanyavasthite avyakte vikāre pratisaṃhṛte ।।sādharmyeṇādhitiṣṭhete pradhānapuruṣāvubhau ।।tamaḥ sattvaguṇāvetau samatvena vyavasthitau ।।anudriktāvanantau tāvotaprotau parasparam ।।guṇasāmye tadā tasminnavibhāge tamodaye ।।śāṃtavātaikanīre ca na prājñāyata kiṃcana ।।aprajñāte jagatyasminneka eva maheśvaraḥ ।।upāsya rajanīṃ kṛtsnāṃ parāṃ māheśvarīṃ tataḥ ।।prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ pradhānapuruṣāvubhau ।।praviśya kṣobhayāmāsa māyāyogānmaheśvaraḥ ।।tataḥ punaraśeṣāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ prabhavāpyayāt ।।avyaktādabhavatsṛṣṭirājñayā parameṣṭhinaḥ ।।viśvottarottaravicitramanorathasya yasyaikaśaktiśakale sakalassamāptaḥ ।।ātmānamadhvapatimadhvavido vadaṃti tasmai namaḥ sakalalokavilakṣaṇāya ।। chapter vāyuruvāca puruṣādhiṣṭhitātpūrvamavyaktādīśvarājñayā ।।buddhyādayo viśeṣāṃtā vikārāścābhavan kramāt ।।tatastebhyo vikārebhyo rudro viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaḥ ।।kāraṇatvena sarveṣāṃ trayo devāḥ prajajñire ।।sarvato bhuvanavyāptiśaktimavyāhatāṃ kvacit ।।jñānamapratimaṃ śaśvadaiśvaryaṃ cāṇimādikam ।।sṛṣṭisthitilayākhyeṣu karmasu triṣu hetutām ।।prabhutvena sahaiteṣāṃ prasīdati maheśvaraḥ ।।kalpāntare punasteṣāmaspardhā buddhimohinām ।।sargarakṣālayācāraṃ pratyekaṃ pradadau ca saḥ ।।ete parasparotpannā dhārayanti parasparam ।।paraspareṇa vardhaṃte parasparamanuvratāḥ ।।kvacidbrahmā kvacidviṣṇuḥ kvacidrudraḥ praśasyate ।।nānena teṣāmādhikyamaiśvaryaṃ cātiricyate ।।mūrkhā niṃdaṃti tānvāgbhiḥ saṃraṃbhābhiniveśinaḥ ।।yātudhānā bhavaṃtyeva piśācāśca na saṃśayaḥ ।।devo guṇatrayātītaścaturvyūho maheśvaraḥ ।।sakalassakalādhāraśakterutpattikāraṇam ।।soyamātmā trayasyāsya prakṛteḥ puruṣasya ca ।।līlākṛtajagatsṛṣṭirīśvaratve vyavasthitaḥ ।।yassarvasmātparo nityo niṣkalaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।।sa eva ca tadādhārastadātmā tadadhiṣṭhitaḥ ।।tasmānmaheśvaraścaiva prakṛtiḥ puruṣastathā ।।sadāśivabhavo viṣṇurbrahmā sarvaśivātmakam ।।pradhānātprathamaṃ jajñe vṛddhiḥ khyātirmatirmahān ।।mahattattvasya saṃkṣobhādahaṃkārastridhā abhavat ।।ahaṃkāraśca bhūtāni tanmātrānīṃdriyāṇi ca ।।vaikārikādahaṃkārātsattvodriktāttu sāttvikaḥ ।।vaikārikaḥ sa sargastu yugapatsaṃpravartate ।।buddhīndriyāṇi pañcaiva pañcakarmeṃdriyāṇi ca ।।ekādaśaṃ manastatra svaguṇenobhayātmakam ।।tamoyuktādahaṃkārādbhūtatanmātrasaṃbhavaḥ ।।bhūtānāmādibhūtatvādbhūtādiḥ kathyate tu saḥ ।।bhūtādeśśabdamātraṃ syāttatra cākāśasaṃbhavaḥ ।।ākāśātsparśa utpannaḥ sparśādvāyusamudbhavaḥ ।।vāyo rūpaṃ tatastejastejaso rasasaṃbhavaḥ ।।rasādāpassamutpannāstebhyo gandhasamudbhavaḥ ।।gandhācca pṛthivī jātā bhūtebhyonyaccarācaram ।।puruṣādhiṣṭhitatvācca avyaktānugraheṇa ca ।।mahadādiviśeṣāntā hyaṇḍamutpādayanti te ।। tatra kāryaṃ ca karaṇaṃ saṃsiddhaṃ brahmaṇo yadā ।।tadaṃḍe supravṛddho abhūt kṣetrajño brahmasaṃjñitaḥ ।।sa vai śarīrī prathamaḥ sa vai puruṣa ucyate ।।ādikartā sa bhūtānāṃ brahmāgre samavartata ।।tasyeśvarasya pratimā jñānavairāgyalakṣaṇā ।।dharmaiśvaryakarī buddhirbrāhmī yajñe abhimāninaḥ ।।avyaktājjāyate tasya manasā yadyadīpsitam ।।vaśī vikṛtvāttraiguṇyātsāpekṣatvātsvabhāvataḥ ।।tridhā vibhajya cātmānaṃ trailokye saṃpravartate ।।sṛjate grasate caiva vīkṣate ca tribhissvayam ।।caturmukhastu brahmatve kālatve cāṃtakassmṛtaḥ ।।sahasramūrdhā puruṣastisrovasthāssvayaṃbhuvaḥ ।।sattvaṃ rajaśca brahmā ca kālatve ca tamo rajaḥ ।।viṣṇutve kevalaṃ sattvaṃ guṇavṛddhistridhā vibhau ।।brahmatve sṛjate lokān kālatve saṃkṣipatyapi ।।puruṣatve atyudāsīnaḥ karma ca trividhaṃ vibhoḥ ।।evaṃ tridhā vibhinnatvādbrahmā triguṇa ucyate ।।caturdhā pravibhaktatvāccāturvyūhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।āditvādādidevo asāvajātatvādajaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।pāti yasmātprajāḥ sarvāḥ prajāpatiriti smṛtaḥ ।।hiraṇmayastu yo merustasyolbaṃ sumahātmanaḥ ।।garbhodakaṃ samudrāśca jarāyuścā api parvatāḥ ।।tasminnaṃḍe tvime lokā aṃtarviśvamidaṃ jagat ।।caṃdrādityau sanakṣatrau sagrahau saha vāyunā ।।adbhirdaśaguṇābhistu bāhyatoṇḍaṃ samāvṛtam ।।āpo daśaguṇenaiva tejasā bahirāvṛtāḥ ।।tejo daśaguṇenaiva vāyunā bahirāvṛtam ।।ākāśenāvṛto vāyuḥ khaṃ ca bhūtādināvṛtam ।।bhūtādirmahatā tadvadavyaktenāvṛto mahān ।।etairāvaraṇairaṇḍaṃ saptabhirbahirāvṛtam ।।etadāvṛttya cānyonyamaṣṭau prakṛtayaḥ sthitāḥ ।।sṛṣṭipālanavidhvaṃsakarmakartryo dvijottamāḥ ।।evaṃ parasparotpannā dhārayaṃti parasparam ।।ādhārādheyabhāvena vikārāstu vikāriṣu ।।kūrmoṃgāni yathā pūrvaṃ prasārya viniyacchati ।।vikārāṃśca tathā avyaktaṃ sṛṣṭvā bhūyo niyacchati ।।avyaktaprabhavaṃ sarvamānulomyena jāyate ।।prāpte pralayakāle tu pratilomyenulīyate ।।guṇāḥ kālavaśādeva bhavaṃti viṣamāḥ samāḥ ।।guṇasāmye layo jñeyo vaiṣamye sṛṣṭirucyate ।।tadidaṃ brahmaṇo yoniretadaṃḍaṃ ghanaṃ mahat ।।brahmaṇaḥ kṣetramuddiṣṭaṃ brahmā kṣetrajña ucyate ।।itīdṛśānāmaṇḍānāṃ koṭyo jñeyāḥ sahasraśaḥ ।।sarvagatvātpradhānasya tiryagūrdhvamadhaḥ sthitāḥ ।। tatra tatra caturvaktrā brahmāṇo harayo bhavāḥ ।।sṛṣṭā pradhānena tathā labdhvā śaṃbhostu sannidhim ।।maheśvaraḥ parovyaktādaṃḍamavyaktasaṃbhavam ।।aṇḍājjajñe vibhurbrahmā lokāstena kṛtāstvime ।।abuddhipūrvaḥ kathito mayaiṣa pradhānasargaḥ prathamaḥ pravṛtaḥ ।।ātyaṃtikaśca pralayontakāle līlākṛtaḥ kevalamīśvarasya ।।yattatsmṛtaṃ kāraṇamaprameyaṃ brahmā pradhānaṃ prakṛteḥ prasūtiḥ ।।anādimadhyāntamanantavīryaṃ śuklaṃ suraktaṃ puruṣeṇa yuktam ।।utpādakatvādrajasotirekāllokasya saṃtānavivṛddhihetūn ।।aṣṭau vikārānapi cādikāle sṛṣṭvā samaśnāti tathāṃtakāle ।।prakṛtyavasthāpitakāraṇānāṃ yā ca sthitiryā ca punaḥ pravṛttiḥ ।।tatsarvamaprākṛtavaibhavasya saṃkalpamātreṇa maheśvarasya ।।
chapter munaya ūcuḥ manvaṃtarāṇi sarvāṇi kalpabhedāṃśca sarvaśaḥ ।।teṣvevāṃtarasargaṃ ca pratisargaṃ ca no vada ।।vāyuruvāca kālasaṃkhyāvivṛttasya parārdho brahmaṇassmṛtaḥ ।।tāvāṃścaivāsya kālonyastasyāṃte pratisṛjyate ।।divase divase tasya brahmaṇaḥ pūrvajanmanaḥ ।।caturdaśamahābhāgā manūnāṃ parivṛttayaḥ ।।anāditvādanaṃtatvādajñeyatvācca kṛtsnaśaḥ ।।manvaṃtarāṇi kalpāśca na śakyā vacanātpṛthak ।।ukteṣvapi ca sarveṣu śṛṇvatāṃ vo vaco mama ।।kimihāsti phalaṃ tasmānna pṛthak vaktumutsahe ।।ya eva khalu kalpeṣu kalpaḥ saṃprati vartate ।।tatra saṃkṣipya vartaṃte sṛṣṭayaḥ pratisṛṣṭayaḥ ।।yastvayaṃ vartate kalpo vārāho nāma nāmataḥ ।।asminnapi dvijaśreṣṭhā manavastu caturdaśa ।।svāyaṃbhuvādayassapta sapta sāvarṇikādayaḥ ।।teṣu vaivasvato nāma saptamo vartate manuḥ ।।manvaṃtareṣu sarveṣu sargasaṃhāravṛttayaḥ ।।prāyaḥ samābhavaṃtīti tarkaḥ kāryo vijānatā ।।pūrvakalpe parāvṛtte pravṛtte kālamārute ।।samunmūlitamūleṣu vṛkṣeṣu ca vaneṣu ca ।।jagaṃti tṛṇavaktrīṇi deve dahati pāvake ।।vṛṣṭyā bhuvi niṣiktāyāṃ viveleṣvarṇaveṣu ca ।।dikṣu sarvāsu magnāsu vāripūre mahīyasi ।।tadadbhiścaṭulākṣepaistaraṃgabhujamaṇḍalaiḥ ।।prārabdhacaṇḍanṛtyeṣu tataḥ pralayavāriṣu ।।brahmā nārāyaṇo bhūtvā suṣvāpa salile sukham ।। imaṃ codāharanmaṃtraṃ ślokaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prati ।।taṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ muniśreṣṭhāstadarthaṃ cākṣarāśrayam ।।āpo nārā iti proktā āpo vai narasūnavaḥ ।।ayanaṃ tasya tā yasmāttena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।śivayogamayīṃ nidrāṃ kurvantaṃ tridaśeśvaram ।।baddhāṃjali puṭāssiddhā janalokanivāsinaḥ ।।stotraiḥ prabodhayāmāsuḥ prabhātasamaye surāḥ ।।yathā sṛṣṭyādisamaye īśvaraṃ śrutayaḥ purā ।।tataḥ prabuddha utthāya śayanāttoyamadhyagāt ।।udaikṣata diśaḥ sarvā yoganidrālasekṣaṇaḥ ।।nāpaśyatsa tadā kiṃcitsvātmano vyatireki yat ।।savismaya ivāsīnaḥ parāṃ ciṃtāmupāgamat ।।kva sā bhagavatī yā tu manojñā mahatī mahī ।।nānāvidhamahāśailanadīnagarakānanā ।।evaṃ saṃciṃtayanbrahmā bubudhe naiva bhūsthitim ।।tadā sasmāra pitaraṃ bhagavaṃtaṃ trilocanam ।।smaraṇāddevadevasya bhavasyāmitatejasaḥ ।।jñātavānsalile magnāṃ dharaṇīṃ dharaṇīpatiḥ ।।tato bhūmessamuddhāraṃ kartukāmaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।।jalakrīḍocitaṃ divyaṃ vārāhaṃ rūpamasmarat ।।mahāparvatavarṣmāṇaṃ mahājaladaniḥsvanam ।।nīlameghapratīkāśaṃ dīptaśabdaṃ bhayānakam ।।pīnavṛttaghanaskaṃdhapīnonnatakaṭītaṭam ।।hrasvavṛttorujaṃghāgraṃ sutīkṣṇapuramaṇḍalam ।।padmarāgamaṇiprakhyaṃ vṛttabhīṣaṇalocanam ।।vṛttadīrghamahāgātraṃ stabdhakarṇasthalojjvalam ।।udīrṇocchvāsaniśvāsaghūrṇitapralayārṇavam ।।visphuratsusaṭācchannakapolaskaṃdhabaṃdhuram ।।maṇibhirbhūṣaṇaiścitrairmahāratnaiḥpariṣkṛtam ।।virājamānaṃ vidyudbhirmeghasaṃghamivonnatam ।।āsthāya vipulaṃ rūpaṃ vārāhamamitaṃ vidhiḥ ।।pṛthivyuddharaṇārthāya praviveśa rasātalam ।।sa tadā śuśubhe atīva sūkaro girisaṃnibhaḥ ।।liṃgākṛtermaheśasya pādamūlaṃ gato yathā ।।tatassa salile magnāṃ pṛthivīṃ pṛthivīṃdharaḥ ।।uddhṛtyāliṃgya daṃṣṭrābhyāmunmamajja rasātalāt ।।taṃ dṛṣṭvā munayassiddhā janalokanivāsinaḥ ।।mumudurnanṛturmūrdhni tasya puṣpairavākiran ।।vapurmahāvarāhasya śuśubhe puṣpasaṃvṛtam ।।patadbhiriva khadyotaiḥ prāśuraṃjanaparvataḥ ।।tataḥ saṃsthānamānīya varāho mahatīṃ mahīm ।।svameva rūpamāsthāya sthāpayāmāsa vai vibhuḥ ।।pṛthivīṃ ca samīkṛtya pṛthivyāṃ sthāpayangirīn ।। bhūrādyāṃścaturo lokān kalpayāmāsa pūrvavat ।।iti saha mahatīṃ mahīṃ mahīdhraiḥ pralayamahājaladheradhaḥsthamadhyāt ।।upari ca viniveśya viśvakarmā caramacaraṃ ca jagatsasarja bhūyaḥ ।। chapter vāyuruvāca sargaṃ ciṃtayatastasya tadā vai buddhipūrvakam ।।pradhyānakāle mohastu prādurbhūtastamomayaḥ ।।tamomoho mahāmohastāmisraścāndhasaṃjñitaḥ ।।avidyā pañcamī caiṣā prādurbhūtā mahātmanaḥ ।।pañcadhā avasthitaḥ sargo dhyāyatastvabhimāninaḥ ।।sarvatastamasātīva bījakumbhavadāvṛtaḥ ।।bahirantaścāprakāśaḥ stabdho niḥsaṃjña eva ca ।।tasmātteṣāṃ vṛtā buddhirmukhāni karaṇāni ca ।।tasmātte saṃvṛtātmāno nagā mukhyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।taṃ dṛṣṭvā asādhakaṃ brahmā prathamaṃ sargamīdṛśam ।।aprasannamanā bhūtvā dvitīyaṃ so abhyamanyata ।।tasyābhidhāyataḥ sargaṃ tiryaksroto abhyavartata ।।antaḥprakāśāstiryaṃca āvṛtāśca bahiḥ punaḥ ।।paśvātmānastato jātā utpathagrāhiṇaśca te ।।tamapyasādhakaṃ jñātvā sargamanyamamanyata ।।tadordhvasrotaso vṛtto devasargastu sāttvikaḥ ।।te sukhaprītibahulā bahirantaśca nāvṛtāḥ ।।prakāśā bahirantaścasvabhāvādeva saṃjñitāḥ ।।tato abhidhyāyatovyaktādarvāksrotastu sādhakaḥ ।।manuṣyanāmā sañjātaḥ sargo duḥkhasamutkaṭaḥ ।।prakāśābahirantaste tamodriktā rajo adhikāḥ ।।pañcamonugrahaḥ sargaścaturdhā saṃvyavasthitaḥ ।।viparyayeṇa śaktyā ca tuṣṭyāsiddhyā tathaiva ca ।।te aparigrāhiṇaḥ sarve saṃvibhāgaratāḥ punaḥ ।।khādanāścāpyaśīlāśca bhūtādyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।।prathamo mahataḥ sargo brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।।tanmātrāṇāṃ dvitīyastu bhūtasargaḥ sa ucyate ।।vaikārikastṛtīyastu sarga aindriyakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।ityeṣa prakṛteḥ sargaḥ sambhṛto abuddhipūrvakaḥ ।।mukhyasargaścaturthastu mukhyā vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।tiryaksrotastu yaḥ proktastiryagyoniḥ sa pañcamaḥ ।।tadūrdhvasrotasaḥ ṣaṣṭho devasargastu sa smṛtaḥ ।।tato arvāk srotasāṃ sargaḥ saptamaḥ sa tu mānuṣaḥ ।।aṣṭamo anugrahaḥ sargaḥ kaumāro navamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।prākṛtāśca trayaḥ pūrve sargāste abuddhipūrvakāḥ ।।
buddhipūrvaṃ pravartante mukhyādyāḥ pañca vaikṛtāḥ ।।agre sasarja vai brahmā mānasānātmanaḥ samān ।।sanandaṃ sanakañcaiva vidvāṃsañca sanātanam ।।ṛbhuṃ sanatkumārañca pūrvameva prajāpatiḥ ।।sarve te yogino jñeyā vītarāgā vimatsarāḥ ।।iśvarāsaktamanaso na cakruḥ sṛṣṭaye matim ।।teṣu sṛṣṭyanapekṣeṣu gateṣu sanakādiṣu ।।sraṣṭukāmaḥ punarbrahmā tatāpa paramaṃ tapaḥ ।।tasyaivaṃ tapyamānasya na kiṃcitsamavartata ।।tato dīrgheṇa kālena duḥkhātkrodho vyajāyata ।।krodhāviṣṭasya netrābhyāṃ prāpatannaśrubindavaḥ ।।tatastebhyo aśrubindubhyo bhūtāḥ pretāstadābhavan ।।sarvāṃstānaśrujāndṛṣṭvā brahmātmānamaniṃdata ।।tasya tīvrā abhavanmūrchā krodhāmarṣasamudbhavā ।।mūrchitastu jahau prāṇānkrodhāviṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।।tataḥ prāṇeśvaro rudro bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ ।।prasādamatulaṃ kartuṃ prādurāsītprabhormukhāt ।।daśadhā caikadhā cakre svātmānaṃ prabhurīśvaraḥ ।।te tenoktā mahātmāno daśadhā caikadhā kṛtāḥ ।।yūyaṃ sṛṣṭā mayā vatsā lokānugrahakāraṇāt ।।tasmātsarvasya lokasya sthāpanāya hitāya ca ।।prajāsantānahetośca prayatadhvamatandritāḥ ।।evamuktāśca rurudurdudruvuśca samantataḥ ।।rodanāddrāvaṇāccaiva te rudrā nāmataḥ smṛtāḥ ।।ye rudrāste khalu prāṇā ye prāṇāste mahātmakāḥ ।।tato mṛtasya devasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।।ghṛṇī dadau punaḥ prāṇānbrahmaputro maheśvaraḥ ।।prahṛṣṭavadano rudraḥ prāṇapratyāgamādvibhoḥ ।।abhyabhāṣata viśveśo brahmāṇaṃ paramaṃ vacaḥ ।।mābhairmābhairmahābhāga viriṃca jagatāṃ guro ।।mayā te prāṇitāḥ prāṇāḥ sukhamuttiṣṭha suvrata ।।svapnānubhūtamiva tacchrutvā vākyaṃ manoharam ।।haraṃ nirīkṣya śanakairnetraiḥ phullāmbujaprabhaiḥ ।।tathā pratyāgataprāṇaḥ snigdhagambhīrayā girā ।।uvāca vacanaṃ brahmā tamuddiśya kṛtāñjaliḥ ।।tvaṃ hi darśanamātreṇa cānandayasi me manaḥ ।।ko bhavān viśvamūrtyā vā sthita ekādaśātmakaḥ ।।tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā vyājahāra maheśvaraḥ ।।spṛśan kārābhyāṃ brahmāṇaṃ susukhābhyāṃ sureśvaraḥ ।।māṃ viddhi paramātmānaṃ tava putratvamāgatam ।।ete caikādaśa rudrāstvāṃ surakṣitumāgatāḥ ।।tasmāttīvrāmimāmmūrchāṃ vidhūya madanugrahāt ।।prabuddhasva yathāpūrvaṃ prajā vai sraṣṭumarhasi ।। evaṃ bhagavatā prokto brahmā prītamanā hyabhūt ।।nānāṣṭakena viśvātmā tuṣṭāva parameśvaram ।। brahmovāca namaste bhagavan rudra bhāskarāmitatejase ।।namo bhavāya devāya rasāyāmbumayātmane ।।śarvāya kṣitirūpāya nandīsurabhaye namaḥ ।। f। īśāya vasave tubhyaṃ namassparśamayātmane ।।paśūnāṃ pataye caiva pāvakāyātitejase ।।bhīmāya vyomarūpāya śabdamātrāya te namaḥ ।। f। ugrāyograsvarūpāya yajamānātmane namaḥ ।।mahādevāya somāya namostvamṛtamūrtaye ।।evaṃ stutvā mahādevaṃ brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।।prārthayāmāsa viśveśaṃ girā praṇatipūrvayā ।।bhagavan bhūtabhavyeśa mama putra maheśvara ।।sṛṣṭihetostvamutpanno mamāṃge anaṃganāśanaḥ ।।tasmānmahati kāryesmin vyāpṛtasya jagatprabho ।।sahāyaṃ kuru sarvatra sraṣṭumarhasi sa prajāḥ ।।tenaiṣāṃ pāvito devo rudrastripuramardanaḥ ।।bāḍhamityeva tāṃ vāṇīṃ pratijagrāha śaṃkaraḥ ।।tatassa bhagavān brahmā hṛṣṭaṃ tamabhinaṃdya ca ।।sraṣṭuṃ tenābhyanujñātastathānyāścāsṛjatprajāḥ ।।marīcibhṛgvaṃgirasaḥ pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum ।।dakṣamatriṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca so asṛjanmanasaiva ca ।।purastādasṛjadbrahmā dharmaṃ saṃkalpameva ca ।। f। ityete brahmaṇaḥ putrā dvādaśādau prakīrtitāḥ ।।saha rudreṇa saṃbhūtāḥ purāṇā gṛhamedhinaḥ ।।teṣāṃ dvādaśa vaṃśāḥ syurdivyā devagaṇānvitāḥ ।।prajāvantaḥ kriyāvanto maharṣibhiralaṃkṛtāḥ ।।atha devāsurapitḥn manuṣyāṃśca catuṣṭayam ।।saha rudreṇa sisṛkṣuraṃbhasyetāni vai vidhiḥ ।।sa sṛṣṭyarthaṃ samādhāya brahmātmānamayūyujat ।।mukhādajanayaddevān pitḥṃścaivopapakṣataḥ ।।jaghanādasurān sarvān prajanādapi mānuṣān ।।avaskare kṣudhāviṣṭā rākṣasāstasya jajñire ।।putrāstamorajaḥprāyā balinaste niśācarāḥ ।।sarpā yakṣāstathā bhūtā gaṃdharvāḥ saṃprajajñire ।।vayāṃsi pakṣataḥ sṛṣṭāḥ pakṣiṇo vakṣaso asṛjat ।।mukhatojāṃstathā pārśvāduragāṃśca vinirmame ।।padbhyāṃ cāśvānsamātaṃgān śarabhān gavayān mṛgān ।।uṣṭrānaśvatarāṃścaiva nyaṃkūnanyāśca jātayaḥ ।।auṣadhyaḥ phalamūlāni romabhyastasya jajñire ।।gāyatrīṃ ca ṛcaṃ caiva trivṛtsāma rathaṃtaram ।।agniṣṭomaṃ ca yajñānāṃ nirmame prathamānmukhāt ।।yajūṃṣi traiṣṭubhaṃ chaṃdaḥstomaṃ pañcadaśaṃ tathā ।। bṛhatsāma tathokthaṃ ca dakṣiṇādasṛjanmukhāt ।।sāmāni jagatīchaṃdaḥ stomaṃ saptadaśaṃ tathā ।।vairūpyamatirātraṃ ca paścimādasṛjan mukhāt ।।ekaviṃśamatharvāṇamāptoryāmāṇameva ca ।।anuṣṭubhaṃ sa vairājamuttarādasṛjanmukhāt ।।uccāvacāni bhūtāni gātrebhyastasya jajñire ।।yakṣāḥ piśācā gaṃdharvāstathaivāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ ।।narakinnararakṣāṃsi vayaḥpaśumṛgoragāḥ ।।avyayaṃ caiva yadidaṃ sthāṇusthāvarajaṃgamam ।।teṣāṃ vai yāni karmāṇi prāksṛṣṭāni prapedire ।।tānyeva te prapadyaṃte sṛjyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।।hiṃsrāhiṃsre mṛdukrūre dharmādharmāvṛtānṛte ।।tadbhāvitāḥ prapadyaṃte tasmāttattasya rocate ।।mahābhūteṣu nānātvamiṃdriyārtheṣu muktiṣu ।।viniyogaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ dhātaiva vyadadhatsvayam ।।nāma rūpaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ prākṛtānāṃ prapañcanam ।।vedaśabdebhya evādau nirmame asau pitāmahaḥ ।।ārṣāṇi caiva nāmāni yāśca vedeṣu vṛttayaḥ ।।śarvaryaṃte prasūtānāṃ tānyevaibhyo dadāvajaḥ ।।yathartāvṛtuliṃgāni nānārūpāṇi paryaye ।।dṛśyaṃte tāni tānyeva tathā bhāvā yugādiṣu ।।ityeṣa karaṇodbhūto lokasargassvayaṃbhuvaḥ ।।mahadādyoviśeṣāṃto vikāraḥ prakṛteḥ svayam ।।caṃdrasūryaprabhājuṣṭo grahanakṣatramaṃḍitaḥ ।।nadībhiśca samudraiśca parvataiśca sa maṃḍitaḥ ।।paraiśca vividhairamyaissphītairjanapadaistathā ।।tasmin brahmavane avyakto brahmā carati sarvavit ।।avyaktabījaprabhava īśvarānugrahe sthitaḥ ।।buddhiskaṃdhamahāśākha indriyāṃtarakoṭaraḥ ।।mahābhūtapramāṇaśca viśeṣāmalapallavaḥ ।।dharmādharmasupuṣpāḍhyaḥ sukhaduḥkhaphalodayaḥ ।।ājīvyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ brahmavṛkṣaḥ sanātanaḥ ।।dyāṃ mūrdhānaṃ tasya viprā vadaṃti khaṃ vai nābhiṃ caṃdrasūryau ca netre ।।diśaḥ śrotre caraṇau ca kṣitiṃ ca so acintyātmā sarvabhūtapraṇetā ।।vaktrāttasya brahmaṇāssaṃprasūtāstadvakṣasaḥ kṣatriyāḥ pūrvabhāgāt ।।vaiśyā urubhyāṃ tasya padbhyāṃ ca śūdrāḥ sarve varṇā gātrataḥ saṃprasūtāḥ ।।
chapter ṛṣaya ūcuḥ bhavatā kathitā sṛṣṭirbhavasya paramātmanaḥ ।।caturmukhamukhāttasya saṃśayo naḥ prajāyate ।।devaśreṣṭho virūpākṣo dīptaśśūladharo haraḥ ।।kālātmā bhagavān rudraḥ kapardī nīlalohitaḥ ।।sabrahmakamimaṃ lokaṃ saviṣṇumapi pāvakam ।। yaḥ saṃharati saṃkruddho yugāṃte samupasthite ।।yasya brahmā ca viṣṇuśca praṇāmaṃ kuruto bhayāt ।।lokasaṃkocakasyāsya yasya tau vaśavartinau ।।yo ayaṃ devaḥ svakādaṃgādbrahmaviṣṇū purāsṛjat ।।sa eva hi tayornityaṃ yogakṣemakaraḥ prabhuḥ ।।sa kathaṃ bhagavān rudra ādidevaḥ purātanaḥ ।।putratvamagamacchaṃbhurbrahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।।prajāpatiśca viṣṇuśca rudrasyaitau parasparam ।।sṛṣṭau parasparasyāṃgāditi prāgapi śuśruma ।।kathaṃ punaraśeṣāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ hetubhūtayoḥ ।।guṇapradhānabhāvena prādurbhāvaḥ parasparāt ।।nāpṛṣṭaṃ bhavatā kiṃcinnāśrutaṃ ca kathaṃcana ।।bhagavacchiṣyabhūtena bhavatā sakalaṃ smṛtam ।।tattvaṃ vada yathā brahmā munīnāmavadadvibhuḥ ।।vayaṃ śraddhālavastāta śrotumīśvarasadyaśaḥ ।। vāyuruvāca sthāne pṛṣṭamidaṃ viprā bhavadbhiḥ praśnakovidaiḥ ।।idameva purā pṛṣṭo mama prāha pitāmahaḥ ।।tadahaṃ sampravakṣyāmi yathā rudrasamudbhavaḥ ।।yathā ca punarutpattirbrahmaviṣṇvoḥ parasparam ।।trayaste kāraṇātmāno jatāssākṣānmaheśvarāt ।।carācarasya viśvasya sargasthityaṃtahetavaḥ ।।paramaiśvaryasaṃyuktāḥ parameśvarabhāvitāḥ ।।tacchaktyādhiṣṭhitā nityaṃ tatkāryakaraṇakṣamāḥ ।।pitrā niyamitāḥ pūrvaṃ trayopi triṣu karmasu ।।brahmā sarge haristrāṇe rudraḥ saṃharaṇe tathā ।।tathāpyanyonyamātsaryādanyonyātiśayāśinaḥ ।।tapasā toṣayitvā svaṃ pitaraṃ parameśvaram ।।labdhvā sarvātmanā tasya prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ ।।brahmanārāyaṇau pūrvaṃ rudraḥ kalpāntare asṛjat ।।kalpāntare punarbrahmā rudraviṣṇū jaganmayaḥ ।।viṣṇuśca bhagavānrudraṃ brahmāṇamasṛjatpunaḥ ।।nārāyaṇaṃ punarbrahmā brahmāṇamasṛjatpunaḥ ।।evaṃ kalpeṣu kalpeṣu brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ ।।paraspareṇa jāyaṃte parasparahitaiṣiṇaḥ ।।tattatkalpāntavṛttāntamadhikṛtya maharṣibhiḥ ।।prabhāvaḥ kathyate teṣāṃ parasparasamudbhavāt ।।śṛṇu teṣāṃ kathāṃ citrāṃ puṇyāṃ pāpapramocinīm ।।kalpe tatpuruṣe vṛttāṃ brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।।purā nārāyaṇo nāma kalpe vai meghavāhane ।।divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu megho bhūtvāvahaddharām ।।tasya bhāvaṃ samālakṣya viṣṇorviśvajagadguruḥ ।।sarvassarvātmabhāvena pradadau śaktimavyayām ।।śaktiṃ labdhvā tu sarvātmā śivātsarveśvarāttadā ।।sasarja bhagāvan viṣṇurviśvaṃ viśvasṛjā saha ।। viṣṇostadvaibhavaṃ dṛṣṭvā sṛṣṭastena pitāmahaḥ ।।īrṣyayā parayā grastaḥ prahasannidamabravīt ।।gaccha viṣṇo mayā jñātaṃ tava sargasya kāraṇam ।।āvayoradhikaścāsti sa rudro nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। f।tasya devādhidevasya prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ ।।sraṣṭā tvaṃ bhagavānādyaḥ pālakaḥ paramārthataḥ ।।ahaṃ ca tapasārādhya rudraṃ tridaśanāyakam ।।tvayā saha jagatsarvaṃ srakṣyāmyatra na saṃśayaḥ ।।evaṃ viṣṇumupālabhya bhagavānabjasambhavaḥ ।।evaṃ vijñāpayāmāsa tapasā prāpya śaṃkaram ।।bhagavan devadeveśa viśveśvara maheśvara ।।tava vāmāṃgajo viṣṇurdakṣiṇāṃgabhavo hyaham ।।mayā saha jagatsarvaṃ tathāpyasṛjadacyutaḥ ।।sa matsarādupālabdhastvadāśrayabalānmayā ।।madbhāvānnādhikasteti bhāvastvayi maheśvare ।।tvatta eva samutpattirāvayossadṛśī yataḥ ।।tasya bhaktyā yathāpūrvaṃ prasādaṃ kṛtavānasi ।।tathā mamāpi tatsarvaṃ dātumarhasi śaṃkara ।।iti vijñāpitastena bhagavān bhaganetrahā ।।nyāyena vai dadau sarvaṃ tasyāpi sa ghṛṇānidhiḥ ।।labdhvaivamīśvarādeva brahmā sarvātmatāṃ kṣaṇāt ।।tvaramāṇotha saṃgamya dadarśa puruṣottamam ।।kṣīrārṇavālaye śubhre vimāne sūryasaṃnibhe ।।hemaratnānvite divye manasā tena nirmite ।।anaṃtabhogaśayyāyāṃ śayānaṃ paṃkajekṣaṇam ।।caturbhujamudārāṃgaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam ।।śaṃkhacakradharaṃ saumyaṃ candrabiṃbasamānanam ।।śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ devaṃ prasannamadhurasmitam ।।dharāmṛdukarāṃbhojasparśaraktapadāṃbujam ।।kṣīrārṇavāmṛtamiva śayānaṃ yoganidrayā ।।tamasā kālarudrākhyaṃ rajasā kanakāṃḍajam ।।sattvena sarvagaṃ viṣṇuṃ nirguṇatve maheśvaram ।।taṃ dṛṣṭvā puruṣaṃ brahmā pragalbhamidamabravīt ।।grasāmi tvāmahaṃ viṣṇo tvamātmānaṃ yathā purā ।।tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā pratibuddhya pitāmaham ।।udaikṣata mahābāhussmitamīṣaccakāra ca ।।tasminnavasare viṣṇurgrastastena mahātmanā ।।sṛṣṭaśca brahmaṇā sadyo bhruvormadhyādayatnataḥ ।।tasminnavasare sākṣādbhagavānindubhūṣaṇaḥ ।।śaktiṃ tayorapi draṣṭumarūpo rūpamāsthitaḥ ।।prasādamatulaṃ kartuṃ purā dattavarastayoḥ ।।āgacchattatra yatremau brahmanārāyaṇau sthitau ।।atha tuṣṭuvaturdevaṃ prītau bhītau ca kautukāt ।।praṇematuśca bahuśo bahumānena dūrataḥ ।।
bhavopi bhagavānetāvanugṛhya pinākadhṛk ।।sādaraṃ paśyatoreva tayoraṃtaradhīyata ।। chapter vāyuruvāca pratikalpaṃ pravakṣyāmi rudrāvirbhāvakāraṇam ।।yato vicchinnasaṃtānā brahmasṛṣṭiḥ pravartate ।।kalpekalpe prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā brahmā brahmāṃḍasaṃbhavaḥ ।।avṛddhihetorbhūtānāṃ mumoha bhṛśaduḥkhitaḥ ।।tasya duḥkhapraśāṃtyarthaṃ prajānāṃ ca vivṛddhaye ।।tattatkalpeṣu kālātmā rudro rudragaṇādhipaḥ ।।nirdiṣṭaḥ pamameśena maheśo nīlalohitaḥ ।।putro bhūtvānugṛhṇāti brahmāṇaṃ brahmaṇonujaḥ ।।sa eva bhagavānīśastejorāśiranāmayaḥ ।।anādinidhanodhātā bhūtasaṃkocako vibhuḥ ।।paramaiśvaryasaṃyuktaḥ parameśvarabhāvitaḥ ।।tacchaktyādhiṣṭhitaśśaśvattaccihnairapi cihnitaḥ ।।tannāmanāmā tadrūpastatkāryakaraṇakṣamaḥ ।।tattulyavyavahāraśca tadājñāparipālakaḥ ।।sahasrādityasaṃkāśaścandrāvayavabhūṣaṇaḥ ।।bhujaṃgahārakeyūravalayo muṃjamekhalaḥ ।।jalaṃdharaviriṃcendrakapālaśakalojjvalaḥ ।।gaṅgātuṃgataraṃgārdhapiṃgalānanamūrdhajaḥ ।।bhagnadaṃṣṭrāṃkurākrāntaprāntakāntadharādharaḥ
