।।sarve prācetasā nāma dhanurvedasya pāragāḥ ।।yeṣāṃ svāyaṃbhuve dakṣaḥ putratvamagamatpurā ।।triyambakasya śāpena cākṣuṣasyāṃtare manoḥ ।।ityete brahmaputrāṇāṃ dharmādīnāmmahātmanām ।।nātisaṃkṣepato viprā nāti vistarataḥ kramāt ।।varṇitā vai mayā vaṃśā divyā devagaṇānvitāḥ ।।kriyāvaṃtaḥ prajāvaṃto mahardhibhiralaṃkṛtāḥ ।।prajānāṃ saṃniveśo ayaṃ prajāpatisamudbhavaḥ ।।na hi śakyaḥ prasaṃkhyātuṃ varṣakoṭiśatairapi ।।rājñāmapi ca yo vaṃśo dvidhā so api pravartate ।।sūryavaṃśassomavaṃśa iti puṇyatamaḥ kṣitau ।। ikṣvākurambarīṣaśca yayātirnāhuṣādayaḥ ।।puṇyaślokāḥ śrutā ye atra te pi tadvaṃśasaṃbhavāḥ ।।anye ca rājaṛṣayo nānāvīryasamanvitā ।।kiṃ taiḥ phalamanutkrāṃtairuktapūrvaiḥ purātanaiḥ ।।kiṃ ceśvarakathā vṛttā yatra tatrānyakīrtanam ।।na sadbhiḥ saṃmataṃ matvā notsahe bahubhāṣitum ।।prasaṃgādīśvarasyaiva prabhāvadyotanādapi ।।sargādayo api kathitā ityatra tatpravistaraiḥ ।।
chapter ṛṣaya ūcuḥ devī dakṣasya tanayā tyaktvā dākṣāyaṇī tanum ।।kathaṃ himavataḥ putrī menāyāmabhavatpurā ।।kathaṃ ca nindito rudro dakṣeṇa ca mahātmanā ।।nimittamapi kiṃ tatra yena syānniṃdito bhavaḥ ।।utpannaśca kathaṃ dakṣo abhiśāpādbhavasya tu ।।cākṣuṣasyāṃtare pūrvaṃ manoḥ prabrūhi māruta ।।vāyuruvāva śṛṇvaṃtu kathayiṣyāmi dakṣasya laghucetasaḥ ।।vṛttaṃ pāpātpramādācca viśvāmaravidūṣaṇam ।।purā surāsurāḥ sarve siddhāśca paramarṣayaḥ ।।kadāciddraṣṭumīśānaṃ himavacchikharaṃ yayuḥ ।।tadā devaśca devī ca divyāsanagatāvubhau ।।darśanaṃ dadatusteṣāṃ devādīnāṃ dvijottamāḥ ।।tadānīmeva dakṣo api gatastatra sahāmaraiḥ ।।jāmātaraṃ haraṃ draṣṭuṃ draṣṭuṃ cātmasutāṃ satīm ।।tadātmagauravāddevo devyā dakṣe samāgate ।।devādibhyo viśeṣeṇa na kadācidabhūtsmṛtiḥ ।।tasya tasyāḥ paraṃ bhāvamajñātuścāpi kevalam ।।putrītyevaṃ vimūḍhasya tasyāṃ vairamajāyata ।।tatastenaiva vaireṇa vidhinā ca pracoditaḥ ।।nājuvāha bhavaṃ dakṣo dīkṣitastāmapi dviṣan ।।anyāñ āmātarassarvānāhūya sa yathākramam ।।śataśaḥ puṣkalāmarcāñcakāra ca pṛthakpṛthak ।।tathā tānsaṃgatāñchrutvā nāradasya mukhāttadā ।।yayau rudrāya rudrāṇī vijñāpya bhavanaṃ pituḥ ।।atha saṃnihitaṃ divyaṃ vimānaṃ viśvatomukham ।।lakṣaṇāḍhyaṃ sukhārohamatimātramanoharam ।।taptajāṃbūnadaprakhyaṃ citraratnapariṣkṛtam ।।muktāmayavitānāgnyaṃ sragdāmasamalaṃkṛtam ।।taptakaṃcananirvyūhaṃ ratnastaṃbhaśatāvṛtam ।।vajrakalpitasopānaṃ vidrumastaṃbhatoraṇam ।। puṣpapaṭṭaparistīrṇaṃ citraratnamahāsanam ।।vajrajālakiracchidramacchidramaṇikuṭṭimam ।।maṇidaṃḍamanojñena mahāvṛṣabhalakṣmaṇā ।।alaṃkṛtapurobhāgamabbhraśubbhreṇa ketunā ।।ratnakaṃcukaguptāṃgaiścitravetrakapāṇibhiḥ ।।adhiṣṭhitamahādvāramapradhṛṣyairguṇeśvaraiḥ ।।mṛdaṃgatālagītādiveṇuvīṇāviśāradaiḥ ।।vidagdhaveṣabhāṣaiśca bahubhiḥ strījanairvṛtam ।।āruroha mahādevī saha priyasakhījanaiḥ ।।cāmāravyañjanaṃ tasyā vajradaṃḍamanohare ।।gṛhītvā rudrakanye dve vivījaturubhe śubhe ।।tadācāmarayormadhye devyā vadanamābabhau ।।anyonyaṃ yudhyatormadhye haṃsayoriva paṃkajam ।।chatraṃ śaśinibhaṃ tasyāścūḍopari sumālinī ।।dhṛtamuktāparikṣiptaṃ babhāra premanirbharā ।।tacchatramujjvalaṃ devyā ruruce vadanopari ।।uparyamṛtabhāṃḍasya maṃḍalaṃ śaśino yathā ।।atha cāgre samāsīnā susmitāsyā śubhāvatī ।।akṣadyūtavinodena ramayāmāsa vai satīm ।।suyaśāḥ pāduke devyāśśubhe ratnapariṣkṛte ।।stanayoraṃtare kṛtvā tadā devīmasevataḥ ।।anyā kāṃcanacārvaṃgī dīptaṃ jagrāha darpaṇam ।।aparā tālavṛntaṃ ca parā tāṃbūlapeṭikām ।।kācitkrīḍāśukaṃ cāru kare akuruta bhāminī ।।kācittu sumanojñāni puṣpāṇi surabhīṇi ca ।।kācidābharaṇādhāraṃ babhāra kamalekṣaṇā ।।kācicca punarālepaṃ suprasūtaṃ śubhāṃjanam ।।anyāśca sadṛśāstāstā yathāsvamucitakriyāḥ ।।āvṛttyā tāṃ mahādevīmasevaṃta samaṃtataḥ ।।atīva śuśubhe tāsāmaṃtare parameśvarī ।।tārāpariṣado madhye caṃdralekheva śāradī ।।tataḥ śaṃkhasamutthasya nādasya samanaṃtaram ।।prāsthāniko mahānādaḥ paṭahaḥ samatāḍyata ।।tato madhuravādyāni saha tālodyataissvanaiḥ ।।anāhatāni sanneduḥ kāhalānāṃ śatāni ca ।।sāyudhānāṃ gaṇeśānāṃ maheśasamatejasām ।।sahasrāṇi śatānyaṣṭau tadānīṃ purato yayuḥ ।।teṣāṃ madhye vṛṣārūḍho gajārūḍho yathā guruḥ ।।jagāma gaṇapaḥ śrīmān somanaṃdīśvarārcitaḥ ।।devaduṃdubhayo nedurdivi divyasukhā ghanāḥ ।।nanṛturmunayassarve mumuduḥ siddhayoginaḥ ।।sasṛjuḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiṃ ca vitānopari vāridāḥ ।।tadā devagaṇaiścānyaiḥ pathi sarvatra saṃgatā ।।kṣaṇādiva piturgehaṃ praviveśa maheśvarī ।।tāṃ dṛṣṭvā kupito dakṣaścātmanaḥ kṣayakāraṇāt ।।tasyā yavīyasībhyo api cakre pūjāma satkṛtām ।। tadā śaśimukhī devī pitaraṃ sadasi sthitam ।।aṃbikā yuktamavyagramuvācākṛpaṇaṃ vacaḥ ।। devyuvāca brahmādayaḥ piśācāṃtā yasyājñāvaśavartinaḥ ।।sa devassāṃprataṃ tāta vidhinā nārcitaḥ kila ।।tadāstāṃ mama jyāyasyāḥ putryāḥ pūjāṃ kimīdṛśīm ।।asatkṛtāmavajñāya kṛtavānasi garhitam ।।evamukto abravīdenāṃ dakṣaḥ krodhādamarṣitaḥ ।।tvattaḥ śreṣṭhā viśiṣṭāśca pūjyā bālāḥ sutā mama ।।tāsāṃ tu ye ca bhartāraste me bahumatā mudā ।।gunaiścāpyadhikāssarvairbhartuste tryaṃbakādapi ।।stabdhātmā tāmasaśśarvastvamimaṃ samupāśritā ।।tena tvāmavamanye ahaṃ pratikūlo hi me bhavaḥ ।।tathoktā pitaraṃ dakṣaṃ kruddhā devī tamabravīt ।।śṛṇvatāmeva sarveṣāṃ ye yajñasadasi sthitāḥ ।।akasmānmama bhartāramajātāśeṣadūṣaṇam ।।vācā dūṣayase dakṣa sākṣāllokamaheśvaram ।।vidyācauro gurudrohī vedeśvaravidūṣakaḥ ।।ta ete bahupāpmānassarve daṃḍyā iti śrutiḥ ।।tasmādatyutkaṭasyāsya pāpasya sadṛśo bhṛśam ।।sahasā dāruṇo daṃḍastava daivādbhaviṣyati ।।tvayā na pūjito yasmāddevadevastriyaṃbakaḥ ।।tasmāttava kulaṃ duṣṭaṃ naṣṭamityavadhāraya ।।ityuktvā pitaraṃ ruṣṭā satī saṃtyaktasādhvasā ।।tadīyāṃ ca tanuṃ tyaktvā himavaṃtaṃ yayau girim ।।sa parvataparaḥ śrīmāṃllabdhapuṇyaphalodayaḥ ।।tadarthameva kṛtavān suciraṃ duścaraṃ tapaḥ ।।tasmāttamanugṛhṇāti bhūdhareśvaramīśvarī ।।svecchayā pitaraṃ cakre svātmano yogamāyayā ।।yadā gatā satī dakṣaṃ viniṃdya bhayavihvalā ।।tadā tirohitā maṃtrā vihataśca tato adhvaraḥ ।।tadupaśrutya gamanaṃ devyāstripurumardanaḥ ।।dakṣāya ca ṛṣibhyaśca cukopa ca śaśāpa tān ।।yasmādavamatā dakṣamatkṛte anāgasā satī ।।pūjitāścetarāḥ sarvāḥ svasutā bhartṛbhiḥ saha ।।vaivasvate aṃtare tasmāttava jāmātarastvamī ।।utpatsyaṃte samaṃ sarve brahmayajñeṣvayonijāḥ ।।bhavitā mānuṣo rājā cākṣuṣasya tvamanvaye ।।prācīnabarhiṣaḥ pautraḥ putraścāpi pracetasaḥ ।।ahaṃ tatrāpi te vighnamācariṣyāmi durmate ।।dharmārthakāmayukteṣu karmasvapi punaḥ punaḥ ।।tenaivaṃ vyāhṛto dakṣo rudreṇāmitatejasā ।।svāyaṃbhuvīṃ tanuṃ tyaktvā papāta bhuvi duḥkhitaḥ ।।tataḥ prācetaso dakṣo jajñe vai cākṣuṣe antare ।।prācīnabarhiṣaḥ pautraḥ putraścaiva pracetasām ।।
bhṛgvādayo api jātā vai manorvaivasvatasya tu ।।aṃtare brahmaṇo yajñe vāruṇīṃ bibhratastanum ।।tadā dakṣasya dharmārthaṃ yajñe tasya durātmanaḥ ।।maheśaḥ kṛtavānvighnaṃ manā vavasvate sati ।। iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe satīdehatyāgo nāmāṣṭādaśo adhyāyaḥ chapter ṛṣaya ūcuḥ kathaṃ dakṣasya dharmārthaṃ pravṛttasya durātmanaḥ ।।maheśaḥ kṛtavān vighnametadicchāma veditum ।।vāyuruvāca viśvasya jagato māturapi devyāstapobalāt ।।pitṛbhāvamupāgamya mudite himavadgirau ।।deve api tatkṛtodvāhe himavacchikharālaye ।।saṃkīḍati tayā sārdhaṃ kāle bahutare gate ।।vaivasvate aṃtare prāpte dakṣaḥ prācetasaḥ svayam ।।aśvamedhena yajñena yakṣyamāṇo anvapadyata ।।tato himavataḥ pṛṣṭhe dakṣo vai yajñamāharat ।।gaṃgādvāre śubhe deśe ṛṣisiddhaniṣevite ।।tasya tasminmakhedevāḥ sarve śakra purogamāḥ ।।gamanāya samāgamya buddhimāpedire tadā ।।ādityā vasavo rudrāssādhyāssaha marudgaṇaiḥ ।।ūṣmapāḥ somapāścaiva ājyapā dhūmapāstathā ।।aśvinau pitaraścaiva tathā cānye maharṣayaḥ ।।viṣṇunā sahitāḥ sarve svāgatā yajñabhāginaḥ ।।dṛṣṭvā devakulaṃ sarvamīśvareṇa vināgatam ।।dadhīco manyunāviṣṭo dakṣamevamabhāṣata ।।dadhīca uvāca aprapūjye caiva pūjā pūjyānāṃ cāpya pūjane ।।naraḥ pāpamavāpnoti mahadvai nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।asatāṃ saṃmatiryatra satāmavamatistathā ।।daṃḍo devakṛtastatra sadyaḥ patati dāruṇaḥ ।।evamuktvā tu viprarṣiḥ punardakṣamabhāṣata ।।pūjyaṃ tu paśubhartāraṃ kasmānnārcayase prabhum ।।dakṣa uvāca saṃti me bahavo rudrāḥ śūlahastāḥ kapardinaḥ ।।ekādaśāvasthitā ye nānyaṃ vedmi maheśvaram ।।dadhīca uvāca kimebhiramarairanyaiḥ pūjitairadhvare phalam ।।rājā cedadhvarasyāsya na rudraḥ pūjyate tvayā ।।brahmaviṣṇumaheśānāṃ sraṣṭā yaḥ prabhuravyayaḥ ।।brahmādayaḥ piśācāṃtā yasya kaiṃkaryavādinaḥ ।।prakṛtīnāṃ paraścaiva puruṣasya ca yaḥ paraḥ ।।ciṃtyate yogavidvadbhi ṛṣibhistattvadarśibhiḥ ।।akṣaraṃ paramaṃ brahma hyasacca sadasacca yat ।।anādimadhyanidhanamapratarkyaṃ sanātanam ।।yaḥ sraṣṭā caiva saṃhartā bhartā caiva maheśvaraḥ ।। tasmādanyaṃ na paśyāmi śaṃkarātmānamadhvare ।। dakṣa uvāca etanmakheśasya suvarṇapātre haviḥ samastaṃ vidhimaṃtrapūtam ।।viṣṇornayāmyapratimasya bhāgaṃ prabhorvibhajyāvahanīyamadya ।।dadhīca uvāca yasmānnārādhito rudrassarvadeveśvareśvaraḥ ।।tasmāddakṣa tavāśeṣo yajño ayaṃ na bhaviṣyati ।।ityuktvā vacanaṃ kruddho dadhīco munisattamaḥ ।।nirgamya ca tato deśājjagāma svakamāśramam ।।nirgate api munau tasmindevā dakṣaṃ na tatyajuḥ ।।avaśyamanubhāvitvādanarthasya tu bhāvinaḥ ।।etasminneva kāle tu jñātvaitatsarvamīśvarāt ।।dagdhuṃ dakṣādhvaraṃ viprā devī devamacodayat ।।devyā saṃcodito devo dakṣādhvarajighāṃsayā ।।sasarja sahasā vīraṃ vīrabhadraṃ gaṇeśvaram ।।sahasravadanaṃ devaṃ sahasrakamalekṣaṇam ।।sahasramudgaradharaṃ sahasraśarapāṇikam ।।śūlaṭaṃkagadāhastaṃ dīptakārmukadhāriṇam ।।cakravajradharaṃ ghoraṃ caṃdrārdhakṛtaśekharam ।।kuliśodyotitakaraṃ taḍijjvalitamūrdhajam ।।daṃṣṭrākarālaṃ bibhrāṇaṃ mahāvaktraṃ mahodaram ।।vidyujjihvaṃ pralaṃboṣṭhaṃ meghasāgaraniḥsvanam ।।vasānaṃ carma vaiyāghraṃ mahadrudhiranisravam ।।gaṇḍadvitayasaṃsṛṣṭamaṇḍalīkṛtakuṇḍalam ।।varāmaraśiromālāvalīkalitaśekharam ।।raṇannūpurakeyūramahākanakabhūṣitam ।।ratnasaṃcayasaṃdīptaṃ tārahārāvṛtorasam ।।mahāśarabhaśārdūlasiṃhaiḥ sadṛśavikramam ।।praśastamattamātaṃgasamānagamanālasam ।।śaṃkhacāmarakuṃdendumṛṇālasadṛśaprabham ।।satuṣāramivādrīndraṃ sākṣājjaṃgamatāṃ gatam ।।jvālāmālāparikṣiptaṃ dīptamauktikabhūṣaṇam ।।tejasā caiva dīvyaṃtaṃ yugāṃta iva pāvakam ।।sa jānubhyāṃ mahīṃ gatvā praṇataḥ prāṃjalistataḥ ।।pārśvato devadevasya paryatiṣṭhadgaṇeśvaraḥ ।।manyunā cāsṛjadbhadrāṃ bhadrakālīṃ maheśvarīm ।।ātmanaḥ karmasākṣitve tena gaṃtuṃ sahaiva tu ।।taṃ dṛṣṭvāvasthitaṃ vīrabhadraṃ kālāgnisannibham ।।bhadrayā sahitaṃ prāha bhadramastviti śaṃkaraḥ ।।sa ca vijñāpayāmāsa saha devyā maheśvaram ।।ājñāpaya mahādeva kiṃ kāryaṃ karavāṇyaham ।।tatastripurahā prāha haimavatyāḥ priyecchayā ।।vīrabhadraṃ mahābāhuṃ vācā vipulanādayā ।।devadeva uvāca prācetasasya dakṣasya yajñaṃ sadyo vināśaya ।।bhadrakālyā sahāsi tvametatkṛtyaṃ gaṇeśvara ।।
ahamapyanayā sārdhaṃ raibhyāśramasapīpataḥ ।।sthitvā vīkṣe gaṇeśāna vikramaṃ tava duḥsaham ।।vṛkṣā kanakhale ye tu gaṃgādvārasamīpagāḥ ।।suvarṇaśṛṃgasya girermerumaṃdarasaṃnibhāḥ ।।tasminpradeśe dakṣasya yujñaḥ saṃprati vartate ।।sahasā tasya yajñasya vighātaṃ kuru mā ciram ।।ityukte sati devena devī himagirīndrajā ।।bhadraṃ bhadraṃ ca saṃprekṣya vatsaṃ dhenurivaurasam ।।āliṃgya ca samāghrāya mūrdhni ṣaḍvadanaṃ yathā ।।sasmitā vacanaṃ prāha madhuraṃ madhuraṃ svayam ।। devyuvāca vatsa bhadra mahābhāga mahābalaparākrama ।।matpriyārthaṃ tvamutpanno mama manyuṃ pramārjaka ।।yajñeśvaramanāhūya yajñakarmarato abhavat ।।dakṣaṃ vaireṇa taṃ tasmādbhiṃdhi yajñaṃ gaṇeśvara ।।yajñalakṣmīmalakṣmīṃ tvaṃ bhadra kṛtvā mamājñayā ।।yajamānaṃ ca taṃ hatvā vatsa hiṃsaya bhadrayā ।।aśeṣāmiva tāmājñāṃ śivayościtrakṛtyayoḥ ।।mūrdhni kṛtvā namaskṛtya bhadro gaṃtuṃ pracakrame ।।athaiṣa bhagavānkruddhaḥ pretāvāsakṛtālayaḥ ।।vīrabhadro mahādevo devyā manyupramārjakaḥ ।।sasarja romakūpebhyo romajākhyāngaṇeśvarān ।।dakṣiṇādbhujadeśāttu śatakoṭigaviśvarān ।।pādāttathorudeśācca pṛṣṭhātpārśvānmukhādgalāt ।।guhyādgulphācchiromadhyātkaṃṭhādāsyāttathodarāt ।।tadā gaṇeśvarairbhadrairbhadratulyaparākramaiḥ ।।saṃchāditamabhūtsarvaṃ sākāśavivaraṃ jagat ।।sarve sahasrahastāste sahasrāyudhapāṇayaḥ ।।rudrasyānucarāssarve sarve rudrasamaprabhāḥ ।।śūlaśaktigadāhastāṣṭaṃkopalaśilādharāḥ ।।kālāgnirudrasadṛśāstrinetrāśca jaṭādharāḥ ।।nipeturbhṛśamākāśe śataśassiṃhavāhanāḥ ।।vineduśca mahānādāñjaladā iva bhadrajāḥ ।।tairbhadrairbhagavānmadrastathā parivṛto babhau ।।kālānalaśatairyukto yathāṃte kālabhairavaḥ ।।teṣāṃ madhye samāruhya vṛṣeṃdraṃ vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ ।।jagāma bhagavānbhadraśśubhamabhraṃ yathā bhavaḥ ।।tasminvṛṣabhamārūḍhe bhadre tu bhasitaprabhaḥ ।।babhāra mauktikaṃ chatraṃ gṛhītasitacāmaraḥ ।।sa tadā śuśubhe pārśve bhadrasya bhasitaprabhaḥ ।।bhagavāniva śailendraḥ pārśve viśvajagadguroḥ ।।so api tena babhau bhadraḥ śvetacāmarapāṇinā ।।bālasomena saumyena yathā śūlavarāyudhaḥ ।।dadhmau śaṃkhaṃ sitaṃ bhadraṃ bhadrasya purataḥ śubham ।।bhānukaṃpo mahātejā hemaratnairalaṃkṛtaḥ ।।devaduṃdubhayo nedurdivyasaṃkulaniḥsvanāḥ ।। vavṛṣuśśataśo mūrdhni puṣpavarṣaṃ balāhakāḥ ।।phullānāṃ madhugarbhāṇāṃ puṣpāṇāṃ gaṃdhabaṃdhavaḥ ।।mārgānukūlasaṃvāhā vabuśca pathi mārutāḥ ।।tato gaṇeśvarāḥ sarve mattā yuddhabaloddhatāḥ ।। nanṛturmumudur edurjahasurjagadurjaguḥ ।।tadā bhadragaṇāṃtaḥstho babhau bhadraḥ sa bhadrayā ।।yathā rudragaṇāṃtaḥ sthastryambakoṃbikayā saha ।।tatkṣaṇādeva dakṣasya yajñavāṭaṃ raṇmayam ।।praviveśa mahābāhurvīrabhadro mahānugaḥ ।।tatastu dakṣapratipāditasya kratupradhānasya gaṇapradhānaḥ ।।prayogabhūmiṃ praviveśa bhadro rudro yathāṃte bhuvanaṃ didhakṣuḥ ।।iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe vīrabhadrotpattivarṇanaṃ nāmaikonaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ
chapter vāyuruvāca tato viṣṇupradhānānāṃ surāṇāmamitaujasām ।।dadarśa ca mahatsatraṃ citradhvajaparicchadam ।।sudarbhaṛtusaṃstīrṇaṃ susamiddhahutāśanam ।।kāṃcanairyajñabhāṃḍaiśca viṣṇussvanāmāṃkaṃ bāṇamavyāhataṃ kvacit ।।sasarja krodharaktā kṣastamuddiśya gaṇeśvaram ।।taṃ bāṇaṃ bāṇavaryeṇa bhadro bhadrāhvayeṇa tu ।। f। aprāptameva bhagavāñciccheda śatadhā pathi ।।athaikeneṣuṇā samupasthitam ।।smayanniva gaṇeśāno vyaṣṭaṃbhayadayatnataḥ ।।staṃbhitāṃgastu taccakraṃ ghoramapratimaṃ kvacit ।।icchannapi samutsraṣṭuṃ na viṣṇurabhavatkṣamaḥ ।।śvasannivaikamuddhṛtya bāhuṃ surāḥ ।।samunnaddhā gaṇendreṇa mṛgeṃdreṇeva govṛṣāḥ ।। f। pragṛhītāyudhā yauddhuṃkruddhāḥ samupatasthire ।।tāndṛṣṭvā samare bhadraḥkṣudrāniva harirmṛgān ।।sākṣādrudratanurvīro varavīragaṇāvṛtaḥ ।।tadā tridaśavīrāṇāmasṛksalilavāhinī ।।
prāvartata nadī ghorā prāṇināṃ bhayaśaṃsinī ।।rudhireṇa pariklinnā yajñabhūmistadā babhau ।।raktārdravasanā śyāmā hataśuṃbheva kaiśikī ।।tasminmahati saṃvṛtte samare bhṛśadāruṇe ।।bhayeneva paritrastā ।।yajamānassvayaṃ dakṣau brahmaputraprajāpatiḥ ।। f।dharmādayassadasyāśca rakṣitā garuḍadhvajaḥ ।।bhāgāṃśca pratigṛhṇaṃti sākṣādiṃdrādayaḥ surāḥ ।।tathāpi yajamānasya yajñasya ca sahartvijaḥ ।।sadya viṣṇupurogamāḥ ।।kṣaṇātkaṣṭāṃ daśāmetya tresuḥ stokāvaśeṣitā ।।trastāṃstānsamare vīrān devānanyāṃśca vai gaṇāḥ ।।pramathāḥ paramakruddhā vīrabhadrapraṇoditāḥ ।।pragṛhya ca tathā doṣaṃ sauminī bhavabandhādvai muktā abhūttava sevanāt ।। viṣṇuruvāca tvaṃ śaṃbho kaharīśāśca rajassattvatamoguṇaiḥ ।।kartā pātā tathā hartā janānugrahakāṃkṣayā ।।sarvagarvāpahārī ca sarvatejovilāsakaḥ kasya syātprasanne parameśvare ।।yadidaṃ devadevānāṃ kṛtamantuṣu dūṣaṇam ।।tadidaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ manyeta aṃgīkāragauravāt ।।iti vijñāpyamānastu brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā ।।vilokya vadanaṃ devyā ।।smayannivāvadatprekṣya mā bhairiti ghṛṇānidhiḥ ।।tathoktvā brahmaṇastasya pituḥ priyacikīrṣayā ।।gāṇapatyaṃ dadau tasmai dakṣāyākṣayamīśvaraḥ ।।tato brahmādayo devā abhivaṃdya kṛta ṃjaliḥ ।।tuṣṭuvuḥ praśrayā vācā śaṃkaraṃ girijādhipam ।।brahmādaya ūcuḥ jaya śaṃkara deveśa dīnānātha mahāprabho ।। kṛpāṃ kuru maheśānāparādhaṃ no kṣamasva vai ।।makhapāla makhādhīśa makhavidhvaṃsakāraka ।।kṛpāṃ kuru maśānāparādhaṃ naḥ kṣamasva vai ।।devadeva pareśāna bhaktaprāṇaprapoṣaka ।।duṣṭadaṇḍaprada svāminkṛpāṃ kuru namo astu te ।।tvaṃ prabho garvahartā vai duṣṭānāṃ tvāmajānatām ।।rakṣako hi viśeṣeṇa satāṃ tvatsaktacetasām ।।adbhutaṃ caritaṃ te hi niścitaṃ kṛpayā tava ।।sarvāparādhaḥ kṣaṃtavyo vibhavo dīnavatsalāḥ ।। vāyuruvāca iti stuto mahādevo brahmādyairamaraiḥ prabhuḥ ।।sa bhaktavatsalassvāmī tutoṣa karuṇodadhiḥ ।।cakārānugrahaṃ teṣāṃ brahmādīnāṃ divaukasām ।।dadau narāṃśca suprītyā śaṃkaro dīnavatsalaḥ ।।sa ca tatastridaśāñcharaṇāgatān paramakāruṇikaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।।anugatasmitalakṣaṇayā ivāmbaratontaradhāddharaḥ ।।atha surā api te vigatavyathāḥ kathitabhadrasubhadraparākramāḥ ।।sapadi khena sukhena yathāsukhaṃ yayuranekamukhāḥ maghavanmukhāḥ ।।

।।śakyamapyasya saundaryaṃ na varṇayitumutsahe ।।parvatāntarasaundaryaṃ sādhāraṇavidhāraṇāt ।।idantu śakyate vaktumasminparvatasundare ।।ṛddhyā kayāpi saundaryamīśvarāvāsayogyatā ।।ata eva hi devena devyāḥ priyacikīrṣayā ।।atīva ramaṇīyoyaṃ girirantaḥpurīkṛtaḥ ।। mekhalābhūmayastasya vimalopalapādapāḥ ।।śivayornityasānnidhyānnyakkurvaṃtyakhilaṃjagat ।।pitṛbhyāṃ jagato nityaṃ snānapānopayogataḥ ।।avāptapuṇyasaṃskāraḥ prasaradbhiritastataḥ ।।laghuśītalasaṃsparśairacchācchairnirjharāmbubhiḥ ।।adhirājyena cādrīṇāmadrīreṣo abhiṣicyate ।।niśāsu śikharaprāntarvartinā sa śiloccayaḥ ।।caṃdreṇācala sāmrājyacchatreṇeva virājate ।।sa śailaścaṃcalībhūtairbālaiścāmarayoṣitām ।।sarvaparvatasāmrājyacāmarairiva vījyate ।।prātarabhyudite bhānau bhūdharo ratnabhūṣitaḥ ।।darpaṇe dehasaubhāgyaṃ draṣṭukāma iva sthitaḥ ।।kūjadvihaṃgavācālairvātoddhṛtalatābhujaiḥ ।।vimuktapuṣpaiḥ satataṃ vyālambimṛdupallavaiḥ ।।latāpratānajaṭilaistarubhistapasairiva ।।jayāśiṣā sahābhyarcya niṣevyata ivādrirāṭ ।।adhomukhairūrdhvamukhaiśśṛṃgaistiryaṅmukhaistathā ।।prapatanniva pātāle bhūpṛṣṭhādutpatanniva ।।parītaḥ sarvato dikṣu bhramanniva vihāyasi ।।paśyanniva jagatsarvaṃ nṛtyanniva nirantaram ।।guhāmukhaiḥ pratidinaṃ vyāttāsyo vipulodaraiḥ ।।ajīrṇalāvaṇyatayā jṛṃbhamāṇa ivācalaḥ ।।grasanniva jagatsarvaṃ pibanniva payonidhim ।।vamanniva tamontasthaṃ mādyanniva khamambudaiḥ ।।nivāsa bhūmayastāstā darpaṇapratimodarāḥ ।।tiraskṛtātapāssnigdhāśramacchāyāmahīruhāḥ ।।saritsarastaḍāgādisaṃparkaśiśirānilāḥ ।।tatra tatra niṣaṇṇābhyāṃ śivābhyāṃ saphalīkṛtāḥ ।।tamimaṃ sarvataḥ śreṣṭhaṃ smṛtvā sāmbastriyambakaḥ ।।raibhyāśramasamīpasthaścāntardhānaṃ gato yayau ।।tatrodyānamanuprāpya devyā saha maheśvaraḥ ।।rarāma ramaṇīyāsu devyāntaḥpurabhūmiṣu ।।tathā gateṣu kāleṣu pravṛddhāsu prajāsu ca ।।daityau śuṃbhaniśuṃbhākhyau bhrātarau saṃbabhūvatuḥ ।।tābhyāṃ tapo balāddattaṃ brahmaṇā parameṣṭinā ।।avadhyatvaṃ jagatyasminpuruṣairakhilairapi ।।ayonijā tu yā kanyā hyaṃbikāṃśasamudbhavā ।।ajātapuṃsparśaratiravilaṃghyaparākramā ।।tayā tu nau vadhaḥ saṃkhye tasyāṃ kāmābhibhūtayoḥ ।।iti cābhyarthito brahmā tābhyāmprāha tathāstviti ।।tataḥ prabhṛti śakrādīnvijitya samare surān ।।niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkāraṃ jagaccakraturakramāt ।।tayorvadhāya deveśaṃ brahmābhyarthitavānpunaḥ ।।viniṃdyāpi rahasyaṃ vāṃ krodhayitvā yathā tathā ।। tadvarṇakośajāṃ śaktimakāmāṃ kanyakātmikām ।।niśumbhaśuṃbhayorhaṃtrīṃ surebhyo dātumarhasi ।।evamabhyarthito dhātrā bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ ।।kālītyāha rahasyaṃ vāṃ nindayanniva sasmitaḥ ।।tataḥ kruddhā tadā devī suvarṇā varṇakāraṇāt ।।smayantī cāha bhartāramasamādheyayā girā ।। devyuvāca īdṛśo mama varṇesminna ratirbhavato asti cet ।।evāvantaṃ ciraṃ kālaṃ kathameṣā niyamyate ।।aratyā vartamāno api kathaṃ ca ramase mayā ।।na hyaśakyaṃ jagatyasminnīśvarasya jagatprabhoḥ ।।svātmārāmasya bhavato ratirna sukhasādhanam ।।iti hetoḥ smaro yasmātprasabhaṃ bhasmasātkṛtaḥ ।।yā ca nābhimatā bharturapi sarvāṃgasundarī ।।sā vṛthaiva hi jāyeta sarvairapi guṇāntaraiḥ ।।bharturbhogaikaśeṣo hi sarga evaiṣa yoṣitām ।।tathāsatyanyathābhūtā nārī kutropayujyate ।।tasmādvarṇamimaṃ tyaktvā tvayā rahasi ninditam ।।varṇāntaraṃ bhajiṣye vā na bhajiṣyāmi vā svayam ।।ityuktvotthāya śayanāddevī sācaṣṭa gadgadam ।।yayāce anumatiṃ bhartustapase kṛtaniścayā ।।tathā praṇayabhaṃgena bhīto bhūtapatiḥ svayam ।।pādayoḥ praṇamanneva bhavānīṃ pratyabhāṣata ।।īśvara uvāca ajānatī ca krīḍoktiṃ priye kiṃ kupitāsi me ।।ratiḥ kuto vā jāyeta tvattaścedaratirmama ।।mātā tvamasya jagataḥ pitāhamadhipastathā ।।kathaṃ tadutpapadyeta tvatto nābhiratirmama ।।āvayorabhikāmo api kimasau kāmakāritaḥ ।।yataḥ kāmasamutpattiḥ prāgeva jagadudbhavaḥ ।।pṛthagjanānāṃ rataye kāmātmā kalpito mayā ।।tataḥ kathamupālabdhaḥ kāmadāhādahaṃ tvayā ।।māṃ vai tridaśasāmānyaṃ manyamāno manobhavaḥ ।।manākparibhavaṃ kurvanmayā vai bhasmasātkṛtaḥ ।।vihāropyāvayorasya jagatastrāṇakāraṇāt ।।tatastadarthaṃ tvayyadya krīḍoktiṃ kṛtavāhanam ।।sa cāyamacirādarthastavaivāviṣkariṣyate ।।krodhasya janakaṃ vākyaṃ hṛdi kṛtvedamabravīt ।।devyuvāca śrutapūrvaṃ hi bhagavaṃstava cāṭu vaco mayā ।।yenaivamatidhīrāhamapi prāgabhivaṃcitā ।।prāṇānapyapriyā bharturnārī yā na parityajet ।।kulāṃganā śubhā sadbhiḥ kutsitaiva hi gamyate ।।bhūyasī ca tavāprītiragauramiti me vapuḥ ।।krīḍoktirapi kālīti ghaṭate kathamanyathā ।।sadbhirvigarhitaṃ tasmāttava kārṣṇyamasaṃmatam ।।
anutsṛjya tapoyogātsthātumeveha notsahe ।। śiva uvāca sa yadyevaṃvidhatāpaste tapasā kiṃ prayojanam ।।mamecchayā svecchayā vā varṇāntaravatī bhava ।।devyuvāca necchāmi bhavato varṇaṃ svayaṃ vā kartumanyathā ।।brahmāṇaṃ tapasārādhya kṣipraṃ gaurī bhavāmyaham ।।īśvara uvāca matprasādātpurā brahmā brahmatvaṃ prāptavānpurā ।।tamāhūya mahādevi tapasā kiṃ kariṣyasi ।।devyuvāca tvatto labdhapadā eva sarve brahmādayaḥ surāḥ ।।tathāpyārādhya tapasā brahmāṇaṃ tvanniyogataḥ ।।purā kila satī nāmnā dakṣasya duhitā abhavam ।।jagatāṃ patimevaṃ tvāṃ patiṃ prāptavatī tathā ।।evamadyāpi tapasā toṣayitvā dvijaṃ vidhim ।।gaurī bhavitumicchāmi ko doṣaḥ kathyatāmiha ।।evamukto mahādevyā vāmadevaḥ smayanniva ।।na tāṃ nirbaṃdhayāmāsa devakāryacikīrṣayā ।।iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe śivamandaragirinivāsakrīḍoktavarṇanaṃ nāma caturviṃśo adhyāyaḥ chapter vāyuruvāca tataḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya patimambā pativratā ।।niyamya ca viyogārtiṃ jagāma himavadgirim ।।tapaḥkṛtavatī pūrvaṃ deśe yasminsakhījanaiḥ ।।tameva deśamavṛnottapase praṇayātpunaḥ ।।tataḥ svapitaraṃ dṛṣṭvā mātaraṃ ca tayorgṛhe ।।praṇamya vṛttaṃ vijñāpya tābhyāṃ cānumatā satī ।।punastapovanaṃ gatvā bhūṣaṇāni visṛjya ca ।।snātvā tapasvino veṣaṃ kṛtvā paramapāvanam ।।saṃkalpya ca mahātīvraṃ tapaḥ paramaduścaram ।।sadā manasi sandhāya bhartuścaraṇapaṃkajam ।।tameva kṣaṇike liṃge dhyātvā bāhyavidhānataḥ ।।trisandhyamabhyarcayantī vanyaiḥ puṣpaiḥ phalādibhiḥ ।।sa eva brahmaṇo mūrtimāsthāya tapasaḥ phalam ।।pradāsyati mametyevaṃ nityaṃ kṛtvā akarottapaḥ ।।tathā tapaścarantīṃ tāṃ kāle bahutithe gate ।।dṛṣṭaḥ kaścinmahāvyāghro duṣṭabhāvādupāgamat ।।tathaivopagatasyāpi tasyātīvadurātmanaḥ ।।gātraṃ citrārpitamiva stabdhaṃ tasyāssakāśataḥ ।।taṃ dṛṣṭvāpi tathā vyāghraṃ duṣṭabhāvādupāgatam ।।na pṛthagjanavaddevī svabhāvena vivicyate ।।sa tu viṣṭabdhasarvāṃgo bubhukṣāparipīḍitaḥ ।।mamāmiṣaṃ tato nānyaditi matvā nirantaram ।।nirīkṣyamāṇaḥ satataṃ devīmeva tadā aniśam ।।atiṣṭhadagratastasyā upāsanamivācarat ।। devyāśca hṛdaye nityaṃ mamaivāyamupāsakaḥ ।।trātā ca duṣṭasattvebhya iti pravavṛte kṛpā ।।tasyā eva kṛpā yogātsadyonaṣṭamalatrayaḥ ।।babhūva sahasā vyāghro devīṃ ca bubudhe tadā ।।nyavartata bubhukṣā ca tasyāṃgastambhanaṃ tathā ।।daurātmyaṃ janmasiddhaṃ ca tṛptiśca samajāyata ।।tadā paramabhāvena jñātvā kārtārthyamātmanaḥ ।।sadyopāsaka evaiṣa siṣeve parameśvarīm ।।duṣṭānāmapi sattvānāṃ tathānyeṣāndurātmanām ।।sa eva drāvako bhūtvā vicacāra tapovane ।।tapaśca vavṛdhe devyāstīvraṃ tīvratarātmakam ।।devāśca daityanirbandhādbrahmāṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।।cakrurnivedanaṃ devāḥ svaduḥkhasyāripīḍanāt ।।yathā ca dadatuḥ śumbhaniśumbhau varasammadāt ।।so api śrutvā vidhirduḥkhaṃ surāṇāṃ kṛpayānvitaḥ ।।āsīddaityavadhāyaiva smṛtvā hetvāśrayāṃ kathām ।।sāmaraḥ prārthito brahmā yayau devyāstapovanam ।।saṃsmaranmanasā devaduḥkhamokṣaṃ svayatnataḥ ।।dadarśa ca suraśreṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhe tapasi niṣṭhitām ।।pratiṣṭhāmiva viśvasya bhavānīṃ parameśvarīm ।।nanāma cāsya jagato mātaraṃ svasya vai hareḥ ।।rudrasya ca piturbhāryāmāryāmadrīśvarātmajām ।।brahmāṇamāgataṃ dṛṣṭvā devī devagaṇaiḥ saha ।।arghyaṃ tadarhaṃ dattvā asmai svāgatādyairupācarat ।।tāṃ ca pratyupacāroktiṃ puraskṛtyābhinaṃdya ca ।।papraccha tapaso hetumajānanniva padmajaḥ ।।
brahmovāca tīvreṇa tapasānena devyā kimiha sādhyate ।।tapaḥphalānāṃ sarveṣāṃ tvadadhīnā hi siddhayaḥ ।।yaścaiva jagatāṃ bhartā tameva parameśvaram ।।bhartāramātmanā prāpya prāptañca tapasaḥ phalam ।।athavā sarvamevaitatkrīḍāvilasitaṃ tava ।।idantu citraṃ devasya virahaṃ sahase katham ।।devyuvāca sargādau bhavato devādutpattiḥ śrūyate yadā ।।tadā prajānāṃ prathamastvaṃ me prathamajaḥ sutaḥ ।।yadā punaḥ prajāvṛddhyai lalāṭādbhavato bhavaḥ ।।utpanno abhūttadā tvaṃ me guruḥ śvaśurabhāvataḥ ।।yadā bhavadgirīndraste putro mama pitā svayam ।।tadā pitāmahastvaṃ me jāto lokapitāmaha ।।tadīdṛśasya bhavato lokayātrāvidhāyinaḥ ।।vṛttavantaḥpure bhartā kathayiṣye kathaṃ punaḥ ।।kimatra bahunā dehe yaścāyaṃ mama kālimā ।।tyaktvā sattvavidhānena gaurī bhavitumutsahe ।। brahmovāca etāvatā kimarthena tīvraṃ devi tapaḥ kṛtam ।।svecchaiva kimaparyāptā krīḍeyaṃ hi tavedṛśī ।।krīḍā api ca jaganmātastava lokahitāya vai ।।ato mameṣṭamanayā phalaṃ kimapi sādhyatām ।।niśuṃbhaśuṃbhanāmānau daityau dattavarau mayā ।।dṛptau devānprabādhete tvatto labdhastayorvadhaḥ ।।alaṃ vilaṃbanenātra tvaṃ kṣaṇena sthirā bhava ।।śaktirvisṛjyamānā adya tayormṛtyurbhaviṣyati ।।brāhmaṇābhyarthitā caiva devī girivarātmajā ।।tvakkośaṃ sahasotsṛjya gaurī sā samajāyata ।।sā tvakkośātmanotsṛṣṭā kauśikī nāma nāmataḥ ।।kālī kālāmbudaprakhyā kanyakā samapadyata ।।sā tu māyātmikā śaktiryoganidrā ca vaiṣṇavī ।।śaṃkhacakratriśūlādisāyudhāṣṭamahābhujā ।।saumyā ghorā ca miśrā ca trinetrā candraśekharā ।।ajātapuṃsparśaratiradhṛṣyā cātisundarī ।।dattā ca brahmaṇe devyā śaktireṣā sanātanī ।।niśuṃbhasya ca śuṃbhasya nihaṃtrī daityasiṃhayoḥ ।।brahmaṇāpi prahṛṣṭena tasyai paramaśaktaye ।।prabalaḥ kesarī datto vāhanatve samāgataḥ ।।vindhye ca vasatiṃ tasyāḥ pūjāmāsavapūrvakaiḥ ।।māṃsairmatsyairapūpaiśca nirvartyāsau samādiśat ।।sā caiva saṃmatā śaktirbrahmaṇo viśvakarmaṇaḥ ।।praṇamya mātaraṃ gaurīṃ brahmāṇaṃ cānupūrvaśaḥ ।।śaktibhiścāpi tulyābhiḥ svātmajābhiranekaśaḥ ।।parītā prayayau vindhyaṃ daityendrau hantumudyatā ।।nihatau ca tayā tatra samare daityapuṃgavau ।।tadbāṇaiḥ kāmabāṇaiśca cchinnabhinnāṃgamānasau ।।tadyuddhavistaraścātra na kṛto anyatra varṇanāt ।।ūhanīyaṃ parasmācca prastutaṃ varṇayāmi vaḥ ।। chapter vāyuruvāca utpādya kauśikīṃ gaurī brahmaṇe pratipādya tām ।।tasya pratyupakārāya pitāmahamathābravīt ।।devyuvāca dṛṣṭaḥ kimeṣa bhavatā śārdūlo madupāśrayaḥ ।।anena duṣṭasattvebhyo rakṣitaṃ mattapovanam ।।mayyarpitamanā eṣa bhajate māmananyadhīḥ ।।asya saṃrakṣaṇādanyatpriyaṃ mama na vidyate ।।bhavitavyamanenāto mamāntaḥpuracāriṇā ।।gaṇeśvarapadaṃ cāsmai prītyā dāsyati śaṃkaraḥ ।।enamagresaraṃ kṛtvā sakhībhirgantumutsahe ।।pradīyatāmanujñā me prajānāṃ patinā tvayā ।। ityuktaḥ prahasanbrahmā devīmmugdhāmiva smayan ।।
tasya tīvraiḥ purāvṛttairdaurātmyaṃ samavarṇayat ।।brahmovāca paśau devi mṛgāḥ krūrāḥ kva ca te anugrahaḥ śubhaḥ ।।āśīviṣamukhe sākṣādamṛtaṃ kiṃ niṣicyate ।।vyāghramātreṇa sanneṣa duṣṭaḥ ko api niśācaraḥ ।।anena bhakṣitā gāvo brāhmaṇāśca tapodhanāḥ ।।tarpayaṃstānyathākāmaṃ kāmarūpī caratyasau ।।avaśyaṃ khalu bhoktavyaṃ phalaṃ pāpasya karmaṇaḥ ।।ataḥ kiṃ kṛpayā kṛtyamīdṛśeṣu durātmasu ।।anena devyāḥ kiṃ kṛtyaṃ prakṛtyā kaluṣātmanā ।।devyuvāca yaduktaṃ bhavatā sarvaṃ tathyamastvayamīdṛśaḥ ।।tathāpi māṃ prapanno abhūnna tyājyo māmupāśritaḥ ।।brahmovāca asya bhaktimavijñāya prāgvṛttaṃ te niveditam ।।bhaktiścedasya kiṃ pāpairna te bhaktaḥ praṇaśyati ।।puṇyakarmāpi kiṃ kuryāttvadīyājñānapekṣayā ।।ajā prajñā purāṇī ca tvameva parameśvarī ।।tvadadhīnā hi sarveṣāṃ baṃdhamokṣavyavasthitiḥ ।।tvadṛte paramā śaktiḥ saṃsiddhiḥ kasya karmaṇā ।।tvameva vividhā śaktiḥ bhavānāmatha vā svayam ।।aśaktaḥ karmakaraṇe kartā vā kiṃ kariṣyati ।।viṣṇośca mama cānyeṣāṃ devadānavarakṣasām ।।tattadaiśvaryasamprāptyai tavaivājñā hi kāraṇam ।।atītāḥ khalvasaṃkhyātā brahmāṇo harayo bhavāḥ ।।anāgatāstvasaṃkhyātāstvadājñānuvidhāyinaḥ ।।tvāmanārādhya deveśi puruṣārthacatuṣṭayam ।।labdhuṃ na śakyamasmābhirapi sarvaiḥ surottamaiḥ ।।vyatyāso api bhavetsadyo brahmatvasthāvaratvayoḥ ।।sukṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ cāpi tvayeva sthāpitaṃ yataḥ ।।tvaṃ hi sarvajagadbhartuśśivasya paramātmanaḥ ।।anādimadhyanidhanā śaktirādyā sanātanī ।।samastalokayātrārthaṃ mūrtimāviśya kāmapi ।।krīḍase vividhairbhāvaiḥ kastvāṃ jānāti tattvataḥ ।।ato duṣkṛtakarmāpi vyāghro ayaṃ tvadanugrahāt ।।prāpnotu paramāṃ siddhimatra kaḥ pratibandhakaḥ ।।ityātmanaḥ paraṃ bhāvaṃ smārayitvānurūpataḥ ।।brahmaṇābhyarthitā gaurī tapaso api nyavartata ।।tato devīmanujñāpya brahmaṇyantarhite sati ।।devīṃ ca mātaraṃ dṛṣṭvā menāṃ himavatā saha ।।praṇamyāśvāsya bahudhā pitarau virahāsahau ।। tapaḥ praṇayino devī tapovanamahīruhān ।।viprayogaśucevāgre puṣpabāṣpaṃ vimuṃcataḥ ।।tattucchākhāsamārūḍhavihago dīritai rutaiḥ ।।vyākulaṃ bahudhā dīnaṃ vilāpamiva kurvataḥ ।।sakhībhyaḥ kathayaṃtyevaṃ sattvarā bhartṛdarśane ।।puraskṛtya ca taṃ vyāghraṃ snehātputramivaurasam ।।dehasya prabhayā caiva dīpayantī diśo daśa ।।prayayau maṃdaraṃ gaurī yatra bhartā maheśvaraḥ ।।sarveṣāṃ jagatāṃ dhātā kartā pātā vināśakṛt ।। chapter ṛṣaya ūcuḥ kṛtvā gauraṃ vapurdivyaṃ devī girivarātmajā ।।kathaṃ dadarśa bhartāraṃ praviṣṭā manditaṃ satī ।।praveśasamaye tasyā bhavanadvāragocaraiḥ ।।gaṇeśaiḥ kiṃ kṛtaṃ devastāndṛṣṭvā kintadā akarot ।।vāyuruvāca pravaktumaṃjasā aśakyaḥ tādṛśaḥ paramo rasaḥ ।।yena praṇayagarbheṇa bhāvo bhāvavatāṃ hṛtaḥ ।।dvāsthaissasaṃbhramaireva devo devyāgamotsukaḥ ।।śaṃkamānā praviṣṭāntastañca sā samapaśyata ।।taistaiḥ praṇayabhāvaiśca bhavanāntaravartibhiḥ ।।gaṇendrairvanditā vācā praṇanāma triyambakam ।।praṇamya notthitā yāvattāvattāṃ parameśvaraḥ ।।pragṛhya dorbhyāmāśliṣya paritaḥ parayā mudā ।।svāṃke dhartuṃ pravṛtto api sā paryaṃke nyaṣīdata ।।paryaṃkato balāddevīṃ soṅkamāropya susmitām ।।sasmito vivṛtairnetraistadvaktraṃ prapibanniva ।।tayā saṃbhāṣaṇāyeśaḥ pūrvabhāṣitamabravīt ।।devadeva uvāca sā daśā ca vyatītā kiṃ tava sarvāṃgasundari ।।yasyāmanunayopāyaḥ ko api kopānna labhyate ।।svecchayāpi na kālīti nānyavarṇavatīti ca ।।tvatsvabhāvāhṛtaṃ cittaṃ subhru ciṃtāvahaṃ mama ।।vismṛtaḥ paramo bhāvaḥ kathaṃ svecchāṃgayogataḥ ।।na sambhavanti ye tatra cittakāluṣyahetavaḥ ।।pṛthagjanavadanyonyaṃ vipriyasyāpi kāraṇam ।।āvayorapi yadyasti nāstyevaitaccarācaram ।।ahamagniśironiṣṭhastvaṃ somaśirasi sthitā ।।agnīṣomātmakaṃ viśvamāvābhyāṃ samadhiṣṭhitam ।।jagaddhitāya caratoḥ svecchādhṛtaśarīrayoḥ ।।āvayorviprayoge hi syānnirālambanaṃ jagat ।।asti hetvantaraṃ cātra śāstrayuktiviniścitam ।।vāgarthamiva me vaitajjagatsthāvarajaṃgamam ।।tvaṃ hi vāgamṛtaṃ sākṣādahamarthāmṛtaṃ param ।।dvayamapyamṛtaṃ kasmādviyuktamupapadyate ।। vidyāpratyāyikā tvaṃ me vedyo ahaṃ pratyayāttava ।।vidyāvedyātmanoreva viśleṣaḥ kathamāvayoḥ ।।na karmaṇā sṛjāmīdaṃ jagatpratisṛjāmi ca ।।sarvasyājñaikalabhyatvādājñātvaṃ hi garīyasī ।।ājñaikasāramaiśvaryaṃ yasmātsvātaṃtryalakṣaṇam ।।ājñayā viprayuktasya caiśvaryaṃ mama kīdṛśam ।।na kadācidavasthānamāvayorviprayuktayoḥ ।।devānāṃ kāryamuddiśya līloktiṃ kṛtavānaham ।।tvayāpyaviditaṃ nāsti kathaṃ kupitavatyasi ।।tatastrilokarakṣārthe kopo mayyapi te kṛtaḥ ।।yadanarthāya bhūtānāṃ na tadasti khalu tvayi ।।iti priyaṃvade sākṣādīśvare parameśvare ।।śṛṃgārabhāvasārāṇāṃ janmabhūmirakṛtrimā ।।svabhartrā lalitantathyamuktaṃ matvā smitottaram ।।lajjayā na kimapyūce kauśikī varṇanātparam ।।tadeva varṇayāmyadya śṛṇu devyāśca varṇanam ।।
devyuvāca kiṃ devena na sā dṛṣṭā yā sṛṣṭā kauśikī mayā ।।tādṛśī kanyakā loke na bhūtā na bhaviṣyati ।।tasyā vīryaṃ balaṃ vindhyanilayaṃ vijayaṃ tathā ।।śuṃbhasya ca niśuṃbhasya māraṇe ca raṇe tayoḥ ।।pratyakṣaphaladānaṃ ca lokāya bhajate sadā ।।lokānāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ śaśvadbrahmā vijñāpayiṣyati ।।iti saṃbhāṣamāṇāyā devyā evājñayā tadā ।।vyāghraḥ sakhyā samānīya puro avasthāpitastadā ।।taṃ prekṣyāha punardevī devānītamupāyatam ।।vyāghraṃ paśya na cānena sadṛśo madupāsakaḥ ।।anena duṣṭasaṃghebhyo rakṣitaṃ mattapovanam ।।atīva mama bhaktaśca viśrabdhaśca svarakṣaṇāt ।।svadeśaṃ ca parityajya prasādārthaṃ samāgataḥ ।।yadi prītirabhūnmattaḥ parāṃ prītiṃ karoṣi me ।।nityamantaḥpuradvāri niyogānnandinaḥ svayam ।।rakṣibhissaha taccihnairvartatāmayamīśvara ।।vāyuruvāca madhuraṃ praṇayodarkaṃ śrutvā devyāḥ śubhaṃ vacaḥ ।।prīto asmītyāha taṃ devassa cādṛśyata tatkṣaṇāt ।।bibhradvetralatāṃ haimīṃ ratnacitraṃ ca kaṃcukam ।।churikāmuragaprakhyāṃ gaṇeśo rakṣaveṣadhṛk ।।yasmātsomo mahādevo nandī cānena nanditaḥ ।।somanandīti vikhyātastasmādeṣa samākhyayā ।।itthaṃ devyāḥ priyaṃ kṛtvā devaścardhendubhūṣaṇaḥ ।।bhūṣayāmāsa tandivyairbhūṣaṇai ratnabhūṣitaiḥ ।।tatassa gaurīṃ giriśo girīndrajāṃ sagauravāṃ sarvamanoharāṃ haraḥ ।।paryaṃkamāropya varāṃgabhūṣaṇairvibhūṣayāmāsa śaśāṃkabhūṣaṇaḥ ।। chapter ṛṣaya ūcuḥ devīṃ samādadhānena devenedaṃ kimīritam ।।agniṣomātmakaṃ viśvaṃ vāgarthātmakamityapi ।।ājñaikasāramaiśvaryamājñā tvamiti coditam ।।tadidaṃ śrotumicchāmo yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।।vāyuruvāca agnirityucyate raudrī ghorā yā taijasī tanuḥ ।।somaḥ śākto amṛtamayaḥ śakteḥ śāntikarī tanuḥ ।।amṛtaṃ yatpratiṣṭhā sā tejo vidyā kalā svayam ।।bhūtasūkṣmeṣu sarveṣu ta eva rasatejasī ।।dvividhā tejaso vṛttisūryātmā cānalātmikā ।।tathaiva rasavṛttiśca somātmā ca jalātmikā ।।vidyudādimayantejo madhurādimayo rasaḥ ।।tejorasavibhedaistu dhṛtametaccarācaram ।।agneramṛtaniṣpattiramṛtenāgniredhate ।।ata eva hi vikrāntamagnīṣomaṃ jagaddhitam ।।haviṣe sasyasampattirvṛṣṭiḥ sasyābhivṛddhaye ।।vṛṣṭereva havistasmādagnīṣomadhṛtaṃ jagat ।।agnirūrdhvaṃ jvalatyeṣa yāvatsaumyaṃ parāmṛtam ।।yāvadagnyāspadaṃ saumyamamṛtaṃ ca sravatyadhaḥ ।।ata eva hi kālāgniradhastācchaktirūrdhvataḥ ।।yāvadādahanaṃ cordhvamadhaścāplāvanaṃ bhavet ।।ādhāraśaktyaiva dhṛtaḥ kālāgnirayamūrdhvagaḥ ।।tathaiva nimnagaḥ somaśśivaśaktipadāspadaḥ ।।śivaścordhvamadhaśśaktirūrdhvaṃ śaktiradhaḥ śivaḥ ।।taditthaṃ śivaśaktibhyānnāvyāptamiha kiñcana ।।asakṛccāgninā dagdhaṃ jagadyadbhasmasātkṛtam ।।agnervīryamidaṃ cāhustadvīryaṃ bhasma yattataḥ ।।yaścetthaṃ bhasmasadbhāvaṃ jñātvā snāti ca bhasmanā ।।agnirityādibhirmantrairbaddhaḥ pāśātpramucyate ।।agnervīryaṃ tu yadbhasma somenāplāvitampunaḥ ।।ayogayuktyā prakṛteradhikārāya kalpate ।।yogayuktyā tu tadbhasma plāvyamānaṃ samantataḥ ।।śāktenāmṛtavarṣeṇa cādhikārānnivartayet ।।ato mṛtyuṃjayāyetthamamṛtaplāvanaṃ sadā ।।śivaśaktyamṛtasparśe labdhaṃ yena kuto mṛtiḥ ।।yo veda dahanaṃ guhyaṃ plāvanaṃ ca yathoditam ।।agnīṣomapadaṃ hitvā na sa bhūyo abhijāyate ।।śivāgninā tanuṃ dagdhvā śaktisaumyā mṛtena yaḥ ।।plāvayedyogamārgeṇa so amṛtatvāya kalpate ।।hṛdi kṛtvemamarthaṃ vai devena samudāhṛtam ।।agnīṣomātmakaṃ viśvaṃ jagadityanurūpataḥ ।। chapter vāyuruvāca nivedayāmi jagato vāgarthātmyaṃ kṛtaṃ yathā ।।ṣaḍadhvavedanaṃ samyak samāsānna tu vistarāt ।।nāsti kaścidaśabdārtho nāpi śabdo nirarthakaḥ ।।tato hi samaye śabdassarvassarvārthabodhakaḥ ।।prakṛteḥ pariṇāmo ayaṃ dvidhā śabdārthabhāvanā ।।tāmāhuḥ prākṛtīṃ mūrtiṃ śivayoḥ paramātmanoḥ ।।śabdātmikā vibhūtiryā sā tridhā kathyate budhaiḥ ।।sthūlā sūkṣmā parā ceti sthūlā yā śrutigocarā ।।sūkṣmā cintāmayī proktā ciṃtayā rahitā parā ।।yā śaktiḥ sā parā śaktiśśivatattvasamāśrayā ।।jñānaśaktisamāyogādicchopodbalikā tathā ।।sarvaśaktisamaṣṭyātmā śaktitattvasamākhyayā ।।samastakāryajātasya mūlaprakṛtitāṃ gatā ।।saiva kuṇḍalinī māyā śuddhādhvaparamā satī ।।sā vibhāgasvarūpaiva ṣaḍadhvātmā vijṛṃbhate ।।tatra śabdāstrayo adhvānastrayaścārthāḥ samīritāḥ ।।sarveṣāmapi vai puṃsāṃ naijaśuddhyanurūpataḥ ।।layabhogādhikārāssyussarvatattvavibhāgataḥ ।।kalābhistāni tattvāni vyāptānyeva yathātatham ।।parasyāḥ prakṛterādau pañcadhā pariṇāmataḥ ।।kalāśca tā nivṛttyādyāḥ paryāptā iti niścayaḥ ।।maṃtrādhvā ca padādhvā ca varṇādhvā ceti śabdataḥ ।।bhuvanādhvā ca tattvādhvā kalādhvā cārthataḥ kramāt ।।atrānyonyaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ vyāpyavyāpakatocyate ।।maṃtrāḥ sarvaiḥ padairvyāptā vākyabhāvātpadāni ca ।।varṇairvarṇasamūhaṃ hi padamāhurvipaścitaḥ ।।varṇāstu bhuvanairvyāptāsteṣāṃ teṣūpalaṃbhanāt ।।bhuvanānyapi tattvaughairutpattyāṃtarbahiṣkramāt ।।vyāptāni kāraṇaistattvairārabdhatvādanekaśaḥ ।।aṃtarādutthitānīha bhuvanāni tu kānicit ।।paurāṇikāni cānyāni vijñeyāni śivāgame ।।sāṃkhyayogaprasiddhāni tattvānyapi ca kānicit ।।śivaśāstraprasiddhāni tatonyānyapi kṛtsnaśaḥ ।।kalābhistāni tattvāni vyāptānyeva yathātatham ।।parasyāḥ prakṛterādau pañcadhā pariṇāmataḥ ।।kalāśca tā nivṛttyādyā vyāptāḥ pañca yathottaram ।।vyāpikātaḥ parā śaktiravibhaktā ṣaḍadhvanām ।।paraprakṛtibhāvasya tatsattvācchivatattvataḥ ।।śaktyādi ca pṛthivyantaṃ śivatattvasamudbhavam ।।vyāptamekena tenaiva mṛdā kuṃbhādikaṃ yathā ।।śaivaṃ tatparamaṃ dhāma yatprāpyaṃ ṣaḍbhiradhvabhiḥ ।। vyāpikā avyāpikā śaktiḥ pañcatattvaviśodhanāt ।।nivṛttyā rudraparyantaṃ sthitiraṇḍasya śodhyate ।।pratiṣṭhayā tadūrdhvaṃ tu yāvadavyaktagocaram ।।tadūrdhvaṃ vidyayā madhye yāvadviśveśvarāvadhi ।।śāntyā tadūrdhvaṃ madhvānte viśuddhiḥ śāntyatītayā ।।yāmāhuḥ paramaṃ vyoma paraprakṛtiyogataḥ ।।etāni pañcatattvāni yairvyāptamakhilaṃ jagat ।।tatraiva sarvamevedaṃ draṣṭavyaṃ khalu sādhakaiḥ ।।adhvavyāptimavijñāya śuddhiṃ yaḥ kartumicchati ।।sa vipralambhakaḥ śuddhernālamprāpayituṃ phalam ।।vṛthā pariśramastasya nirayāyaiva kevalam ।।śaktipātasamāyogādṛte tattvāni tattvataḥ ।।tadvyāptistadvivṛddhiśca jñātumevaṃ na śakyate ।।śaktirājñā parā śaivī cidrūpā marameśvarī ।।śivo adhitiṣṭhatyakhilaṃ yayā kāraṇabhūtayā ।।nātmano naiva māyaiṣā na vikāro vicārataḥ ।।na baṃdho nāpi muktiśca baṃdhamuktividhāyinī ।।sarvaiśvaryaparākāṣṭā śivasya vyabhicāriṇī ।।samānadharmiṇī tasya taistairbhāvairviśeṣataḥ ।।sa tayaiva gṛhī sāpi tenaiva gṛhiṇī sadā ।।tayorapatyaṃ yatkāryaṃ paraprakṛtijaṃ jagat ।।sa kartā kāraṇaṃ seti tayorbhedo vyavasthitaḥ ।।eka eva śivaḥ sākṣāddvidhā asau samavasthitaḥ ।।strīpuṃsabhāvena tayorbheda ityapi kecana ।।apare tu parā śaktiḥ śivasya samavāyinī ।।prabheva bhānościdrūpā bhinnaiveti vyavasthitaḥ ।।tasmācchivaḥ paro hetustasyājñā parameśvarī ।।tayaiva preritā śaivī mūlaprakṛtiravyayā ।।mahāmāyā ca māyā ca prakṛtistriguṇeti ca ।।trividhā kāryavedhena sā prasūte ṣaḍadhvanaḥ ।।sa vāgarthamayaścādhvā ṣaḍvidho nikhilaṃ jagat ।।asyaiva vistaraṃ prāhuḥ śāstrajātamaśeṣataḥ ।।
chapter ṛṣaya ūcuḥ caritāni vicitrāṇi gṛhyāṇi gahanāni ca ।।durvijñeyāni devaiśca mohayaṃti manāṃsi naḥ ।।śivayostattvasambandhe na doṣa upalabhyate ।।caritaiḥ prākṛto bhāvastayorapi vibhāvyate ।।brahmādayo api lokānāṃ sṛṣṭisthityantahetavaḥ ।।nigrahānugrahau prāpya śivasya vaśavartinaḥ ।।śivaḥ punarna kasyāpi nigrahānugrahāspadam ।।ato anāyattamaiśvaryaṃ tasyaiveti viniścitam ।। yadyevamīdṛśaiśvaryaṃ tattu svātantryalakṣaṇam ।।svabhāvasiddhaṃ caitasya mūrtimattāspadaṃ bhavet ।।na mūrtiśca svataṃtrasya ghaṭate mūlahetunā ।।mūrterapi ca kāryatvāttatsiddhiḥ syādahaitukī ।।sarvatra paramo bhāvo aparamaścānya ucyate ।।paramāparamau bhāvau kathamekatra saṃgatau ।।niṣphalo hi svabhāvo asya paramaḥ paramātmanaḥ ।।sa eva sakalaḥ kasmātsvabhāvo hyaviparyayaḥ ।।svabhāvo viparītaścetsvataṃtraḥ svecchayā yadi ।।na karoti kimīśāno nityānityaviparyayam ।।mūrtātmā sakalaḥ kaścitsa cānyo niṣphalaḥ śivaḥ ।।śivenādhiṣṭhitaśceti sarvatra laghu kathyate ।।mūrtyātmaiva tadā mūrtiḥ śivasyāsya bhavediti ।।tasya mūrtau mūrtimatoḥ pārataṃtryaṃ hi niścitam ।।anyathā nirapekṣeṇa mūrtiḥ svīkriyate katham ।।mūrtisvīkaraṇaṃ tasmānmūrtau sādhyaphalepsayā ।।na hi svecchāśarīratvaṃ svātaṃtryāyopapadyate ।।svecchaiva tādṛśī puṃsāṃ yasmātkarmānusāriṇī ।।svīkartuṃ svecchayā dehaṃ hātuṃ ca prabhavantyuta ।।brahmādayaḥ piśācāṃtāḥ kiṃ te karmātivartinaḥ ।।icchayā dehanirmāṇamindrajālopamaṃ viduḥ ।।aṇimādiguṇaiśvaryavaśīkārānatikramāt ।।viśvarūpaṃ dadhadviṣṇurdadhīcena maharṣiṇā ।।yudhyatā samupālabdhastadrūpaṃ dadhatā svayam ।।sarvasmādadhikasyāpi śivasya paramātmanaḥ ।।śarīravattayānyātmasādharmyaṃ pratibhāti naḥ ।।sarvānugrāhakaṃ prāhuśśivaṃ paramakāraṇam ।।sa nirgṛhṇāti devānāṃ sarvānugrāhakaḥ katham ।।ciccheda bahuśo devo brahmaṇaḥ pañcamaṃ śiraḥ ।।śivanindāṃ prakurvaṃtaṃ putreti kumaterhaṭhāt ।।viṣṇorapi nṛsiṃhasya rabhasā śarabhākṛtiḥ ।।bibheda padbhyāmākramya hṛdayaṃ nakharaiḥ kharaiḥ ।।devastrīṣu ca deveṣu dakṣasyādhvarakāraṇāt ।।vīreṇa vīrabhadreṇa na hi kaścidadaṇḍitaḥ ।।puratrayaṃ ca sastrīkaṃ sadaityaṃ saha bālakaiḥ ।।kṣaṇenaikena devena netrāgneriṃdhanīkṛtam ।।prajānāṃ ratihetuśca kāmo ratipatissvayam ।।krośatāmeva devānāṃ huto netrahutāśane ।।gāvaśca kaściddugdhaughaṃ sravantyo mūrdhni khecarāḥ ।।saruṣā prekṣya devena tatkṣaṇe bhasmasātkṛtaḥ ।।jalaṃdharāsuro dīrṇaścakrīkṛtya jalaṃ padā ।।baddhvānaṃtena yo viṣṇuṃ cikṣepa śatayojanam ।।tameva jalasaṃdhāyī śūlenaiva jaghāna saḥ ।।taccakraṃ tapasā labdhvā labdhavīryo harissadā ।। jighāṃsatāṃ surārīṇāṃ kulaṃ nirghṛṇacetasām ।।triśūlenāndhakasyoraḥ śikhinaivopatāpitam ।।kaṇṭhātkālāṃganāṃ sṛṣṭvā dārako api nipātitaḥ ।।kauśikīṃ janayitvā tu gauryāstvakkośagocarām ।।śuṃbhassaha niśuṃbhena prāpito maraṇaṃ raṇe ।।śrutaṃ ca mahadākhyānaṃ skānde skandasamāśrayam ।।vadhārthe tārakākhyasya daityendrasyendravidviṣaḥ ।।brahmaṇābhyarthito devo mandarāntaḥpuraṃ gataḥ ।।vihṛtya suciraṃ devyā vihārā atiprasaṅgataḥ ।।rasāṃ rasātalaṃ nītāmiva kṛtvābhidhāṃ tataḥ ।।devīṃ ca vaṃcayaṃstasyāṃ svavīryamatidurvaham ।।avisṛjya visṛjyāgnau haviḥ pūtamivāmṛtam ।।gaṃgādiṣvapi nikṣipya vahnidvārā tadaṃśataḥ ।।tatsamāhṛtya śanakaistokaṃstokamitastataḥ ।।svāhayā kṛttikārūpātsvabhartrā ramamāṇayā ।।suvarṇībhūtayā nyastaṃ merau śaravaṇe kvacit ।।saṃdīpayitvā kālena tasya bhāsā diśo daśa ।।rañjayitvā girīnsarvānkāṃcanīkṛtya meruṇā ।।tataścireṇa kālena saṃjāte tatra tejasi ।।kumāre sukumārāṃge kumārāṇāṃ nidarśane ।।tacchaiśavaṃ svarūpaṃ ca tasya dṛṣṭvā manoharam ।।saha devasurairlokairvismite ca vimohite ।।devo api svayamāyātaḥ putradarśanalālasaḥ ।।saha devyāṃkamāropya tato asya smeramānanam ।।pītāmṛtamiva snehavivaśenāntarātmanā ।।deveṣvapi ca paśyatsu vītarāgaistapasvibhiḥ ।।svasya vakṣaḥsthale svairaṃ nartayitvā kumārakam ।।anubhūya ca tatkrīḍāṃ saṃbhāvya ca parasparam ।।stanyamājñāpayandevyāḥ pāyayitvāmṛtopamam ।।tavāvatāro jagatāṃ hitāyetyanuśāsya ca ।।svayandevaśca devī ca na tṛptimupajagmatuḥ ।।tataḥ śakreṇa saṃdhāya bibhyatā tārakāsurāt ।।kārayitvābhiṣekaṃ ca senāpatye divaukasām ।।putramantarataḥ kṛtvā devena tripuradviṣā ।।svayamaṃtarhitenaiva skandamindrādirakṣitam ।।tacchaktyā krauñcabhedinyā yudhi kālāgnikalpayā ।।cheditaṃ tārakasyāpi śiraśśakrabhiyā saha ।।stutiṃ cakrurviśeṣeṇa haridhātṛmukhāḥ surāḥ ।।tathā rakṣodhipaḥ sākṣādrāvaṇo balagarvitaḥ ।।uddharansvabhujairdīrghaiḥ kailāsaṃ girimātmanaḥ ।।tadāgo asahamānasya devadevasya śūlinaḥ ।।padāṃguṣṭhaparispandānmamajja mṛdito bhuvi ।।baṭoḥ kenacidarthena svāśritasya gatāyuṣaḥ ।। tvarayāgatya devena pādāṃtaṃ gamitontakaḥ ।।svavāhanamavijñāya vṛṣendraṃ vaḍavānalaḥ ।।sagalagrahamānītastato astyekodakaṃ jagat ।।alokaviditaistaistairvṛttairānandasundaraiḥ ।।aṃgahārasvasenedamasakṛccālitaṃ jagat ।।śānta eva sadā sarvamanugṛhṇāti cecchivaḥ ।।sarvāṇi pūrayedeva kathaṃ śaktena mocayet ।।anādikarma vaicitryamapi nātra niyāmakam ।।kāraṇaṃ khalu karmāpi bhavedīśvarakāritam ।।kimatra bahunoktena nāstikyaṃ hetukārakam ।।yathā hyāśu nivarteta tathā kathaya māruta ।।
chapter vāyuruvāca sthane saṃśayitaṃ viprā bhavadbhirhetucoditaiḥ ।।jijñāsā hi na nāstikyaṃ sādhayetsādhubuddhiṣu ।।pramaṇamatra vakṣyāmi satāmmohanivartakam ।।asatāṃ tvanyathābhāvaḥ prasādena vinā prabhoḥ ।।śivasya paripūrṇasya parānugrahamantarā ।।na kiṃcidapi kartavyamiti sādhu viniścitam ।।svabhāva eva paryāptaḥ parānugrahakarmaṇi ।।anyathā nissvabhavena na kimapyanugṛhyate ।।paraṃ sarvamanugrāhyaṃ paśupāśātmakaṃ jagat ।।parasyānugrahārthaṃ tu patyurājñāsamanvayaḥ ।।patirājñāpakaḥ sarvamanugṛhṇāti sarvadā ।।tadarthamarthasvīkāre parataṃtraḥ kathaṃ śivaḥ ।।anugrāhyanapekṣo asti na hi kaścidanugrahaḥ ।।ataḥ svātantryaśabdārthānanapekṣatvalakṣaṇaḥ ।।etatpunaranugrāhyaṃ parataṃtraṃ tadiṣyate ।।anugrahādṛte tasya bhuktimuktyorananvayāt ।।mūrtātmano apyanugrāhyā śivājñānanivartanāt ।।ajñānādhiṣṭhitaṃ śambhorna kiṃcidiha vidyate ।।yenopalabhyate asmābhissakalenāpi niṣkalaḥ ।।sa mūrtyātmā śivaḥ śaivamūrtirityupacaryate ।।na hyasau niṣkalaḥ sākṣācchivaḥ paramakāraṇam ।।sākāreṇānubhāvena kenāpyanupalakṣitaḥ ।।pramāṇagamyatāmātraṃ tatsvabhāvopapādakam ।।na tāvatātropekṣādhīrupalakṣaṇamaṃtarā ।।ātmopamolvaṇaṃ sākṣānmūrtireva hi kācana ।।śivasya mūrtirmūrtyātmā parastasyopalakṣaṇam ।।yathā kāṣṭheṣvanārūḍho na vahnirupalabhyate ।।evaṃ śivo api mūrtyātmanyanārūḍha iti sthitiḥ ।।yathāgnimānayetyukte jvalatkāṣṭhādṛte svayam ।।nāgnirānīyate tadvatpūjyo mūrtyātmanā śivaḥ ।।ata eva hi pūjādau mūrtyātmaparikalpanam ।।mūrtyātmani kṛtaṃ sākṣācchiva eva kṛtaṃ yataḥ ।।liṃgādāvapi tatkṛtyamarcāyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।।tattanmūrtyātmabhāvena śivo asmābhirupāsyate ।।yathānugṛhyate so api mūrtyātmā pārameṣṭhinā ।।tathā mūrtyātmaniṣṭhena śivena paśavo vayam ।।lokānugrahaṇāyaiva śivena parameṣṭhinā ।।sadāśivādayassarve mūrtyātmano apyadhiṣṭhitāḥ ।।ātmanāmeva bhogāya mokṣāya ca viśeṣataḥ ।।tattvātattvasvarūpeṣu mūrtyātmasu śivānvayaḥ ।।bhogaḥ karmavipākātmā sukhaduḥkhātmako mataḥ ।।na ca karma śivo astīti tasya bhogaḥ kimātmakaḥ ।।sarvaṃ śivo anugṛhṇāti na nigṛhṇāti kiṃcana ।।nigṛhṇatāṃ tu ye doṣāśśive teṣāmasaṃbhavāt ।।ye punarnigrahāḥ kecidbrahmādiṣu nidarśitāḥ ।।te api lokahitāyaiva kṛtāḥ śrīkaṇṭhamūrtinā ।।brahmāṇḍasyādhipatyaṃ hi śrīkaṇṭhasya na saṃśayaḥ ।।śrīkaṇṭhākhyāṃ śivo mūrtiṃ krīḍatīmadhitiṣṭhati ।।sadoṣā eva devādyā nigṛhītā yathoditam ।।tatastepi vipāpmānaḥ prajāścāpi gatajvarāḥ ।।nigraho api svarūpeṇa viduṣāṃ na jugupsitaḥ ।।ata eva hi daṇḍyeṣu daṇḍo rājñāṃ praśasyate ।।yatsiddhirīśvaratvena kāryavargasya kṛtsnaśaḥ ।।na sa cedīśatāṃ kuryājjagataḥ kathamīśvaraḥ ।।īśecchā ca vidhātṛtvaṃ vidherājñāpanaṃ param ।।ājñāvaśyamidaṃ kuryānna kuryāditi śāsanam ।।tacchāsanānuvartitvaṃ sādhubhāvasya lakṣaṇam ।।viparītasamādhoḥ syānna sarvaṃ tattu dṛśyate ।।sādhu saṃrakṣaṇīyaṃ cedvinivartyamasādhu yat ।।nivartate ca sāmāderaṃte daṇḍo hi sādhanam ।।hitārthalakṣaṇaṃ cedaṃ daṇḍāntamanuśāsanam ।।ato yadviparītaṃ tadahitaṃ saṃpracakṣate ।।hite sadā niṣaṇṇānāmīśvarasya nidarśanam ।।sa kathaṃ duṣyate sadbhirasatāmeva nigrahāt ।।ayuktakāriṇo loke garhaṇīyāvivekitā ।।yadudvejayate lokantadayuktaṃ pracakṣate ।।sarvo api nigraho loke na ca vidveṣapūrvakaḥ ।।na hi dveṣṭi pitā putraṃ yo nigṛhyāti śikṣayet ।।mādhyasthenāpi nigrāhyānyo nigṛhṇāti mārgataḥ ।।tasyāpyavaśyaṃ yatkiṃcinnairghṛṇyamanuvartate ।।anyathā na hinastyeva sadoṣānapyasau parān ।।hinasti cāyamapyajñānparaṃ mādhyasthyamācaran ।।tasmādduḥkhātmikāṃ hiṃsāṃ kurvāṇo yaḥ sanirghṛṇaḥ ।। iti nirbaṃdhayaṃtyeke niyamo neti cāpare ।।nidānajñasya bhiṣajo rugṇo hiṃsāṃ prayuṃjataḥ ।।na kiṃcidapi nairghṛṇyaṃ ghṛṇaivātra prayojikā ।।ghṛṇāpi na guṇāyaiva hiṃsreṣu pratiyogiṣu ।।tādṛśeṣu ghṛṇī bhrāntyā ghṛṇāntaritanirghṛṇaḥ ।।upekṣāpīha doṣāha rakṣyeṣu pratiyogiṣu ।।śaktau satyāmupekṣāto rakṣyassadyo vipadyate ।।sarpasyā a asyagatampaśyanyastu rakṣyamupekṣate ।।doṣābhāsānsamutprekṣya phalataḥ so api nirghṛṇaḥ ।।tasmād ghṛṇā guṇāyaiva sarvatheti na saṃmatam ।।saṃmataṃ prāptakāmitvaṃ sarvaṃ tvanyadasammatam ।।mūrtyātmasvapi rāgādyā doṣāḥ santyeva vastutaḥ ।।tathāpi teṣāmevaite na śivasya tu sarvathā ।।agnāvapi samāviṣṭaṃ tāmraṃ khalu sakālikam ।। f।iti nāgnirasau duṣyettāmrasaṃsargakāraṇāt ।।nāgneraśucisaṃsargādaśucitvamapekṣate ।।aśucestvagnisaṃyogācchucitvamapi jāyate ।।evaṃ śodhyātmasaṃsargānna hyaśuddhaḥ śivo bhavet ।।śivasaṃsargatastveṣa śodhyātmaiva hi śudhyati ।।ayasyagnau samāviṣṭe dāho agnereva nāyasaḥ ।।mūrtātmanyevamaiśvaryamīśvarasyaiva nātmanām ।।na hi kāṣṭhaṃ jvalatyūrdhvamagnireva jvalatyasau ।।kāṣṭhasyāṃgāratā nāgnerevamatrāpi yojyatām ।।ata eva jagatyasminkāṣṭhapāṣāṇamṛtsvapi ।।śivāveśavaśādeva śivatvamupacaryate ।।maitryādayo guṇā gauṇāstasmātte bhinnavṛttayaḥ ।।tairguṇairuparaktānāṃ doṣāya ca guṇāya ca ।।yattu gauṇamagauṇaṃ ca tatsarvamanugṛhṇataḥ ।।na guṇāya na doṣāya śivasya guṇavṛttayaḥ ।। f।na cānugrahaśabdārthaṃ gauṇamāhurvipaścitaḥ ।।saṃsāramocanaṃ kiṃ tu śaivamājñāmayaṃ hitam ।।hitaṃ tadājñākaraṇaṃ yaddhitaṃ tadanugrahaḥ ।।sarvaṃ hite niyuñjāvaḥ sarvānugrahakārakaḥ ।।yastūpakāraśabdārthastamapyāhuranugraham ।।tasyāpi hitarūpatvācchivaḥ sarvopakārakaḥ ।।hite sadā niyuktaṃ tu sarvaṃ cidacidātmakam ।।svabhāvapratibandhaṃ tatsamaṃ na labhate hitam ।।yathā vikāsayatyeva raviḥ padmāni bhānubhiḥ ।।samaṃ na vikasantyeva svasvabhāvānurodhataḥ ।।svabhāvo api hi bhāvānāṃ bhāvino arthasya kāraṇam ।।na hi svabhāvo naśyantamarthaṃ kartṛṣu sādhayet ।।suvarṇameva nāṃgāraṃ drāvayatyagnisaṃgamaḥ ।।evaṃ pakvamalāneva mocayenna śivaparān ।। yadyathā bhavituṃ yogyaṃ tattathā na bhavetsvayam ।।vinā bhāvanayā kartā svatantrassantato bhavet ।।svabhāvavimalo yadvatsarvānugrāhakaśśivaḥ ।।svabhāvamalināstadvadātmano jīvasaṃjñitāḥ ।।anyathā saṃsarantyete niyamānna śivaḥ katham ।।karmamāyānubandhosya saṃsāraḥ kathyate budhaiḥ ।।anubandho ayamasyaiva na śivasyeti hetumān ।।sa heturātmanāmeva nijo nāgantuko malaḥ ।।āgantukatve kasyāpi bhāvyaṃ kenāpi hetunā ।।yo ayaṃ heturasāvekastvavicitrasvabhāvataḥ ।।ātmatāyāḥ samatve api baddhā muktāḥ pare yataḥ ।।baddheṣveva punaḥ kecillayabhogādhikārataḥ ।।jñānaiśvaryādivaiṣamyaṃ bhajante sottarādharāḥ ।।kecinmūrtyātmatāṃ yānti kecidāsannagocarāḥ ।।mūrtyātmasu śivāḥ kecidadhvanāṃ mūrdhasu sthitāḥ ।।madhye maheśvarā rudrāstvarvācīnapade sthitāḥ ।।āsanne api ca māyāyāḥ parasmātkāraṇāttrayam ।।tatrāpyātmā sthito adhastādantarātmā ca madhyataḥ ।।parastātparamātmeti brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ ।।vartante vasavaḥ kecitparamātmapadāśrayāḥ ।।antarātmapade kecitkecidātmapade tathā ।।śāntyatītapade śaivāḥ śānte māheśvare tataḥ ।।vidyāyāntu yathā raudrāḥ pratiṣṭhāyāṃ tu vaiṣṇavāḥ ।।nivṛttau ca tathātmāno brahmā brahmāṃgayonayaḥ ।।devayonyaṣṭakaṃ mukhyaṃ mānuṣyamatha madhyamam ।।pakṣyādayo adhamāḥ pañcayonayastāścaturdaśa ।।uttarādharabhāvo api jñeyassaṃsāriṇo malaḥ ।।yathāmabhāvo muktasya pūrvaṃ paścāttu pakvatā ।।malo apyāmaśca pakvaśca bhavetsaṃsārakāraṇam ।।āme tvadharatā puṃsāṃ pakve tūttaratā kramāt ।।paśvātmānastridhābhinnā ekadvitrimalāḥ kramāt ।।atrottarā ekamalā dvimalā madhyamā matāḥ ।।trimalāstvadhamā jñeyā yathottaramadhiṣṭhitāḥ ।। f।trimalānadhitiṣṭhaṃti dvimalaikamalāḥ kramāt ।।itthamaupādhiko bhedo viśvasya parikalpitaḥ ।।ekadvitrimalānsarvāñchiva eko adhitiṣṭhati ।।aśivātmakamapyetacchivenādhiṣṭhitaṃ yathā ।।arudrātmakamityevaṃ rudrairjagadadhiṣṭhitam ।।aṇḍāntā hi mahābhūmiśśatarudrādyadhiṣṭhitā ।।māyāntamantarikṣaṃ tu hyamareśādibhiḥ kramāt ।।aṃguṣṭhamātraparyantaissamaṃtātsaṃtataṃ tatam ।।mahāmāyāvasānā dyaurvāyvādyairbhuvanādhipaiḥ ।। anāśritāntairadhvāntarvartibhissamadhiṣṭhitāḥ ।।te hi sākṣāddiviṣadastvantarikṣasadastathā ।।pṛthivīpada ityevaṃ devā devavrataiḥ stutā ।।evantribhirmalairāmaiḥ pakvaireva pṛthakpṛthak ।।nidānabhūtaissaṃsārarogaḥ puṃsāṃ pravartate ।।asya rogasya bhaiṣajyaṃ jñānameva na cāparam ।।bhiṣagājñāpakaḥ śambhuśśivaḥ paramakāraṇam ।।aduḥkhenā api śakto asau paśūnmocayituṃ śivaḥ ।।kathaṃ duḥkhaṃ karotīti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।।duḥkhameva hi sarvo api saṃsāra iti niścitam ।।kathaṃ duḥkhamaduḥkhaṃ syātsvabhāvo hyaviparyayaḥ ।।na hi rogī hyarogī syādbhiṣagbhaiṣajyakāraṇāt ।।rogārtaṃ tu bhiṣagrogādbhaiṣajaissukhamuddharet ।।evaṃ svabhāvamalinānsvabhāvādduḥkhinaḥ paśūn ।।svājñauṣadhavidhānena duḥkhānmocayate śivaḥ ।।na bhiṣakkāraṇaṃ roge śivaḥ saṃsārakāraṇam ।।ityetadapi vaiṣamyaṃ na doṣāyāsya kalpate ।।duḥkhe svabhāvasaṃsiddhe kathantatkāraṇaṃ śivaḥ ।।svābhāviko malaḥ puṃsāṃ sa hi saṃsārayatyamūn ।।saṃsārakāraṇaṃ yattu malaṃ māyādyacetanam ।।tatsvayaṃ na pravarteta śivasānnidhyamantarā ।।yathā maṇirayaskāṃtassānnidhyādupakārakaḥ ।।ayasaścalatastadvacchivo apyasyeti sūrayaḥ ।।na nivartayituṃ śakyaṃ sānnidhyaṃ sadakāraṇam ।।adhiṣṭhātā tato nityamajñāto jagataśśivaḥ ।।na śivena vinā kiṃcitpravṛttamiha vidyate ।।tatpreritamidaṃ sarvaṃ tathāpi na sa muhyati ।।śaktirājñātmikā tasya niyantrī viśvatomukhī ।।tayā tatamidaṃ śaśvattathāpi sa na duṣyati ।।anidaṃ prathamaṃ sarvamīśitavyaṃ sa īśvaraḥ ।।īśanācca tadīyājñā tathāpi sa na duṣyati ।।yo anyathā manyate mohātsa vinaṣyati durmatiḥ ।।tacchaktivaibhavādeva tathāpi sa na duṣyati ।।etasminnaṃtare vyomnaḥ śrutāḥ vāgarīriṇī ।।satyamomamṛtaṃ saumyamityāvirabhavatsphuṭam ।।tato hṛṣṭatarāḥ sarve vinaṣṭāśeṣasaṃśayāḥ ।।munayo vismayāviṣṭāḥ preṇemuḥ pavanaṃ prabhum ।।tathā vigatasandehānkṛtvāpi pavano munīn ।।naite pratiṣṭhitajñānā iti matvaivamabravīt ।।
vāyuruvācva parokṣamaparokṣaṃ ca dvividhaṃ jñānamiṣyate ।।parokṣamasthiraṃ prāhuraparokṣaṃ tu susthiram ।।hetūpadeśagamyaṃ yattatparokṣaṃ pracakṣate ।। aparokṣaṃ punaḥ śreṣṭhādanuṣṭhānādbhaviṣyati ।।nāparokṣādṛte mokṣa iti kṛtvā viniścayam ।।śreṣṭhānuṣṭhānasiddhyarthaṃ prayatadhvamatandritāḥ ।। chapter ṛṣaya ūcuḥ kiṃ tacchreṣṭamanuṣṭhānaṃ mokṣo yenaparokṣitaḥ ।।tattasya sādhanaṃ cādya vaktumarhasi māruta ।।vāyuruvāca śaivo hi paramo dharmaḥ śreṣṭhānuṣṭhānaśabditaḥ ।।yatrāparokṣo lakṣyeta sākṣānmokṣapradaḥ śivaḥ ।।sa tu pañcavidho jñeyaḥ pañcabhiḥ parvabhiḥ kramāt ।।kriyātapojapadhyānajñānātmabhiranuttaraiḥ ।।taireva sottaraissiddho dharmastu paramo mataḥ ।।parokṣamaparokṣaṃ ca jñānaṃ yatra ca mokṣadam ।।paramo aparamaścobhau dharmau hi śruticoditau ।।dharmaśabdābhidheyerthe pramāṇaṃ śrutireva naḥ ।।paramo yogaparyanto dharmaḥ śrutiśirogataḥ ।।dharmastvaparamastadvadadhaḥ śrutimukhotthitaḥ ।।apaśvātmādhikāratvādyo dharamaḥ paramo mataḥ ।।sādhāraṇastato anyastu sarveṣāmadhikārataḥ ।।sa cāyaṃ paramo dharmaḥ paradharmasya sādhanam ।।dharmaśāstrādibhissamyak sāṃga evopabṛṃhitaḥ ।।śaivo yaḥ paramo dharmaḥ śreṣṭhānuṣṭhānaśabditaḥ ।।itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ kathaṃcidupabṛṃhitaḥ ।।śaivāgamaistu saṃpannaḥ sahāṃgopāṃvistaraḥ ।।tatsaṃskārādhikāraiśca samyagevopabṛṃhitaḥ ।।śaivāgamo hi dvividhaḥ śrauto aśrautaśca saṃskṛtaḥ ।।śrutisāramayaḥ śrautassvataṃtra itaro mataḥ ।।svataṃtro daśadhā pūrvaṃ tathāṣṭādaśadhā punaḥ ।।kāmikādisamākhyābhissiddhaḥ siddhāntasaṃjñitaḥ ।।śrutisāramayo yastu śatakoṭipravistaraḥ ।।paraṃ pāśupataṃ yatra vrataṃ jñānaṃ ca kathyate ।।yugāvarteṣu śiṣyeta yogācāryasvarūpiṇā ।।tatratatrāvatīrṇena śivenaiva pravartyate ।।saṃkṣipyāsya pravaktāraścatvāraḥ paramarṣaya ।।rururdadhīco agastyaśca upamanyurmahāyaśāḥ ।।te ca pāśupatā jñeyāssaṃhitānāṃ pravartakāḥ ।।tatsaṃtatīyā guravaḥ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।।tatroktaḥ paramo dharmaścaryādyātmā caturvidhaḥ ।।teṣu pāśupato yogaḥ śivaṃ pratyakṣayeddṛḍham ।।tasmācchreṣṭhamanuṣṭhānaṃ yogaḥ pāśupato mataḥ ।।tatrāpyupāyako yukto brahmaṇā sa tu kathyate ।।nāmāṣṭakamayo yogaśśivena parikalpitaḥ ।।tena yogena sahasā śaivī prajñā prajāyate ।।prajñayā paramaṃ jñānamacirāllabhate sthiram ।। prasīdati śivastasya yasya jñānaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।।prasādātparamo yogo yaḥ śivaṃ cāparokṣayet ।।śivāparokṣātsaṃsārakāraṇena viyujyate ।।tataḥ syānmuktasaṃsāro muktaḥ śivasamo bhavet ।।brahmaprokta ityupāyaḥ sa eva pṛthagucyate ।।śivo maheśvaraścaiva rudro viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaḥ ।।saṃsāravaidyaḥ sarvajñaḥ paramātmeti mukhyataḥ ।।nāmāṣṭakamidaṃ mukhyaṃ śivasya pratipādakam ।।ādyantu pañcakaṃ jñeyaṃ śāntyatītādyanukramāt ।।saṃjñā sadāśivādīnāṃ pañcopādhiparigrahāt ।।upādhivinivṛttau tu yathāsvaṃ vinivartate ।।padameva hi tannityamanityāḥ padinaḥ smṛtāḥ ।।padānāṃ pratikṛttau tu mucyante padino yataḥ ।।parivṛttyantare bhūyastatpadaprāptirucyate ।।ātmāntarābhidhānaṃ syādyadādyaṃ nāma pañcakam ।।anyattu tritayaṃ nāmnāmupādānādiyogataḥ ।।trividhopādhivacanācchiva evānuvartate ।।anādimalasaṃśleṣaḥ prāgabhāvātsvabhāvataḥ ।।atyaṃtaṃ pariśuddhātmetyato ayaṃ śiva ucyate ।।athavāśeṣakalyāṇaguṇaikadhana īśvaraḥ ।।śiva ityucyate sadbhiśśivatattvārthavādibhiḥ ।।trayoviṃśatitattvebhyaḥ prakṛtirhi parā matā ।।prakṛtestu paraṃ prāhuḥ puruṣaṃ pañcaviṃśakam ।।yaṃ vedādau svaraṃ prāhurvācyavācakabhāvataḥ ।।vedaikavedyayāthātmyādvedānte ca pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।।tasya prakṛtilīnasya yaḥ parassa maheśvaraḥ ।।tadadhīnapravṛttitvātprakṛteḥ puruṣasya ca ।।athavā triguṇaṃ tattvamupeyamidamavyayam ।।māyāntu prakṛtiṃ vidyānmāyinaṃ tu maheśvaram ।।māyāvikṣobhako anaṃto maheśvarasamanvayāt ।।kālātmā paramātmādiḥ sthūlaḥ sūkṣmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।rudduḥkhaṃ duḥkhaheturvā tadrāvayati naḥ prabhuḥ ।।rudra ityucyate sadbhiḥ śivaḥ paramakāraṇam ।।tattvādibhūtaparyantaṃ śarīrādiṣvatandritaḥ ।।vyāpyādhitiṣṭhati śivastato rudra itastataḥ ।।jagataḥ pitṛbhūtānāṃ śivo mūrtyātmanāmapi ।।pitṛbhāvena sarveṣāṃ pitāmaha udīritaḥ ।।nidānajño yathā vaidyo rogasya vinivartakaḥ ।।upāyairbheṣajaistadvallayabhogādhikārataḥ ।।saṃsārasyeśvaro nityaṃ samūlasya nivartakaḥ ।।saṃsāravaidya ityuktaḥ sarvatattvārthavedibhiḥ ।।daśārthajñānasiddhyarthamindriyeṣveṣu satsvapi ।।trikālabhāvino bhāvānsthūlānsūkṣmānaśeṣataḥ ।।aṇavo naiva jānanti māyayaiva malāvṛtāḥ ।।asatsvapi ca sarveṣu sarvārthajñānahetuṣu ।।
yadyathāvasthitaṃ vastu tattathaiva sadāśivaḥ ।।ayatnenaiva jānāti tasmātsarvajña ucyate ।।sarvātmā paramairebhirguṇairnityasamanvayāt ।।svasmātparātmavirahātparamātmā śivaḥ svayam ।।nāmāṣṭakamidaṃ caiva labdhvācāryaprasādataḥ ।।nivṛttyādikalāgranthiṃ śivādyaiḥ pañcanāmabhiḥ ।।yathāsvaṃ kramaśaśchitvā śodhayitvā yathāguṇam ।।guṇitaireva soddhātairaniruddhairathāpi vā ।।hṛtkaṇṭhatālubhrūmadhyabrahmarandhrasamanvitām ।।chittvā paryaṣṭakākāraṃ svātmānaṃ ca suṣumṇayā ।।dvādaśāṃtaḥsthitasyendornītvopari śivaujasi ।।saṃhṛtyaṃ vadanaṃ paścādyathāsaṃskaraṇaṃ layāt ।।śāktenāmṛtavarṣeṇa saṃsiktāyāṃ tanau punaḥ ।।avatārya svamātmānamamṛtātmākṛtiṃ hṛdi ।।dvādaśāṃtaḥsthitasyendoḥ parastācchvetapaṃkaje ।।samāsīnaṃ mahādevaṃ śaṃkarambhaktavatsalam ।।ardhanārīśvaraṃ devaṃ nirmalaṃ madhurākṛtim ।।śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ prasannaṃ śītaladyutim ।।dhyātvā hi mānase devaṃ svasthacitto atha mānavaḥ ।।śivanāmāṣṭakenaiva bhāvapuṣpaissamarcayet ।।abhyarcanānte tu punaḥ prāṇānāyamya mānavaḥ ।।samyakcittaṃ samādhāya śārvaṃ nāmāṣṭakaṃ japet ।।nābhau cāṣṭāhutīrhutvā pūrṇāhutyā namastataḥ ।।aṣṭapuṣpapradānena kṛtvābhyarcanamaṃtimam ।।nivedayetsvamātmānaṃ culukodakavartmanā ।।evaṃ kṛtvā cirādeva jñānaṃ pāśupataṃ śubham ।।labhate tatpratiṣṭhāṃ ca vṛttaṃ cānuttamaṃ tathā ।।yogaṃ ca paramaṃ labdhvā mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। chapter ṛṣaya ūcuḥ bhagavañchrotumicchāmo vrataṃ pāśupataṃ param ।।brahmādayo api yatkṛtvā sarve pāśupatāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।vāyuruvāca rahasyaṃ vaḥ pravakṣyāmi sarvapāpanikṛntanam ।।vrataṃ pāśupataṃ śrautamatharvaśirasi śrutam ।।kālaścaitrī paurṇamāsī deśaḥ śivaparigrahaḥ ।।kṣetrārāmādyaraṇyaṃ vā praśastaśśubhalakṣaṇaḥ ।।tatra pūrvaṃ trayodaśyāṃ susnātaḥ sukṛtāhnikaḥ ।।anujñāpya svamācāryaṃ saṃpūjya praṇipatya ca ।।pūjāṃ vaiśeṣikīṃ kṛtvā śuklāṃbaradharaḥ svayam ।।śuklayajñopavītī ca śuklamālyānulepanaḥ ।।darbhāsane samāsīno darbhamuṣṭiṃ pragṛhya ca ।। prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā prāṅmukho vāpyudaṅmukhaḥ ।।dhyātvā devaṃ ca devīṃ ca tadvijñāpanavartmanā ।। f।vratametatkaromīti bhavetsaṃkalpya dīkṣitaḥ ।।yāvaccharīrapātaṃ vā dvādaśābdamathāpi vā ।।tadardhaṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā māsadvādaśakaṃ tu vā ।।tadardhaṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā māsamekamathāpi vā ।।dinadvādaśakaṃ vā atha dinaṣaṭkamathāpi vā ।।tadardhaṃ dinamekaṃ vā vratasaṃkalpanāvadhi ।।agnimādhāya vidhivadvirajāhomakāraṇāt ।।hutvājyena samidbhiśca caruṇā ca yathākramam ।।pūrṇāmāpūrya tāṃ bhūyastattvānāṃ śuddhimuddiśan ।।juhuyānmūlamantreṇa taireva samidādibhiḥ ।। tattvānyetāni maddehe śuddhyaṃtām tyanusmaran ।।pañcabhūtāni tanmātrāḥ pañcakarmendriyāṇi ca ।।jñānakarmavibhedena pañcakarmavibhāgaśaḥ ।।tvagādidhātavassapta pañca prāṇādivāyavaḥ ।।manobuddhirahaṃ khyātirguṇāḥ prakṛtipūruṣau ।।rāgo vidyākale caiva niyatiḥ kāla eva ca ।।māyā ca śuddhividyā ca ca ।।vinyasyāgnau ca samprokṣya dine tasminhaviṣyabhuk ।।prabhāte tu caturdaśyāṃ kṛtvā sarvaṃ puroditam ।।dine tasminnirāhāraḥ kālaṃ śeṣaṃ samāpayet ।।prātaḥ parvaṇi cāpyevaṃ kṛtvā homā vasānataḥ ।।upasaṃhṛtya rudrāgniṃ gṛhṇīyādbhasma yatnataḥ ।।tataśca jaṭilo muṇḍī śikhaikajaṭa eva vā ।।bhūtvā snātvā tato vītalajjaścetsyāddigambaraḥ ।।api kāṣāyavasanaścarmacīrāmbaro atha vā ।।ekāmbaro valkalī ।।tatpadmakarṇikāmadhye kṛtvā liṃgaṃ kanīyasam ।।sphīṭikaṃ pīṭhikopetaṃ pūjayedvidhivatkramāt ।।pratiṣṭhāpya vidhānena talliṃgaṃ kṛtaśodhanam ।।parikalpyāsanaṃ mūrtiṃ pañcavaktraprakārataḥ ।।śrīpatrotpalapadmānāṃ saṃkhyā sāhasrikī matā ।।pratyekamaparā saṃkhyā śatamaṣṭottaraṃ dvijāḥ ।।tatrāpi ca viśeṣeṇa na tyajedbilvapatrakam ।।haimamekaṃ paraṃ prāhuḥ padmaṃ padmasahasrakāt ।।nīlotpalādiṣvapyetatsamānaṃ bilbapatrakaiḥ ।।puṣpāntare na niyamo yathālābhaṃ nivedayet ।।aṣṭāṅgamarghyamutkṛṣṭaṃ dhūpālepau viśeṣataḥ ।।candanaṃ vāmadevākhye haritālaṃ ca pauruṣe ।।īśāne bhasitaṃ ।।prathamāvaraṇe pūjyo kramāddherambaṣaṇmukhau ।।brahmāṃgāni tataścaiva prathamāvaraṇercite ।।dvitīyāvaraṇe pūjyā vighneśāścakravartinaḥ ।।tṛtīyāvaraṇe pūjyā bhavādyā aṣṭamūrtayaḥ ।।
mahādevādayastatra tathaikādaśamūrtayaḥ ।।caturthāvaraṇe pūjyāḥ sarva eva gaṇeśvarāḥ ।।bahireva tu padmasya pañcamāvaraṇe kramāt ।।daśadikpatayaḥ pūjyāḥ sāstrāḥ sānucarāstathā ।।brahmaṇo mānasāḥ vratametatsamācaret ।।arkavāre tathārdrāyāṃ pañcadaśyāṃ ca pakṣayoḥ ।।aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ śaktastūpavasedapi ।।pākhaṇḍipatitodakyāssūtakāntyajapūrvakān ।।varjayetsarvayatnena manasā karmaṇā girā ।।kṣamadānadayāsatyāhiṃsāśīlaḥ sadā bhavet ।।saṃtuṣṭaśca praśāntaśca japadhyānaratastathā ।।kuryāttriṣavaṇasnānaṃ bhasmasnānamathāpi vā ।।pūjāṃ vaiśeṣikīṃ caiva manasā vacasā girā ।।bahunātra kimuktena nācaredaśivaṃ vratī ।।pramādāttu tathācāre nirūpya gurulāghave ।। ucitāṃ niṣkṛtiṃ kuryātpūjāhomajapādibhiḥ ।।āsamāptervratasyaivamācarenna pramādataḥ ।।godānaṃ ca vṛṣotsargaṃ kuryātpūjāṃ ca saṃpadā ।।bhaktaśca śivaprītyarthaṃ sarvakāmavivarjitaḥ ।।sāmānyametatkathitaṃ vratasyāsya samāsataḥ ।।pratimāsaṃ viśeṣaṃ ca pravadāmi yathāśrutam ।।vaiśākhe vajraliṃgaṃ tu jyeṣṭhe mārakataṃ śubham ।।āṣāḍhe mauktikaṃ vidyācchrāvaṇe nīlanirmitam ।।māse bhādrapade caiva padmarāgamayaṃ param ।।āśvine māsi vidyādvai liṃgaṃ gomedakaṃ varam ।।kārtikyāṃ vaidrumaṃ liṃgaṃ vaidūryaṃ mārgaśīrṣake ।।puṣparāgamayaṃ pauṣe māghe dyumaṇijantathā ।।phālguṇe candrakāntotthaṃ caitre tadvyatyayo athavā ।।sarvamāseṣu ratnānāmalābhe haimameva vā ।।haimābhāve rājataṃ vā tāmrajaṃ śailajantathā ।।mṛnmayaṃ vā yathālābhaṃ jātuṣaṃ cānyadeva vā ।।sarvagaṃdhamayaṃ vātha liṃgaṃ kuryādyathāruci ।।vratāvasānasamaye samācaritanityakaḥ ।।kṛtvā vaiśeṣikīṃ pūjāṃ hutvā caiva yathā purā ।।saṃpūjya ca tathācāryaṃ vratinaśca viśeṣataḥ ।।deśikenāpyanujñātaḥ prāṅmukho vāpyudaṅmukhaḥ ।।darbhāsano darbhapāṇiḥ prāṇāpānau niyamya ca ।।japitvā śaktito mūlaṃ dhyātvā sāmbaṃ triyambakam ।।anujñāpya yathāpūrvaṃ namaskṛtya kṛtāñjaliḥ ।।samutsṛjāmi bhagavanvratametattvadājñayā ।।ityuktvā liṃgamūlasthāndarbhānuttaratastyajet ।।tato daṇḍajaṭācīramekhalā api cotsṛjet ।।punarācamya vidhivatpañcākṣaramudīrayet ।।yaḥ kṛtvātyaṃtikīṃ dīkṣāmādehāntamanākulaḥ ।।vratametatprakurvīta sa tu vai naiṣṭhikaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।so atyāśramī ca vijñeyo mahāpāśupatastathā ।।sa eva tapatāṃ śreṣṭha sa eva ca mahāvratī ।।na tena sadṛśaḥ kaścitkṛtakṛtyo mumukṣuṣu ।।yo yatirnaiṣṭhiko jātastamāhurnaiṣṭhikottamam ।।yo anvahaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ vā vratametatsamācaret ।।so api naiṣṭhikatulyaḥ syāttīvravratasamanvayāt ।।ghṛtākto yaścaredetadvrataṃ vrataparāyaṇaḥ ।।dvitraikadivasaṃ vāpi sa ca kaścana naiṣṭhikaḥ ।।kṛtyamityeva niṣkāmo yaścaredvratamuttamam ।।śivārpitātmā satataṃ na tena sadṛśaḥ kvacit ।।bhasmacchanno dvijo vidvānmahāpātakasaṃbhavaiḥ ।।pāpaissudāruṇaissadyo mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।rudrāgniryatparaṃ vīryantadbhasma parikīrtitam ।।tasmātsarveṣu kāleṣu vīryavānbhasmasaṃyutaḥ ।। bhasmaniṣṭhasya naśyanti deṣā bhasmāgnisaṃgamāt ।।bhasmasnānaviśuddhātmā bhasmaniṣṭha iti smṛtaḥ ।।bhasmanā digdhasarvāṃgo bhasmadīptatripuṃḍrakaḥ ।।bhasmasnāyī ca puruṣo bhasmaniṣṭha iti smṛtaḥ ।।bhūtapretapiśāsāśca rogāścātīva dussahāḥ ।।bhasmaniṣṭhasya sānnidhyādvidravaṃti na saṃśayaḥ ।।bhāsanādbhāsitaṃ proktaṃ bhasma kalmaṣabhakṣaṇāt ।।bhūtibhūtikarī caiva rakṣā rakṣākarī param ।।kimanyadiha vaktavyaṃ bhasmamāhātmyakāraṇam ।।vratī ca bhasmanā snātassvayaṃ devo maheśvaraḥ ।।paramāstraṃ ca śaivānāṃ bhasmaitatpārameśvaram ।।dhaumyāgrajasya tapasi vyāpado yannivāritāḥ ।।tasmātsarvaprayatnena kṛtvā pāśupatavratam ।।dhanavadbhasma saṃgṛhya bhasmasnānarato bhavet ।। chapter ṛṣaya ūcuḥ dhaumyāgrajena śuśunā kṣīrārthaṃ hi tapaḥ kṛtam ।।tasmāt kṣīrārṇavo dattastasmai devena śūlinā ।।sa kathaṃ śiśuko lebhe śivaśāstrapravaktṛtām ।।kathaṃ vā śivasadbhāvaṃ jñātvā tapasi niṣṭhitaḥ ।।kathaṃ ca labdhavijñānastapaścaraṇaparvaṇi ।।rudrāgneryatparaṃ vīryaṃ labhe bhasma svarakṣakam ।।vāyuruvāca na hyeṣa śiśukaḥ kaścitprākṛtaḥ kṛtavāṃstapaḥ ।।munivaryasya tanayo vyāghrapādasya dhīmataḥ ।।janmāntareṇa saṃsiddhaḥ kenāpi khalu hetunā ।।svapadapracyuto diṣṭyā prāpto munikumāratām ।।mahādevaprasādasya bhāgyāpannasya bhāvinaḥ ।।dugdhābhilāṣaprabhavadvāratāmagamattapaḥ ।।ataḥ sarvagaṇeśatvaṃ kumāratvaṃ ca śāśvatam ।।saha dugdhābdhinā tasmai pradadau śaṃkaraḥ svayam ।।tasya jñānāgamopyasya prasādādeva śāṃkarāt ।।kaumāraṃ hi paraṃ sākṣājjñānaṃ śaktimayaṃ viduḥ ।।śivaśāstrapravaktṛtvamapi tasya hi tatkṛtam ।।kumāro munito labdhajñānābdhiriva nandanaḥ ।।dṛṣṭaṃ tu kāraṇaṃ tasya śivajñānasamanvaye ।।svamātṛvacanaṃ sākṣācchokajaṃ kṣīrakāraṇāt ।।kadācitkṣīramatyalpaṃ pītavānmātulāśrame ।।īrṣayayā mātulasutaṃ saṃtṛptakṣīramuttamam ।।pītvā sthitaṃ yathākāmaṃ dṛṣṭvā vai mātulātmajam ।।upamanyurvyāghrapādiḥ prītyā provāca mātaram ।।upamanyuruvāca mātarmātarmahābhāge mama dehi tapasvini ।।
gavyaṃ kṣīramatisvādu nālpamuṣṇaṃ pibāmyaham ।। vāyuruvāca tacchrutvā putravacanaṃ tanmātā ca tapasvinī ।।vyāghrapādasya mahiṣī duḥkhamāpattadā ca sā ।।upalālyātha suprītyā putramāliṃgya sādaram ।।duḥkhitā vilalāpātha smṛtvā nairdhanyamātmanaḥ ।।smṛtvāsmṛtvā punaḥ kṣīramupamanyussa bālakaḥ ।।dehi dehīti tāmāha rudranbhūyo mahādyutiḥ ।।taddhaṭhaṃ sā parijñāya dvijapatnī tapasvinī ।।śāntaye taddhaṭhasyātha śubhopāyamarīracat ।।uñchavṛttyārjitānbījānsvayaṃ dṛṣṭvā ca sā tadā ।।bījapiṣṭamathāloḍya toyena kalabhāṣiṇī ।।ehyehi mama putreti sāmapūrvaṃ tatassutam ।।āliṃgyādāya duḥkhārtā pradadau kṛtrimaṃ payaḥ ।।pītvā ca kṛtrimaṃ kṣīraṃ mātrāṃ dattaṃ sa bālakaḥ ।।naitatkṣīramiti prāha mātaraṃ cātivihvalaḥ ।।duḥkhitā sā tadā prāha saṃprekṣyāghrāya mūrdhani ।।samārjya netra putrasya karābhyāṃ kamalāyate ।।jananyuvāca taṭinī ratnapūrṇāstāssvargapātālagocarāḥ ।।bhāgyahīnā na paśyanti bhaktihīnāśca ye śive ।।rājyaṃ svargaṃ ca mokṣaṃ ca bhojanaṃ kṣīrasaṃbhavam ।।na labhante priyāṇyeṣāṃ na tuṣyati yadā śivaḥ ।।bhavaprasādajaṃ sarvaṃ nānyaddevaprasādajam ।।anyadeveṣu niratā duḥkhārtā vibhramanti ca ।।kṣīraṃ tatra kuto asmākaṃ vane nivasatāṃ sadā ।।kva dugdhasādhanaṃ vatsa kva vayaṃ vanavāsinaḥ ।।kṛtsnābhāvena dāridryānmayā te bhāgyahīnayā ।।mithyādugdhamidaṃ dattampiṣṭamāloḍya vāriṇā ।।tvaṃ mātulagṛhe svalpaṃ pītvā svādu payaḥ śṛtam ।।jñātvā svādu tvayā pītaṃ tajjātīyamanusmaran ।।dattaṃ na paya ityuktvā rudan duḥkhīkaroṣi mām ।।prasādena vinā śaṃbho payastava na vidyate ।।pādapaṃkajayostasya sāmbasya sagaṇasya ca ।।bhaktyā samarpitaṃ yattatkāraṇaṃ sarvasampadām ।।adhunā vasudosmābhirmahādevo na pūjitaḥ ।।sakāmānāṃ yathākāmaṃ yathoktaphaladāyakaḥ ।।dhanānyuddiśya nāsmābhiritaḥ prāgarcitaḥ śivaḥ ।।ato daridrāssaṃjātā vayaṃ tasmānna te payaḥ ।।pūrvajanmani yaddattaṃ śivamuddiśya vai sutaḥ ।।tadeva labhyate nānyadviṣṇumuddiśya vā prabhum ।।vāyuruvāca iti mātṛvacaḥ śrutvā tathyaṃ śokādisūcakam ।।bālo apyanutapannaṃtaḥ pragalbhamidamabravīt ।। upamanyuruvāca śokenālamito mataḥ sāṃbo yadyasti śaṃkaraḥ ।।tyaja śokaṃ mahābhāge sarvaṃ bhadraṃ bhaviṣyati ।।śṛṇu mātarvaco medya mahādevo asti cetkvacit ।।cirādvā hyacirādvāpi kṣīrodaṃ sādhayāmyaham ।।vāyuruvāca iti śrutvā vacastasya bālakasya mahāmateḥ ।।praytuvāca tadā mātā suprasannā manasvinī ।।mātovāca śubhaṃ vicāritaṃ tāta tvayā matprītivardhanam ।।vilaṃbaṃ mā kathāstvaṃ hi bhaja sāṃbaṃ sadāśivam ।।sarvasmādadhiko astyeva śivaḥ paramakāraṇam ।।tatkṛtaṃ hi jagatsarvaṃ brahmādyāstasya kiṃkarāḥ ।।tatprasādakṛtaiśvaryā dāsāstasya vayaṃ prabhoḥ ।।taṃ vinānyaṃ na jānīmaśśaṃkaraṃ lokaśaṃkaram ।।anyāndevānparityajya karmaṇā manasā girā ।।tameva sāṃbaṃ sagaṇaṃ bhaja bhāvapurassaram ।।tasya devādhidevasya śivasya varadāyinaḥ ।।sākṣānnamaśśivāyeti maṃtro ayaṃ vācakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।saptakoṭimahāmaṃtrāḥ sarve sapraṇavāḥ pare ।।tasminneva vilīyaṃte punastasmādvinirgatāḥ ।।saprasādāśca te maṃtrāḥ svādhikārādyapekṣayā ।।sarvādhikārastveko ayaṃ maṃtra eveśvarājñayā ।।yathā nikṛṣṭānutkṛṣṭānsarvānapyātmanaḥ śivaḥ ।।kṣamate rakṣituṃ tadvanmaṃtro ayamapi sarvadā ।।prabalaśca tathā hyeṣa maṃtro mantrāntarādapi ।।sarvarakṣākṣamo apyeṣa nāparaḥ kaścidiṣyate ।।tasmānmantrāntarāṃstyaktvā pañcākṣaraparo bhava ।।tasmiñjihvāṃtaragate na kiṃcidiha durlabham ।।adhorāstraṃ ca śaivānāṃ rakṣāheturanuttamam ।।tacca tatprabhavaṃ matvā tatparo bhava nānyathā ।।bhasmedantu mayā labdhaṃ pitureva tavottamam ।।virajānalasaṃsiddhaṃ mahāvyāpannivāraṇam ।।maṃtraṃ ca te mayā dattaṃ gṛhāṇa madanujñayā ।।anenaivāśu japtena rakṣā tava bhaviṣyati ।।vāyuruvāca evaṃ mātrā samādiśya śivamastvityudīrya ca ।।visṛṣṭastadvaco mūrdhni kurvanneva tadā muniḥ ।।tāṃ praṇamyaivamuktvā ca tapaḥ kartuṃ pracakrame ।।tamāha ca tadā mātā śubhaṃ kurvaṃtu te surāḥ ।।anujñātastayā tatra tapastepe sa duścaram ।।himavatparvataṃ prāpya vāyubhakṣaḥ samāhitaḥ ।।aṣṭeṣṭakābhiḥ prasādaṃ kṛtvā liṃgaṃ ca mṛnmayam ।।tatrāvāhya mahādevaṃ sāṃbaṃ sagaṇamavyayam ।। bhaktyā pañcākṣareṇaiva putraiḥ puṣpairvanodbhavaiḥ ।।samabhyarcya ciraṃ kālaṃ cacāra paramaṃ tapaḥ ।।tatastapaścarattaṃ taṃ bālamekākinaṃ kṛśam ।।upamanyuṃ dvijavaraṃ śivasaṃsaktamānasam ।।purā marīcinā śaptāḥ kecinmunipiśācakāḥ ।।saṃpīḍya rākṣasairbhāvaistapasovighnamācaran ।।sa ca taiḥ pīḍyamāno api tapaḥ kurvankathañcana ।।sadā namaḥ śivāyeti krośati smārtanādavat ।।tannādaśravaṇādeva tapaso vighnakāriṇaḥ ।।te taṃ bālaṃ samutsṛjya munayassamupācaran ।।tapasā tasya viprasya copamanyormahātmanaḥ ।।carācaraṃ ca munayaḥ pradīpitamabhūjjagat ।।
chapter vāyuruvāca atha sarve pradīptāṃgā vaikuṇṭhaṃ prayayurdrutam ।।praṇamyāhuśca tatsarvaṃ haraye devasattamāḥ ।।śrutvā teṣāṃ tadā vākyaṃ bhagavānpuruṣottamaḥ ।।kimidantviti saṃcintya jñātvā tatkāraṇaṃ ca saḥ ।।jagāma mandaraṃ tūrṇaṃ maheśvaradidṛkṣayā ।।dṛṣṭvā devaṃ praṇamyaivaṃ provāca sukṛtāṃjaliḥ ।।viṣṇuruvāca bhagavanbrāhmaṇaḥ kaścidupamanyuriti śrutaḥ ।।kṣīrārthamadahatsarvaṃ tapasā tannivāraya ।।vāyuruvāca iti śrutvā vaco viṣṇoḥ prāha devo maheśvaraḥ ।।śiśuṃ nivārayiṣyāmi tattvaṃ gaccha svamāśramam ।।tacchrutvā śaṃbhuvacanaṃ sa viṣṇurdevavallabhaḥ ।।jagāmāśvāsya tānsarvānsvalokamamarādikān ।।etasminnaṃtare devaḥ pinākī parameśvaraḥ ।।śakrasya rūpamāsthāya gantuṃ cakre matiṃ tataḥ ।।atha jagāma munestu tapovanaṃ gajavareṇa sitena sadāśivaḥ ।।saha surāsurasiddhamahoragairamararājatanuṃ svayamāsthitaḥ ।।sa vāraṇaścāru tadā vibhuṃ taṃ nivījya vālavyajanena divyam ।।dadhāra śacyā sahitaṃ sureṃdraṃ kareṇa vāmena śitātapatram ।।rarāja bhagavānsomaḥ śakrarūpī sadāśivaḥ ।।tenātapatreṇa yathā candrabiṃbena mandaraḥ ।।āsthāyaivaṃ hi śakrasya svarūpaṃ parameśvaraḥ ।।jagāmānugrahaṃ kartumupamanyostadāśramam ।।taṃ dṛṣṭvā parameśānaṃ śakrarūpadharaṃ śivam ।।praṇamya śirasā prāha mahāmunivaraḥ svayam ।।upamanyuruvāca pāvitaścāśramasso ayaṃ mama deveśvara svayam ।।prāpto yattvaṃ jagannātha bhagavandevasattama ।।vāyuruvāca evamuktvā sthitaṃ prekṣya kṛtāṃjalipuṭaṃ dvijam ।। prāha gaṃbhīrayā vācā śakrarūpadharo haraḥ ।। śakra uvāca tuṣṭo asmi te varaṃ brūhi tapasānena suvrata ।।dadāmi cepsitānsarvāndhaumyāgraja mahāmune ।।vāyuruvāca evamuktastadā tena śakreṇa munipuṃgavaḥ ।।vārayāmi śive bhaktimityuvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ ।।tanniśamya hariḥ prāha māṃ na jānāsi lekhapam ।।trailokyādhipatiṃ śakraṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam ।।madbhakto bhava viprarṣe māmevārcaya sarvadā ।।dadāmi sarvaṃ bhadraṃ te tyaja rudraṃ ca nirguṇam ।।rudreṇa nirguṇenāpi kiṃ te kāryaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।devapaṅktibahirbhūto yaḥ piśācatvamāgataḥ ।।vāyuruvāca tacchrutvā prāha sa munirjapanpañcākṣaraṃ manum ।।manyamāno dharmavighnaṃ prāha taṃ kartumāgatam ।।upamanyuruvāca tvayaivaṃ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ bhavaniṃdāratena vai ।।prasaṃgādeva devasya nirguṇatvaṃ mahātmanaḥ ।।tvaṃ na jānāmi vai rudraṃ sarvadeveśvareśvaram ।।brahmaviṣṇumaheśānāṃ janaka prakṛteḥ param ।।sadasadvyaktamavyaktaṃ yamāhurbrahmavādinaḥ ।।nityamekamanekaṃ ca varaṃ tasmādvṛṇomyaham ।।hetuvādavinirmuktaṃ sāṃkhyayogārthadamparam ।।upāsate yaṃ tattvajñā varaṃ tasmādvṛṇomyaham ।।nāsti śaṃbhoḥ paraṃ tattvaṃ sarvakāraṇakāraṇāt ।।brahmaviṣṇvādidevānāṃ sraṣṭurguṇaparādvibhoḥ ।।bahunātra kimuktena mayādyānumitaṃ mahat ।।bhavāṃtare kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ śrutā nindā bhavasya cet ।।śrutvā niṃdāṃ bhavasyātha tatkṣaṇādeva santyajet ।।svadehaṃ tannihatyāśu śivalokaṃ sa gacchati ।।āstāṃ tāvanmameccheyaṃ kṣīraṃ ghoramaghorāstrābhimaṃtritam ।।visṛjya śakramuddiśya nanāda sa munistadā ।।smṛtvā śaṃbhupadadvaṃdvaṃ svadehaṃ dugdhumudyataḥ ।।āgneyīṃ dhāraṇāṃ bibhradupamanyuravasthitaḥ ।।evaṃ vyavasite vipre bhagavānbhaganetrahā ।।vārayāmāsa saumyena dhāraṇāṃ tasya yoginaḥ ।।tadvisṛṣṭamaghorāstraṃ naṃdīśvaraniyogataḥ ।।jagṛhe madhyataḥ kṣiptaṃ nandī śaṃkaravallabhaḥ ।। svaṃ rūpameva bhagavānāsthāya parameśvaraḥ ।।darśayāmāsa śiprāya bālendukṛtaśekharam ।।kṣīrārṇavasahasraṃ ca pīyūṣārṇavameva vā ।।dadhyāderarṇavāṃścaiva ghṛtodārṇavameva ca ।।phalārṇavaṃ ca bālasya bhakṣya bhojyārṇavaṃ tathā ।।apūpānāṃ giriṃ caiva darśayāmāsa sa prabhuḥ ।।evaṃ sa dadṛśe devo devyā sārdhaṃ vṛṣopari ।।gaṇeśvaraistriśūlādyairdivyāstrairapi saṃvṛtaḥ ।।divi duṃdubhayo neduḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papāta ca ।।viṣṇubrahmendrapramukhairdevaiśchannā diśo daśa ।।athopamanyurānandasamudrormibhirāvṛtaḥ ।।papāta daṇḍavadbhūmau bhaktinamreṇa cetasā ।।etasminsamaye tatra sasmito bhagavānbhavaḥ ।।ehyehīti tamāhūya mūrdhnyāghrāya dadau varān ।।
śiva uvāca bhakṣyabhojyānyathākāmaṃ bāndhavairbhukṣva sarvadā ।।sukhī bhava sadā duḥkhānnirmuktā bhaktimānmama ।।upamanyo mahābhāga tavāmbaiṣā hi pārvatī ।।mayā putrīkṛto hyadya dattaḥ kṣīrodakārṇavaḥ ।।madhunaścārṇavaścaiva dadhyannārṇava eva ca ।।ājyaudanārṇavaścaiva phalādyarṇava eva ca ।।apūpagirayaścaiva bhakṣyabhojyārṇavastathā ।।ete dattā mayā te hi tvaṃ gṛhṇīṣva mahāmune ।।pitā tava mahādevo mātā vai jagadambikā ।।amaratvaṃ mayā dattaṃ gāṇapatyaṃ ca śāśvatam ।।varānvaraya suprītyā mano abhilaṣitānparān ।।prasanno ahaṃ pradāsyāmi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।।vāyuruvāca evamuktvā mahādevaḥ karābhyāmupagṛhyatam ।।mūrdhnyāghrāya sutaste ayamiti devyai nyavedayat ।।devī ca guhavatprītyā mūrdhni tasya karāmbujam ।।vinyasya pradadau tasmai kumārapadamavyayam ।।kṣīrābdhirapi sākāraḥ kṣīraṃ svādu kare dadhat ।।upasthāya dadau piṇḍībhūtaṃ kṣīramanaśvaram ।।yogaiśvaryaṃ sadā tuṣṭiṃ brahmavidyāmanaśvarām ।।samṛddhiṃ paramāntasmai dadau saṃtuṣṭamānasaḥ ।।atha śaṃbhuḥ prasannātmā dṛṣṭvā tasya tapomahaḥ ।।punardadau varaṃ divyaṃ munaye hyupamanyave ।।vrataṃ pāśupataṃ jñānaṃ vratayogaṃ ca tattvataḥ ।।dadau tasmai pravaktṛtvapāṭavaṃ suciraṃ param ।।so api labdhvā varāndivyānkumāratvaṃ ca sarvadā ।।tasmācchivācca tasyāśca śivāyā mudito abhavat ।।tataḥ prasannacetaskaḥ supraṇamya kṛtāṃjaliḥ ।।yayāce sa varaṃ vipro devadevānmaheśvarāt ।।upamanyuruvāca prasīda devadeveśa prasīda parameśvara ।।svabhaktindehi paramāndivyāmavyabhicāriṇīm ।। śraddhāndehi mahādeva dvasambandhiṣu me sadā ।।svadāsyaṃ paramaṃ snehaṃ sānnidhyaṃ caiva sarvadā ।।evamuktvā prasannātmāharṣagadgadayā girā ।।satuṣṭāva mahādevamupamanyurdvijottamaḥ ।। upamanyuruvāca devadeva mahādeva śaraṇāgatavatsala ।।prasīda karuṇāsiṃdho sāmba śaṃkara sarvadā ।।vāyuruvāca evamukto mahādevaḥ sarveṣāṃ ca varapradaḥ ।।pratyuvāca prasannātmopamanyuṃ munisattamam ।।śiva uvāca vatsopamanyo tuṣṭo asmi sarvaṃ dattaṃ mayā hi te ।।dṛḍhabhakto asi viprarṣe mayā vijñāsito hyasi ।।ajaraścāmaraścaiva bhava tvanduḥkhavarjitaḥ ।।yaśasvī tejasā yukto divyajñānasamanvitaḥ ।।akṣayā bāndhavāścaiva kulaṃ gotraṃ ca te sadā ।।bhaviṣyati dvijaśreṣṭha mayi bhaktiśca śāśvatī ।।sānnidhyaṃ cāśrame nityaṃ kariṣyāmi dvijottama ।।upakaṃṭhaṃ mama tvaṃ vai sānandaṃ vihariṣyasi ।।evamuktvā sa bhagavānsūryakoṭisamaprabhaḥ ।।īśānassa varāndattvā tatraivāntardadhe haraḥ ।।upamanyuḥ prasannātmā prāpya tasmādvarādvarān ।।jagāma jananīsthānaṃ sukhaṃ prāpādhikaṃ ca saḥ ।। iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe vaiyāsikyāṃ caturviṃśatisāhasryāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ tadantargatāyāṃ saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ pūrvakhaṇḍe upamanyucaritavarṇanaṃ nāma pañcatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ samāpto ayaṃ saptamyā vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāḥ pūrvakhaṇḍaḥ ।।
śrīḥ ।। śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ ।। śrīgaurīśaṃkarābhyāṃ namaḥ ।। atha saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍaḥ prārabhyate ।।

saṃhriyate punaḥ ।।na tanniyantā kaścitsyāttena sarvaṃ niyamyate ।।ityuktvā sā mahādevī tatraivāṃtaradhatta vai ।।devāśca vismitāḥ sarve tāṃ praṇamya divaṃ yayuḥ ।। chapter upamanyuruvāca śṛṇu kṛṣṇa maheśasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ ।।mūrtyātmabhistataṃ kṛtsnaṃ jagadetaccarācaram ।।sa śivassarvamevedaṃ svakīyābhiśca mūrtibhiḥ ।।adhitiṣṭhatyameyātmā hyetatsarvamanusmṛtam ।।brahmā viṣṇustathā rudro maheśānassadāśivaḥ ।।mūrtayastasya vijñeyā yābhirviśvamidaṃ tatam ।।athānyāścāpi tanavaḥ pañca brahmasamāhvayāḥ ।।tanūbhistābhirāvyāptamiha kiṃcinna vidyate ।।īśānaḥ puruṣo aghoro vāmaḥ sadyastathaiva ca ।।brahmāṇyetāni devasya mūrtayaḥ pañca viśrutāḥ ।।īśānākhyā tu yā tasya mūrtirādyā garīyasī ।।bhoktāraṃ prakṛteḥ sākṣātkṣetrajñamadhitiṣṭhati ।।sthāṇostatpuruṣākhyā yā mūrtirmūrtimataḥ prabhoḥ ।।guṇāśrayātmakaṃ bhogyamavyaktamadhitiṣṭhati ।।dharmādyaṣṭāṃgasaṃyuktaṃ buddhitattvaṃ pinākinaḥ ।।adhitiṣṭhatyaghorākhyā mūrtiratyaṃtapūjitā ।।vāmadevāhvayāṃ mūrtiṃ mahādevasya vedhasaḥ ।।ahaṃkṛteradhiṣṭhātrīmāhurāgamavedinaḥ ।।sadyo jātāhvayāṃ mūrtiṃ śambhoramitavarcasaḥ ।।mānasaḥ samadhiṣṭhātrīṃ matimaṃtaḥ pracakṣate ।।śrotrasya vācaḥ śabdasya vibhorvyomnastathaiva ca ।।īśvarīmīśvarasyemāmīśākhyāṃ hi vidurbudhāḥ ।।tvakpāṇisparśavāyūnāmīśvarīṃ mūrtimaiśvarīm ।।puruṣākhyaṃ vidussarve purāṇārthaviśāradāḥ ।।cakṣuṣaścaraṇasyāpi rūpasyāgnestathaiva ca ।।aghorākhyāmadhiṣṭhātrīṃ mūrtimāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ ।।ramanāyāśca pāyośca rasasyāpāṃ tathaiva ca ।।īśvarīṃ vāmadevākhyāṃ mūrtiṃ tanniratāṃ viduḥ ।।ghrāṇasya caivopasthasya gaṃdhasya ca bhuvastathā ।।sadyo jātāhvayāṃ mūrtimīśvarīṃ saṃpracakṣate ।।mūrtayaḥ pañca devasya vaṃdanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ ।।śreyorthibhirnarairnityaṃ śreyasāmekahetavaḥ ।।tasya devādidevasya mūrtyaṣṭakamayaṃ jagat ।।tasminvyāpya sthitaṃ viśvaṃ sūtre maṇigaṇā iva ।।śarvo bhavastathā rudra ugro bhīmaḥ paśoḥ patiḥ ।।
īśānaśca mahādevo mūrtayaścāṣṭa viśrutāḥ ।।bhūmyaṃbhognimarudvyomakṣetrajñārkaniśākarāḥ ।।adhiṣṭhitā maheśasya śarvādyairaṣṭamūrtibhiḥ ।।carācarātmakaṃ viśvaṃ dhatte viśvaṃbharātmikā ।।śārvīrśivāhvayā ghorarūpiṇī ।।spaṃdayatyanilātmadaṃ bibharti spaṃdate svayam ।।augrīti kathyate sadbhirmūrtirugrasya vedhasaḥ ।।sarvāvakāśadā sarvavyāpikā gaganātmikā ।।mūrtirbhīmasya bhīmākhyā bhūtavṛṃdasya bhedikā ।।sarvātmanāmadhiṣṭhātrī sarvakṣetranivāsinī ।।mūrtiḥ paśupaterjñeyā paśupāśanikṛṃtanī ।।dīpayaṃtī jagatsarvaṃ divākarasamāhvayā ।।īśānākhyamaheśasya mūrtirdivi visarpati ।।āpyāyayati yo viśvamamṛtāṃśurniśākaraḥ ।।mahādevasya sā mūrtirmahādevasamāhvayā ।।ātmā tasyāṣṭamī mūrtiḥ śivasya paramātmanaḥ ।।vyāpiketaramūrtīnāṃ viśvaṃ tasmācchivātmakam ।।vṛkṣasya mūlasekena śākhāḥ puṣyaṃti vai yathā ।।śivasya pūjayā tadvatpuṣyatyasya vapurjagat ।।sarvābhayapradānaṃ ca sarvānugrahaṇaṃ tathā ।।sarvopakārakaraṇaṃ śivasyārādhanaṃ viduḥ ।।yatheha putrapautrādeḥ prītyā prīto bhavetpitā ।।tathā sarvabhāvena rudraḥ paramakāraṇam ।। chapter kṛṣṇa uvāca bhagavanparameśasya śarvasyāmitatejasaḥ ।।mūrtibhirviśvamevedaṃ yathā vyāptaṃ tathā śrutam ।।athaitajjñātumicchāmi yāthātmyaṃ pameśayoḥ ।।strīpuṃbhāvātmakaṃ cedaṃ tābhyāṃ kathamadhiṣṭhitam ।।upamanyuruvāca śrīmadvibhūtiṃ śivayoryāthātmyaṃ ca samāsataḥ ।।vakṣye tadvistarādvaktuṃ bhavenāpi na śakyate ।।śaktiḥ sākṣānmahādevī mahādevaśca śaktimān ।।tayorvibhūtileśo vai sarvametaccarācaram ।।vastu kiṃcidacidrūpaṃ kiṃcidvastu cidātmakam ।। dvayaṃ śuddhamaśuddhaṃ ca paraṃ cāparameva ca ।।yatsaṃsarati ciccakramaciccakrasamanvitam ।।tadevāśuddhamaparamitaraṃ tu paraṃ śubham ।।aparaṃ ca paraṃ caiva dvayaṃ cidacidātmakam ।।śivasya ca śivāyāśca svāmyaṃ caitatsvabhāvataḥ ।।śivayorvai vaśe viśvaṃ na viśvasya vaśe śivau ।।īśitavyamidaṃ yasmāttasmādviśveśvarau śivau ।।yathā śivastathā devī yathā devī tathā śivaḥ ।।nānayoraṃtaraṃ vidyāccaṃdracandrikayoriva ।।caṃdro na khalu bhātyeṣa yathā caṃdrikayā vinā ।।na bhāti vidyamāno api tathā śaktyā vinā śivaḥ ।।prabhayā hi vināyadvadbhānureṣa na vidyate ।।prabhā ca bhānunā tena sutarāṃ tadupāśrayā ।।evaṃ parasparāpekṣā śaktiśaktimatoḥ sthitā ।।na śivena vinā śaktirna śaktyā ca vinā śivaḥ ।।śaktauyayā śivo nityaṃ bhaktau muktau ca dehinām ।।ādyā saikā parā śaktiścinmayī śivasaṃśrayā ।।yāmāhurakhileśasya taistairanuguṇairguṇaiḥ ।।samānadharmiṇīmeva śivasya paramātmanaḥ ।।saikā parā ca cidrūpā śaktiḥ prasavadharmiṇī ।।vibhajya bahudhā viśvaṃ vidadhāti śivecchayā ।।sā mūlaprakṛtirmāyā triguṇā ca tridhā smṛtā ।।śivayā ca viparyastaṃ yayā tatamidaṃ jagat ।।ekadhā ca dvidhā caiva tathā śatasahasradhā ।।śaktayaḥ khalu bhidyaṃte bahudhā vyavahārataḥ ।।śivecchayā parāśaktiḥ śivatattvaikatāṃ gatā ।।tataḥ parisphuratyādau sarge tailaṃ tilādiva ।।tataḥ kriyākhyayā śaktyā śaktau śaktimadutthayā ।।tasyāṃ vikṣobhyamāṇāyāmādau nādaḥ samudbabhau ।।nādādviniḥsṛto biṃdurbiṃdodevassadāśivaḥ ।।tasmānmaheśvaro jātaḥ śuddhavidyā maheśvarāt ।।sā vācāmīśvarī
