raudrī sā śaktirviṣṇaurvai vaiṣṇavī matā ।।brahmāṇī brahmaṇaḥ proktā cendrasyaiṃdrīti kathyate ।।kimatra bahunoktena yadviśvamiti kīrtitam ।।śakyātmanaiva tadvyāptaṃ yathā dehe aṃtarātmanā ।।tasmācchaktimayaṃ sarvaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṃgamam ।।kalā yā paramā śaktiḥ kathitā paramātmanaḥ ।।evameṣā parā śaktirīśvarecchānuyāyinī ।।sthiraṃ caraṃ ca yadviśvaṃ sṛjatīti viniścayaḥ ।।jñānakriyā caṃdrārdhaśekharaścaṃdro rohiṇī rudravallabhā ।।īśānaḥ parameśānastadāryā parameśvarī ।।anaṃtavalayo anaṃto hyanaṃtānaṃtavallabhā ।।kālāgnirudraḥ kālāriḥ kālī kālāṃtakapriyā ।।puruṣākhyo manuśśaṃbhuḥ śatarūpā śivapriyā ।।dakṣassākṣānmahādevaḥ prasūtiḥ parameśvarī ।।rucirbhavo bhavānī ca budhairākūtirucyate ।।bhṛgurbhagākṣihā devaḥ khyātistrinayanapriyā ।।marīcibhagavānrudraḥ saṃbhūtiśśarvavallabhā ।।gaṃgādharo aṃgirā jñeyaḥ smṛtiḥ sākṣādumā smṛtā ।।pulastyaḥ śaśabhṛnmauliḥ prītiḥ kāṃtā pinākinaḥ ।।pulahastripuradhvaṃsī tatpriyā tu śivapriyā ।।kratudhvaṃsī kratuḥ proktaḥ saṃnatirdayitā vibhoḥ ।।trinetro atrirumā sākṣādanasūyā smṛtā budhaiḥ ।।kaśyapaḥ kālahā devo devamātā maheśvarī ।।vasiṣṭho manmathārātirdevī sākṣādaruṃdhatī ।।śaṃkaraḥ puruṣāssarve striyassarvā maheśvarī ।।sarve strīpuruṣāstasmāttayoreva vibhūtayaḥ ।।viṣayī bhagavānīśo viṣayaḥ parameśvarī ।।śrāvyaṃ sarvamumārūpaṃ śrotā śūlavarāyudhaḥ ।।praṣṭavyaṃ vastujātaṃ tu dhatte śaṃkaravallabhā ।।praṣṭā sa eva viśvātmā bālacandrāvataṃsakaḥ ।।draṣṭavyaṃ vasturūpaṃ tu bibharti vaktavallabhā ।।draṣṭā viśveśvaro devaḥ śaśikhaṃḍaśikhāmaṇiḥ ।।rasajātaṃ mahādevī devo rasayitā śivaḥ ।।preyajātaṃ ca girijā preyāṃścaiva ।।prāṇaḥ pinākī sarveṣāṃ prāṇināṃ bhagavānprabhuḥ ।।prāṇasthitistu sarveṣāmaṃbikā cāṃburūpiṇī ।।bibharti kṣetratāṃ devī tripurāṃtakavallabhā ।।kṣetrajñatvaṃ tadā dhatte bhagavānaṃtakāṃtakaḥ ।।ahaḥ śūlāyudho devaḥ śūlapāṇipriyā niśā ।।ākāśaḥ śaṃkaro devaḥ pṛthivī śaṃkarapriyā ।।samudro bhagavānīśo velā śailendrakanyakā ।।vṛkṣo vṛṣadhvajo devo latā viśveśvarapriyā ।।puṃlliṃgamakhilaṃ dhatte devānāmagrataḥ prabhuḥ ।।apahṛtya svalīlārthaṃ teṣāṃ jñānaṃ maheśvaraḥ ।।tamapṛcchaṃstato devāḥ ko bhavāniti mohitāḥ ।।so abravīdbhagavānrudro hyahamekaḥ purātanaḥ ।।
āsaṃ prathamamevāhaṃ vartāmi ca surottamāḥ ।।bhaviṣyāmi ca mattonyo vyatirikto na kaścana ।।ahameva jagatsarvaṃ tarpayāmi svatejasā ।।matto adhikaḥ samo nāsti māṃ yo veda sa mucyate ।।ityuktvā bhagavānrudrastatraivāṃtaradhatta sa ।।apaśyaṃtastamīśānaṃ stuvaṃtaścaiva sāmabhiḥ ।। f। vrataṃ pāśupataṃ kṛtvā tvatharvaśirasi sthitam ।।bhasmasaṃchannasarvāṃgā babhūvuramarāstadā ।।atha teṣāṃ prasādārthaṃ paśūnāṃ patirīśvaraḥ ।।sagaṇaścomayā sārdhaṃ sānnidhyamakarotprabhuḥ ।।yaṃ vinidrā jitaśvāsā yogino dagdhakilbiṣāḥ ।।hṛdi paśyaṃti taṃ devaṃ dadṛśurdevapuṃgavāḥ ।।yāmāhuḥ paramāṃ śaktimīśvarecchānuvartinīm ।।tāmapaśyanmaheśasya vāmato vāmalocanām ।।ye vinirdhūtasaṃsārāḥ prāptāḥ śaivaṃ paraṃ padam ।।nityasiddhāśca ye vānyaṃ te ca dṛṣṭā gaṇeśvarāḥ ।।atha taṃ tuṣṭuvurdevā devyā saha maheśvaram ।।stotrairmāheśvarairdivyaiḥ śrotaiḥ paurāṇikairapi ।।devo api devānālokya ghṛṇayā vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ ।।tuṣṭo asmītyāha suprītassvabhāvamadhurāṃ giram ।।atha suprītamanasaṃ praṇipatya vṛṣadhvajam ।।arthamahattamaṃ devāḥ papracchurimamādarāt ।। f। devā ūcuḥ bhagavankena mārgeṇa pūjanīyo asi bhūtale ।।kasyādhikāraḥ pūjāyāṃ vaktumarhasi tattvataḥ ।।tataḥ sasmitamālokya devīṃ devavaroharaḥ ।।svarūpaṃ darśayāmāsa ghoraṃ sūryātmakaṃ param ।।sarvaiśvaryaguṇopetaṃ sarvatejomayaṃ param ।।śaktibhirmūrtibhiścāṃgairgrahairdevaiśca saṃvṛtam ।।aṣṭabāhuṃ caturvaktramardhanārīkamadbhutam ।।dṛṣṭvaivamadbhutākāraṃ devā viṣṇupurogamāḥ ।।buddhvā divākaraṃ devaṃ devīṃ caiva niśākaram ।।pañcabhūtāni śeṣāṇi tanmayaṃ ca carācaram ।।evamuktvā namaścakrustasmai cārghyaṃ pradāya vai ।।siṃdūravarṇāya sumaṇḍalāya suvarṇavarṇābharaṇāya tubhyam ।।padmābhanetrāya sapaṃkajāya brahmendranārāyaṇakāraṇāya ।।suratnapūrṇaṃ sasuvarṇatoyaṃ sukuṃkumādyaṃ sakuśaṃ sapuṣpam ।।pradattamādāya sahemapātraṃ praśastamarghyaṃ bhagavanprasīda ।।namaśśivāya śāṃtāya sagaṇāyādihetave ।। rudrāya viṣṇave tubhyaṃ brahmaṇe sūryamūrtaye ।।yaśśivaṃ maṇḍale saure saṃpūjyaiva samāhitaḥ ।।prātarmadhyāhnasāyāhne pradadyādarghyamuttamam ।।praṇamedvā paṭhedetāñchlokāñchrutimukhānimān ।।na tasya durllabhaṃ kiṃcidbhaktaścenmucyate dṛḍham ।।tasmādabhyarcayenityaṃ śivamādityarūpiṇam ।।dharmakāmārthamuktyarthaṃ manasā karmaṇā girā ।।atha devānsamālokya maṇḍalastho maheśvaraḥ ।।sarvāgamottaraṃ dattvā śāstramaṃtaradhāddharaḥ ।।tatra pūjādhikāro ayaṃ brahmakṣatraviśāmiti ।।jñātvā praṇamya deveśaṃ devā jagmuryathāgatam ।।atha kālena mahatā tasmiñchāstre tirohite ।।bhartāraṃ paripapraccha tadaṃkasthā maheśvarī ।।tayā sa codito devo devyā candravibhūṣaṇaḥ ।।avadatkaramuddhṛtya śāstraṃ sarvāgamottaram ।।pravartitaṃ ca talloke niyogātparameṣṭhinaḥ ।।mayāgastyena guruṇā dadhīcena maharṣiṇā ।।svayamapyavatīryorvyāṃ yugāvarteṣu śūladhṛk ।।svāśritānāṃ vimuktyarthaṃ kurute jñānasaṃtatim ।।ṛbhussatyo bhārgavaśca hyaṃgirāḥ savitā dvijāḥ ।।mṛtyuḥ śatakraturdhīmānvasiṣṭho munipuṃgavaḥ ।।sārasvatastridhāmā ca trivṛto munipuṃgavaḥ ।।śatatejāssvayaṃ dharmo nārāyaṇa iti śrutaḥ ।।svarakṣaścāruṇirdhīmāṃstathā caiva kṛtaṃjayaḥ ।।kṛtaṃjayo bharadvājo gautamaḥ kaviruttamaḥ ।।vācaḥsravā munissākṣāttathā sūkṣmāyaṇiḥ śuciḥ ।।tṛṇabiṃdurmuniḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śaktiḥ śākteya uttaraḥ ।।jātūkarṇyo harissākṣātkṛṣṇadvaipāyano muniḥ ।।vyāsāvatārāñchṛṇvaṃtu kalpayogeśvarānkramāt ।।laiṃge vyāsāvatārā hi dvāparāṃ teṣu suvratāḥ ।।yogācāryāvatārāśca tathā śiṣyeṣu śūlinaḥ ।।tatra tatra vibhoḥ śiṣyāścatvāraḥ syurmahaujasaḥ ।।śiṣyāsteṣāṃ praśiṣyāśca śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।।teṣāṃ saṃbhāvanālloke śaivājñākaraṇādibhiḥ ।।bhāgyavaṃto vimucyaṃte bhaktyā cātyaṃtabhāvitāḥ ।। chapter kṛṣṇa uvāca yugāvarteṣu sarveṣu yogācāryacchalena tu ।।avatārānhi śarvasya śiṣyāṃśca bhagavanvada ।।upamanyuruvāca śvetaḥ sutāro madanaḥ suhotraḥ kaṅka eva ca ।।laugākṣiśca mahāmāyo jaigīṣavyastathaiva ca ।।dadhivāhaśca ṛṣabho munirugro atrireva ca ।। supālako gautamaśca tathā vedaśirā muniḥ ।।gokarṇaśca guhāvāsī śikhaṇḍī cāparaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।jaṭāmālī cāṭṭahāso dāruko lāṃgulī tathā ।।mahākālaśca śūlī ca ḍaṃḍī muṇḍīśa eva ca ।।saviṣṇussomaśarmā ca lakulīśvara eva ca ।।ete vārāha kalpe asminsaptamasyāṃtaro manoḥ ।।aṣṭāviṃśatisaṃkhyātā yogācāryā yugakramāt ।।śiṣyāḥ pratyekameteṣāṃ catvāraśśāṃtacetasaḥ ।।śvetādayaśca ruṣyāṃtāṃstānbravīmi yathākramam ।।śvetaśśvetaśikhaścaiva śvetāśvaḥ śvetalohitaḥ ।।dundubhiśśatarūpaśca ṛcīkaḥ ketumāṃstathā ।।vikośaśca vikeśaśca vipāśaḥ pāśanāśanaḥ ।।sumukho durmukhaścaiva durgamo duratikramaḥ ।।sanatkumārassanakaḥ sanaṃdaśca sanātanaḥ ।।sudhāmā virajāścaiva śaṃkhaścāṃḍaja eva ca ।।sārasvataśca meghaśca meghavāhassuvāhakaḥ ।।kapilaścāsuriḥ pañcaśikho bāṣkala eva ca ।।parāśarāśca gargaśca bhārgavaścāṃgirāstathā ।।balabandhurnirāmitrāḥ ketuśṛṃgastapodhanaḥ ।।laṃbodaraśca laṃbaśca lambātmā laṃbakeśakaḥ ।।sarvajñassamabuddhiśca sādhyasiddhistathaiva ca ।।sudhāmā kaśyapaścaiva vasiṣṭho virajāstathā ।।atrirugro guruśreṣṭhaḥ śravanotha śraviṣṭakaḥ ।।kuṇiśca kuṇibāhuśca kuśarīraḥ kunetrakaḥ ।।kāśyapo hyuśanāścaiva cyavanaśca bṛhaspatiḥ ।।utathyo vāmadevaśca mahākālo mahā anilaḥ ।।vācaḥśravāḥ suvīraśca śyāvakaśca yatīśvaraḥ ।।hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyo lokākṣiḥ kuthumistathā ।।sumanturjaiminiścaiva kubandhaḥ kuśakandharaḥ ।।plakṣo dārbhāyaṇiścaiva ketumāngautamastathā ।।bhallavī madhupiṃgaśca śvetaketustathaiva ca ।।uśijo bṛhadaśvaśca devalaḥ kavireva ca ।।śālihotraḥ suveṣaśca yuvanāśvaḥ śaradvasuḥ ।।akṣapādaḥ kaṇādaśca ulūko vatsa eva ca ।।kulikaścaiva gargaśca mitrako ruṣya eva ca ।।ete śiṣyā maheśasya yogācāryasvarūpiṇaḥ ।।saṃkhyā ca śatameteṣāṃ saha dvādaśasaṃkhyayā ।।sarve pāśupatāḥ siddhā bhasmoddhūlitavigrahāḥ ।।sarvaśāstrārthatattvajñā vedavedāṃgapāragāḥ ।।śivāśramaratāssarve śivajñānaparāyaṇāḥ ।।sarve saṃgavinirmuktāḥ śivaikāsaktacetasaḥ ।।sarvadvaṃdvasahā dhīrāḥ sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ ।।ṛjavo mṛdavaḥ svasthā jitakrodhā jiteṃdriyāḥ ।।rudrākṣamālābharaṇāstripuṃḍrāṃkitamastakāḥ ।।śikhājaṭāssarvajaṭā ajaṭā muṃḍaśīrṣakāḥ ।।phalamūlāśanaprāyāḥ prāṇāyāmaparāyaṇāḥ ।।
śivābhimānasaṃpannāḥ śivadhyānaikatatparāḥ ।।samunmathitasaṃsāraviṣavṛkṣāṃkurodgamāḥ ।।prayātumeva sannaddhāḥ paraṃ śivapuraṃ prati ।।sadeśikānimānmatvā nityaṃ yaśśivamarcayet ।।sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। chapter kṛṣṇa uvāca bhagavansarvayogīṃdra gaṇeśvara munīśvara ।।ṣaḍānanasamaprakhya sarvajñānanidhe guro ।।prāyastvamavatīryorvyāṃ pāśavicchittaye nṛṇām ।।maharṣivapurāsthāya sthito asi parameśvara ।।anyathā hi jagatyasmin devo vā dānavo api vā ।।tvattonyaḥ paramaṃ bhāvaṃ ko jānīyācchivātmakam ।।tasmāttava mukhodgīrṇaṃ sākṣādiva pinākinaḥ ।।śivajñānāmṛtaṃ pītvā na me tṛptamabhūnmanaḥ ।।sākṣātsarvajagatkarturbharturaṃkaṃ samāśritā ।।bhagavankinnu papraccha bhartāraṃ parameśvarī ।।upamanyuruvāca sthāne pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā kṛṣṇa tadvakṣyāmi yathātatham ।।bhavabhaktasya yuktasya tava kalyāṇacetasaḥ ।।mahīdharavare divye maṃdare cārukaṃdare ।।devyā saha mahādevo divyo dhyānagato abhavat ।।tadā devyāḥ priyasakhī susmitāsyā śubhāvatī ।।phullānyatimanojñāni puṣpāṇi samudāharat ।।tataḥ svamaṃkamāropya devīṃ devavarorahaḥ ।।alaṃkṛtya ca taiḥ puṣpairāste hṛṣṭataraḥ svayam ।।athāṃtaḥpuracāriṇyo devyo divyavibhūṣaṇāḥ ।।aṃtaraṃgā gaṇendrāśca sarvalokamaheśvarīm ।।bhartāraṃ paripūrṇaṃ ca sarvalokamaheśvaram ।।cāmarāsaktahastāśca devīṃ devaṃ siṣevire ।।tataḥ priyāḥ kathā vṛttā vinodāya maheśayoḥ ।।trāṇāya ca nṛṇāṃ loke ye śivaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।।tadāvasaramālokya sarvalokamaheśvarī ।।bhartāraṃ paripapraccha sarvalokamaheśvaram ।।devyuvāca kena vaśyo mahādevo martyānāṃ maṃdacetasām ।।ātmatattvādyaśaktānāmātmanāmakṛtātmanām ।।īśvara uvāca na karmaṇā na tapasā na japairnāsanādibhiḥ ।।na jñānena na cānyena vaśyo ahaṃ śraddhayā vinā ।।śraddhā mayyasti cetpuṃsāṃ yena kenāpi hetunā ।।vaśyaḥ spṛśyaśca dṛśyaśca pūjyassaṃbhāṣya eva ca ।।sādhyā tasmānmayi śaddhā māṃ vaśīkartumicchatā ।।śraddhā hetussvadharmasya rakṣaṇaṃ varṇināmiha ।।svavarṇāśramadharmeṇa vartate yastu mānavaḥ ।।tasyaiva bhavati śraddhā mayi nānyasya kasyacit ।। āmnāyasiddhamakhilaṃ dharmamāśramiṇāmiha ।।brahmaṇā kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ mamaivājñāpurassaram ।।sa tu paitāmaho dharmo bahuvittakriyānvitaḥ ।।nātyanta phalabhūyiṣṭhaḥ kleśāyā sasamanvitaḥ ।।tena dharmeṇa mahatāṃ śraddhāṃ prāpya sudurllabhām ।। f।varṇino ye prapadyaṃte māmananyasamāśrayāḥ ।।teṣāṃ sukhena mārgeṇa dharmakāmārthamuktayaḥ ।।varṇāśramasamācāro mayā bhūyaḥ prakalpitaḥ ।।tasminbhaktimatāmeva ।।paramaṃ mama sādharmyaṃ prāpya nirvṛtimāyayuḥ ।। f।tasmāllabdhvāpyalabdhvā vā varṇadharmaṃ mayeritam ।।āśritya mama bhaktaścetsvātmanātmānamuddharet ।।alabdhalābha evaiṣa koṭikoṭiguṇādhikaḥ kāyo na cetaraḥ ।।madarcākarma vijñeyaṃ bāhye yāgādinocyate ।।madarthe dehasaṃśoṣastapaḥ kṛcchrādi no matam ।।japaḥ pañcākṣarābhyāsaḥ praṇavābhyāsa eva ca ।।rudrādhyāyādikābhyāso na vedādhyayanādikam ।।dhyānammadrūpaciṃtādyaṃ nātmādyarthasamādhayaḥ ।।mamāgamārthavijñānaṃ jñānaṃ nānyārthavedanam ।।bāhye vābhyaṃtare vātha yatra syānmanaso ratiḥ ।।prāgvāsanāvaśāddevi tattvaniṣṭhāṃ samācaret ।।bāhyādābhyaṃtaraṃ śreṣṭhaṃ bhavecchataguṇādhikam ।।asaṃkaratvāddoṣāṇāṃ dṛṣṭānāmapyasambhavāt ।।śaucamābhyaṃtaraṃ vidyānna bāhyaṃ śaucamucyate ।।aṃtaḥ śaucavimuktātmā śucirapyaśuciryataḥ ।।bāhyamābhyaṃrtaraṃ caiva bhajanaṃ bhavapūrvakam ।।na bhāvarahitaṃ devi vipralaṃbhaikakāraṇam ।।kṛtakṛtyasya pūtasya mama kiṃ kriyate naraiḥ ।।bahirvābhyaṃtaraṃ vātha mayā bhāvo hi gṛhyate ।।bhāvaikātmā kriyā devi mama dharmassanātanaḥ ।।manasā karmaṇā vācā hyanapekṣya phalaṃ kvacit ।।phaloddeśena deveśi laghurmama samāśrayaḥ ।।phalārthī tadabhāve māṃ parityaktuṃ kṣamo yataḥ ।।
phalārthino api yasyaiva mayi cittaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।।bhāvānurūpaphaladastasyāpyahamanindite ।।phalānapekṣayā yeṣāṃ mano matpravaṇaṃ bhavet ।।prārthayeyuḥ phalaṃ paścādbhaktāste api mama priyāḥ ।।prāk saṃskāravaśādeva ye viciṃtya phalāphale ।।vivaśā māṃ prapadyaṃte mama priyatamā matāḥ ।।mallābhānna paro lābhasteṣāmasti yathātatham ।।mamāpi lābhastallābhānnāparaḥ parameśvari ।।madanugrahatasteṣāṃ bhāvo mayi samarpitaḥ ।।phalaṃ paramanirvāṇaṃ prayacchati balādiva ।।mahātmanāmananyānāṃ mayi saṃnyastacetasām ।।aṣṭadhā lakṣaṇaṃ prāhurmama dharmādhikāriṇām ।।madbhaktajanavātsalyaṃ pūjāyāṃ cānumodanam ।।svayamabhyarcanaṃ caiva madarthe cāṃgaceṣṭitam ।।matkathāśravaṇe bhaktiḥ svaranetrāṃgavikriyāḥ ।।mamānusmaraṇaṃ nityaṃ yaśca māmupajīvati ।।evamaṣṭavidhaṃ cihnaṃ yasmin mlecche api vartate ।।sa viprendro muniḥ śrīmānsa yatissa ca paṃḍitaḥ ।।na me priyaścaturvedī madbhakto śvapaco api yaḥ ।।tasmai deyaṃ tato grāhyaṃ sa ca pūjyo yathā hyaham ।।patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ toyaṃ yo me bhaktyā prayacchati ।।tasyāhaṃ na praṇaśyāmi sa ca me na praṇaśyati ।। chapter īśvara uvāca atha vakṣyāmi deveśi bhaktānāmadhikāriṇām ।।viduṣāṃ dvijamukhyānāṃ varṇadharmasamāsataḥ ।।triḥ snānaṃ cāgnikāryaṃ ca liṃgārcanamanukramam ।।dānamīśrarabhāvaśca dayā sarvatra sarvadā ।।satyaṃ saṃtoṣamāstikyamahiṃsā sarvajaṃtuṣu ।।hrīśraddhādhyayanaṃ yogassadādhyāpanameva ca ।।vyākhyānaṃ brahmacaryaṃ ca śravaṇaṃ ca tapaḥ kṣamā ।।śaucaṃ śikhopavītaṃ ca uṣṇīṣaṃ cottarīyakam ।।niṣiddhāsevanaṃ caiva bhasmarudrākṣadhāraṇam ।।parvaṇyabhyarcanaṃ devi caturdaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।pānaṃ ca brahmakūrcasya māsi māsi yathāvidhi ।।abhyarcanaṃ viśeṣeṇa tenaiva snāpya māṃ priye ।।sarvakriyānna santyāgaḥ śraddhānnasya ca varjanam ।।tathā paryuṣitānnasya yāvakasya viśeṣataḥ ।।madyasya madyagandhasya naivedyasya ca varjanam ।।sāmānyaṃ sarvavarṇānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।kṣamā śāṃtiśca santoṣassatyamasteyameva ca ।।brahmacaryaṃ mama jñānaṃ vairāgyaṃ bhasmasevanam ।। sarvasaṃganivṛttiśca daśaitāni viśeṣataḥ ।।liṃgāni yogināṃ bhūyo divā bhikṣāśanaṃ tathā ।।vānaprasthāśramasthānāṃ samānamidamiṣyate ।।rātrau na bhojanaṃ kāryaṃ sarveṣāṃ brahmacāriṇām ।।adhyāpanaṃ yājanaṃ ca kṣatriyasyāpratigrahaḥ ।।vaiśyasya ca viśeṣeṇa mayā nātra vidhīyate ।।rakṣaṇaṃ sarvavarṇānāṃ yuddhe śatruvadhastathā ।।duṣṭapakṣimṛgāṇāṃ ca duṣṭānāṃ śātanaṃ nṛṇām ।।aviśvāsaśca sarvatra viśvāso mama yogiṣu ।।strīsaṃsargaśca kāleṣu camūrakṣaṇameva ca ।।sadā saṃcāritaiścārairlokavṛttāṃtavedanam ।।sadāstradhāraṇaṃ caiva bhasmakaṃcukadhāraṇam ।।rājñāṃ mamāśramasthānāmeṣa dharmasya saṃgrahaḥ ।।gorakṣaṇaṃ ca vāṇijyaṃ kṛṣirvaiśyasya kathyate ।।śuśrūṣetaravarṇānāṃ dharmaḥ śūdrasya kathyate ।।udyānakaraṇaṃ caiva mama kṣetrasamāśrayaḥ ।।dharmapatnyāstu gamanaṃ gṛhasthasya vidhīyate ।।brahmacaryaṃ vanasthānāṃ yatīnāṃ brahmacāriṇām ।।strīṇāṃ tu bhartṛśuśrūṣā dharmo nānyassanātanaḥ ।।mamārcanaṃ ca kalyāṇi niyogo bharturasti cet ।।yā nārī bhartṛśuśrūṣāṃ vihāya vratatatparā ।।sā nārī narakaṃ yāti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।।atha bhartṛvihīnāyā vakṣye dharmaṃ sanātanam ।।vrataṃ dānaṃ tapaḥ śaucaṃ bhūśayyānaktabhojanam ।।brahmacaryaṃ sadā snānaṃ bhasmanā salilena vā ।।śāṃtirmaunaṃ kṣamā nityaṃ saṃvibhāgo yathāvidhi ।।aṣṭābhyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।ekādaśyāṃ ca vidhivadupavāsomamārcanam ।।iti saṃkṣepataḥ prokto mayāśramaniṣeviṇām ।।brahmakṣatraviśāṃ devi yatīnāṃ brahmacāriṇām ।।tathaiva vānaprasthānāṃ gṛhasthānāṃ ca sundari ।।śūdrāṇāmatha nārīṇāṃ dharma eṣa sanātanaḥ ।।dhyeyastvayāhaṃ deveśi sadā jāpyaḥ ṣaḍakṣaraḥ ।।vedoktamakhilaṃ dharmamiti dharmārthasaṃgrahaḥ ।।atha ye mānavā loke svecchayā dhṛtavigrahāḥ ।।bhāvātiśayasaṃpannāḥ pūrvasaṃskārasaṃyutāḥ ।।viraktā vānuraktā vā stryādīnāṃ viṣayeṣvapi ।। pāpairna te viliṃpaṃte padmapatramivāṃbhasā ।।teṣāṃ mamātmavijñānaṃ viśuddhānāṃ vivekinām ।।matprasādādviśuddhānāṃ duḥkhamāśramarakṣaṇāt ।।nāsti kṛtyamakṛtyaṃ ca samādhirvā parāyaṇam ।।na vidhirna niṣedhaśca teṣāṃ mama yathā tathā ।।
tatheha paripūrṇasya sādhyaṃ mama na vidyate ।।tathaiva kṛtakṛtyānāṃ teṣāmapi na saṃśayaḥ ।।madbhaktānāṃ hitārthāya mānuṣaṃ bhāvamāśritāḥ ।।rudralokātparibhraṣṭāste rudrā nātra saṃśayaḥ pravartaṃte praśastaphalasūcakāḥ ।।mayi bhāvavatāṃ puṃsāṃ prāgadṛṣṭārthagocarāḥ ।।kaṃpasvedo aśrupātaśca kaṇṭhe ca svaravikriyā ।।ānaṃdādyupalabdhiśca bhavedākasmikī muhuḥ ।।sa tairvyastaissamastairvā ।।prathamaṃ karma yajñāderbhaktyā vittānusārataḥ ।।bāhyebhyarcya śivaṃ paścādaṃtaryāgarato bhavet ।।ratirabhyaṃtare yasya na bāhye puṇyagauravāt ।।na karma karaṇīyaṃ hi bahistasya mahātmanāḥ ।।jñānāmṛtena tṛptasya bhaktyā śaivaśivātmanaḥ ।।nāṃtarna ca bahiḥ kṛṣṇa kṛtyamasti kadācana ।।tasmātkrameṇa saṃtyajya bāhyamābhyaṃtaraṃ tathā ।।jñānena jñeyamālokyājñānaṃ cāpi parityajet ।।naikāgraṃ proktaṃ tathā hi śṛṇu sundari ।।rahasyamiti matvaitadgopitaṃ yanmayā purā ।।samaṃtrakaṃ māṃ patitaḥ pūjayedyadi mohitaḥ ।।nārakī syānna sandeho mama pañcākṣaraṃ vinā ।।abbhakṣā vāyubhakṣāśca ye cānye vratakarśitāḥ ।।teṣāmetairvratairnāsti mama lokasamāgamaḥ ।।bhaktyā pañcākṣareṇaiva yo hi māṃ sakṛdarcayet ।।so api gacchenmama sthānaṃ mantrasyāsyaiva gauravāt ।।tasmāttapāṃsi yajñāśca vratāni pañcākṣare sthitāḥ ।।te nāśaṃ naiva saṃprāptā macchaktyā hyanupālitāḥ ।।tatassṛṣṭirabhūnmattaḥ prakṛtyātmaprabhedataḥ ।।guṇamūrtyātmanāṃ caiva tatovāṃtarasaṃhṛtiḥ ।।tadā nārāyaṇaśśete devo māyāmayīṃ chapter īśvara uvāca ājñāhīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ śraddhāhīnaṃ varānane ।।ājñārthaṃ dakṣiṇāhīnaṃ sadā japtaṃ ca niṣphalam ।।ājñāsiddhaṃ kriyāsiddhaṃ śraddhāsiddhaṃ mamātmakam ।।evaṃ ceddakṣiṇāyuktaṃ gaṃdhasragvastrabhūṣaṇaiḥ ।।puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvā ca brāhmaṇānabhipūjya ca ।।samudratīre nadyāṃ ca goṣṭhe devālaye api vā ।।śucau deśe gṛhe vāpi kāle siddhikare tithau ।।nakṣatre śubhayoge ca ।।sarvāvasthāṃ gatasyāpi mayi bhaktimataḥ param ।।sidhyatyeva na saṃdeho nāparasya tu kasyacit ।।na lagnatithinakṣatravārayogādayaḥ priye ।।asyātyaṃtamavekṣyāḥ syurnaiṣa saptassadoditaḥ ।।
na kadācinna kasyāpi ripureṣa mahāmanuḥ ।।susiddho vāpi siddho vā sādhyo vāpi bhaviṣyati ।।siddhena guruṇādiṣṭassusiddha iti kathyate ।।asiddhenāpi vā dattassiddhasādhyastu kevalaḥ ।।asādhitassādhito vā sidhyatvena na saṃśayaḥ ।।śraddhātiśayayuktasya mayi maṃtre tathā gurau ।। tasmānmaṃtrāntarāṃstyaktvā sāpāyān dhikārataḥ ।।āśrametparamāṃ vidyāṃ sākṣātpañcākṣarīṃ budhaḥ ।।maṃtrāntareṣu siddheṣu maṃtra eṣa na sidhyati ।।siddhe tvasminmahāmaṃtre te ca siddhā bhavaṃtyuta ।।yathā deveṣvalabdho asmi labdheṣvapi maheśvari ।।mayi labdhe tu te labdhā maṃtreṣveṣu samo vidhiḥ ।।ye doṣāssarvamaṃtrāṇāṃ na te asminsaṃbhavaṃtyapi ।।asya maṃtrasya jātyādīnanapekṣya pravartanāt ।।tathāpi naiva kṣudreṣu phaleṣu prati yogiṣu ।।sahasā viniyuṃjīta tasmādeṣa mahābalaḥ ।।upamanyuruvāca evaṃ sākṣānmahādevyai mahādevena śūlinā ।।hitā ya jagatāmuktaḥ pañcākṣaravidhiryathā ।।ya idaṃ kīrtayedbhaktyā śṛṇuyādvā samāhitaḥ ।।sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ prayāti paramāṃ gatim ।। chapter śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca bhagavānmaṃtramāhātmyaṃ bhavatā kathitaṃ prabho ।।tatprayogavidhānaṃ ca sākṣācchrutisamaṃ yathā ।।idānīṃ śrotumicchāmi śivasaṃskāramuttamam ।।maṃtrasaṃgrahaṇe kiṃcitsūcitanna tu vismṛtam ।।upamanyuruvāca hanta te kathayiṣyāmi sarvapāpaviśodhanam ।।saṃskāraṃ paramaṃ puṇyaṃ śivena patibhāṣitam ।।samyak kṛtādhikāraḥ syātpūjādiṣu naro yataḥ ।।saṃskāraḥ kathyate tena ṣaḍadhvapariśodhanam ।।dīyate yena vijñānaṃ kṣīyate pāśabaṃdhanam ।।tasmātsaṃskāra evāyaṃ dīkṣetyapi ca kathyate ।।śāṃbhavī caiva śāktī ca māṃtrī caiva śivāgame ।।dīkṣopadiśyate tredhā śivena paramātmanā ।।gurorālokamātreṇa sparśātsaṃbhāṣaṇādapi ।।sadyassaṃjñā bhavejjaṃtoḥ pāśopakṣayakāriṇī ।।sā dīkṣā śāṃbhavī proktā sā punarbhidyate dvidhā ।।tīvrā tīvratarā ceti pāśo pakṣayabhedataḥ ।।yayā syānnirvṛtiḥ sadyassaiva tīvratarā matā ।। tīvrā tu jīvatotyaṃtaṃ puṃsaḥ pāpaviśodhikā ।।śaktī jñānavatī dīkṣā śiṣyadehaṃ praviśya tu ।।guruṇā yogamārgeṇa kriyate jñānacakṣuṣā ।।māṃtrī kriyāvatī dīkṣā kuṃḍamaṃḍalapūrvikā ।।maṃdamaṃdataroddeśātkartavyā guruṇā bahiḥ ।।śaktipātānusāreṇa śiṣyo anugrahamarhati ।।śaivadharmānusārasya tanmūlatvātsamāsataḥ ।।yatra śaktirna patitā tatra śuddhirna jāyate ।।na vidyā na śivācāro na muktirna ca siddhayaḥ ।।tasmālliṃgāni saṃvīkṣya śaktipātasya bhūyasaḥ ।।jñānena kriyayā vātha guruśśiṣyaṃ viśodhayet ।।yo anyathā kurute mohātsa vinaśyati durmatiḥ ।।tasmātsarvaprakāreṇa guruḥ śiṣyaṃ parīkṣayet ।।lakṣaṇaṃ śaktipātasya prabodhānaṃdasaṃbhavaḥ ।।sā yasmātparamā śaktiḥ prabodhānaṃdarūpiṇī ।।ānaṃdabodhayorliṃgamaṃtaḥkaraṇavikriyāḥ ।।yathā syātkaṃparomāṃcasvaranetrāṃgavikriyāḥ ।।śiṣyopi lakṣaṇairebhiḥ kuryādguruparīkṣaṇam ।।tatsaṃparkaiḥ śivārcādau saṃgatairvātha tadgataiḥ ।।śiṣyastu śikṣaṇīyatvādgurorgauravakāraṇāt ।।tasmātsarvaprayatnena gurorgauravamācaret ।।yo gurussa śivaḥ prokto yaḥ śivaḥ sa guruḥ smṛtaḥ ।।gururvā śiva evātha vidyākāreṇa saṃsthitaḥ ।।yathā śivastathā vidyā yathā vidyā tathā guruḥ ।।śivavidyā gurūṇāṃ ca pūjayā sadṛśaṃ phalam ।।sarvadevātmakaścāsau sarvamaṃtramayo guruḥ ।।tasmātsarvaprayatnena yasyājñāṃ śirasā vahet ।।śreyo arthī yadi gurvājñāṃ manasāpi na laṃghayet ।।gurvājñāpālako yasmājjñānasaṃpattimaśnute ।।gacchaṃstiṣṭhansvapanbhuṃjannānyatkarma samācaret ।।samakṣaṃ yadi kurvīta sarvaṃ cānujñayā guroḥ ।।gurorgṛhe samakṣaṃ vā na yatheṣṭāsano bhavet ।।gururdevo yataḥ sākṣāttadgṛhaṃ devamandiram ।।pāpināṃ ca yathā saṃgāttatpāpātpatito bhavet ।।yatheha vahnisaṃparkānmalaṃ tyajati kāṃcanam ।।tathaiva gurusaṃparkātpāpaṃ tyajati mānavaḥ ।।yathā vahnisamīpastho ghṛtakumbho vilīyate ।।tathā pāpaṃ vilīyeta hyācāryasya samīpataḥ ।।yathā prajvalito vahniḥ śuṣkamārdraṃ ca nirdahet ।।tathāyamapi saṃtuṣṭo guruḥ pāpaṃ kṣaṇāddahet ।।manasā karmaṇā vācā guroḥ krodhaṃ na kārayet ।।tasya krodhena dahyaṃte hyāyuḥśrījñānasatkriyāḥ ।।tatkrodhakāriṇo ye syusteṣāṃ yajñāśca niṣphalāḥ ।।
yamaśca niyamāścaiva nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।।gurorviruddhaṃ yadvākyaṃ na vadejjātucinnaraḥ ।।vadedyadi mahāmohādrauravaṃ narakaṃ vrajet ।।manasā karmaṇā vācā gurumuddiśya yatnataḥ ।।śreyorthī cennaro dhīmānna mithyācāramācaret ।।gurorhitaṃ priyaṃ kuryādādiṣṭo vā na vā sadā ।।asamakṣaṃ samakṣaṃ vā tasya kāryaṃ samācaret ।।itthamācāravānbhakto nityamudyuktamānasaḥ ।।gurupriyakaraḥ śiṣyaḥ śaivadharmāṃstato arhati ।।guruścedguṇavānprājñaḥ paramānaṃdabhāsakaḥ ।।tattvavicchivasaṃsakto muktido na tu cāparaḥ ।।saṃvitsaṃjananaṃ tattvaṃ paramānaṃdasaṃbhavam ।।tattattvaṃ viditaṃ yena sa evānaṃdadarśakaḥ ।।na punarnāmamātreṇa saṃvidārahitastu yaḥ ।।anyonyaṃ tārayennaukā kiṃ śilā tārayecchilām ।।etasyā nāmamātreṇa muktirvai nāmamātrikā ।।yaiḥ punarviditaṃ tattvaṃ te muktā mocayantyapi ।।tattvahīne kuto bodhaḥ kuto hyātmaparigrahaḥ ।।parigrahavinirmuktaḥ paśurityabhidhīyate ।।paśubhiḥ preritaścāpi paśutvaṃ nātivartate ।।tasmāttattvavideveha mukto mocaka iṣyate ।।sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaḥ sarvaśāstravidapyayam ।।sarvopāyavidhijño api tattvahīnastu niṣphalaḥ ।।yasyānubhavaparyaṃtā buddhistattve pravartate ।।tasyāvalokanādyaiśca parānando abhijāyate ।।tasmādyasyaiva saṃparkātprabodhānaṃdasaṃbhavaḥ ।।guruṃ tameva vṛṇuyānnāparaṃ matimānnaraḥ ।।sa śiṣyairvinayācāracaturairucito guruḥ ।।yāvadvijñāyate tāvatsevanīyo mumukṣubhiḥ ।।jñāte tasminsthirā bhaktiryāvattattvaṃ samāśrayet ।।na tu tattvaṃ tyajejjātu nopekṣeta kathaṃcana ।।yatrānaṃdaḥ prabodho vā nālpamapyupalabhyate ।।vatsarādapi śiṣyeṇa so anyaṃ gurumupāśrayet ।।gurumanyaṃ prapanne api nāvamanyeta paurvikam ।।gurorbhrātḥṃstathā putrānbodhakānprerakānapi ।। f।tatrādāvupasaṃgamya brāhmaṇaṃ vedapāragam ।।gurumārādhayetprājñaṃ śubhagaṃ priyadarśanam ।।sarvābhayapradātāraṃ karuṇākrāṃtamānasam ।।toṣayettaṃ prayatnena manasā karmaṇā girā ।।tāvadārādhayecchiṣyaḥ prasannosau bhavedyathā ।।tasminprasanne śiṣyasya sadyaḥ pāpakṣayo bhavet ।।tasmāddhanāni ratnāni kṣetrāṇi ca gṛhāṇi ca ।।bhūṣaṇāni ca vāsāṃsi yānaśayyāsanāni ca ।।etāni gurave dadyādbhaktyā vittānusārataḥ ।। vittaśāṭhyaṃ na kurvīta yadīcchetparamāṃ gatim ।।sa eva janako mātā bhartā bandhurdhanaṃ sukham ।।sakhā mitraṃ ca yattasmātsarvaṃ tasmai nivedayet ।।nivedya paścātsvātmānaṃ sānvayaṃ saparigraham ।।samarpya sodakaṃ tasmai nityaṃ tadvaśago bhavet ।।yadā śivāya svātmānaṃ dattavān deśikātmane ।।tadā śaivo bhaveddehī na tato asti punarbhavaḥ ।।guruśca svāśritaṃ śiṣyaṃ varṣamekaṃ parīkṣayet ।।brāhmaṇaṃ kṣatriyaṃ vaiśyaṃ dvivarṣaṃ ca trivarṣakam ।।prāṇadravyapradānādyairādeśaiśca samāsamaiḥ ।।uttamāṃścādhame kṛtvā nīcānuttamakarmaṇi ।।ākruṣṭāstāḍitā vāpi ye viṣādaṃ na yāntyapi ।।te yogyāḥ saṃyatāḥ śuddhāḥ śivasaṃskārakarmaṇi ।।ahiṃsakā dayāvaṃto nityamudyuktacetasaḥ ।।amānino buddhimaṃtastyaktaspardhāḥ priyaṃvadāḥ ।।ṛjavo mṛdavaḥ svacchā vinītāḥ sthiracetasaḥ ।।śaucācārasamāyuktāḥ śivabhaktā dvijātayaḥ ।।evaṃ vṛttasamopetā vāṅmanaḥkāyakarmabhiḥ ।।śodhyā bodhyā yathānyāyamiti śāstreṣu niścayaḥ ।।nādhikāraḥ svato nāryāḥ śivasaṃskārakarmaṇi ।।niyogādbharturastyeva bhaktiyuktā yadīśvare ।।tathaiva bhartṛhīnāyā putrāderabhyanujñayā ।।adhikāro bhavatyeva kanyāyāḥ piturājñayā ।।śūdrāṇāṃ martyajātīnāṃ patitānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। f।tathā saṃkarajātīnāṃ nādhvaśuddhirvidhīyate ।।taipyakṛtrimabhāvaścecchive paramakāraṇe ।।pādodakapradānādyaiḥ kuryuḥ pāpaviśodhanam ।।atrānulomajātā ye yuktā eva dvijātiṣu ।।teṣāmadhvaviśuddhyādi kuryānmātṛkulocitam ।।yā tu kanyā svapitrādyaiśśivadharme niyojitā ।।sā bhaktāya pradātavyā nāparāya virodhine ।।dattā cetpratikūlāya gurvadhīnaścetsaṃskriyā na prabhidyate ।।gurorālokanādeva sparśātsaṃbhāṣaṇādapi ।। yasya saṃjāyate prajñā tasya nāsti parājayaḥ ।।manasā yastu saṃskāraḥ kriyate yogavartmanā ।।sa neha kathito guhyo guruvaktraikagocaraḥ ।।kriyāvānyastu saṃskāraḥ kuṃḍamaṃḍapapūrvakaḥ ।।sa vakṣyate samāsena tasya śakyo na vistaraḥ ।। f। chapter upamanyuruvāca puṇye ahani śucau deśe bahudoṣavivarjite ।।deśikaḥ prathamaṃ kuryātsaṃskāraṃ samayāhvayam ।।parīkṣya bhūmiṃ vidhivadgaṃdhavarṇarasādibhiḥ ।।śilpiśāstroktamārgeṇa maṇḍapaṃ tatra kalpayet ।।kṛtvā vediṃ ca tanmadhye kuṇḍāni parikalpayet ।।aṣṭadikṣu tathā ।।vrīhitaṃdulasiddhārthatilapuṣpakuśāstṛte ।।tatra lakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ śivakuṃbhaṃ prasādhayet ।।sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ vāpi tāmrajaṃ mṛnmayaṃ tu vā ।।gandhapuṣpākṣatākīrṇaṃ kuśadūrvāṃkurācitam ।।sitasūtrāvṛtaṃ kaṃṭhe navavastrayugāvṛtam ।।śuddhāmbupūrṇamutkūrcaṃ sadravyaṃ sapidhānakam ।।bhṛṅgāraṃ vardhanīṃ cāpi śaṃkhaṃ ca cakrameva vā ।।vinā sūtrādikaṃ sarvaṃ padmapatramathāpi vā ।।tasyāsanāraviṃdasya kalpayeduttare dale ।।agrataścaṃdanāṃbhobhirastrarājasya vardhanīm ।।maṇḍalasya tataḥ prācyāṃ maṃtrakuṃbhe ca pūrvavat ।।kṛtvā vidhivadīśasya mahāpūjāṃ samācaret ।।athārṇavasya tīre vā nadyāṃ goṣṭhe api vā girau ।।devāgare gṛhe vāpi deśe anyasminmanohare ।।kṛtvā pūrvoditaṃ sarvaṃ vinā vā maṃḍapādikam ।।maṃḍalaṃ pūrvavatkṛtvā sthaṃḍilaṃ ca vibhāvasoḥ ।।praviśya pūjābhavanaṃ mahāpūjāṃ maheśasya kṛtvā maṇḍalamadhyataḥ ।।śivakuṃbhe tathā bhūyaḥ śivamāvāhya pūjayet ।।paścimābhimukhaṃ dhyātvā yajñarakṣakamīśvaram ।।arcayedastravardhanyāmastramīśasya dakṣiṇe ।।mantrakumbhe ca vinyasya mantraṃ mantraviśāradaḥ ।।kṛtvā mudrādikaṃ sarvaṃ mantrayāgaṃ samācaret ।।tataśśivānale homaṃ kuryāddeśikasattamaḥ ।।pradhānakuṇḍe parito juhuyuścāpare dvijāḥ ।।ācāryātpādamardhaṃ vā homasteṣāṃ vidhīyate ।।pradhānakuṇḍa evātha juhuyāddeśikottamaḥ ।।svādhyāyamapare kuryuḥ stotraṃ maṃgalavācanam ।।japaṃ ca vidhivaccānye śivabhaktiparāyaṇāḥ ।।nṛtyaṃ gītaṃ ca vādyaṃ ca maṃgalānyaparāṇi ca ।।pūjanaṃ ca sadasyānāṃ kṛtvā samyagvidhānataḥ ।।puṇyāhaṃ kārayitvātha punaḥ saṃpūjya śaṃkaram ।।prārthayeddeśiko devaṃ śiṣyānugrahakāmyayā ।।prasīda devadeveśa dehamāviśya māmakam ।।vimocayainaṃ viśveśa ghṛṇayā ca ghṛṇānidhe ।।atha caivaṃ karomīti labdhānujñastu deśikaḥ ।।ānīyopoṣitaṃ śiṣyaṃ haviṣyāśinameva vā ।।ekāśanaṃ vā virataṃ snātaṃ prātaḥkṛtakriyam ।।japaṃtaṃ praṇavaṃ śaṃbhorācarettriḥ pradakṣiṇam ।।tatassuvarṇasaṃmiśraṃ dattvā puṣpāṃjaliṃ prabhoḥ ।।prāṅmukhaścodaṅmukho vā praṇameddaṃḍavatkṣito ।।tatassaṃprokṣya mūlena śirasyastreṇa pūrvavat ।।saṃtāḍya deśikastasya mocayennetrabaṃdhanam ।।sa dṛṣṭvā maṃḍalaṃ bhūyaḥ praṇametsāñjaliḥ prabhum ।।athāsīnaṃ śivācāryo maṃḍalasya tu dakṣiṇe ।।upaveśyātmanassavye śiṣyaṃ darbhāsane guruḥ ।।ārādhya ca mahādevaṃ śivahastaṃ pravinyaset ।।śivatejomayaṃ pāṇiṃ śivamaṃtramudīrayet ।।śivābhimānasaṃpanno nyasecchiṣyasya mastake ।।sarvāṃgālaṃbanaṃ caiva kuryāttenaiva deśikaḥ ।।śiṣyo api praṇamedbhūmau deśikākṛtamīśvaram ।।tataśśivānale devaṃ samabhyarcya yathāvidhi ।।hutāhutitrayaṃ śiṣyamupaveśya yathā purā ।। darbhāgraiḥ saṃspṛśaṃstaṃ ca vidyayātmānamāviśet ।।namaskṛtya mahādevaṃ nāḍīsaṃdhānamācaret ।।śivaśāstroktamārgeṇa kṛtvā prāṇasya nirgamam ।।śiṣyadehapraveśaṃ ca smṛtvā maṃtrāṃstu tarpayet ।।saṃtarpaṇāya mūlasya tenaivāhutayo daśa ।।deyāstisrastathāṃgānāmaṃgaireva yathākramam ।।tataḥ pūrṇāhutiṃ dattvā prāyaścittāya deśikaḥ ।।punardaśāhutīnkuryānmūlamaṃtreṇa maṃtravit ।।punaḥ saṃpūjya deveśaṃ samyagācamya deśikaḥ ।।hutvā caiva yathānyāyaṃ svajātyā vaiśyamuddharet ।।tasyaivaṃ janayetkṣātramuddhāraṃ ca tataḥ punaḥ ।।kṛtvā tathaiva vipratvaṃ janayedasya deśikaḥ ।।rājanyaṃ caivamuddhṛtya kṛtvā vipraṃ punastayoḥ ।।rudratvaṃ janayedvipre rudranāmaiva sādhayet ।।prokṣaṇaṃ tāḍanaṃ kṛtvā śiśossvātmānamātmani ।।śivātmakamanusmṛtya sphuraṃtaṃ visphuliṃgavat ।।nāḍyā yathoktayā vāyuṃ recayenmaṃtrato guruḥ ।।nirgamya praviśennāḍyā śiṣyasya hṛdayaṃ tathā ।।praviśya tasya caitanyaṃ nīlabindunibhaṃ smaran ।।svatejasāpāstamalaṃ jvalaṃtamanuciṃtayet ।।tamādāya tayā nāḍyā maṃtrī saṃhāramudrayā ।।na pūrakeṇa niveśyainamekībhāvārthamātmanaḥ ।।kuṃbhakena tathā nāḍyā recakena yathā purā ।।tasmādādāya śiṣyasya hṛdaye tanniveśayet ।।tamālabhya śivāllabdhaṃ tasmai dattvopavītakam ।।hutvā a ahutitrayaṃ paścāddadyātpūrṇāhutiṃ tataḥ ।।devasya dakṣiṇe śiṣyamupaveśyavarāsane ।।kuśapuṣpaparistīrṇe baddhāṃjalirudaṅmukham ।।svastikāsanamārūḍhaṃ vidhāya prāṅmukhaḥ svayam ।।varāsanasthito maṃtrairmahāmaṃgalaniḥsvanaiḥ ।।samādāya ghaṭaṃ pūrṇaṃ pūrṇameva prasāditam ।।dhyāyamānaḥ śivaṃ śiṣyamābhiṣiṃceta deśikaḥ ।।athāpanudya snānāṃbu paridhāya sitāṃbaram ।।ācāntolaṃkṛtaśśiṣyaḥ prāṃjalirmaṃḍapaṃ vrajet ।।upaveśya yathāpūrvaṃ taṃ gururdarbhaviṣṭare ।।saṃpūjya maṃḍalaṃ devaṃ karanyāsaṃ samācaret ।।tatastu bhasmanā devaṃ dhyāyanmanasi deśikaḥ ।।samālabheta pāṇibhyāṃ śiśuṃ śivamudīrayet ।।atha tasya śivācāryo dahanaplāvanādikam ।।sakalīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā mātṛkānyāsavartmanā ।।tataḥ śivāsanaṃ dhyātvā śiṣyamūrdhni deśikaḥ ।।tatrāvāhya yathānyāyamarcayenmanasā śivam ।।prārthayetprāṃjalirdevaṃ nityamatra sthito bhava ।।iti vijñāpya taṃ śaṃbhostejasā bhāsuraṃ smaret ।। saṃpūjyātha śivaṃ śaivīmājñāṃ prāpya śivātmikām ।।karṇe śiṣyasya śanakaiśśivamantramudīrayet ।।sa tu baddhāṃjaliḥ śrutvā mantraṃ tadgatamānasaḥ ।।śanaistaṃ vyāharecchiṣyaśivācāryasya śāsanāt ।।tataḥ śāktaṃ ca saṃdiśya mantraṃ mantravicakṣaṇaḥ ।।uccārayitvā ca sukhaṃ tasmai maṃgalamādiśet ।।tatassamāsānmantrārthaṃ vācyavācakayogataḥ ।।samadiśyeśvaraṃ rūpaṃ yogamāsanamādiśet ।।atha gurvājñayā śiṣyaḥ śivāgnigurusannidhau ।।bhaktyaivamabhisaṃdhāya dīkṣāvākyamudīrayet ।।varaṃ prāṇaparityāgaśchedanaṃ śiraso api vā ।।na tvanabhyarcya bhuṃjīya bhagavantaṃ trilocanam ।।sa eva dadyānniyato yāvanmohaviparyayaḥ ।।tāvadārādhayeddevaṃ tanniṣṭhastatparāyaṇaḥ ।।tataḥ sa samayo nāma bhaviṣyati śivāśrame ।।labdhādhikāro gurvājñāpālakastadvaśo bhavet ।।ataḥ paraṃ nyastakaro bhasmādāya svahastataḥ ।।dadyācchiṣyāya mūlena rudrākṣaṃ cābhimaṃtritam ।।pratimā vāpi devasya gūḍhadehamathāpi vā ।।pūjāhomajapadhyānasādhanāni ca saṃbhave ।।sopi śiṣyaḥ śivācāryāllabdhāni bahumānataḥ ।।ādadītājñayā tasya deśikasya na cānyathā ।।ācāryādāptamakhilaṃ śirasyādhāya bhaktitaḥ ।।rakṣayetpūjayecchaṃbhuṃ maṭhe vā gṛha evavā ।।ataḥ paraṃ śivācāramādiśedasya deśikaḥ ।।bhaktiśraddhānusāreṇa prajñāyāścānusārataḥ ।।yaduktaṃ yatsamājñātaṃ yaccaivānyatprakīrtitam ।।śivācāryeṇa samaye tatsarvaṃ śirasā vahet ।।śivāgamasya grahaṇaṃ vācanaṃ śravaṇaṃ tathā ।।deśikadeśataḥ kuryānna svecchāto na cānyataḥ ।।iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktaḥ saṃskāraḥ samayāhvayaḥ ।।sākṣācchivapuraprāptau nṛṇāṃ paramasādhanam ।। chapter upamanyuruvāca ataḥ paraṃ samāvekṣya guruḥ śiṣyasya yogyatām ।।ṣaḍadhvaśuddhiṃ kurvīta sarvabaṃdhavimuktaye ।।kalāṃ tattvaṃ ca bhuvanaṃ varṇaṃ padamataḥ param ।।maṃtraśceti samāsena ṣaḍadhvā paripaṭhyate ।।nivṛttyādyāḥ kalāḥ pañca kalādhvā kathyate budhaiḥ ।।vyāptāḥ kalābhiritare tvadhvānaḥ pañca pañcabhiḥ ।।
śivatattvādibhūmyaṃtaṃ tattvādhvā samudāhṛtaḥ ।।ṣaḍviṃśatsaṃkhyayopetaḥ śuddhāśuddhobhayātmakaḥ ।।ādhārādyunmanāṃtaśca bhuvanādhvā prakīrtitaḥ ।।vinā bhedopabhedābhyāṃ ṣaṣṭisaṃkhyāsamanvitaḥ ।।pañcāśadrudrarūpāstu varṇā varṇādhvasaṃjñitāḥ ।।anekabhedasaṃpannaḥ padādhvā samudāhṛtaḥ ।।sarvopamaṃtrairmaṃtrādhvā vyāptaḥ paramavidyayā ।।yathā śivo na tattveṣu gaṇyate tattvanāyakaḥ ।।maṃtrādhvani na gaṇyeta tathāsau maṃtranāyakaḥ ।।kalādhvano vyāpakatvaṃ vyāpyatvaṃ cetarādhvanām ।।na vetti tattvato yasya naivārhatyadhvaśodhanam ।।ṣaḍvidhasyādhvano rūpaṃ na yena viditaṃ bhavet ।।vyāpyavyāpakatā tena jñātumeva na śakyate ।।tasmādadhvasvarūpaṃ ca vyāpyavyāpakatāṃ tathā ।।yathāvadavagamyaiva kuryādadhvaviśodhanam ।।kuṃḍamaṃḍalaparyaṃtaṃ tatra kṛtvā yathā purā ।।dvihastamānaṃ kurvīta prācyāṃ kalaśamaṃḍalam ।।tataḥ snātaśśivācāryaḥ saśiṣyaḥ kṛtanaityakaḥ ।।praviśya maṃḍalaṃ śaṃbhoḥ pūjāṃ pūrvavadācaret ।।tatrāḍhakāvaraissiddhaṃ taṃdulaiḥ pāyasaṃ prabhoḥ ।।ardhaṃ nivedya homārthaṃ śeṣaṃ samupakalpayet ।।purataḥ kalpite vātha maṃḍale varṇimaṃḍite ।।sthāpayetpañcakalaśāndikṣu madhye ca deśikaḥ ।।teṣu brahmāṇi mūlārṇairbindunādasamanvitaiḥ ।।nama ādyairyakarāṃtaiḥ kalpayetkalpavittamaḥ ।।īśānaṃ madhyame kuṃbhe puruṣaṃ purataḥ sthite ।।aghoraṃ dakṣiṇe vāme vāmaṃ sadyaṃ ca paścime ।।rakṣāṃ vidhāya mudrā ca baddhvā kuṃbhābhimaṃtraṇam ।।kṛtvā śivānalairhomaṃ prārabhet yathā purā ।।yadardhaṃ pāyasaṃ pūrvaṃ homārthaṃ parikalpitam ।।hutvā śiṣyasya taccheṣaṃ bhoktuṃ samupakalpayet ।।tarpaṇāṃtaṃ ca maṃtrāṇāṃ kṛtvā karma yathā purā ।।hutvā pūrṇāhutiṃ teṣāṃ tataḥ kuryātpradīpanam ।।oṃkārādanu huṃkāraṃ tato mūlaṃ phaḍaṃtakam ।।svāhāṃtaṃ dīpane prāhuraṃgāni ca yathākramam ।।teṣāmāhutayastisro deyā dīpanakarmaṇi ।।maṃtrairekaikaśastaistu vicintyā dīptamūrtayaḥ ।।triguṇaṃ triguṇī kṛtya dvijakanyākṛtaṃ sitam ।।sūtraṃ sūtreṇa saṃmaṃtrya śikhāgre baṃdhayecchiśoḥ ।।caraṇāṃguṣṭhaparyaṃtamūrdhvakāyasya tiṣṭhataḥ ।।laṃbayitvā tu tatsūtraṃ suṣumṇāṃ tatra yojayet ।।śāṃtayā mudrayādāya mūlamaṃtreṇa maṃtravit ।।hutvāhutitrayaṃ tasyāssānnidhyamupakalpayet ।।hṛdi saṃtāḍya śiṣyasya puṣpakṣepeṇa pūrvavat ।। caitanyaṃ samupādāya dvādaśāṃte nivedya ca ।।sūtraṃ sūtreṇa saṃyojya saṃrakṣyāstreṇa varmaṇā ।।avaguṃṭhyātha tatsūtraṃ śiṣyadehaṃ viciṃtayet ।।mūlatrayamayaṃ pāśaṃ bhogabhogyatvalakṣaṇam ।।viṣayendriyadehādijanakaṃ tasya bhāvayet ।।vyomādibhūtarūpiṇyaḥ śāṃtyatītādayaḥ kalāḥ ।।sūtre svanāmabhiryojyaḥ pūjyaścaiva namoyutaiḥ ।।athavā bījabhūtaistatkṛtvā pūrvoditaṃ kramāt ।।tato malādestattvādau vyāptiṃ samalokayet ।।kalāvyāptiṃ malādau ca hutvā saṃdīpayetkalāḥ ।।śiṣyaṃ śirasi saṃtāḍya sūtraṃ dehe yathākramam ।।śāṃtyatītapade sūtraṃ lāñchayenmaṃtramuccaran ।।evaṃ kṛtvā nivṛttyantaṃ śāṃtyatītamanukramāt ।।hutvāhutitrayaṃ paścānmaṇḍale ca śivaṃ yajet ।।devasya dakṣiṇe śiṣyamupaveśyottarāmukham ।।sadarbhe maṇḍale dadyāddhomaśiṣṭaṃ caruṃ guruḥ ।।śiṣyastadguruṇā dattaṃ satkṛtya śivapūrvakam ।।bhuktvā paścāddvirācamya śivamantramudīrayet ।।apare maṇḍale dadyātpañcagavyaṃ tathā guruḥ ।।so api tacchaktitaḥ pītvā dvirācamya śivaṃ smaret ।।tṛtīye maṇḍale śiṣyamupaveśya yathā purā ।।pradadyāddaṃtapavanaṃ yathāśāstroktalakṣaṇam ।।agreṇa tasya mṛdunā prāṅmukho vāpyudaṅmukhaḥ ।।vācaṃ niyamya cāsīnaśśiṣyo daṃtānviśodhayet ।।prakṣālya daṃtapavanaṃ tyaktvācamya śivaṃ smaret ।।praviśeddeśikādiṣṭaḥ prāṃjaliḥ śivamaṇḍalam ।।tyaktaṃ taddantapavanaṃ dṛśyate guruṇā yadi ।।prāgudakpaścime vāgre śivamanyacchivetaram ।।aśastāśāmukhe tasmingurustaddoṣaśāṃtaye ।।śatamardhaṃ tadardhaṃ vājuhuyānmūlamantrataḥ ।।tataḥ śiṣyaṃ samālabhya japitvā karṇayoḥ śivam ।।devasya dakṣiṇe bhāge taṃ śiṣyamadhivāsayet ।।ahatāstaraṇāstīrṇe sa darbhaśayane śuciḥ ।।maṃtrite antaḥ śivaṃ dhyāyañśayīta prākchirā niśi ।।śikhāyāṃ baddhasūtrasya śikhayā tacchikhāṃ guruḥ ।।ābadhyāhatavastreṇa tamācchādya ca varmaṇā ।।rekhātrayaṃ ca parito bhasmanā tilasarṣapaiḥ ।।kṛtvāstrajaptaistadvāhye digīśānāṃ baliṃ haret ।।śiṣyo api parato anaśnankṛtvaivamadhivāsanam ।।prabudhyotthāya gurave svapnaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ nivedayet ।। chapter upamanyuruvāca tataḥ snānādikaṃ sarvaṃ samāpyācāryacoditaḥ ।।gacchedbaddhāṃjalirdhyāyañchivamaṇḍalapārśvataḥ ।।atha pūjāṃ vinā sarvaṃ kṛtvā pūrvadine yathā ।।netrabaṃdhanaparyaṃtaṃ darśayenmaṇḍalaṃ guruḥ ।।baddhanetreṇa śiṣyeṇa puṣpāvakiraṇe kṛte ।।yatrāpataṃti puṣṇāṇi tasya nāmā asya saṃdiśet ।।taṃ copanīya nirmālyamaṇḍale asminyathā purā ।।pūjayeddevamīśānaṃ juhuyācca śivānale ।।śiṣyeṇa yadi duḥsvapno dṛṣṭastaddoṣaśāṃtaye ।।śatamardhaṃ tadardhaṃ vā juhuyānmūlavidyayā ।।tataḥ sūtraṃ śikhābaddhaṃ laṃbayitvā yathā purā ।।ādhārapūjāprabhṛti yannivṛttikalāśrayam ।।vāgīśvarīpūjanāṃtaṃ kuryāddhomapurassaram ।।atha praṇamya vāgīśaṃ nivṛttervyāpikāṃ satīm ।।maṇḍale devamabhyarcya hutvā caivāhutitrayam ।।prāpayecca śiśoḥ prāptiṃ yugapatsarvayoniṣu ।।sūtradehe atha śiṣyasya tāḍanaprokṣaṇādikam ।।kṛtvātmānaṃ samādāya dvādaśāṃte nivedya ca ।।tato apyādāya mūlena mudrayā śāstradṛṣṭayā ।।yojayenmanasācāryo yugapatsarvayoniṣu ।।devānāṃ jātayaścāṣṭau tiraścāṃ pañca jātayaḥ ।।jātyaikayā ca mānuṣyā yonayaśca caturdaśa ।।tāsu sarvāsu yugapatpraveśāya śiśordhiyā ।।vāgīśānyāṃ yathānyāyaṃ śiṣyātmānaṃ niveśayet ।।garbhaniṣpattaye devaṃ saṃpūjya praṇipatya ca ।।hutvā caiva yathānyāyaṃ niṣpannaṃ tadanusmaret ।।niṣpannasyaivamutpattimanuvṛttiṃ ca karmaṇā ।।ārjavaṃ bhoganiṣpattiḥ kuryātprītiṃ parāṃ tathā ।।niṣkṛtyarthaṃ ca jātyāyurbhogasaṃskārasiddhaye ।।hutvāhutitrayaṃ devaṃ prārthayeddeśikottamaḥ ।।bhoktṛtvaviṣayāsaṃgamalaṃ tatkāyaśodhanam ।।kṛtvaivameva śiṣyasya chiṃdyātpāśatrayaṃ tataḥ ।।nikṛtyā pari baddhasya pāśasyātyaṃtabhedataḥ ।।kṛtvā śiṣyasya caitanyaṃ svacchaṃ manyeta kevalam ।।hutvā pūrṇāhutiṃ vahnau brahmāṇaṃ pūjayettataḥ ।।hutvāhutitrayaṃ tasmai śivājñāmanusaṃdiśet ।।pitāmaha tvayā nāsya yātuḥ śaivaṃ paraṃ padam ।।pratibandho vidhātavyaḥ śaivājñaiṣā garīyasī ।।ityādiśya tamabhyarcya visṛja ca vidhānataḥ ।। samabhyarcya mahādevaṃ juhuyādāhutitrayam ।।nivṛttyā śuddhamuddhṛtya śiṣyātmānaṃ yathā purā ।।niveśyātmani sūtre ca vāgīśaṃ pūjayettataḥ ।।hutvāhutitrayaṃ tasmai praṇamya ca visṛjya tām ।।kuryānnivṛttaḥ saṃdhānaṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ kalayā saha ।।saṃdhāne yugapatpūjāṃ kṛtvā hutvāhutitrayam ।।śiṣyātmanaḥ pratiṣṭhāyāṃ praveśaṃ tvatha bhāvayet ।।tataḥ pratiṣṭhāmāvāhya kṛtvāśeṣaṃ puroditam ।।tadvyāptiṃ vyāpikāṃ tasya vāgīśānīṃ ca bhāvayet ।।pūrṇedumaṃḍalaprakhyāṃ kṛtvā śeṣaṃ ca pūrvavat ।।viṣṇave saṃviśedājñāṃ śivasya paramātmanaḥ ।।viṣṇorvisarjanādyaṃ ca kṛtvā śeṣaṃ ca vidyayā ।।pratiṣṭhāmanusaṃdhāya tasyāṃ cāpi yathā purā ।।kṛtvānucintya tadvyāptiṃ vāgīśāṃ ca yathākramam ।।dīptāgnau pūrṇahomāntaṃ kṛtvā śeṣaṃ ca pūrvavat ।।nīlarudramupasthāpya tasmai pūjādikaṃ tathā ।।kṛtvā karma śivājñāṃ ca dadyātpūrvoktavartmanā ।।tapastamapi codvāsya kṛtvā tasyātha śāṃtaye ।।vidyākalāṃ samādhāya tadvyāptiṃ cāvalokayet ।।svātmano vyāpikāṃ tadvadvāgīśīṃ ca yathā purā ।।bālārkasadṛśākārāṃ bhāsayaṃtīṃ diśo daśa ।।tataḥ śeṣaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ kṛtvā devaṃ maheśvaram ।।āvāhyārādhya hutvāsmai śivājñāṃ manasā diśet ।।maheśvaraṃ tathotsṛjya kṛtvānyāṃ ca kalāmimām ।।śāṃtyatītāṃ kalāṃ nītvā tadvyāptimavalokayet ।।svātmano vyāpikāṃ tadvadvāgīśāṃ ca viciṃtayet ।।nabhomaṃḍalasaṃkāśāṃ pūrṇāṃtaṃ cāpi pūrvavat ।।kṛtvā śeṣavidhānena samabhyarcya sadāśivam ।।tasmai samādiśedājñāṃ śaṃbhoramitakarmaṇaḥ ।।tatrāpi ca yathāpūrvaṃ śivaṃ śirasi pūrvavat ।।samabhyarcya ca vāgīśaṃ praṇamya ca visarjayet ।।tataśśivena samprokṣya śiṣyaṃ śirasi pūrvavat ।।vilayaṃ śāṃtyatītāyāḥ śaktitattve atha ciṃtayet ।।ṣaḍadhvanaḥ pare pāre sarvādhvavyāpinī parām ।।koṭisūryapratīkāśaṃ śaivīṃ śaktiñca cintayet ।।tadagre śiṣyamānīya śuddhasphaṭikanirmalam ।।prakṣālya kartarīṃ paścācchivaśāstroktamārgataḥ ।।kuryāttasya śikhācchedaṃ saha sūtreṇa deśikaḥ ।।tatastāṃ gomaye nyasya śivāgnau juhuyācchikhām ।।vauṣaḍaṃtena mūlena punaḥ prakṣālya kartarīm ।।haste śiṣyasya caitanyaṃ taddehe vinivartayet ।।
tataḥ snātaṃ samācāṃtaṃ kṛtasvastyayanaṃ śiśum ।।praveśya maṃḍalābhyāsaṃ praṇipatya ca daṃḍavat ।।pūjāṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ kriyāvaikalyaśuddhaye ।।vācakenaiva maṃtreṇa juhuyādāhutitrayam ।।upāṃśūccārayogena juhuyādāhutitrayam ।।punassaṃpūjya deveśaṃ mantravaikalyaśuddhaye ।।mānasoccārayogena juhuyādāhutitrayam ।।tatra śaṃbhuṃ samārādhya maṃḍalasthaṃ sahāṃbayā ।।hutvāhutitrayaṃ paścātprārthayetprāṃjalirguruḥ ।। f।bhagavaṃstvatprasādena śuddhirasya ṣaḍadhvanaḥ ।।kṛtā tasmātparaṃ dhāma gamayainaṃ tavāvyayam ।।iti vijñāpya devāya nāḍīsaṃdhānapūrvakam ।।pūrṇāṃtaṃ pūrvavatkṛtvā tato bhūtāni śodhayet ।।sthirāsthire tataḥ śuddhyai śītoṣṇe ca tataḥ pade ।।dhyāyedvyāptyaikatākāre bhūtaśodhanakarmaṇi ।।bhūtānāṃ graṃthivicchedaṃ kṛtvā tyaktvā sahādhipaiḥ ।।bhūtāni sthitayogena yo japetparame śive ।।viśodhyāsya tanuṃ dagdhvā plāvayitvā sudhākaṇaiḥ ।।sthāpyātmānaṃ tataḥ kuryādviśuddhādhvamayaṃ vapuḥ ।।tatrādau śāntyatītāṃ tu vyāpikāṃ svādhvanaḥ kalām ।।śuddhāmeva śiśormūrdhni nyasecchāntimukhe tathā ।।vidyāṃ galādinābhyaṃtaṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ tadadhaḥ kramāt ।।jānvaṃtaṃ tadadho nyasyennivṛttiṃ cānuciṃtayet ।।svabījaissūtramaṃtraṃ ca nyasyāṃ gaistaṃ śivātmakam ।।buddhvā taṃ hṛdayāṃbhoje devamāvāhya pūjayet ।।āśāsya nityasāṃnidhyaṃ śivasvātmyaṃ śiśau guruḥ ।।śivatejomayasyāsya śiśorāpādayedguṇān ।।aṇimādīnprasīdeti pradadyādāhutitrayam ।।tathaiva tu guṇāneva punarasyopapādayet ।।sarvajñātāṃ tathā tṛptiṃ bodhaṃ cādyantavarjitam ।।aluptaśaktiṃ svātantryamanaṃtāṃ śaktimeva ca ।।tato devamanujñāpya sadyādikalaśaistu tam ।।abhiṣiṃceta deveśaṃ dhyāyanhṛdi yathākramam ।।athopaveśya taṃ śiṣyaṃ śivamabhyarcya pūrvavat ।।labdhānujñaḥ śivācchaivīṃ vidyāmasmai samādiśet ।।oṃkārapūrvikāṃ tatra saṃpuṭāntu namo aṃtagām ।।śivaśaktiyutāñcaiva śaktividyāṃ ca tādṛśīm ।।ṛṣiṃ chandaśca devaṃ ca śivatāṃ śivayostathā ।।pūjāṃ sāvaraṇāṃ śambhorāsanāni ca sandiśet ।।punaḥ saṃpūjya deveśaṃ yanmayā samanuṣṭhitam ।।sukṛtaṃ kuru tatsarvamiti vijñāpayecchivam ।।sahaśiṣyo gururdevaṃ daṇḍavatkṣitimaṃḍale ।।praṇamyodvāsayettasmānmaṃḍalātpāvakādapi ।। tataḥ sadasikāḥ sarve pūjyāḥ pūjārhakāḥ kramāt ।।sevyā vittānusāreṇa sadasyāśca sahartvijaḥ ।।vittaśāṭhyaṃ na kurvīta yadīcchecchivamātmanaḥ ।। chapter upamanyuruvāca ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi sādhakaṃ nāma nāmataḥ ।।saṃskāramantramāhātmyaṃ kathane sūcitaṃ mayā ।।saṃpūjya maṃḍale devaṃ sthāpya kumbhe ca pūrvavat ।।hutvā śiṣyamanuṣṇīṣaṃ prāpayedbhuvi maṃḍale ।।pūrvāṃtaṃ pūrvavatkṛtvā hutvāhutiśataṃ tathā ।।saṃtarpya mūlamantreṇa kalaśairdeśikottamaḥ ।।sandīpya ca yathāpūrvaṃ kṛtvā pūrvoditaṃ kramāt ।।abhiṣicya yathāpūrvaṃ pradadyānmantramuttamam ।।tatra vidyopadeśāṃtaṃ kṛtvā vistaraśaḥ kramāt ।।puṣpāmbunā śiśoḥ pāṇau vidyāṃ śaivīṃ samarpayet ।।tavaihikāmuṣmikayoḥ sarvasiddhiphalapradaḥ ।।bhavatyeva mahāmantraḥ prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ ।।ityutvā devamabhyarcya labdhānujñaḥ śivādguruḥ ।।sādhanaṃ śivayogaṃ ca sādhakāya samādiśet ।।tacchrutvā gurusaṃdeśaṃ kramaśo maṃtrasādhakaḥ ।।purato viniyogasya mantrasādhanamācaret ।।sādhanaṃ mūlamantrasya puraścaraṇamucyate ।।purataścaraṇīyatvādviniyogākhyakarmaṇaḥ ।।nātyantaṃ karaṇīyantu mumukṣormantrasādhanam ।।kṛtantu tadihānyatra tāsyāpi śubhadaṃ bhavet ।।śubhe ahani śubhe deśe kāle vā doṣavarjite ।।śukladantanakhaḥ snātaḥ kṛtapūrvāhṇikakriyaḥ ।।alaṃkṛtya yathā labdhairgaṃdhamālyavibhūṣaṇaiḥ ।।soṣṇīṣaḥ sottarāsaṃgaḥ sarvaśuklasamāhitaḥ ।।devālaye gṛhe anyasmindeśe vā sumanohare ।।sukhenābhyastapūrveṇa tvāsanena kṛtāsanaḥ ।।tanuṃ kṛtvātmanaḥ śaivīṃ śivaśāstroktavartmanā ।।saṃpūjya devadeveśaṃ nakulīśvaramīśvaram ।।nivedya pāyasaṃ tasmai samapyārādhanaṃ kramāt ।।praṇipatya ca taṃ devaṃ prāptānujñaśca tanmukhāt ।।koṭivāraṃ tadardhaṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā japecchivam ।।lakṣaviṃśatikaṃ vāpi daśalakṣamathāpi vā ।।tataśca pāyasākṣāralavaṇaikamitāśanaḥ ।।ahiṃsakaḥ kṣamī śāṃto dāṃtaścaiva sadā bhavet ।।alābhe pāyasasyāśnanphalamūlādikāni vā ।।vihitāni śivenaiva viśiṣṭānyuttarottaram ।।caruṃ bhakṣyamatho saktukaṇānyāvakameva ca ।। śākaṃ payo dadhi ghṛtaṃ mūlaṃ phalamathodakam ।।abhimaṃtrya ca mantreṇa bhakṣyabhojyādikāni ca ।।sādhane asminviśeṣeṇa nityaṃ bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ ।।mantrāṣṭaśatapūtena jalena śucinā vratī ।।snāyānnadīnadotthena prokṣayedvātha śaktitaḥ ।।tarpayecca tathā nityaṃ juhuyācca śivānale ।।saptabhiḥ pañcabhirdravyaistribhirvātha ghṛtena vā ।।itthaṃ bhaktyā śivaṃ śaivo yaḥ sādhayati sādhakaḥ ।।tasyehāmutra duṣprāpaṃ na kiṃcidapi vidyate ।।athavā aharaharmaṃtraṃ japedekāgramānasaḥ ।।anaśnanneva sāhasraṃ vinā mantrasya sādhanam ।।na tasya durlabhaṃ kiṃcinna tasyāstyaśubhaṃ kvacit ।।iha vidyāṃ śriyaṃ saukhyaṃ labdhvā muktiṃ ca viṃdati ।।sādhane viniyoge ca nitye naimittike tathā ।।japejjalairbhasmanā ca snātvā mantreṇa ca kramāt ।।śucirbaddhaśikhassūtrī sapavitrakarastathā ।।dhṛtatripuṃḍrarudrākṣo vidyāṃ pañcākṣarīṃ japet ।।
chapter upamanyuruvāca athaivaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ śiṣyaṃ kṛtapāśupatavratam ।।ācāryatve abhiṣiṃceta tadyogatvena cānyathā ।।maṇḍalaṃ pūrvavatkṛttvā saṃpūjya parameśvaram ।।sthāpayatpañcakalaśāndikṣu madhye ca pūrvavat ।।nivṛttiṃ purato nyasya pratiṣṭhāṃ paścime ghaṭe ।।vidyāṃ dakṣiṇataḥ śāṃtimuttare madhyataḥ parām ।।kṛtvā rakṣādikaṃ tatra baddhvā mudrāṃ ca dhainavīm ।।abhimaṃtrya ghaṭānhutvā pūrṇāṃtaṃ ca yathā purā ।।praveśya maṃḍale śiṣyamanuṣṇīṣaṃ ca deśikaḥ ।।tarpaṇādyaṃ tu maṃtrāṇāṃ kuryātpūrvāvasānakam ।।tataḥ saṃpūjya deveśamanujñāpya ca pūrvavat ।।abhiṣekāya taṃ śiṣyamāsanaṃ tvadhirohayet ।।sakalīkṛtya taṃ paścātkalāpañcakarūpiṇam ।।nyastamaṃtratanuṃ baddhvā śivaṃ śiṣyaṃ samarpayet ।।tato nivṛttikuṃbhādighaṭānuddhṛtya vai kramāt ।।madhyamāntācchivenaiva śiṣyaṃ tamabhiṣecayat ।।śivahastaṃ samarpyātha śiśoḥ śirasi deśikaḥ ।।śivabhāvasamāpannaḥ śivācāryaṃ tamādiśet ।।athālaṃkṛtya taṃ devamārādhya śivamaṇḍale ।।śatamaṣṭottaraṃ hutvā dadyātpūrṇāhutiṃ tataḥ ।।punaḥ sampūjya deveśaṃ praṇamya bhuvi daṃḍavat ।।śirasyaṃjalimādhāya śivaṃ vijñāpayedguruḥ ।।bhagavaṃstvatprasādena deśikoyaṃ mayā kṛtaḥ ।।anugṛhya tvayā deva divyājñāsmai pradīyatām ।।evaṃ vijñāpya śiṣyeṇa saha bhūyaḥ praṇamya ca ।। śivaṃ śivāgamaṃ divyaṃ pūjayecchivavadguruḥ ।।punaḥ śivamanujñāpya śivajñānasya pustakam ।।ubhābhyāmatha pāṇibhyāṃ dadyācchiṣyāya deśikaḥ ।।sa tāmmūrdhni samādhāya vidyāṃ vidyāsanopari ।।adhiropya yathānyāyamabhivaṃdya samarcayet ।।atha tasmai gururdadyādrājopakaraṇānyapi ।।ācāryapadavīṃ prāpto rājyaṃ cāpi yato arhati ।।athānuśāsanaṃ kuryātpūrvairācaritaṃ yathā ।।yathā ca śivaśāstroktaṃ yathā lokeṣu pūjyate ।।śiṣyānparikṣya yatnena śivaśāstroktalakṣaṇaiḥ ।।saṃskṛtya ca śivajñānaṃ tebhyo dadyācca deśikaḥ ।।evaṃ sarvamanāyāsaṃ śaucaṃ kṣāṃtiṃ dayāṃ tathā ।।aspṛhāmapyasūyāṃ ca yatnena ca vibhāvayet ।।itthamādiśya taṃ śiṣyaṃ śivamudvāsya maṃḍalāt ।।śivakuṃbhānalādīṃśca sadasyānapi pūjayet ।।yugapadvātha saṃskārānkurvīta sagaṇo guruḥ ।।tatra yatra dvayaṃ likheduddhūlanaṃ vinā ।।rudrākṣāndhārayedmūrdhni kaṃṭhe śrote kare tathā ।।suvarṇavarṇamacchinnaṃ śubhaṃ nānyairdhṛtaṃ śubham ।।viprādīnāṃ kramācchreṣṭhaṃ pītaṃ raktamathāsitam ।।tadalābhe yathālābhaṃ pūjayetparameśvaram ।।prajāsthānaṃ samāsādya baddhvā ruciramāsanam ।।dhyāyeddevaṃ ca devīṃ ca prāṅmukho vāpyudaṅmukhaḥ ।।śvetādīnnakulīśāṃtāṃstacchiṣyānpraṇamedgurum ।।punardevaṃ śivaṃ natvā tato ।।aṃguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhāṃtaṃ sthitinyāsa udāhṛtaḥ ।।dakṣiṇāṃguṣṭhamārabhya vāmāṃguṣṭhāntameva ca ।।utpattinyāsa ākhyāto viparītastu saṃhṛtiḥ ।।sabiṃdukānnakārādīnvarṇānnyasyedanukramāt ।।aṃgulīṣu śivaṃ ।।punaścāmṛtavarṣeṇa siṃcedvidyāmayaṃ vapuḥ ।।tataḥ kuryātkaranyāsaṃ karaśodhanapūrvakam ।।dehanyāsaṃ tataḥ paścānmahatyā mudrayā caret ।।aṃganyāsaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā śivoktena tu vartmanā ।।varṇanyāsaṃ tālunyaḥ prayojyo yathākramam ।।kavargaṃ dakṣiṇe haste nyasetpañcasu saṃdhiṣu ।।cavargaṃ ca tathā vāmahastasaṃdhiṣu vinyaset ।।ṭavargaṃ ca tavargaṃ ca pādayorubhayorapi ।।paphau tu pārśvayoḥ pṛṣṭhe karmayajñaratāḥ kecittapoyajñaratāḥ pare ।।japayajñaratāścānye dhyānayajñaratāstathā ।।jñānayajñaratāścānye viśiṣṭāścottarottaram ।।kramayajño dvidhā proktaḥ kāmākāmavibhedataḥ ।।kāmānkāmī tato jāyate bhuvi mānavaḥ ।।japadhyānarato martyastadvaiśiṣṭyavaśādiha ।।jñānaṃ labdhvācirādeva śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt ।।tasmānmukto śivājñaptaḥ karmayajño api dehinām ।।akāmaḥ kāmasaṃyukto bandhāyaiva bhaviṣyati ।।tasmātpañcasu yajñeṣu dhyānajñānaparo bhavet ।।dhyānaṃ jñānaṃ ca yasyāsti tīrṇastena bhavārṇavaḥ ।।hiṃsādidoṣanirmukto viśuddhaścittasādhanaḥ ।।dhyānayajñaḥ parastasmādapavargaphalapradaḥ ।।bahiḥ karmakarā yadvannātīva phalabhāginaḥ ।।dṛṣṭvā narendrabhavane tadvadatrāpi karmiṇaḥ ।।dhyānināṃ hi vapuḥ sūkṣmaṃ bhavetpratyakṣamaiśvaram ।।yatheha karmaṇāṃ sthūlaṃ mṛtkāṣṭhādyaiḥ prakalpitam ।।dhyānayajñaratāstasmāddevānpāṣāṇamṛṇmayān ।।nātyaṃtaṃ pratipadyaṃte śivayāthātmyavedanāt ।।ātmasthaṃ yaḥ śivaṃ tyaktvā bahirabhyarcayennaraḥ ।।hastasthaṃ phalamutsṛjya lihetkūrparamātmanaḥ param ।।tathaivācamanīyasya pātraṃ ceti catuṣṭayam ।।prakṣālya prokṣya vīkṣyātha kṣipetteṣu jalaṃ śivam ।।puṇyadravyāṇi sarvāṇi yathālābhaṃ vinikṣipet ।।ratnāni rajataṃ hema gandhapuṣpākṣatādayaḥ kāryā vicāraṇā ।।arudro vā sarudro vā sūktena śivamarcayet ।।yaḥ sakṛtpatito vāpimūḍho vā mucyate naraḥ ।। ṣaḍakṣareṇa vā devaṃ sūktamantreṇa pūjayet ।।śivabhakto jitakrodho hyalabdho labdha eva ca ।।alabdhāllabdha evātra viśiṣṭo nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।sa brahmāṃgena vā tena sahaṃsena vimucyate ।।tasmānnityaṃ śivaṃ bhaktyā sūktamantreṇa pūjayet ।।ekakālaṃ dvikālaṃ vā trikālaṃ nityameva vā ।।ye arcayaṃti mahādevaṃ vijñeyāste maheśvarāḥ ।।jñānenātmasahāyena nārcito bhagavāñchivaḥ ।।sa ciraṃ saṃsaratyasminsaṃsāre duḥkhasāgare ।।durllabhaṃ prāpya mānuṣyaṃ mūḍho nārcayate śivam ।।niṣphalaṃ tasya tajjanma mokṣāya na bhavedyataḥ ।।durllabhaṃ prāpya mānuṣyaṃ ye arcayanti pinākinam ।।teṣāṃ hi saphalaṃ janma kṛtārthāste narottamāḥ ।।bhavabhaktiparā ye ca bhavapraṇatacetasaḥ ।।bhavasaṃsmaraṇodyuktā na te duḥkhasya bhāginaḥ ।।bhavanāni manojñāni vibhramābharaṇāḥ striyaḥ ।।dhanaṃ cātṛptiparyantaṃ śivapūjāvidheḥ phalam ।।ye vāñchanti mahābhogānrājyaṃ ca tridaśālaye ।।te vāñchanti sadākālaṃ harasya caraṇāmbujam ।।saubhāgyaṃ kāntimadrūpaṃ sattvaṃ tyāgārdrabhāvatā ।।śauryaṃ vai jagati khyātiśśivamarcayato bhavet ।।tasmātsarvaṃ parityajya śivaikāhitamānasaḥ ।।śivapūjāvidhiṃ kuryādyadīcchecchivamātmanaḥ ।।tvaritaṃ jīvitaṃ yāti tvaritaṃ yāti yauvanam ।।tvaritaṃ vyādhirabhyeti tasmātpūjyaḥ pinākadhṛk ।।yāvannāyāti maraṇaṃ yāvannākramate jarā ।।yāvannendriyavaikalyaṃ tāvatpūjaya śaṃkaram ।।na śivārcanatulyo asti dharmo anyo bhuvanatraye ।।iti vijñāya yatnena pūjanīyassadāśivaḥ ।।dvārayāgaṃ javanikāṃ parivārabalikriyām ।।nityotsavaṃ ca kurvīta prasāde yadi pūjayet ।।havirnivedanādūrdhvaṃ svayaṃ cānucaro api vā ।।prasādaparivārebhyo baliṃ dadyādyathākramam ।।nirgamya saha vāditraistadāśābhimukhaḥ sthitaḥ ।।puṣpaṃ dhūpaṃ ca dīpañca dadyādannaṃ jalaiḥ saha ।।tato dadyānmahāpīṭhe tiṣṭhanbalimudaṅmukhaḥ ।।tato niveditaṃ deve yattadannādikaṃ purā ।।tatsarvaṃ sāvaśeṣaṃ vā caṇḍāya vinivedayet ।।hutvā ca vidhivatpaścātpūjāśeṣaṃ samāpayet ।।kṛtvā prayogaṃ vidhivadyāvanmantraṃ japaṃ tataḥ ।।nityotsavaṃ prakurvīta yathoktaṃ śivaśāsane ।। vipule taijase pātre raktapadmopaśobhite ।।astraṃ pāśupataṃ divyaṃ tatrāvāhya samarcayet ।।śivasyāropyaḥ tatpātraṃ dvijasyālaṃkṛtasya ca ।।nyastāstravapuṣā tena dīptayaṣṭidharasya ca ।।prāsādaparivārebhyo bahirmaṃgalaniḥsvanaiḥ ।।nṛtyageyādibhiścaiva saha dīpadhvajādibhiḥ ।।pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kṛtvā na drutaṃ cāvilambitam ।।mahāpīṭhaṃ samāvṛtya triḥpradakṣiṇayogataḥ ।।punaḥ praviṣṭo dvārastho yajamānaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ ।।ādāyābhyaṃtaraṃ nītvā hyastramudvāsayet tataḥ ।। f।pradakṣiṇādikaṃ kṛtvā yathāpūrvoditaṃ kramāt ।।ādāya cāṣṭapuṣpāṇi pūjāmatha samāpayet ।। chapter upamanyuruvāca athāgnikāryaṃ vakṣyāmi kuṇḍe vā sthaṃḍile api vā ।।vedyāṃ vā hyāyase pātre mṛnmaye vā nave śubhe ।।ādhāyāgniṃ vidhānena saṃskṛtya ca tataḥ param ।।tatrārādhya mahādevaṃ homakarma samācaret ।।kuṇḍaṃ dvihastamānaṃ vā hastamātramathāpi vā ।।vṛttaṃ vā caturasraṃ vā kuryādvediṃ ca maṇḍalam ।।kuṇḍaṃ vistāravannimnaṃ tanmadhye aṣṭadalāmbujam ।।caturaṃgulamutsedhaṃ tasya dvyaṃgulameva vā ।।vitastidviguṇonnatyā nābhimantaḥ pracakṣate ।।madhyaṃ ca madhyamāṃgulyā madhyamottamaparvaṇoḥ ।।aṃgulaiḥ kathyate sadbhiścaturviṃśatibhiḥ karaḥ ।।mekhalānāṃ trayaṃ vāpi dvayamekamathāpi vā ।।yathāśobhaṃ prakurvīta ślakṣṇamiṣṭaṃ mṛdā sthiram ।।aśvatthapatravadyoniṃ gajādhāravadeva vā ।।mekhalāmadhyataḥ kuryātpaścime dakṣiṇe api vā ।।śobhanāmagnitaḥ kiṃcinnimnāmunmīlikāṃ śanaiḥ ।।agreṇa kuṇḍābhimukhīṃ kiṃcidutsṛjya mekhalām ।।notsedhaniyamo vedyāḥ sā mārdī vātha saikatī ।।maṃḍalaṃ gośakṛttoyairmānaṃ pātrasya noditam ।।kuṇḍaṃ ca mṛnmayaṃ vedimālipedgomayāṃbunā ।।prakṣālya tāpayetpātraṃ prokṣayedanyadaṃbhasā ।।svasūtroktaprakāreṇa kuṇḍādau villikhettataḥ ।।saṃprokṣya kalpayeddarbhaiḥ puṣpairvā vahniviṣṭaram ।।arcanārthaṃ ca homārthaṃ sarvadravyāṇi sādhayet ।।prakṣālyakṣālanīyāni prokṣaṇyā prokṣya śodhayet ।।maṇijaṃ kāṣṭhajaṃ vātha śrotriyāgārasambhavam ।।
anyaṃ vābhyarhitaṃ vahniṃ tataḥ sādhāramānayet ।।triḥ pradakṣiṇamāvṛtya kuṇḍāderupari kramāt ।।vahnibījaṃ samuccārya tvādadhītāgnimāsane ।।yonimārgeṇa vā tadvadātmanaḥ saṃmukhena vā ।।niyogaḥ pradeśa sarvaṃ kuṃḍaṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ ।।svanābhyaṃtaḥsthitaṃ vahniṃ tadraṃdhrādvisphuliṃgavad ।।nirgamya pāvake bahye līnaṃ biṃbākṛti smaret ।।ājyasaṃskāraparyaṃtamanvādhānapurassaram ।।svasūtroktakramātkuryānmūlamantreṇa mantravit ।।śivamūrtiṃ samabhyarcya tato dakṣiṇapārśvataḥ ।।nyasya mantraṃ ghṛte mudrāṃ darśayeddhenusaṃjñitām ।।sruksruvau taijasau grāhyau na kāṃsyāyasasaisakau ।।yajñadārumayau vāpi smārtau vā śilpasammatau ।।parṇe vā brahmavṛkṣāderacchidre madhya utthite ।।saṃsṛjya darbhaistau vahnau saṃtāpya prokṣayetpunaḥ ।।pārārṣarcyasvasūtroktakrameṇa śivapūrvakaiḥ ।।juhuyādaṣṭabhirbījairagnisaṃskārasiddhaye ।।bhruṃstuṃbruśruṃ krameṇaiva puṃḍraṃdramityataḥ param ।।bījāni sapta saptānāṃ jihvānāmanupūrvaśaḥ ।।triśikhā madhyamā jihvā bahurūpasamāhvayā ।।raktāgneyī nairṛtī ca kṛṣṇānyā suprabhā matā ।।atiriktā marujjihvā svanāmānuguṇaprabhā ।।svabijānantaraṃ vācyā svāhāṃtañca yathākramam ।।jihvāmaṃtraistu tairhutvājyaṃ jihvāstvekaikaśa kramāt ।।raṃ vahnayeti svāheti madhye hutvāhutitrayam ।।sarpiṣā vā samidbhirvā pariṣecanamācaret ।।evaṃ kṛte śivāgniḥ syātsmarettatra śivāsanam ।।tatrāvāhya yajeddevamardhanārīśvaraṃ śivam ।।dīpāntaṃ pariṣicyātha samiddhomaṃ samācaret ।। f।tāḥ pālāśyaḥ parā vāpi yājñiyā dvādaśāṃgulāḥ ।।avakrā na svayaṃ śuṣkāssatvaco nirvraṇāḥ samāḥ ।।daśāṃgulā vā vihitāḥ kaniṣṭhāṃgulisaṃmitāḥ ।।prādeśamātrā vālābhe hotavyāḥ sakalā api ।।dūrvāpatrasamākārāṃ caturaṃgulamāyatām ।।dadyādājyāhutiṃ paścādannamakṣapramāṇataḥ ।।lājāṃstathā sarṣapāṃśca yavāṃścaiva tilāṃstathā ।।sarpiṣāktāni bhakṣyāṇi lehyacoṣyāṇi sambhave ।।daśaivāhutayastatra pañca vā tritayaṃ ca vā ।।hotavyāḥ śaktito dadyādekamevātha vāhutim ।।śruveṇājyaṃ samityādyāsrucāśeṣātkareṇa vā ।।tatra divyena hotavyaṃ tīrthenārṣeṇa vā tathā ।।dravyeṇaikena vā alābhe juhuyācchraddhayā punaḥ ।।prāyaścittāya juhuyānmaṃtrayitvāhutitrayam ।। tato homaviśiṣṭena ghṛtenāpūrya vai srucam ।।nidhāya puṣpaṃ tasyāgre śruveṇādhomukhena tām ।।sadarbhena samācchādya mūlenāṃjalinotthitaḥ ।।vauṣaḍaṃtena juhuyāddhārāṃ tu yavasaṃmitām ।।itthaṃ pūrṇāhutiṃ kṛtvā pariṣiṃcecca pūrvavat ।।tata udvāsya deveśaṃ gopayettu hutāśanam ।।tamapyudvāsya vā nābhau yajetsaṃdhāya nityaśaḥ ।।athavā vahnimānīya śivaśāstroktavartmanā ।।vāgīśīgarbhasaṃbhūtaṃ saṃskṛtya vidhivadyajet ।।anvādhānaṃ punaḥ kṛtvā paridhīn paridhāya ca ।।pātrāṇi dvandvarūpeṇa nikṣipyeṣṭvā śivaṃ tataḥ ।।saṃśodhya prokṣaṇīpātraṃ prokṣyatāni tadaṃbhasā ।।praṇītāpātramaiśānyāṃ vinyasyā pūritaṃ jalaiḥ ।।ājyasaṃskāraparyaṃtaṃ kṛtvā saṃśodhya sraksruvau ।।garbhādhānaṃ puṃsavanaṃ sīmantonnayanaṃ tataḥ ।।kṛtvā pṛthakpṛthagghutvā jātamagniṃ vicintayet ।।tripādaṃ saptahastaṃ ca catuḥśṛṃgaṃ dviśīrṣakam ।।madhupiṃgaṃ trinayanaṃ sakapardenduśekharam ।।raktaṃ raktāmbarālepaṃ mālyabhūṣanabhūṣitam ।।sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannaṃ sopavītaṃ trimekhalam ।।śaktimantaṃ sruksruvau ca dadhānaṃ dakṣiṇe kare ।।tomaraṃ tālavṛṃtaṃ ca ghṛtapātraṃ tathetaraiḥ ।।jātaṃ dhyātvaivamākāraṃ jātakarma samācaret ।।nālāpanayanaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ saṃśodhya sūtakam ।।śivāgnirucināmāsya kṛtvāhutipurassaram ।।pitrorvisarjanaṃ kṛtvā caulopanayanādikam ।।aptoryāmāvasānāntaṃ kṛtvā saṃskāramasya tu ।।ājyadhārādihomaṃ ca kṛtvā sviṣṭakṛtaṃ tataḥ ।।ramityanena bījena pariṣiṃcettataḥ param ।।brahmaviṣṇuśiveśānāṃ lokeśānāṃ tathaiva ca ।।tadastrāṇāṃ ca paritaḥ kṛtvā pūjāṃ yathākramam ।।dhūpadīpādisiddhyarthaṃ vahnimuddhṛtya kṛtyavit ।।sādhayitvājyapūrvāṇi dravyāṇi punareva ca ।।kalpayitvāsanaṃ vahnau tatrāvāhya yathāpurā ।।saṃpūjya devaṃ devīṃ ca tataḥ pūrṇāṃtamācaret ।।atha vā svāśramoktaṃ tu vahnikarma śivārpaṇam ।।buddhvā śivāśramī kuryānna ca tatrāparo vidhiḥ ।।śivāgnerbhasmasaṃgrāhyamagnihotrodbhavaṃ tu vā ।।vaivāhognibhavaṃ vāpi pakvaṃ śuci sugaṃdhi ca ।।kapilāyāḥ śakṛcchastaṃ gṛhītaṃ gagane patat ।।na klinnaṃ nātikaṭhinaṃ na durgandhaṃ na śoṣitam ।।uparyadhaḥ parityajya gṛhṇīyātpatitaṃ yadi ।।piṃḍīkṛtya śivāgnyādau tatkṣipenmūlamaṃtrataḥ ।। apakvamatipākvaṃ ca saṃtyajya bhasitaṃ sitam ।।ādāya vā samāloḍya bhasmādhāre vinikṣipet ।।taijasaṃ dāravaṃ vāpi mṛnmayaṃ śailameva ca ।।anyadvā śobhanaṃ śuddhaṃ bhasmādhāraṃ prakalpayet ।।same deśe śubhe śuddhe dhanavadbhasma nikṣipet ।।na cāyuktakare dadyānnaivāśucitale kṣipet ।।na saṃspṛśecca nīcāṃgairnopekṣeta na laṃghayet ।।tasmādbhasitamādāya viniyuṃjīta mantrataḥ ।।kāleṣūkteṣu nānyatra nāyogyebhyaḥ pradāpayet ।।bhasmasaṃgrahaṇaṃ kuryāddeve anudvāsite sati ।।udvāsane kṛte yasmāccaṇḍabhasma prajāpate ।।agnikārye kṛte paścācchivaśāstroktamārgataḥ ।।svasūtroktaprakārādvā balikarma samācaret ।।atha vidyāsanaṃ nyasya supralipte tu maṇdale ।।vidyākośaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya yajetpuṣpādibhiḥ kramāt ।।vidyāyāḥ purataḥ kṛtvā gurorapi ca maṇḍalam ।।tatrāsanavaraṃ kṛtvā puṣpādyai gurumarcayet ।।tatonupūjayetpūjyān bhojayecca bubhukṣitān ।।tatassvayaṃ ca bhuṃjīta śuddhamannaṃ yathāsukham ।।niveditaṃ ca vā deve taccheṣaṃ cātmaśuddhaye ।।śraddadhāno na lobhena na caṇḍāya samarpitam ।।gandhamālyādi yaccānyattatrāpyeṣa samo vidhiḥ ।।na tu tatra śivosmīti buddhiṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ ।।bhuktvācamya śivaṃ dhyātvā hṛdaye mūlamuccaret ।।kālaśeṣaṃ nayedyogyaiḥ śivaśāstrakathādibhiḥ ।।rātrau vyatīte pūrvāṃśe kṛtvā pūjāṃ manoharām ।।śivayoḥ śayanaṃ tvekaṃ kalpayedatiśobhanam ।।bhakṣyabhojyāṃbarālepapuṣpamālādikaṃ tathā ।।manasā karmaṇā vāpi kṛtvā sarvaṃ manoharam ।।tato devasya devyāśca pādamūle śucissvapet ।।gṛhastho bhāryayā sārdhaṃ tadanye api tu kevalāḥ ।।pratyūṣasamayaṃ buddhvā mātrāmādyāmudīrayet ।।praṇamya manasāṃ devaṃ sāṃbaṃ sagaṇamavyayam ।।deśakālocitaṃ kṛtvā śaucādyamapi śaktitaḥ ।।śaṃkhādininadairdivyairdevaṃ devīṃ ca bodhayet ।।tatastatsamayonnidraiḥ puṣpairatisugaṃdhibhiḥ ।।nirvartya śivayoḥ pūjāṃ prārabheta puroditam ।। chapter upamanyuruvāca ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi śivāśramaniṣeviṇām ।।śivaśāstroktamārgeṇa naimittikavidhikramam ।।sarveṣvapi ca māseṣu pakṣayorubhayorapi ।।
aṣṭābhyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ tathā parvāṇi ca kramāt ।।ayane viṣuve caiva grahaṇeṣu viśeṣataḥ ।।kartavyā mahatī pūjā hyadhikā vāpi śaktitaḥ ।।māsimāsi yathānyāyaṃ brahmakūrcaṃ prasādhya tu ।।snāpayitvā śivaṃ tena pibeccheṣamupoṣitaḥ ।।brahmahatyādidoṣāṇāmatīva mahatāmapi ।।niṣkṛtirbrahmakūrcasya pānānnānyā viśiṣyate ।।pauṣe puṣyanakṣatre kuryānnīrājanaṃ vibhoḥ ।।māghe maghākhye nakṣatre pradadyād ghṛtakaṃbalam ।।phālgune cottarānte vai prārabheta mahotsavam ।।caitre citrāpaurṇamāsyāṃ dolāṃ kuryādyathāvidhi ।।vaiśākhyāṃ tu viśākhāyāṃ kuryātpuṣpamahālayam ।।jyeṣṭhe mūlākhyanakṣatre śītakumbhaṃ pradāpayet ।।āṣāḍhe cottarāṣāḍhe pavitrāropaṇaṃ tathā ।।śrāvaṇe prākṛtānyāpi maṇḍalāni prakalpayet ।।śraviṣṭhākhye tu nakṣatre prauṣṭhapadyāṃ tataḥ param ।।prokṣayecca jalakrīḍāṃ pūrvāṣāḍhāśraye dine ।।āśvayujyāṃ tato dadyātpāyasaṃ ca navodanam ।।agnikāryaṃ ca tenaiva kuryācchatabhiṣagdine ।।kārtikyāṃ kṛtikāyoge dadyāddīpasahasrakam ।।mārgaśīrṣe tathārdrāyāṃ ghṛtena snāpayecchivam ।।aśaktasteṣu kāleṣu kuryādutsavameva vā ।।āsthānaṃ vā mahāpūjāmadhikaṃ vā samarcanam ।।āvṛtte api ca kalyāṇe praśasteṣvapi karmasu ।।daurmanasye durācāre duḥsvapne duṣṭadarśane ।।utpāte vāśubhenyasminroge vā prabale atha vā ।।snānapūjājapadhyānahomadānādikāḥ kriyaḥ ।।nirmitānuguṇāḥ kāryāḥ puraścaraṇapūrvikāḥ ।।śivānale ca vihate punassandhānamācaret ।।ya evaṃ śarvadharmiṣṭho vartate nityamudyataḥ ।।tasyaikajanmanā muktiṃ prayacchati maheśvaraḥ ।।etadyathottaraṃ kuryānnityanaimittikeṣu yaḥ ।।divyaṃ śrīkaṃṭhanāthasya sthānamādyaṃ sa gacchati ।।tatra bhuktvā mahābhogānkalpakoṭiśatannaraḥ ।।kālāṃtarecyutastasmādaumaṃ kaumārameva ca ।।saṃprāpya vaiṣṇavaṃ brāhmaṃ rudralokaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।tatroṣitvā ciraṃ kālaṃ bhuktvā bhogānyathoditān ।।punaścordhvaṃ gatastasmādatītya sthānapañcakam ।।śrīkaṇṭhājjñānamāsādya tasmācchaivapuraṃ vrajet ।।ardhacaryārataścāpi dvirāvṛttyaivameva tu ।।paścājjñānaṃ samāsādya śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt ।।ardhārdhacarito yastu dehī dehakṣayātparam ।।aṃḍāṃtaṃ sadyapādaṃ ca tanmūrtimaṣṭatriṃśatkalāmayam ।।mātṛkāmayamīśānaṃ pañcabrahmamayaṃ tathā ।।oṃkārākhyamayaṃ caiva haṃsaśaktyā samanvitam ।।tathecchātmikayā śaktyā samārūḍhāṃkamaṃḍalam ।।jñānākhyayā aniruddhaṃ dakṣiṇataḥ pradyumnaṃ paścime tataḥ ।।saumye saṃkarṣaṇaṃ paścādvyatyastau vā yajedimau ।।prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śubham ।।matsyaḥ kūrmo varāhaśca narasiṃhotha vāmanaḥ sṛṣṭisaṃharaṇakṣamāḥ ।।parasparānuraktāśca parasparamanuvratāḥ ।।parasparamatisnigdhāḥ parasparanamaskṛtāḥ ।।śivapriyatamā nityaṃ śivalakṣaṇalakṣitāḥ ।।saumyādhārāstathā miśrāścāṃtarāladvayātmikāḥ ।।virūpāśca surūpāśca nānārūpadharāstathā ।।satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ te me kāmaṃ diśaṃtu vai ।।devyā priyasakhīvargo devīlakṣaṇalakṣitaḥ ।।sahito rudrakanyābhiḥ śaktibhiścāpyanekaśaḥ ।।tṛtīyāvaraṇe śaṃbhorbhaktyā nityaṃ samarcitaḥ ।।satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ sa me diśatu maṃgalam ।।divākaro maheśasya mūrtirdīptisumaṃḍalaḥ ।।nirguṇo guṇasaṃkīrṇastathaiva guṇakevalaḥ ।।avikārātmakaścādya ekassāmānyavikriyaḥ ।।asādhāraṇakarmā ca sṛṣṭisthitilayakramāt ।।evaṃ tridhā caturdhā ca vibhaktāḥ pañcadhā punaḥ ।।caturthāvaraṇe śaṃbhoḥ pūjitaścānugaiḥ saha ।।śivapriyaḥ śivāsaktaḥ śivapādārcane rataḥ ।।satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ sa me diśatu maṃgalam ।।divākaraṣaḍaṃgāni dīptādyāścāṣṭaśaktayaḥ ।।ādityo bhāskaro bhānū raviścetyanupūrvaśaḥ ।।arko brahmā tathā rudro viṣnuścādityamūrtayaḥ ।।vistarāsutarābodhinyāpyāyinyaparāḥ punaḥ ।।
uṣā prabhā tathā prājñā saṃdhyā cetyapi śaktayaḥ ।।somādiketuparyaṃtā grahāśca śivabhāvitāḥ ।।śivayorājñayānunnā maṃgalaṃ pradiśaṃtu me ।।athavā dvādaśādityāstathā dvādaśa śaktayaḥ ।।ṛṣayo devagaṃdharvāḥ pannagāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ ।।grāmaṇyaśca tathā yakṣā rākṣasāścāsurāstathā ।।saptasaptagaṇāścaite saptacchaṃdomayā hayāḥ ।।vālakhilyā dayaścaiva sarve śivapadārcakāḥ ।।satkṛtyaśivayorājñāṃ maṃgalaṃ pradiśaṃtu me ।।brahmātha devadevasya mūrtirbhūmaṇḍalādhipaḥ ।।catuḥṣaṣṭiguṇaiśvaryo buddhitattve pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।।nirguṇo guṇasaṃkīrṇastathaiva guṇakevalaḥ ।।avikārātmako devastatassādhāraṇaḥ puraḥ ।।asādhāraṇakarmā ca sṛṣṭisthitilayakramāt ।।bhuvaṃ tridhā caturdhā ca vibhaktaḥ pañcadhā punaḥ ।।caturthāvaraṇe śaṃbho pūjitaśca sahānugaiḥ ।।śivapriyaḥ śivāsaktaśśivapādārcane rataḥ ।।satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ sa me diśatu maṃgalam ।।hiraṇyagarbho lokeśo virāṭ kālaśca pūruṣaḥ ।।sanatkumāraḥ sanakaḥ sanaṃdaśca sanātanaḥ ।।prajānāṃ patayaścaiva dakṣādyā brahmasūnavaḥ ।।ekādaśa sapatnīkā dharmassaṃkalpa eva ca ।।śivārcanaratāścaite śivabhaktiparāyaṇāḥ ।।śivājñāvaśagāssarve diśaṃtu mama maṃgalam ।।catvāraśca tathā vedāssetihāsapurāṇakāḥ ।।dharmaśāstrāṇi vidyābhirvaidikībhissamanvitāḥ ।।parasparaviruddhārthāḥ śivaprakṛtipādakāḥ ।।satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ maṃgalaṃ pradiśaṃtu me ।।atha rudro mahādevaḥ śaṃbhormūrtirgarīyasī ।।vāhneyamaṇḍalādhīśaḥ pauruṣaiśvaryavānprabhuḥ ।।śivābhimānasaṃpanno nirguṇastriguṇātmakaḥ ।।kevalaṃ sāttvikaścāpi rājasaścaiva tāmasaḥ ।।avikārarataḥ pūrvaṃ tatastu samavikriyaḥ ।।asādhāraṇakarmā ca sṛṣṭyādikaraṇātpṛthak ।।brahmaṇopi śiraśchettā janakastasya tatsutaḥ ।।janakastanayaścāpi viṣṇorapi niyāmakaḥ ।।bodhakaśca tayornityamanugrahakaraḥ prabhuḥ ।।aṃḍasyāṃtarbahirvartī rudro lokadvayādhipaḥ ।।śivapriyaḥ śivāsaktaḥ śivapādārcane rataḥ ।।śivasyājñāṃ puraskṛtya sa me diśatu maṃgalam ।।tasya brahma ṣaḍaṃgāni vidyeśāṃtaṃ tathāṣṭakam ।।catvāro mūrtibhedāśca śivapūrvāḥ śivārcakāḥ ।।śivo bhavo haraścaiva mṛḍaścaiva tathāparaḥ ।। śivasyājñāṃ puraskṛtya maṃgalaṃ pradiśaṃtu me ।। f।atha viṣṇurmaheśasya śivasyaiva parā tanuḥ ।।vāritattvādhipaḥ sākṣādavyaktapadasaṃsthitaḥ ।।nirguṇassattvabahulastathaiva guṇakevalaḥ ।।avikārābhimānī ca trisādhāraṇavikriyaḥ ।।asādhāraṇakarmā ca sṛṣṭyādikaraṇātpṛthak ।।dakṣiṇāṃgabhavenāpi spardhamānaḥ svayaṃbhuvā ।।ādyena brahmaṇā sākṣātsṛṣṭaḥ sraṣṭā ca tasya tu ।।aṃḍasyāṃtarbahirvartī viṣṇurlokadvayādhipaḥ ।।asurāṃtakaraścakrī śakrasyāpi tathānujaḥ ।।prādurbhūtaśca daśadhā bhṛguśāpacchalādiha ।।bhūbhāranigrahārthāya svecchayāvātarakṣitau ।।aprameyabalo māyī māyayā mohayañjagat ।।mūrtiṃ kṛtvā mahāviṣṇuṃ sadāśiṣṇumathāpi vā ।।vaiṣṇavaiḥ pūjito nityaṃ mūrtitrayamayāsane ।।śivapriyaḥ śivāsaktaḥ śivapādārcane rataḥ ।।śivasyājñāṃ puraskṛtya sa me diśatu maṃgalam ।।vāsudevo aniruddhaśca pradyumnaśca tataḥ paraḥ ।।saṃkarṣaṇassamākhyātāścatasro mūrtayo hareḥ ।।matsyaḥ kūrmo varāhaśca nārasiṃho atha vāmanaḥ ।।rāmatrayaṃ tathā kṛṣṇo viṣṇusturagavaktrakaḥ ।।cakraṃ nārāyaṇasyāstraṃ pāṃcajanyaṃ ca śārṅgakam ।।satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ maṃgalaṃ pradiśaṃtu me ।।prabhā sarasvatī gaurī lakṣmīśca śivabhāvitā ।।śivayoḥ śāsanādetā maṃgalaṃ pradiśaṃtu me ।।indro agniśca yamaścaiva nirṛtirvaruṇastathā ।।vāyuḥ somaḥ kuberaśca tatheśānastriśūladhṛk ।।sarve śivārcanaratāḥ śivasadbhāvabhāvitāḥ ।।satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ maṃgalaṃ pradiśaṃtu me ।।triśūlamatha vajraṃ ca tathā paraśusāyakau ।।khaḍgapāśāṃkuśāścaiva pinākaścāyudhottamaḥ ।।divyāyudhāni devasya devyāścaitāni nityaśaḥ ।।satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ rakṣāṃ kurvaṃtu me sadā ।।vṛṣarūpadharo devaḥ saurabheyo mahābalaḥ ।।vaḍavākhyānalaspardhāṃ pañcagomātṛbhirvṛtaḥ ।।vāhanatvamanuprāptastapasā parameśayoḥ ।।tayorājñāṃ puraskṛtya sa me kāmaṃ prayacchatu ।।naṃdā sunaṃdā surabhiḥ suśīlā sumanāstathā ।।pañcagomātarastvetāśśivaloke vyavasthitāḥ ।।śivabhaktiparā nityaṃ śivārcanaparāyaṇāḥ ।।śivayoḥ śāsanādeva diśaṃtu mama vāṃchitam ।।kṣetrapālo mahātejā nīla jīmūtasannibhaḥ ।।daṃṣṭrākarālavadanaḥ sphuradraktādharojjvalaḥ ।।raktordhvamūrdhajaḥ śrīmānbhrukuṭīkuṭilekṣaṇaḥ ।। raktavṛttatrinayanaḥ śaśipannagabhūṣaṇaḥ ।।nagnastriśūlapāśāsikapālodyatapāṇikaḥ ।।bhairavo bhairavaiḥ siddhairyoginībhiśca saṃvṛtaḥ ।।kṣetrekṣetre samāsīnaḥ sthito yo rakṣakassatām ।।śivapraṇāmaparamaḥ śivasadbhāvabhāvitaḥ ।।śivaśritānviśeṣeṇa rakṣanputrānivaurasān ।।satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ sa me diśatu maṅgalam ।।tālajaṅghādayastasya prathamāvaraṇercitāḥ ।।satkṛtya śivayorājñāṃ catvāraḥ samavantu mām ।।bhairavādyāśca ye cānye samaṃtāttasya veṣṭitāḥ ।।te api māmanugṛhṇaṃtu śivaśāsanagauravāt ।।nāradādyāśca munayo divyā devaiśca pūjitāḥ ।।sādhyā māgāśca ye devā janalokanivāsinaḥ ।।vinivṛttādhikārāśca maharlokanivāsinaḥ ।।saptarṣayastathānye vai vaimānikaguṇaissaha ।।sarve śivārcanaratāḥ śivājñāvaśavartinaḥ ।। śivayorājñayā mahyaṃ diśaṃtu mama kāṃkṣitam ।।gaṃdharvādyāḥ piśācāṃtāścatasro devayonayaḥ ।।siddhā vidyādharādyāśca ye api cānye nabhaścarāḥ ।।asurā rākṣasāścaiva pātālatalavāsinaḥ ।।anaṃtādyāśca nāgendrā vainateyādayo dvijāḥ ।।kūṣmāṃḍāḥ pretavetālā grahā bhūtagaṇāḥ pare ।।ḍākinyaścāpi yoginyaḥ śākinyaścāpi tādṛśāḥ ।।kṣetrārāmagṛhādīni tīrthānyāyatanāni ca ।।dvīpāḥ samudrā nadyaśca nadāścānye sarāṃsi ca ।।girayaśca sumervādyāḥ kananāni samaṃtataḥ ।।paśavaḥ pakṣiṇo vṛkṣāḥ kṛmikīṭādayo mṛgāḥ ।।bhuvanānyapi sarvāṇi bhuvanānāmadhīśvaraḥ ।।aṇḍānyāvaraṇaissārdhaṃ māsāśca daśa diggajāḥ ।।varṇāḥ padāni maṃtrāśca tattvānyapi sahādhipaiḥ ।।brahmāṃḍadhārakā rudrā rudrāścānye saśaktikāḥ ।।yacca kiṃcijjagatyasmindṛṣṭaṃ cānumitaṃ śrutam ।।sarve kāmaṃ prayacchantu śivayoreva śāsanāt ।।atha vidyā parā śaivī paśupāśavimocinī ।।pañcārthasaṃjñitā divyā paśuvidyābahiṣkṛtā ।।śāstraṃ ca śivadharmākhyaṃ dharmākhyaṃ ca taduttaram ।।śaivākhyaṃ śivadharmākhyaṃ purāṇaṃ śrutisaṃmitam ।।śaivāgamāśca ye cānye kāmikādyāścaturvidhāḥ ।।śivābhyāmaviśeṣeṇa satkṛtyeha samarcitāḥ ।।
tābhyāmeva samājñātā mamābhipretasiddhaye ।।karmedamanumanyaṃtāṃ saphalaṃ sādhvanuṣṭhitam ।।śvetādyā nakulīśāṃtāḥ saśiṣyāścāpi deśikāḥ ।।tatsaṃtatīyā guravo viśeṣādguravo mama ।।śaivā māheśvarāścaiva jñānakarmaparāyaṇāḥ ।।karmedamanumanyaṃtāṃ saphalaṃ sādhvanuṣṭhitam ।।laukikā brāhmaṇāssarve kṣatriyāśca viśaḥ kramāt ।।vedavedāṃgatattvajñāḥ sarvaśāstraviśāradāḥ ।।sāṃkhyā vaiśeṣikāścaiva yaugā naiyāyikā narāḥ ।।saurā brahmāstathā raudrā vaiṣṇavāścāpare narāḥ ।।śiṣṭāḥ sarve viśiṣṭā ca śivaśāsanayaṃtritāḥ ।।karmedamanumanyaṃtāṃ mamābhipretasādhakam ।।śaivāḥ siddhāṃtamārgasthāḥ śaivāḥ pāśupatāstathā ।।śaivā mahāvratadharāḥ śaivāḥ kāpālikāḥ pare ।।śivājñāpālakāḥ pūjyā mamāpi śivaśāsanāt ।।sarve mamānugṛhṇaṃtu śaṃsaṃtu saphalakriyām ।।dakṣiṇajñānaniṣṭhāśca dakṣiṇottaramārgagāḥ ।।avirodhena vartaṃtāṃ maṃtraśreyo arthino mama ।।nāstikāśca śaṭhāścaiva kṛtaghnāścaiva tāmasāḥ ।।pāṣaṃḍāścātipāpāśca vartaṃtāṃ dūrato mama ।।bahubhiḥ kiṃ stutairatra ye api ke apicidāstikāḥ ।।sarve māmanugṛhṇaṃtu saṃtaḥ śaṃsaṃtu maṃgalam ।।namaśśivāya sāṃbāya sasutāyādihetave ।।pañcāvaraṇarūpeṇa prapañcenāvṛtāya te ।।ityuktvā daṃḍavadbhūmau praṇipatya śivaṃ śivām ।।japetpañcākṣarīṃ vidyāmaṣṭottaraśatāvarām ।।tathaiva śaktividyāṃ ca japitvā tatsamarpaṇam ।।kṛtvā taṃ kṣamayitveśaṃ pūjāśeṣaṃ samāpayet ।।etatpuṇyatamaṃ stotraṃ śivayorhṛdayaṃgamam ।।sarvābhīṣṭapradaṃ sākṣādbhuktimuktyaikasādhanam ।।ya idaṃ kīrtayennityaṃ śṛṇuyādvā samāhitaḥ ।।sa vidhūyāśu pāpāni śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt ।।goghnaścaiva kṛtaghnaśca vīrahā bhrūṇahāpi vā ।।śaraṇāgataghātī ca mitraviśraṃbhaghātakaḥ ।।duṣṭapāpasamācāro mātṛhā pitṛhāpi vā ।।stavenānena japtena tattatpāpātpramucyate ।।duḥsvapnādimahānarthasūcakeṣu bhayeṣu ca ।।yadi saṃkīrtayedetanna tato nārthabhāgbhavet ।।āyurārogyamaiśvaryaṃ yaccānyadapi vāñchitam ।।stotrasyāsya jape tiṣṭhaṃstatsarvaṃ labhate naraḥ ।।asaṃpūjya śivastotraṃ japātphalamudāhṛtam ।।saṃpūjya ca jape tasya phalaṃ vaktuṃ na śakyate ।। āstāmiyaṃ phalāvāptirasminsaṃkīrtite sati ।।sārdhamaṃbikayā devaḥ śrutyaivaṃ divi tiṣṭhati ।।tasmānnabhasi saṃpūjya devaṃ devaṃ sahomayā ।।kṛtāṃjalipuṭastiṣṭhaṃstotrametadudīrayet ।। chapter saṃsādhayetpūrvaṃ mantraṃ mantrārthavittamaḥ ।।dṛṣṭasiddhikaraṃ karma nānyathā phaladaṃ yataḥ ।।siddhamantro apyadṛṣṭena prabalena tu kenacit ।।pratibandhaphalaṃ karma na kuryātsahasā budhaḥ ।।tasya tu pratibandhasya kartuṃ śakyeha niṣkṛtiḥ ।।parīkṣya śakunādyaistadādau niṣkṛtimācaret ।।yo anyathā kurute mohātkarmaihikaphalaṃ naraḥ ।।na tena phalabhāksa syātprāpnuyāccopahāsyatām ।।abisrabdho na kurvīta karma dṛṣṭaphalaṃ kvacit ।।sa khalvaśraddhadhānaḥ syānnāśraddhaḥ phalamṛcchati ।।nāparādhosti devasya karmaṇyapi tu niṣphale ।।yathoktakāriṇāṃ puṃsāmihaiva phaladarśanāt ।।sādhakaḥ siddhamaṃtraśca nirastapratibaṃdhakaḥ ।।viśvastaḥ śraddhadhānaśca kurvannāpnoti tatphalam ।।athavā tatphalāvāptyai brahmacaryarato bhavet ।।rātrau haviṣyamaśnīyātpāyasaṃ vā phalāni vā ।।hiṃsādi yanniṣiddhaṃ syānna kuryānmanasāpi tat ।।sadā bhasmānuliptāṃ gassuveṣaśca śucirbhavet ।।itthamācāravānbhūtvā svānukūle śubhe ahani ।।pūrvoktalakṣaṇe deśe puṣpadāmādyalaṃkṛte ।।ālipya śakṛtā bhūmiṃ hastamānāvarāṃ yathā ।।vilikhetkamale bhadre dīpyamānaṃ svatejasā ।।taptajāṃbūnadamayamaṣṭapatraṃ sakesaram ।।madhye karṇikayā yuktaṃ sarvaratnairalaṃkṛtam ।।svākārasadṛśenaiva nālena ca samanvitam ।।tādṛśe svarṇanirmāṇe kaṃde samyagvidhānataḥ ।।tatrāṇimādikaṃ sarvaṃ saṃkalpya manasā punaḥ ।।ratnajaṃ vātha sauvarṇaṃ sphaṭikaṃ vā salakṣaṇam ।।liṅgaṃ savedikaṃ caiva sthāpayitvā vidhānataḥ ।। f। tatrāvāhya yajeddevaṃ sāṃbaṃ sagaṇamavyayam ।।tatra māheśvarī kalpyā mūrtirmūrtimataḥ prabhoḥ ।। caturbhujā caturvaktrā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā ।।śārdūlacarmavasanā kiṃcidvihasitānanā ।।varadābhayahastā ca mṛgaṭaṃkadharā tathā ।।atha vāṣṭabhujā ciṃtyā ciṃtakasya yathāruci ।।tadā triśūlaparaśukhaḍgavajrāṇi dakṣiṇe ।।vāme pāśāṃkuśau tadvatkheṭaṃ nāgaṃ ca bibhratī ।।bālārkasadṛśaprakhyā prativaktraṃ trilocanā ।।tasyāḥ pūrvamukhaṃ saumyaṃ svākārasadṛśaprabham ।।dakṣiṇaṃ nīlajīmūtasadṛśaṃ ghoradarśanam ।।uttaraṃ vidrumaprakhyaṃ nīlālakavibhūṣitam ।।paścimaṃ pūrṇacaṃdrābhaṃ saumyamiṃdukalādharam ।।tadaṃkamaṃḍalārūḍhā śaktirmāheśvarī parā ।।mahālakṣmīriti khyātā śyāmā sarvamanoharā ।।mūrtiṃ kṛtvaivamākārāṃ sakalīkṛtya ca kramāt ।।mūrtimaṃtamathāvāhya yajetparamakāraṇam ।।snānārthe kalpayettatra pañcagavyaṃ tu kāpilam ।।pañcāmṛtaṃ ca pūrṇāni bījāni ca viśeṣataḥ ।।purastānmaṇḍalaṃ kṛtvā ratnacūrṇādyalaṃkṛtam ।।karṇikāyāṃ pravinyasyedīśānakalaśaṃ punaḥ ।।sadyādikalaśānpaścātparitastasya kalpayet ।।tato vidyeśakalaśānaṣṭau pūrvādivatkramāt ।।tīrthāmbupūritānkṛtvā sūtreṇāveṣṭya pūrvavat ।।puṇyadravyāṇi nikṣipya samantraṃ savidhānakam ।।dukūlādyena vastreṇa samācchādya samaṃtataḥ ।।sarvatra maṃtraṃ vinyasya tattanmaṃtrapurassaram ।।snānakāle tu saṃprāpte sarvamaṅgalanisvanaiḥ ।।pañcagavyādibhiścaiva snāpayetparameśvaram ।।tataḥ kuśodakādyāni svarṇaratnodakānyapi ।।gaṃdhapuṣpādisiddhāni mantrasiddhāni ca kramāt ।।uddhṛtyoddhṛtya mantreṇa taistaissnāpya maheśvaram ।।gaṃdhaṃ puṣpādidīpāṃśca pūjākarma samācaret ।।palāvaraḥ syādālepa ekādaśapalottaraḥ ।।suvarṇaratnapuṣpāṇi śubhāni surabhīṇi ca ।।nīlotpalādyutpalāni bilvapatrāṇyanekaśaḥ ।।kamalāni ca raktāni śvetānyapi ca śaṃbhave ।।kṛṣṇāgurūdbhavo dhūpaḥ sakarpūrājyaguggulaḥ ।।kapilāghṛtasaṃsiddhā dīpāḥ karpūravartijāḥ ।।pañcabrahmaṣaḍaṃgāni pūjyānyāvaraṇāni ca ।।naivedyaḥ payasā siddhaḥ sa guḍājyo mahācaruḥ ।।pāṭalotpalapadmādyaiḥ pānīyaṃ ca sugandhitam ।।pañcasaugaṃdhikopetaṃ tāṃbūlaṃ ca susaṃskṛtam ।।suvarṇaratnasiddhāni bhūṣaṇāni viśeṣataḥ ।।
vāsāṃsi ca vicitrāṇi sūkṣmāṇi ca navāni ca ।।darśanīyāni deyāni gānavādyādibhissaha ।।japaśca mūlamaṃtrasya lakṣaḥ paramasaṃkhyayā ।।ekāvarā tryuttarā ca pūjā phalavaśādiha ।।daśasaṃkhyāvaro homaḥ pratidravyaṃ śatottaraḥ ।।ghorarūpaśśivaściṃtyo māraṇoccāṭanādiṣu ।।śivaliṃge śivāgnau ca hyanyāsu pratimāsu ca ।।ciṃtyassaumyatanuśśaṃbhuḥ kārye śāṃtikapauṣṭike ।।āyasau sruksruvau kāryau māraṇādiṣu madhunā punaḥ ।।staṃbhanaṃ sarṣapeṇāpi laśunena tu pātanam ।।tāḍanaṃ rudhireṇa syātkharasyoṣṭrasya cobhayoḥ ।।māraṇoccāṭane kuryādrohibījaistilānvitaiḥ ।।vidveṣaṇaṃ ca tailena kuryāllāṃgalakasya tu pratīkārāṃtaraṃ na cet ।।ātatāyinamuddiśya prakuryādābhicārikam ।।svarāṣṭrapatimuddiśya na kuryādābhicārikam ।।yadyāstikassudharmiṣṭho mānyo vā yo api kopi vā ।।tamuddiśyāpi no kuryādātatāyinamapyuta ।।manasā karmaṇā vācā yo api kopi śivāśritaḥ ।। svarāṣṭrapatimuddiśya śivā śritamathāpi vā ।।kṛtvābhicārikaṃ karma sadyo vinipatennaraḥ ।।svarāṣṭrapālakaṃ tasmācchivabhaktaṃ ca kañcana ।।na atha vā liṃge ārṣake vaidike api vā ।।abhāve hemaratnānāmaśaktau ca tadarjane ।।manasaivācaredetaddravyairvā pratirūpakaiḥ ।।kvacidaṃśe tu yaḥ śaktastvaśaktaḥ kvacidaṃśake ।।so api śaktyanusāreṇa kurvaṃścetphalamṛcchati ।।karmaṇyanuṣṭhite apyasminphalaṃ yatra na dṛśyate ।।dvistrirvāvartayettatra sarvathā dṛśyate phalam ।।pūjopayuktaṃ yaddravyaṃ hemaratnādyanuttamam ।।tatsarvaṃ gurave sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ śivaloke mahīyate ।।etadvratottamaṃ guhyaṃ śivaliṃgamahāvratam ।।bhaktasya te samākhyātaṃ na deyaṃ yasya kasyacit ।।deyaṃ ca śivabhaktebhyaḥ śivena kathitaṃ purā ।। chapter upamanyuruvāca nityanaimittikātkāmyādyā siddhiriha kīrtitā ।।sā sarvā labhyeta sadyo liṃgaberapratiṣṭhayā ।।sarvo liṃgamayo lokassarvaṃ liṃge pratiṣṭhitam ।।tasmātpratiṣṭhite liṃge bhavetsarvaṃ patiṣṭhitam ।।brahmaṇā viṣṇunā vāpi rudreṇānyena kena vā ।।liṃgapratiṣṭhāmutsṛjya kriyate svapadasthitiḥ ।।kimanyadiha vaktavyaṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ prati kāraṇam ।।partiṣṭhitaṃ śivenāpi liṃgaṃ vaiśveśvaraṃ yataḥ ।।tasmātsarvaprayatnena paratreha ca śarmaṇe ।।sthāpayetparameśasya liṃgaṃ beramathāpi vā ।।śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca kimidaṃ liṃgamākhyātaṃ kathaṃ liṃgī maheśvaraḥ ।।kathaṃ ca liṃgabhāvo asya liṃgamājñāpayedyataḥ ।।yato na tadanājñātaṃ kāryāya prabhavetsvataḥ ।।tato jātasya viśvasya tatraiva vilayo yataḥ ।।anena liṃgatāṃ tasya bhavennānyena kenacit ।।liṃgaṃ ca śivayordehastābhyāṃ rūpamasthāya gatavānadhaḥ ।।evaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu tvaran viṣṇuradhogataḥ ।।nāpaśyadalpamapyasya mūlaṃ liṃgasya sūkaraḥ ।।tāvatkālaṃ gataścordhvaṃ tasyāṃtaṃ jñātumicchayā ।।śrāṃtotyaṃtamadṛṣṭvāṃtaṃ pāpatādhaḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। tathaiva bhagavān viṣṇuḥ śrāṃtaḥ saṃvignalocanaḥ ।।kleśena mahatā tūrṇamadhastādutthito abhavat ।।samāgatāvathānyonyaṃ vismayasmeravīkṣaṇau ।।māyayā mohitau śaṃbhoḥ kṛtyākṛtyaṃ na jagmatuḥ ।।pṛṣṭhataḥ pārśvatastasya cāgrataśca sthitāvubhau ।।praṇipatya kimātmedamityaciṃtayatāṃ tadā ।।
chapter upamanyuruvāca athāvirabhavattatra sanādaṃ śabdalakṣaṇam ।।omityekākṣaraṃ brahma brahmaṇaḥ pratipādakam ।।tadapyaviditaṃ tāvadbrahmaṇā viṣṇunā tathā ।।rajasā tamasā cittaṃ madhyataḥ ।।ardhamātrātmako nādaḥ śrūyate liṃgamūrdhani ।।vibhakte api tadā tasminpraṇave paramākṣare ।।vibhāvārthaṃ ca tau devau na kiṃcidavajagmatuḥ ।।vedātmanā tadāvyaktaḥ praṇavo vikṛtiṃ gataḥ
