।।mahāpūjāmathārabhya saṃpūjya kalaśāndaśa ।।śivamaṃtramanusmṛtya śivakuṃbhajalāṃtare ।।aṃguṣṭhānāmikāyogādādāya tamudīrayet ।।nyasedīśānabhāgasya madhye liṃgasya maṃtravit ।। śaktiṃ nyasettathā vidyāṃ vidyeśāṃśca yathākramam ।।liṅgamūle śivajalaistato liṃgaṃ niṣecayet ।।vardhanyāṃ piṃḍikāliṃgaṃ vidyeśakalaśaiḥ punaḥ ।।abhiṣicyāsanaṃ paścādādhārādyaṃ prakalpayet ।।kṛtvā pañcakalānyāsaṃ dīptaṃ liṃgamanusmaret ।।āvāhayecchivau sākṣātprāñjaliḥ prāgudaṅmukhaḥ ।।vṛṣādhirājamāruhya vimānaṃ vā nabhastalāt ।।alaṃkṛtaṃ sahāyāṃtaṃ devyā devamanusmaran ।।sarvābharaṇaśobhāḍhyaṃ sarvamaṃgalanisvanaiḥ ।। f।brahmaviṣṇumaheśārkaśakrādyairdevadānavaiḥ ।।ānaṃdaklinnasarvāṃgairvinyastāṃjalimastakaiḥ ।।stuvadbhireva nṛtyadbhirnāmadbhirabhito vṛtam ।।tataḥ pañcopacārāṃśca kṛtvā pūjāṃ samāpayet ।।nātaḥ parataraḥ kaścidvidhiḥ pañcopacārakāt ।।pratiṣṭhāṃ liṃgavatkuryātpratimāsvapi sarvataḥ ।।lakṣaṇoddhārasamaye kāryaṃ nayanamocanam ।।jalādhivāse śayane śāyayettāntvadhomukhīm ।।kumbhodaśāyitāṃ maṃtrairhṛdi tāṃ sanniyojayet ।।kṛtālayāṃ parāmāhuḥ pratiṣṭhāmakṛtālayāt ।।śaktaḥ kṛtālayaḥ paścātpratiṣṭhāvidhimācaret ।।aśaktaścetpratiṣṭhāpya liṃgaṃ beramathāpi vā ।।śakteranuguṇaṃ paścātprakurvīta śivālayam ।।gṛhārcāṃ ca punarvakṣye pratiṣṭhāvidhimuttamam ।।kṛtvā kanīyasaṃberaṃ liṃgaṃ vā lakṣaṇānvitam ।।ayane cottare prāpte śuklapakśe śubhe dine ।।devīṃ kṛtvā śubhe deśe tatrābjaṃ pūrvavallikhet ।।vikīrya patrapuṣpādyairmadhye kuṃbhaṃ nidhāya ca ।।paritastasya caturaḥ kalaśān dikṣu vinyaset ।।pañca brahmāṇi tadbījaisteṣu pañcasu pañcabhiḥ ।।nyasya saṃpūjya mudrādi darśayitvābhirakṣya ca ।।viśodhya liṃgaṃ beraṃ vā mṛttoyādyairyathā purā ।।sthāpayetpuṣpasaṃchannamuttarasthe varāsane ।।nidhāya puṣpaṃ śirasi prokṣayetprokṣaṇījalaiḥ ।।samabhyarcya punaḥ puṣpairjayaśabdādipūrvakam ।।kumbhairīśānavidyāṃtaiḥ snāpayenmūlavidyayā ।।tataḥ pañcakalānyāsaṃ kṛtvā pūjāṃ ca pūrvavat ।।nityamārādhayettatra devyā devaṃ trilocanam ।।ekamevātha vā kuṃbhaṃ mūrtimantrasamanvitam ।।nyasya padmāṃtare sarvaṃ śeṣaṃ pūrvavadācaret ।।atyaṃtopahataṃ liṃgaṃ viśodhya sthāpayetpunaḥ ।।saṃprokṣayedupahatamanāgupahataṃ yajet ।।liṃgāni bāṇasaṃjñāni sthāpanīyāni vā na vā ।।tāni pūrvaṃ śivenaiva saṃskṛtāni yatastataḥ ।।śeṣāṇi sthāpanīyāni yāni dṛṣṭāni bāṇavat ।।svayamudbhūtaliṃge ca divye cārṣe tathaiva ca ।।
apīṭhe pīṭhamāveśya kṛtvā saṃprokṣaṇaṃ vidhim ।।yajettatra śivaṃ teṣāṃ pratiṣṭhā na vidhīyate ।।dagdhaṃ ślathaṃ kṣatāṃgaṃ ca kṣipelliṃgaṃ jalāśaye ।।saṃdhānayogyaṃ saṃdhāya pratiṣṭhāvidhimācaret ।।berādvā vikalālliṃgāddevapūjāpurassaram ।।udvāsya hṛdi saṃdhānaṃ tyāgaṃ vā yuktamācaret ।।ekāhapūjāvihatau kuryāddviguṇamarcanam ।।dvirātre ca mahāpūjāṃ saṃprokṣaṇamataḥ param ।।māsādūrdhvamanekāhaṃ pūjā yadi vihanyate ।।pratiṣṭhā procyate kaiścitkaiścitsaṃprokṣaṇakramaḥ ।।saṃprokṣaṇe tu liṃgāderdevamudvāsya pūrvavat ।।aṣṭapañcakrameṇaiva snāpayitvā mṛdaṃbhasā ।।gavāṃ rasaiśca saṃsnāpya darbhatoyairviśodhya ca ।।prokṣayetprokṣaṇītoyairmūlenāṣṭottaraṃ śatam ।।sapuṣpaṃ sakuśaṃ pāṇiṃ nyasya liṃgasya mastake ।।pañcavāraṃ japenmūlamaṣṭottaraśataṃ tataḥ ।।tato mūlena mūrdhādipīṭhāṃtaṃ saṃspṛśedapi ।।pūjāṃ ca mahatīṃ kuryāddevamāvāhya pūrvavat ।।alabdhe sthāpite liṃge śivasthāne jale atha vā ।।vahnau ravau tathā vyomni bhagavaṃtaṃ śivaṃ yajet ।। chapter śīkṛṣṇa uvāca jñāne kriyāyāṃ caryāyāṃ sāramuddhṛtya saṃgrahāt ।।uktaṃ bhagavatā sarvaṃ śrutaṃ śrutisamaṃ mayā ।।idānīṃ śrotumicchāmi yogaṃ paramadurlabham ।।sādhikāraṃ ca sāṃgaṃ ca savidhiṃ saprayojanam ।।yadyasti maraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ yogādyanupamardataḥ ।।sadyaḥ sādhayituṃ śakyaṃ yena syānnātmahā naraḥ ।।tacca tatkāraṇaṃ caiva tatkālakaraṇāni ca ।।tadbhedatāratamyaṃ ca vaktumarhasi tattvataḥ ।।upamanyuruvāca sthāne pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā kṛṣṇa sarvapraśnārthavedinā ।।tataḥ krameṇa tatsarvaṃ vakṣye śṛṇu samāhitaḥ ।।niruddhavṛttyaṃtarasyaṃ śive cittasya niścalā ।।yā vṛttiḥ sa samāsena yogaḥ sa khalu pañcadhā ।।maṃtrayogaḥsparśayogo bhāvayogastathāparaḥ ।।abhāvayogassarvebhyo mahāyogaḥ paro mataḥ ।।maṃtrābhyāsavaśenaiva maṃtravācyārthagocaraḥ ।।avyākṣepā manovṛttirmaṃtrayoga udāhṛtaḥ ।।prāṇāyāmamukhā saiva sparśe yogobhidhīyate ।।sa maṃtrasparśanirmukto bhāvayogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।vilīnāvayavaṃ viśvaṃ rūpaṃ saṃbhāvyate yataḥ ।। abhāvayogaḥ saṃprokto anābhāsādvastunaḥ sataḥ ।।śivasvabhāva evaikaściṃtyate nirupādhikaḥ ।।yathā śaivamanovṛttirmahāyoga ihocyate ।।dṛṣṭe tathānuśravike viraktaṃ viṣaye manaḥ ।।yasya tasyādhikārosti yoge nānyasya kasyacit ।।viṣayadvayadoṣāṇāṃ guṇānāmīśvarasya ca ।।darśanādeva satataṃ viraktaṃ jāyate manaḥ ।।aṣṭāṃgo vā ṣaḍaṃgo vā sarvayogaḥ samāsataḥ ।।yamaśca niyamaścaiva svastikādyaṃ tathāsanam ।।prāṇāyāmaḥ pratyāhāro dhāraṇā dhyānameva ca ।।samādhiriti yogāṃgānyaṣṭāvuktāni sūribhiḥ ।।āsanaṃ prāṇasaṃrodhaḥ pratyāhārotha dhāraṇā ।।dhyānaṃ samādhiryogasya ṣaḍaṃgāni samāsataḥ ।।pṛthaglakṣaṇameteṣāṃ śivaśāstre samīritam ।।śivāgameṣu cānyeṣu viśeṣātkāmikādiṣu ।।yogaśāstreṣvapi tathā purāṇeṣvapi keṣu ca ।।ahiṃsā satyamasteyaṃ brahmacaryāparigrahaḥ ।।yama ityucyate sadbhiḥ pañcāvayavayogataḥ ।। f।śaucaṃ tuṣṭistapaścaiva japaḥ praṇidhireva ca ।।iti pañcaprabhedassyānniyamaḥ svāṃśabhedataḥ ।।svastikaṃ padmamadhyeṃduṃ vīraṃ yogaṃ prasādhitam ।।paryaṃkaṃ ca yatheṣṭaṃ ca proktamāsanamaṣṭadhā ।।prāṇaḥ svadehajo vāyustasyāyāmo nirodhanam ।।tadrocakaṃ pūrakaṃ ca kuṃbhakaṃ ca tridhocyate ।।nāsikāpuṭamaṃgulyā pīḍyaikamapareṇa tu ।।audaraṃ recayedvāyuṃ tathāyaṃ recakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।bāhyena marutā dehaṃ dṛtivatparipūrayet ।।nāsāpuṭenāpareṇa pūraṇātpūrakaṃ matam ।।na muṃcati na gṛhṇāti vāyumaṃtarbahiḥ sthitam ।।saṃpūrṇaṃ kuṃbhavattiṣṭhedacalaḥ sa tu kuṃbhaka ।।recakādyaṃ trayamidaṃ na drutaṃ na vilaṃbitam ।।tadyataḥ kramayogena tvabhyasedyogasādhakaḥ ।।recakādiṣu yobhyāso nāḍīśodhanapūrvakaḥ ।।svecchotkramaṇaparyaṃtaḥ prokto yogānuśāsane ।।kanyakādikramavaśātprāṇāyāmanirodhanam ।।taccaturdhopadiṣṭaṃ syānmātrāguṇavibhāgataḥ ।।kanyakastu caturdhā syātsa ca dvādaśamātrakaḥ ।।madhyamastu dviruddhātaścaturviṃśatimātrakaḥ ।।uttamastu triruddhātaḥ ṣaḍviṃśanmātrakaḥ paraḥ ।।svedakaṃpādijanakaḥ prāṇāyāmastaduttaraḥ ।।ānaṃdodbhavaromāṃcanetrāśrūṇāṃ vimocanam ।।jalpabhramaṇamūrchādyaṃ jāyate yoginaḥ param ।।jānuṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya na drutaṃ na vilaṃbitam ।।aṃgulīsphoṭanaṃ kuryātsā mātreti prakīrtitā ।। mātrākrameṇa vijñeyāścodvātakramayogataḥ ।।nāḍīviśuddhipūrvaṃ tu prāṇāyāmaṃ samācaret ।।agarbhaśca sagarbhaśca prāṇāyāmo dvidhā smṛtaḥ ।।japaṃ dhyānaṃ vināgarbhaḥ sagarbhastatsamanvayāt ।।agarbhādgarbhasaṃyuktaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥśatādhikaḥ ।।tasmātsagarbhaṃ kurvanti yoginaḥ prāṇasaṃyamam ।।
prāṇasya vijayādeva jīyaṃte deha āyavaḥ ।।prāṇo apānaḥ samānaśca hyudāno vyāna eva ca ।।nāgaḥ kūrmaśca kṛkalo devadatto dhanaṃjayaḥ ।।prayāṇaṃ kurute yasmāttasmātprāṇo abhidhīyate ।।avāṅnayatyapānākhyo yadāhārādi bhujyate ।।vyāno vyānaśayatyaṃgānyaśeṣāṇi vivardhayan ।।udvejayati marmāṇītyudāno vāyurīritaḥ ।।samaṃ nayati sarvāṃgaṃ samānastena gīyate ।।udgāre nāga ākhyātaḥ kūrma unmīlane sthitaḥ ।।kṛkalaḥ kṣavathau jñeyo devadatto vijṛṃbhaṇe ।।na jahāti mṛtaṃ cāpi sarvavyāpī dhanaṃjayaḥ ।।krameṇābhyasyamānoyaṃ prāṇāyāmapramāṇavān ।।nirdahatyakhilaṃ doṣaṃ karturdehaṃ ca rakṣati ।।prāṇe tu vijite samyak taccihnānyupalakṣayet ।।viṇmūtraśleṣmaṇāṃ tāvadalpabhāvaḥ prajāyate ।।bahubhojanasāmarthyaṃ cirāducchvāsanaṃ tathā ।।laghutvaṃ śīghragāmitvamutsāhaḥ svarasauṣṭhavam ।।sarvarogakṣayaścaiva balaṃ tejaḥ surūpatā ।।dhṛtirmedhā yuvatvaṃ ca sthiratā ca prasannatā ।।tapāṃsi pāpakṣayatā yajñadānavratādayaḥ ।।prāṇāyāmasya tasyaite kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ।।indriyāṇi prasaktāni yathāsvaṃ viṣayeṣviha ।।āhatya yannigṛhṇāti sa pratyāhāra ucyate ।।namaḥpūrvāṇīṃdriyāṇi svargaṃ narakameva ca ।।nigṛhītanisṛṣṭāni svargāya narakāya ca ।।tasmātsukhārthī matimāñjñānavairāgyamāsthitaḥ ।।iṃdriyāśvānnigṛhyāśu svātmanātmānamuddharet ।।dhāraṇā nāma cittasya sthānabandhassamāsataḥ ।।sthānaṃ ca śiva evaiko nānyaddoṣatrayaṃ yataḥ ।।kālaṃ kaṃcāvadhīkṛtya sthāne avasthāpitaṃ manaḥ ।।na tu pracyavate lakṣyāddhāraṇā syānna cānyathā ।।manasaḥ prathamaṃ sthairyaṃ dhāraṇātaḥ prajāyate ।।tasmāddhīraṃ manaḥ kuryāddhāraṇābhyāsayogataḥ ।।dhyai ciṃtāyāṃ smṛto dhātuḥ śivaciṃtā muhurmuhuḥ ।।avyākṣiptena manasā dhyānaṃ nāma taducyate ।।dhyeyāvasthitacittasya sadṛśaḥ pratyayaśca yaḥ ।। pratyayāntaranirmuktaḥ pravāho dhyānamucyate ।।sarvamanyatparityajya śiva eva śivaṃkaraḥ ।।paro dhyeyo adhideveśaḥ samāptātharvaṇī śrutiḥ ।।tathā śivā parā dhyeyā sarvabhūtagatau śivau ।।tau śrutau smṛtiśāstrebhyaḥ sarvagau sarvadoditau ।।sarvajñau satataṃ dhyeyau nānārūpavibhedataḥ ।।vimuktiḥ pratyayaḥ pūrvaḥ pratyayaścāṇimādikam ।।ityetaddvividhaṃ jñeyaṃ dhyānasyāsya prayojanam ।।dhyātā dhyānaṃ tathā dhyeyaṃ yacca dhyānaprayojanam ।।etaccatuṣṭayaṃ jñātvā yogaṃ yuñjīta yogavit ।।jñānavairāgyasaṃpannaḥ śraddadhānaḥ kṣamānvitaḥ ।।nirmamaśca sadotsāhī dhyātetthaṃ puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।japācchrāṃtaḥ punardhyāyeddhyānācchrāṃtaḥ punarjapet ।।japadhyanābhiyuktasya kṣipraṃ yogaḥ prasiddhyati ।।dhāraṇā dvādaśāyāmā dhyānaṃ dvādaśadhāraṇam ।।dhyānadvādaśakaṃ yāvatsamādhirabhidhīyate ।।samādhirnnāma yogāṃgamantimaṃ parikīrtitam ।।samādhinā ca sarvatra prajñālokaḥ pravartate ।।yadarthamātranirbhāsaṃ stimito dadhivatsthitam ।।svarūpaśūnyavadbhānaṃ samādhirabhidhīyate ।।dhyeye manaḥ samāveśya paśyedapi ca susthiram ।।nirvāṇānalavadyogī samādhisthaḥ pragīyate ।।na śṛṇoti na cāghrāti na jalpati na paśyati ।।na ca sparśaṃ vijānāti na saṃkalpayate manaḥ ।।navābhimanyate kiṃcidbadhyate na ca kāṣṭavat ।।evaṃ śive vilīnātmā samādhistha ihocyate ।।yathā dīpo nivātasthaḥ spandate na kadācana ।।tathā samādhiniṣṭho api tasmānna vicaletsudhīḥ ।।evamabhyasataścāraṃ yogino yogamuttamam ।।tadantarāyā naśyaṃti vighnāḥ sarve śanaiḥśanaiḥ ।।oṃ iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāṃ vāyunaimiṣeyarṣisaṃvāde uttarakhaṇḍe yogagativarṇanaṃ nāma saptatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ chapter upamanyuruvāca ālasyaṃ vyādhayastīvrāḥ pramādaḥ sthānasaṃśayaḥ ।।anavasthitacittatvamaśraddhā bhrāṃtidarśanam ।।duḥkhāni daurmanasyaṃ ca viṣayeṣu ca lolatā ।।daśaite yuñjatāṃ puṃsāmantarāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।ālasyamalasattvaṃ tu yogināṃ dehacetanoḥ ।।dhātuvaiṣamyajā doṣā vyādhayaḥ karmadoṣajāḥ ।।pramādo nāma yogasya sādhanā nāma bhāvanā ।।idaṃ vetyubhayākrāntaṃ vijñānaṃ sthānasaṃśayaḥ ।।apratiṣṭhā hi manasastvanavasthitirucyate ।। aśraddhā bhāvarahitā vṛttirvai yogavartmani ।।viparyastā matiryā sā bhrāṃtirityabhidhīyate ।।duḥkhamajñānajaṃ puṃsāṃ cittasyādhyātmikaṃ viduḥ ।।ādhibhautikamaṃgotthaṃ yacca duḥkhaṃ purā kṛtaiḥ ।।ādhidaivikamākhyātamaśanyastraviṣādikam ।।icchāvighātajaṃ mokṣaṃ daurmanasyaṃ pracakṣate ।।viṣayeṣu vicitreṣu vibhramastatra lolatā ।।śānteṣveteṣu vighneṣu yogāsaktasya yoginaḥ ।।upasargāḥ pravartaṃte divyāste siddhisūcakāḥ ।।pratibhā śravaṇaṃ vārtā darśanāsvādavedanāḥ ।।upasargāḥ ṣaḍityete vyaye yogasya siddhayaḥ ।।sūkṣme vyavahite atīte viprakṛṣṭe tvanāgate ।।pratibhā kathyate yo arthe pratibhāso yathātatham ।।śravaṇaṃ sarvaśabdānāṃ śravaṇe cāprayatnataḥ ।।vārttā vārttāsu vijñānaṃ sarveṣāmeva dehinām ।।darśanaṃ nāma divyānāṃ darśanaṃ cāprayatnataḥ ।।tathāsvādaśca divyeṣu raseṣvāsvāda ucyate ।।sparśanādhigamastadvadvedanā nāma viśrutā ।।gandhādīnāṃ ca divyānāmābrahmabhuvanādhipāḥ ।।saṃtiṣṭhante ca ratnāni prayacchaṃti bahūni ca ।।svacchandamadhurā vāṇī vividhāsyātpravartate ।।rasāyanāni sarvāṇi divyāścauṣadhayastathā ।।sidhyaṃti praṇipatyainaṃ diśaṃti surayoṣitaḥ ।।yogasiddhyaikadeśe api dṛṣṭe mokṣe bhavenmatiḥ ।।dṛṣṭametanmayā yadvattadvanmokṣo bhavediti ।।kṛśatā sthūlatā bālyaṃ vārdhakyaṃ caiva yauvanam ।।nānācātisvarūpaṃ ca caturṇāṃ dehadhāraṇam ।।pārthivāṃśaṃ vinā nityaṃ surabhirgandhasaṃgrahaḥ ।।evamaṣṭaguṇaṃ prāhuḥ paiśācaṃ pārthivaṃ padam ।।jale nivasanaṃ caiva bhūmyāmevaṃ vinirgamaḥ ।।icchecchaktaḥ svayaṃ pātuṃ samudramapi nāturaḥ ।।yatrecchati jagatyasmiṃstatraiva jaladarśanam ।।vinā kumbhādikaṃ pāṇau jalasañcayadhāraṇam ।।yadvastu virasañcāpi bhoktumicchati tatkṣaṇāt ।।rasādikaṃ bhaveccānyattrayāṇāṃ dehadhāraṇam ।।nirvraṇatvaṃ śarīrasya pārthivaiśca samanvitam ।।tadidaṃ ṣoḍaśaguṇamāpyamaiśvaryamadbhutam ।।śarīrādagninirmāṇaṃ tattāpabhayavarjanam ।।śaktirjagadidaṃ dagdhuṃ yadīcchedaprayatnataḥ ।।sthāpanaṃ vānalasyā apsu pāṇau pāvakadhāraṇam ।।dagdhe sarge yathāpūrvaṃ mukhe cānnādipācanam ।।dvābhyāṃ dehavinirmāṇamāpyaiśvaryasamanvitam ।। f।etaccaturviṃśatidhā taijasaṃ paricakṣate ।।manojavatvaṃ bhūtānāṃ kṣaṇādantaḥpraveśanam ।।
parvatādimahābhāradhāraṇañcāprayatnataḥ ।।gurutvañca laghutvañca pāṇāvaniladhāraṇam ।।aṃgulyagranipātādyairbhūmerapi ca kampanam ।।ekena dehaniṣpattiryuktaṃ bhogaiśca taijasaiḥ ।।ākāśapiṇḍīkaraṇamaśarīratvameva ca ।।anilaiśvaryasaṃyuktaṃ catvāriṃśadguṇaṃ mahat ।।aindramaiśvaryamākhyātamāmbaraṃ tatpracakṣate ।।yathākāmopalabdhiśca yathākāmavinirgamaḥ ।।sarvasyābhibhavaścaiva sarvaguhyārthadarśanam ।।karmānurūpanirmāṇaṃ vaśitvaṃ priyadarśanam ।।saṃsāradarśanaṃ caiva bhogairaindraissamanvitam ।।etaccāṃdramasaiśvaryaṃ mānasaṃ guṇato adhikam ।।chedanaṃ tāḍanaṃ caiva baṃdhanaṃ ।।sargaḥ saṃkalpamātreṇa trāṇaṃ saṃharaṇaṃ tathā ।।svādhikāraśca sarveṣāṃ bhūtacittapravartanam ।।asādṛśyaṃ ca sarvasya nirmāṇaṃ jagataḥ pṛthak ।।śubhāśubhasya karaṇaṃ prājāpatyaiśca saṃyutam ।।catuṣṣaṣṭhiguṇaṃ brāhmamaiśvaryaṃ ca pracakṣate ।।bauddhādasmātparaṃ gauṇamaiśvaryaṃ prākṛtaṃ viduḥ ।।vaiṣṇavaṃ tatsamākhyātaṃ tasyaiva bhuvanasthitiḥ ।।brahmaṇā tatpadaṃ sarvaṃ vaktumanyairna śakyate ।। f।tatpauruṣaṃ ca gauṇaṃ ca gaṇeśaṃ padamaiśvaram ।।viṣṇunā tatpadaṃ kiṃcijjñātumanyairna śakyate ।।vijñānasiddhayaścaiva sarvā evaupasargikāḥ ।।niroddhavyā prayatnena varrāgyeṇa pareṇa tu ।।pratibhāseṣvaśuddheṣu guṇeṣvāsaktacetasaḥ ।।na sidhyetparamaiśvaryamabhayaṃ sārvakāmikam ।।tasmādguṇāṃśca bhogāṃśca devāsuramahībhṛtām ।।tṛṇavadyastyajettasya yogasiddhiḥ parā bhavet ।।athavānugrahecchāyāṃ jagato vicarenmuniḥ ।।yathākāmaṃguṇānbhogānbhuktvā muktiṃ prayāsyati ।।atha prayogaṃ yogasya vakṣye śṛṇu samāhitaḥ ।।śubhe kāle śubhe deśe śivakṣetrādike punaḥ ।।vijane jaṃturahite niḥśabde bādhavarjite ।। f।supralipte sthale saumye gandhadhūpādivāsite ।।muktapuṣpasamākīrṇe vitānādi vicitrite ।।kuśapuṣpasamittoyaphalamūlasamanvite ।।nāgnyabhyāśe jalābhyāśe ।।na jīrṇodyānagoṣṭhādau nāniṣṭe na ca niṃdite ।।nājīrṇāmlarasodgāre na ca viṇmūtradūṣite ।।nacchardyāmātisāre vā nātibhuktau śramānvite ।।na cāticiṃtākulito na cātikṣutpipāsitaḥ ।।nāpi viṣṭabhya cāgrataḥ ।।saṃprekṣya nāsikāgraṃ svaṃ diśaścānavalokayan ।।saṃbhṛtaprāṇasaṃcāraḥ pāṣāṇa iva niścalaḥ ।।svadehāyatanasyāṃtarviciṃtya śivamaṃbayā ।।hṛtpadmapīṭhikāmadhye dhyānayajñena pūjayet ।।mūle nāsāgrato nābhau kaṃṭhe vā tāluraṃdhrayoḥ ।।bhrūmadhye dvāradeśe vā lalāṭe mūrdhni vā smaret ।।parikalpya yathānyāyaṃ śivayoḥ paramāsanam ।।tatra sāvaraṇaṃ vāpi nirāvaraṇameva vā hemābhasya yathākramam ।।vakārādisakārāntā varṇāḥ parṇamayāḥ sthitāḥ ।। f। eteṣvathāraviṃdeṣu yatraivābhirataṃ manaḥ ।।tatraiva devaṃ devīṃ ca ciṃtayeddhīrayā dhiyā ।।aṃguṣṭhamātramamalaṃ dīpyamānaṃ ।।kṣityāditattvavijayaṃ dhyātā yadyapi vāñchati ।।tattattattvādhipāmeva mūrtiṃ sthūlāṃ viciṃtayet ।।sadāśivāṃtā brahmādyabhavādyāścāṣṭamūrtayaḥ ।।śivasya mūrtayaḥ sthūlāḥ śivaśāstre viniścitāḥ ।।ghorā muktirviśeṣeṇa śāṃtiḥ prajñā prasidhyati ।।sidhyaṃti siddhayaścātra kramaśo nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।oṃ iti śrīśivamahāpurāṇe saptamyāṃ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāmuttarakhaṇḍe yogagatau vighnotpattivarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ chapter upamanyuruvāca śrīkaṃṭhanāthaṃ smaratāṃ sadyaḥ sarvārthasiddhayaḥ ।।prasidhyaṃtīti matvaike taṃ vai dhyāyaṃti yoginaḥ ।।sthityarthaṃ manasaḥ kecitsthūladhyānaṃ tattaddhyāyetpunaḥ punaḥ ।।dhyānamādau saviṣayaṃ tato nirviṣayaṃ jaguḥ ।।tatra nirviṣayaṃ dhyānaṃ nāstītyeva satāṃ matam ।।buddherhi santatiḥ kāciddhyānamityabhidhīyate ।।tena nirviṣayā buddhiḥ kevaleha pravartate ।।tasmātsaviṣayaṃ dhyānaṃ bālārkakiraṇāśrayam ।।sūkṣmāśrayaṃ nirviṣayaṃ nāparaṃ paramārthataḥ ।।yadvā saviṣayaṃ dhyānaṃ tatsākārasamāśrayam ।।nirākārātmasaṃvittirdhyānaṃ nirviṣayaṃ sidhyaṃti devyāḥ śāṃtyādayaḥ kramāt ।।śāṃtiḥ praśāṃtirdīptiśca prasādaśca tataḥ param ।।śamaḥ sarvāpadāṃ caiva śāṃtirityabhidhīyate ।।
tamaso antabahirnāśaḥ praśāntiḥ parigīyate ।।bahirantaḥprakāśo yo dīptirityabhidhīyate ।।svasthatā yā tu sā buddhaḥ prasādaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।kāraṇāni ca sarvāṇi sabāhyābhyaṃtarāṇi ca ।।buddheḥ yastyajetprāṇāñchivabhaktārthameva vā ।।na tena sadṛśaḥ kaścinmuktimārgasthito naraḥ ।।tasmācchīghratarā muktistasya saṃsāramaṃḍalāt ।।eteṣvanyatamopāyaṃ kathamapyavalambya vā ।।ṣaḍadhvaśuddhiṃ vidhivatprāpto vā mriyate yadi ।।paśūnāmiva tasyeha na kuryādaurdhvadaihikam ।।naivāśaucaṃ prapadyeta tatputrādiviśeṣataḥ ।।śivacārārthamathavā śivavidyārthameva vā ।।khanedvā bhuvi taddehaṃ dahedvā śucināgninā ।। f।kṣipedvāpsu śivāsveva tyajedvā kāṣṭhaloṣṭavat ।।athainamapi coddiśya karma cetkartumīpsitam ।।kalyāṇameva kurvīta śaktyā bhaktāṃśca tarpayet ।।dhanaṃ tasya bhajecchaivaḥ śaivī cetasya santatiḥ ।।nāsti cettacchive dadyānnadadyātpaśusantatiḥ ।। f।
chapter śrīsūta uvāca iti sa vijitamanyoryādavenopamanyoradhigatamabhidhāya jñānayogaṃ munibhyaḥ ।।praṇatimupagatebhyastebhya udbhāvitātmā sapadi viyati vāyuḥ sāyamantarhito abhūt ।।tataḥ prabhātasamaye naimiṣīyāstapodhanāḥ ।।satrānte avabhṛthaṃ kartuṃ sarva eva samudyayuḥ ।।tadā brahmasamādeśāddevī sākṣātsarasvatī ।।prasannā svādusalilā prāvartata nadīśubhā ।।sarasvatīṃ nadīṃ dṛṣṭvā munayo hṛṣṭamānasāḥ ।।samāpya satraṃ prārabdhaṃ cakrustatrāvagāhanam ।।atha saṃtarpya devādīṃstadīyaiḥ salilaiḥ śivaiḥ ।।smarantaḥ pūrvavṛttāntaṃ yayurvārāṇasīṃ prati ।।tadā te himavatpādātpaṃtatīṃ dakṣiṇāmukhīm ।।dṛṣṭvā bhāgīrathī tatra snātvā tattīrato yayuḥ ।।tato vārāṇasīṃ prāpya muditāssarva eva te ।।tadottarapravāhāyāṃ gaṃgāyāmavagāhya ca ।।avimukteśvaraṃ liṃgaṃ dṛṣṭvābhyarcya vidhānataḥ ।।prayātumudyatāstatra dadṛśurdivi bhāsvaram ।।sūryakoṭipratīkāśaṃ tejodivyaṃ mahādbhutam ।।ātmaprabhāvitānena vyāptasarvadigantaram ।।atha pāśupatāḥ siddhāḥ bhasmasañchannavigrahāḥ ।।munayo abhyetya śataśo līnāḥ syustatra tejasi ।। tathā vilīyamāneṣu tapasviṣu mahātmasu ।।sadyastirodadhe tejastadadbhutamivābhavat ।।taddṛṣṭvā mahadāścaryaṃ naimiṣīyā maharṣayaḥ ।।kimetadityajānanto yayurbrahmavanaṃ prati ।।prāgevaiṣāṃ tu gamanātpavano lokapāvanaḥ ।।darśanaṃ naimiṣīyāṇāṃ saṃvādastairmahātmanaḥ ।।śaddhāṃ buddhiṃ tatasteṣāṃ sāṃbe sānucare śive ।।samāptiṃ cāpi satrasya dīrghapūrvasya satriṇām ।।vijñāpya jagatāṃ dhātre brahmaṇe brahmayonaye ।।svakārye tadanujñāto jagāma svapuraṃ prati ।।atha sthānagato brahmā tumburornāradasya ca ।।paraspara spardhitayorgāne vivadamānayoḥ ।।tadudbhāvitagānottharasairmādhyasthamācaran ।।gandharvairapsarobhiśca sukhamāste niṣevitaḥ ।।tadānavasarādeva dvāḥsthairdvāri nivāritāḥ ।।munayo brahmabhavanādbahiḥ pārśvamupāviśan ।।atha tumburuṇā gāne samatāṃ prāpya nāradaḥ ।।sāhacaryeṣvanujñāto brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā ।।tyaktvā parasparaspardhāṃ maitrīṃ ca paramāṃ gataḥ ।।saha tenāpsarobhiśca gandharvaiśca samāvṛtaḥ ।।upavīṇayituṃ devaṃ nakulīśvaramīśvaram ।।bhavanānniryayau dhāturjaladādaṃśumāniva ।।taṃ dṛṣṭvā ṣaṭkulīyāste nāradaṃ munigovṛṣam ।।praṇamyāvasaraṃ śaṃbhoḥ papracchuḥ paramādarāt ।।sa cāvasara evāyamitoṃtargamyatāmiti ।।vadanyayāvanyaparastvarayā parayā yutaḥ ।।tato dvāri sthitā ye vai brahmaṇe tānnyavedayan ।।tena te viviśurveśma piṃḍībhūyāṃḍajanmanaḥ ।।praviśya dūrato devaṃ praṇamya bhuvi daṃḍavat ।।samīpe tadanujñātāḥ parivṛtyopatasthire ।।tāṃstatrāvasthitān pṛṣṭvā kuśalaṃ kamalāsanaḥ ।।vṛttāṃtaṃ vo mayā jñātaṃ vāyurevāha no yataḥ ।।bhavadbhiḥ kiṃ kṛtaṃ paścānmāruteṃtarhite sati ।।ityuktavati deveśe munayo avabhṛthātparam ।।gaṃgātīrthesya gamanaṃ yātrāṃ vārāṇasīṃ prati ।।darśanaṃ tatra liṃgānāṃ sthāpitānāṃ sureśvaraiḥ ।।avimukteśvarasyāpi liṃgasyābhyarcanaṃ sakṛt ।।ākāśe mahatastasya tejorāśeśca ।।vārāṇasyāṃ tu yuṣmābhiryaddṛṣṭaṃ divi dīptimat ।।talliṃgasaṃjñitaṃ sākṣāttejo māheśvaraṃ param ।।tatra līnāśca munayaḥ śrautapāśupatavratāḥ ।।muktā babhūvuḥ svasthāśca naiṣṭhikā dagdhakilbiṣāḥ ।।prāpyānena yathā muktiracirādbhavatāmapi ।।sa cāyamarthaḥ sūcyeta yuṣmaddṛṣṭena tejasā ।।tatra vaḥ kāla evaiṣa daivādupanataḥ svayam ।।prayāta dakṣiṇaṃ meroḥ śikharaṃ devasevitam ।।sanatkumāro yatrāste mama putraḥ paro muniḥ ।।pratīkṣyāgamanaṃ sākṣādbhūtanāthasya naṃdinaḥ ।।purā sanatkumāropi dṛṣṭvāpi parameśvaram ।।ajñānātsarvayogīndramānī vinayadūṣitaḥ ।।abhyutthānādikaṃ yuktamakurvannatinirbhayaḥ ।।tato aparādhātkruddhena mahoṣṭro naṃdinā kṛtaḥ ।।atha kālena mahatā tadarthe śocatā mayā ।।upāsya devaṃ devīñca naṃdinaṃ cānunīya vai ।।kathaṃciduṣṭratā tasya prayatnena nivāritā ।।prāpito hi yathāpūrvaṃ sanatpūrvāṃ kumāratām ।।tadāha ca mahādevaḥ smayanniva gaṇādhipam ।।avajñāya hi māmeva tathāhaṃkṛtavānmuniḥ ।।atastvameva yāthātmyaṃ mamāsmai kathayānagha ।।brahmaṇaḥ pūrvajaḥ putro māṃ mūḍha iva saṃsmaran ।।mayaiva śiṣyate datto mama jñānapravartakaḥ ।।dharmādhyakṣābhiṣekaṃ ca tava nirvartayiṣyati ।।sa evaṃ vyāhṛto bhūyassarvabhūtagaṇāgraṇīḥ ।।yatparājñāpanaṃ mūrdhnā prātaḥ pratigṛhītavān ।।tathā sanatkumāro api merau madanuśāsanāt ।।prasādārthaṃ gaṇasyāsya tapaścarati duścaram ।।draṣṭavyaśceti yuṣmābhiḥ prāggaṇeśasamāgamāt ।।tatprasādārthamacirānnaṃdī tatrāgamiṣyati ।।iti satvaramādiśya preṣitā viśvayoginā ।।kumāraśikharaṃ merordakṣiṇaṃ munayo yayuḥ ।। chapter sūta uvāca tatra skaṃdasaro nāma sarassāgarasannibham ।।amṛtasvāduśiśirasvacchā gādhalaghūdakam ।।samaṃtataḥ saṃghaṭitaṃ sphaṭiko palasaṃcayaiḥ ।।sarvartukusumaiḥ phullaiśchāditākhiladiṅmukham ।।śaivalairutpalaiḥ padmaiḥ kumudaistārakopamaiḥ ।।taraṃgairabhrasaṃkāśairākāśamiva tatrāvatīrṇaiśca yathā tatrottīrṇaśca bhūyasā ।।snātaiḥ sitopavītaiśca śuklākaupīnavalkalaiḥ ।।jaṭāśikhāyanairmuṃḍaistripuṃḍrakṛtamaṃḍanaiḥ ।।virāgavivaśasmeramukhairmunikumārakaiḥ ।।ghaṭaiḥ bhaktimāpnoti bhakto bhaktisamṛddhibhāk ।।punaḥ śrute ca sadbhaktirmuktissyācca śruteḥ punaḥ ।।tasmātpunaḥpunaścaiva śrotavyaṃ hi mumukṣubhiḥ ।। pañcāvṛttiḥ prakartavyā purāṇasyāsya saddhiyā ।।paraṃ
